[kakawin sumanasāntaka,
#Awiǥnama astu#

<jagadđita>:1 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

%saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ pinakādidewa ni karas para kawi makatattwa ŋ akṣara,saŋ saṅkan paran iŋ palambaŋ atiduṙllaƀa kahanan ira n kawīśwara,saŋ sūkṣmê kukus iŋ tanaḥ kinikiṙ iŋ kuku ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ aṅrĕgĕp laṅö,māyākāra winimba nitya sinamāđi manurunana caṇḍi pustaka*1:1:1*

sambanđanya k aṅaṙccanê pada nirâhyun ajaṙ ajara milwa riŋ kawi,yekī kāraṇa ni ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti ri sira magawe namaskrĕti,luṅgaḥ niŋ kalaṅön sapuṅgĕl asĕkaṙ kakawin inuparĕṅgan iŋ laṅö,puṣpāñjalya ri jöŋ nira n sumanasāntaka caritakĕnâstu sanmatan*1:2:2*

pūṙwwaprastuti niŋ kaŧā hana sira dwija taruṇa suśīla subrata,śiṣyâgastya sira prakāśa karĕṅö kasutapan ira nora tan wruha,ꝁyātîŋ rāt trĕṇawindu nāma pinakesi niŋ ujaṙ ujaṙ iŋ kadewatan,sakweḥ niŋ hyaŋ anaṅśayê hyuna nirâṅadĕha ri paṅadĕg surāđipa*1:3:3*

ndan saŋ hyaŋ suranāŧa muꝁya pinakādi niŋ awĕdi manaṅśayê hati,lwiṙ tan duḥka sira ndan i twas awiweka riŋ aṅĕnana de niŋ olaha,gūḋākāra nira n wikalpa kadi tan hana panaha nahā nirâlaha,prāyê saŋ suyaśa n tĕka ŋ ƀaya sakêŋ musuḥ awĕdi kaciry-anâwĕdi*1:4:4*

wwantĕn rakwa warāpsarī linĕwiḥ iŋ sa haripada wagĕd wicakṣaṇa,prajña dyaḥ hariṇīṅaranya tuwi waṅśaja wĕka wĕka dewaputrikā,sākṣāt hrū nikaŋ indracāpa suƀagêṅid iṅidan i hayunya dug siṅī,Aṅhiŋ sāra hiḍĕp hyaŋ indra śaraṇāśraya paṅalaha śakti niŋ tapa*1:5:5*

yekī rakwa kinon hyaŋ indra marĕkâṅucap ucapa rahasya riŋ taman,śīǥrânĕmbaḥ acum wulat nika sinuṅsuŋ iŋ ujaṙ amanis priyambada,Om putrī saŋ anĕmwa kāṣṭaguṇan aṅhilaṅakĕna kaśaktin iŋ tapa,Aṅhiŋ māsku sinamƀawâsiha paṅöbana niŋ aśaraṇêŋ kadewatan*1:6:6*

wwantĕn brāhmaṇa sidđiśakti magawe tapa katĕka tĕkêŋ surālaya,maṅde saṅśaya ni ṅhulun ndan alĕmĕḥ katĕṅĕra ri wikalpa niŋ hati,saŋkṣepanya lumampahânaku mamañcana maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,Eñjiŋ māsku lumakwa wörakĕna riŋ hima sumiliba tan hana wruha*1:7:7*

nāhan de nira mojaṙ asru paṅutus nira lumarisa tan wruḥ iŋ ƀaya,kepwan dyaḥ hariṇī katon gĕgĕḥ i suṅsut ira yadin apakṣa laṅǥana,rĕs lāwan pagĕḥ iŋ kaƀaktin ika kāraṇa niki n uƀaya n lumampaha,paṅgil paṅhwata janma liŋnya sĕḍĕṅanya karahatana riŋ pamañcanan*1:8:8*

mantuk dyaḥ hariṇī manĕmbaḥ i surendra ri wijila nikā madandana,Eñjiŋ maṅkat akañcugâdarupa ƀūṣaṇa nika pinasaŋnya tūt hĕnū,tan kwâmbĕknya lumampa lampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kasusu laku nikâṅhade hade,denyâđaṙmma ri de nirâṅutus amiǥnanana tapa tatan hanâṅrwaṅi*1:9:9*

ṅūni n pamwit i jöŋ surendra mamĕgĕŋ taṅis inimuṙ imuṙ kinölakĕn,maṅke n sāmpun adoḥ lakunya wĕnaŋ aṅlĕpasakĕna taṅisnya riŋ hawan,lagy-ânambatakĕn laranya kasihan pati sĕsĕl anĕsĕl purākrĕta,tūt māṙggāmbara luḥnya tan papĕgatan drawa kadi titis iŋ maṇik bañu*1:10:10*

kāṅĕn denya katuhwan iŋ giṇa mamiǥnani tapa wipaŧâgawe hala,yadyastun kawaśā pira ŋ suꝁa tĕmun yan amuhara hala ndya don ikā,mwaŋ yan tan kawaśā katon tĕtĕp i śāpa nira paṅawaśanya tan wuruŋ,kodāsīnan irêka ta pwa pinalaṙ palaṙ ika siha saŋ hyaŋ īśwara*1:11:11*

mampĕḥ mātra laranya luḥnya pinakembuḥ i manis i matanya yan wulat,luṅsuṙ luṅsuṙ ikaŋ tapiḥ pinakatambĕḥ i raras i tĕṅaḥ nikâlaris,hrĕknyâlwan ya samaṙ samaṙ tuna tunâmuwuhi manis i de nikâṅucap,Aśrī waṙṇna nikâṅĕliḥ wĕnĕs ikâṅhalĕpi kadi wĕnĕs niŋ abrata*1:12:12*

luṅhā lampaḥ ikânĕlat ri hirĕŋ iŋ gagana hanan awās hanan samar,rĕp mukṣânusup iŋ rĕmĕŋ kadi wulan lumaku kasaputan lamad lamad,lwiṙ wintaŋ sumurup katonan ika riŋ wĕkasan asĕmu maṙmmakê kapö,rĕm niŋ meǥa tinūtakĕnya manicip nicipi jawuḥ awaṙṇna cātaka*1:13:13*

rāmyanya n pamĕgat laṅit lĕpas adoḥ tĕka ri sadawatā nikaŋ limut,Agyā de ni panas hyaŋ aṙkka karaṇanya n alisuḥ atawĕŋ tawĕŋ hima,prāpta ŋ truḥ sumaput praƀāwa ni lakunya wahu mari huyaŋnya kāṅinan,tūt gaṅgâhawan indracāpa tumurun lari nika suꝁa mampiṙ iŋ wukir*1:14:14*

watw-ânuṅgul amaṙwwatâhrit aguhâtupis atiba tiban latāṅkura,ṅkā teka n dumunuŋ lukaṙ ni darupanya pinahayu lugas siniṅsĕtan,tistis tan hana tīṙŧayātra wiku śakty-atapa katĕmu śūnya kewala,Aṅhiŋ handiwa handiwâgarawalan katĕmu marĕk anuṅsuŋ iŋ guyu*1:15:15*

priṅgâtyanta ruhuṙnya mānuṣa paran wĕnaṅa mara ri doḥnya duṙggama,ṅhiŋ saŋ paṇḍita saŋ huwus tumĕmu ŋ aṣṭaguṇa sira wĕnaŋ marêrika,hetu dyaḥ hariṇī wĕnaŋ mara kajanman ika saꝑala dewakanyakā,lĕṙ denya n tumurun sawaŋ garagatī tumurun ahawan antiḥ antihan*1:16:16*

tiṅhalnyâbayaṅan mamet i patapan saŋ atapa parananya bañcanan,riŋ winđyācala rîndrakīla salĕbak wukiṙ ika pinaran katuṅkulan,mwaŋ riŋ rewatakāgra ganđamadanādri masamun apa tan hanâtapa,hetunya n ƀramitâpĕgâkuliliṅan kadi pakalaṅan iŋ niśākara*1:17:17*

lambuŋ niŋ himawān kidul hana ta paṙwwata śuci patapan hañaṙ katon,tumraŋ teja nika praƀāwa nira saŋ sutapa tilaka niŋ jitendriya,Aṅlīlâṅililan pahoman ira söḥ kukus ika maṅadĕg nirantara,lwīṙ oṅkāra mawindunāda kadi hĕnwa nira hĕlĕm anĕmwa śūnyatā*1:18:18*

budđi dyaḥ hariṇī tumiṅhal irikaŋ patapan asĕmu haṙṣa niścaya,byaktâwās trĕṇawindu ta pwa makapājaran iki liŋ ikânĕhĕṙ marĕk,līlâṅambaḥ i hambal iŋ jalada saŋsaya samaṙ asamun hibĕk jawuḥ,miṅsoṙ lwīṙ ahawan turun turunan iŋ gupura suꝁa hanan kadînulur*1:19:19*

prāptêŋ paṙwwata śūnya kaywan ika pakṣa wukiṙ asĕgĕḥ iŋ hañaṙ ḍatĕŋ,haṙyyan mwaŋ hujuṅan sakêŋ pisaŋ alasnya rumarasaḥ amet kalālatā,sakweḥ niŋ wulakan sumaṅgraha bañunya walahaṙ ika pakṣa sāgara,jaṅgâṅambĕki pakṣa kasturi waṅinya hinaturakĕn iŋ drĕs iŋ barat*1:20:20*

wahw-âron anak iŋ pakis haji katon sukĕt i pasusupanya duṙggama,sakweḥ niŋ kayu nora tan pagati de niŋ anila tĕka riŋ trĕṇāṅkura,ndan trāsâsĕpi tan paron kapanasan paḍa ragas amalaṙ malaṙ jawuḥ,waṅkal seṅwan alīt alīt bataŋ agöṅa hĕlĕm i paṅadĕgnya riŋ juraŋ*1:21:21*

lwiṙ tan pahyaŋ ikāŋ alas hana giraŋnya wahu linawad iŋ warāpsarī,tapwan maṙmma dahat panuṅsuŋ ika kewala kusuma yayā maweḥ suꝁa,lumrâkweḥ tumibêŋ gĕluŋ kadi tinap sawaŋ aṅit aṅitan sĕkaṙ taji,kady-âṅĕmbaŋ akon aṅantya pakamaṅgala nika tanĕmĕn ya dewatī*1:22:22*

lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ talagânamaṙ tasik anak tuna tuna kawi nora maṅlĕṅĕŋ,paṅgaŋ wwadnya kakumbaḥ iŋ bañu suluṙnya wahu mĕtu satuŋtuŋ iŋ tanaḥ,I groŋ groŋ i pasiṙ pasiṙnya mawatu dyan aniru niru piṇḍa niŋ karas,līlâṅanti darā putiḥnya kadi śaṅꝁa maduluṙ aṅurambat iŋ hĕnī*1:23:23*

ṅkā ta dyaḥ hariṇī marâdyus amĕḍaṙ tĕṅaḥ abuṅaḥ amawwahan gaḍiŋ,māliḥ ṣaṭpada niŋ saroruha maliwran i wĕtis ika kesisan tapiḥ,romanyâwilĕtan marê susu nikâniru niru rakĕt iŋ lumut lumut,kĕmbaŋ niŋ kumudâṅliliṙ kadi tinaṅhi winulatan ikâṅdadak mĕkar*1:24:24*

<jagadnāŧa>:2 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^ri sāmpun ika mĕntas aṅliga ligā kadi taman aśarīra dewatī,titis titis ikaŋ wĕhaŋ satitis iŋ bañu wulakan anumbĕṙ iŋ paras,lumöŋ amiluluk gaḍiŋ kahudanan susu nika kasarambahan bañu,sirat ni bañu niŋ gĕluŋ kinirab aṅhiribi kukus i sāri niŋ puḍak*2:1:25*

titis ni mađu niŋ mađubrata baṅun lĕṅa waṅi humaḍaŋ hanêŋ śilā,pawitra hana tīṙŧa niṙmmala sumaṅgraha ri harĕp awaṙṇna pahyasan,hrĕbuk hrĕbuk i kĕmbaŋ iŋ sarasijâsĕmu hawu hawu muṅgu riŋ cupu,hirĕŋ ni kucup iŋ trikañcu sumĕlat kadi sipat awawan puḍak puḍak*2:2:26*

lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ kaṅelan apa tan tahu mahas ahas iŋ wanāśrama,sĕkaṙ niŋ asanâmayuŋ kuniŋ apiṇḍa mamayuṅana kāla niŋ panas,paḍâṅrĕs atatā ŋ wuluḥ kadi harĕp tĕkĕnakĕna tan intaṙ aṅhaḍaŋ,gaḍuŋ kadi kamāsihĕn paḍa lumuŋ baṅun aharĕp anuntunêŋ hĕnū*2:3:27*

huwus tĕka riŋ āśramâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ry-ulaha nika mĕne n panĕmbaha,nĕhĕṙ lumaku muṅgaḥ iŋ gupura saṅśaya manaha nahā marê dalĕm,Aluṅguḥ irikaŋ bukuṙ paṅaraṅanya nĕhĕṙ asidĕhâṅure gĕluŋ,cĕcĕk masahuran sakê wuri pinakpak ika pinakadūta niŋ hala*2:4:28*

<nawahaṙṣa>:3 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^ƀagawān trĕṇawindu sĕḍĕŋ ajapa nitya śiwasmaraṇa,Asamāđi kumöl katĕmu hĕniŋ i budđi nira n humĕnĕŋ,dwija śukla suśīla sira pinakadaṙśśana riŋ patapan,kadi wꜽṣṇawawimba pawulatan ira n pamutĕṙ guduha*3:1:29*

I rare nira ṅūni hati nira hibĕk sukĕt aṅrahabi,Inĕnö ni rajaḥ tamaḥ ira karaṇanya n aron asĕwö,Atuha pwa sira wruḥ aṅaji guṇa niŋ guru nora kari,hana sattwaguṇâmaṅani sukĕt i budđi nira n patapa*3:2:30*

wijayêŋ patapan dwijawara makasāđana yoga nira,Anukūla ri jöŋ nira sahana niŋ indriya nora wani,Aṇimā laǥimādi kakaratala de ni samāđi nira,kamumukṣuhan aṅhaḍa marĕk akĕliṙ swaśarīra nira*3:3:31*

ri huwus ni samāđi nira linĕsu rakwa harĕp mijila,Anĕlat rarab iŋ rĕrĕb aṅuraṅi tan panĕlĕs harĕpan,larap iŋ kilat iŋ gagana kadi dinĕmwan aganti lumöŋ,paṅapö ni gĕrĕḥnya kadi mamisiki n hana wāhu ḍatĕŋ*3:4:32*

<jagadnāŧa>:4 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^mijil muniwarâhawan hĕniŋ i budđi nira laku nirâṅhade hade,pijĕṙ mulat i posik iŋ jalađi rāmya tĕpi nika katuṅku tuṅkulan,ri tiṅhal ira riŋ bukuṙ saŋ araras winulatan ira maṅligā ligā,ya kāraṇa nira n parâgarawalan saŋ ahayu tumuluy madan tapiḥ*4:1:33*

saŋ ugratapa niṙwikāra tamuyan wĕkas iŋ ahayu riŋ kadewatan,salaḥ sĕmu manis manis nira baṅun manis iŋ anĕmu mitra riŋ hĕnū,dudū suꝁa nira n mulat paḍa lawan suꝁa niŋ atamuyan kadaŋ kadaŋ,Ikaŋ turida rāga sāmpun amatĕḥ milu milu mamiratyakĕn manaḥ*4:2:34*

Aniṅsĕti hĕniŋ ni budđi nira śudđa ni basahan ira n siniṅsĕtan,subadđa daluwaŋ siṅī pinakabadđa nira pamađa riŋ rajaḥ tamaḥ,samaṙ tura turaḥ ni ƀasma nira paṅgĕsĕŋ ira wiṣayâtĕmaḥ hawu,jamaŋ kadi mahā taraṅtaṅĕn i sampĕt ira huwus anampĕtîndriya*4:3:35*

marĕk sira sulakṣaṇâdara maṅakṣama kamĕna nira n paluṅguha,katon upaśamâtalaṅkup aṅagĕm kayu kanaka supattralepana,tamuy nira masewa đaṙmma pakatonan i manaḥ ika ƀakti kewala,prasidđa guru śiṣya rūpa nira kāliḥ i papupul irêrikaŋ bukur*4:4:36*

Anĕmbaḥ ikaŋ apsarī mĕtu rarasnya tan asarag aṅambĕk ambĕki,lĕmĕs ni luṅayanya kāliḥ ajajaṙ kadi pĕpĕsa kahambĕŋ iŋ susu,laris ni jarijinya sāmpun atalaṅkup inayat inamĕṙ marêŋ muꝁa,Amatyakĕn i raśmi raśmi ni liriŋnya n api miṅay aṅīrakĕn wulat*4:5:37*

lanâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt dwijeśwara tumon hayu nika winiweka riŋ hati,tulis kanaka wahw-inuṅkaban aṅāśraya ri buṅaḥ ika n paƀūṣaṇa,Ahadyan ahĕnĕŋ nĕhĕṙ masidĕhâsĕmu taruban i kāla niŋ gawe,yadin haliwatêŋ saƀā tan alaraŋ halĕpakĕna maḍampa mās tatur*4:6:38*

sinaṅśaya nirâlumâluñuta mađya nika kulayĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,suśūnya winaliŋ nirêmwa gamĕlĕn ri kahiḍĕpan ikôṇḍuḥ oṇḍuhan,wĕtisnya kadi maṙwwi maṅgarita paṅkwakĕna kahiḍĕpanya de nira,muꝁanya gumawaŋ ya rakwa tinahâlwaṅa hilaṅa ri kāla niŋ tilĕm*4:7:39*

hyaŋ iŋ nagara kālasan pawulatanya n anuruni rikaŋ wanāśrama,mađubrata baṅun pinañjiṅan ikâṅidĕri salaga mĕtta riŋ sĕkar,puḍak kadi panĕmpa nĕmpahan ikâsĕmu maniliha lambay iŋ ṭikā,Amānuṣa hayunya kenaka nikâmulaṅunakĕna riŋ jitendriya*4:8:40*

kayogyan iŋ apiṇḍa ratna liniṅiṙ saparana nika ta pwa hĕmbanĕn,hade kumĕḍapa n wulat yan aṅadĕg tĕhĕṙ aṅadĕga tan paluṅguha,yadin lukara kenya tan wruḥ amahaywa kahalĕp ika denya n aṅligā,sawaŋ sawaŋ iŋ aṅhĕmū guyu kapantĕs ika pamapaganya riŋ wulat*4:9:41*

<basantatilaka>:5 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^Āścaṙyya budđi ƀagawān trĕṇawindu denya,ndātan hana hyun ira mātra sumöṅa riŋ twas,kewalya susŧira manaḥ nira tan prapañca,maswāgatâmanis ujaṙ nira sāṙjjawâtwaŋ*5:1:42*

rakryan kṣamākĕna kamîbu paran kitâri,strī tan wruḥ iŋ ƀaya ri duṙggama niŋ wanādri,Aṅhiŋ katon kita wĕnaŋ mara niṙwikāra,prāptâṅĕnĕs maniluman baṅun indrajāla*5:2:43*

Āsĕṅka ni ṅhulun i māsku tĕkanta maṅko,strī niŋ wiśeṣapuruṣa praƀu cakrawaṙtti,tan saḥ kinuṇḍaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ niŋ aburwa burwan,ndā ṅke n katĕmwa samayanta lawan priyanta*5:3:44*

strī tan pađaṙmma ta kunaŋ kita kāri śoka,swāminta tan pahamĕṅan kawi tan pawasŧa,Ambĕkta wikwa manusup nusupêŋ alas göŋ,sambin hiḍĕpta wulikĕn palarĕn katĕmwa*5:4:45*

Anwam kunaŋ kita katuṅhapan iŋ bapebu,muṅgw-iŋ kadaŋ maṅupapīra maweḥ larâmbĕk,māṙgganta lampus aṅusiṙ wanadeśa śūnya,Ahyun lumakwa wiku kilya rarā wiratya*5:5:46*

hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ āśrama kunaŋ kita diwyacakṣuḥ,wruḥ riŋ jitendriya sadābrata tan kĕnêŋ strī,budđinta moǥa mawĕlas mulat iŋ daridra,prāptânurun paran ikā paṅanugrahanta*5:6:47*

rakryan hiḍĕpku ri hayunta sakêŋ wanādri,Ambĕt ni sinwam iŋ aśoka marê tĕṅaḥta,molaḥ kadînĕluk ĕluk luŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ mrik,tan saḥ katon i luṅayanta lĕmĕs lĕmĕsnya*5:7:48*

Amraŋ baŋ iŋ katiraḥ aṙjja hanê laṭinta,tuñjuŋ birū mĕkaṙ alurw-akusū suganđa,māliḥ lurunya mamanis kawawê matanta,mimbâmarāśraya tikĕlnya hanê halista*5:8:49*

polaḥ nikaŋ kusumasāri hanê wiwalta,maṅgiṣṭa wāhu rinĕmĕk tumibê kĕcapta,paṅhrĕŋ nikaŋ ƀramara muṅgw-i taṅis taṅista,hīs niŋ tusāra rumarab makajanma luḥta*5:9:50*

sandeha budđi mami de ni halĕpta māsku,dūra n manuṣya kita kewala dewaputrī,de niŋ manaṙkka ri ḍatĕŋta mahāpraƀāwa,saṅkê hyaŋ indra mapa donta waraḥ kamîbu*5:10:51*

nāhan panaṙkka nira maṙmma dahat rasanya,mambö tilam kadi huwus wruḥ i rumrum iŋ strī,śrĕṅgāra dewaduhitā kawĕlad hatinya,maṅgĕḥ ri budđi ƀagawān kĕna bañcananya*5:11:52*

<Akrĕti>:6 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^suraputrikā sumahuṙ ādara mulat awiraŋ tumuṅkul anaṅis,ƀagawān rĕṅön pawaraḥ i ṅhulun aṅusiṙ aṅāśrayê kadi kita,taha tan sakê surapati n ḍatĕŋ aṅĕnĕs amet pradeśa wĕgilĕn,mwaŋ asamƀawa n hyaṅa niŋ āśrama panaha nahā dwijeśwara hade*6:1:53*

tuwi tan manuṣya maniwi praƀu maduluṙ aburwa burwa riŋ alas,hayu ni ṅhulun taha tan antuk iŋ aṅalap alap sakêŋ giriwana,riŋ apa n rarâharĕpa wikwa manusupa manĕmbahêŋ wiku talun,pisaniṅw-ajalwa kawi mūṙcꞓita layat alaṅö manambaŋ anadin*6:2:54*

ƀagawān manĕḥta huniṅan humulunakĕn awaknya tan patĕbusan,tuwi hetu niŋ mara ri jöŋ dwija taruṇa ƀaṭāra đaṙmma maṅutus,I ratĕŋ nikaŋ brata samāđi kakawaśa tĕkapta sāmpun amatĕḥ,mĕtu tan pasaṅkan inucap wulatana tariman ṅhulun ꝑala nika*6:3:55*

hyaṅĕn i ṅhulun ri pada saŋ dwija taruṇa kaśudđyanôtus utusĕn,pisanīṅw-anĕṅgaha mĕne n pasuruhana sĕkaṙ lawan bañu damu,marĕkêŋ paturwan aṅisapwakĕna suku munīndra riŋ pakasutan,tan asamƀawa n hulun anaṅhuluna yan apuyĕŋ dwijaṙṣi majapa*6:4:56*

Arĕnaḥ tĕkapnya n aṅucap kama riŋ ujaṙ amiǥnani brata tapa,mata mesi luḥ saha taṅis winulatakĕn ikā wineḥ amanisa,Ajajaṙ pasaṅgraha nikā susu waṅi ni pipinya lāgi sumaji,kadi pādapâṅliḥ alaris tĕṅaḥ ika pasĕnāha ri dwijawara*6:5:57*

Umĕnĕŋ dwijaṙṣi rumase wacana nika tĕkā waśâṅhamu hamu,smaradūta kewala manisnya n aṅucap ataṅis lanâmĕlas arĕp,wĕkasan dwijendra wihikan ry-aƀimata nika yan pamiǥnani tapa,mĕtu kadwijātyan ira nora kawĕdi nira sāhasânapaŧani*6:6:58*

<jagadnāŧa>:7 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^Aḍā wipaŧa ko pakojaṙ iku đūṙtta tan aharĕp i haywa niŋ tapa,huwus wruḥ aku yan pakona suranāŧa karaṇamu ḍatĕŋ mamañcana,Ikaŋ hala gawemu tan wuruŋ amaṅsulana malĕsanêri ko mĕne,manuṣya tĕmahamwa tan waluya riŋ surapada wĕkasamwa dewatī*7:1:59*

yadin śatasahasraƀāgan i suꝁaṅku n ataki taki niṣparigraha,taŧāpi kapana n samaṅkana suꝁaṅkwa k aṅusira suꝁêŋ surālaya,hana pwa suꝁa niŋ manuṣya masamāgama mapa ta gawe nikâđama,lĕhĕŋ juga ŋ anĕmwa pātaka sakêŋ katuduhana kabañcanâtapa*7:2:60*

nahan liŋ ira sāhasâṅḍawuhi śāpa nĕhĕṙ anudiṅî kiwâṅdĕlö,prapañca surakanyakā kahilaṅan hurip apĕga ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,ri doṣa nika rāga rāga n aṅusiṙ sutapa pisaniṅūn kabañcana,Alum kadi gaḍuŋ pinuṅgĕl aṅayuḥ sĕkaṙ iŋ asana tan wuruŋ pĕjaḥ*7:3:61*

tumuṅkul i harĕp dwijaṙṣi makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ nira,hanan kadi waśâṅdĕlö nĕhĕṙ aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ surālaya,mĕhāḥ salahasâtĕpak jaja manĕmbaḥ aḍĕkuḥ amalaṙ kasanmata,Apan harĕp iŋ antaśāpa karaṇanya n aṅucap amanis maṅañjali*7:4:62*

dwijaṙṣi huripĕn ṅhulun titisanâmrĕta waluyakĕnêŋ kadewatan,Ĕmās maṇik anekawastu kĕta ŋ enaka panĕbusa ni ṅhulun hurip,ṅhulun pwa kasihan muwaḥ syapa pametana pirak i rikaŋ tapowana,mataŋnya k anaṅis panĕmbaha ri jöŋta panĕbusa ri jīwa ni ṅhulun*7:5:63*

tuhanku ƀagawānku hāḥ sipi lalista wulatana manĕḥta kāsy-asiḥ,harĕp muliha tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ aṅantya ri kita kita melik i ṅhulun,Unĕŋ niŋ abapebu tiṅhalana denta mapa karika hetu niŋ hĕnĕŋ,kĕdö harĕp anona māti kĕna śāpa karika kita tan wruḥ iŋ wĕlas*7:6:64*

Ahā mpu wihikan ṅhulun ri wuyuṅanta kalalarana śudđa niŋ tapa,kṣamākĕna manĕḥta tan tugĕtananta sakasalaḥ i śīla ni ṅhulun,prasidđa kita paṇḍitânumata riŋ wiguṇa wipaŧa tan wruḥ iŋ krama,si sĕmbaḥ ika jampya niŋ kadi kita n lumĕkasa wuyuŋ iŋ kadi ṅhulun*7:7:65*

kucup niŋ asanâluru ndan amalaṙ karirisana ri taṅgal iŋ kapat,gaḍuŋ lumay aṅolakĕn tawaŋ aluŋluṅan amalaṙ anĕmwa rambatan,hĕlaŋ midĕṙ anambayaŋ saha taṅis kapanasan amalaṙ drĕs iŋ jawuḥ,ṅhulun pwa kalaran mataŋnya k amalaṙ turunana wara de dwijeśwara*7:8:66*

Ahā pahalawö ta koŋ awakana ŋ kapalaŋ alaŋ i demu n apsarī,kadaŋ kadaṅa de bapebu pĕkulĕmwa paḍa kari sirêŋ kadewatan,pĕjaḥ ṅaran iki syapêka ta taṅis taṅisana mulatâsihêri ko,wĕlasku ri hayunya sis mapa tikī hamĕṅana niki yan pĕjaḥ mĕne*7:9:67*

ƀaṭāra suranāŧa tiṅhalana de nrĕpati kasiḥ arĕp patik haji,huwus kalĕmahan śināpa kapana n maluya muwaḥ i pāda saŋ praƀu,hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥ surāđipati tan wuruṅa pĕjaha riŋ pamañcanan,riŋ āśrama wĕkas ni jīwita patik haji wiꝑala pakon surāđipa*7:10:68*

praƀu praƀu rĕṅön taṅis ni hariṇī kapĕgan aputĕk aṅhiḍĕp lara,pĕjaḥ pinatiwaṙ kinonakĕn i tan kawĕnaŋ ika gawe dinohakĕn,Ikaŋ gati śināpa sis ya katahā ya katĕmu tuluṅĕn patik haji,pati pwa balik iŋ hurip lara lalis pwa balika ni wĕlas surāđipa*7:11:69*

wijil sahana saŋ hyaŋ iŋ kusuma wāhu sumalaga nihan lawad ṅhulun,hurip gĕlisa ni ṅhulun ya palakunta ri yatiwara haywa tâsuwe,kunaŋ yan agĕgĕḥ dwijaṙṣi palalun sawuyuŋ ira sadenya saṅkulĕn,tuhun kita lumĕṇḍwa lĕṇḍwa ri śawaṅku gĕsĕṅĕn i pañaṇḍi niŋ wuṅū*7:12:70*

manis ni mata ni ṅhulun labuhĕn iŋ jalađi luḥ irikaŋ tasik mađu,raras ni waja ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ śrigaḍiŋ i pucak iŋ gunuŋ gula,lĕmĕs ni lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun lĕpasĕn iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅĕliḥ aṅolakĕn tawaŋ,laris ni wĕtis i ṅhulun kĕkĕsananta kĕmitana ni dèwa niŋ puḍak*7:13:71*

kĕlab ni tapiḥ i ṅhulun suji ya teki pupulakĕn i posik iŋ sĕkar,pataṅkis i giriṅsiŋ i ṅhulun aṅantya ri lĕṅĕŋ i kiriñciŋ iŋ bañu,pĕnĕd ni laku ni ṅhulun tan asarag waluyakĕna ri lampaḥ iŋ liman,pĕpö ni panaṅisku tan kahuniṅā ḍawuhakĕna ri śabda niŋ cucur*7:14:72*

Ameta maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kita pamorana ni kusut i roma ni ṅhulun,ri mimba ni taman ta paṅlĕpasananta ri rĕṅu ni halisku yan tikĕl,gĕmuḥ ni susu ni ṅhulun wahu mijil tuhañaṅakĕna riŋ pucaŋ gaḍiŋ,wĕnĕs ni muꝁa ni ṅhulun hañutĕn iŋ wulan inĕmukan iŋ lamad lamad*7:15:73*

pamādapa ni mađya ni ṅhulun aros kirimakĕn iŋ aśokapādapa,Ĕbun hana ri tuŋtuŋ iŋ trĕṇalatāṅkura patuwawanê luḥ i ṅhulun,lawan pañurigênunus ni paṅawakku rakĕtakĕna denta riŋ tulis,luṅid ni kuku ni ṅhulun turuŋ aṅanya ri jaja jajaṙ iŋ sĕkaṙ taji*7:16:74*

nahan śruti ni de nikânaṅis atuŋtuŋ ucapan amĕlas mĕlas harĕp,samasta para dèwa sūkṣma humĕnĕŋ tinaṅisan ika tan hanâṅlawad,Arĕs hawa hawākĕnâwĕdi kumöl wruḥ i gĕgĕḥ i wuyuŋ dwijeśwara,paḍâṅrĕs anaṅis naṅis taṅis ikā piniturun ika muṅgu riŋ waneḥ*7:17:75*

taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ kusuma sūkṣma tinaṅisakĕn iŋ mađubrata,taṅis niŋ amarāśrayêŋ wulan awā tinaṅisakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur,taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ jalada cātaka manaṅisakĕn hanêŋ tawaŋ,taṅis taṅis i dèwa niŋ masa kapat tinaṅisakĕn i gĕntĕṙ iŋ patĕr*7:18:76*

muwaḥ dyaḥ anu mojaṙ asrĕt ucapanya tuna tuna sinambaṅan taṅis,mpu ḍaŋ hyaŋ apa tāḥ inanti ni manĕḥta paṅuṣađa ri duḥka ni ṅhulun,yatan hana hineṙ manĕḥ dwijawarâsiha humuripana ṅhuwus pĕjaḥ,kṣamākĕna magöŋ ṅhulun mpu warahĕn duga duga mara tan harĕp harĕp*7:19:77*

nahan rasa ni de nikânaṅis aminta winaluyakĕn iŋ kadewatan,Uđāni ƀagawān paṅawruhana de nira mulat amanis wawaŋ lipur,Apuy siniram iŋ jawuḥ paḍa ni suṅsut ira tan agĕgĕḥ wawaŋ paḍĕm,sĕrĕḥ waṅi lawan duḥ iŋ wwaḥ aramĕs ri waja paḍa ni de nirâṅucap*7:20:78*

paran karika tan sihaṅkwa ri kitânaku kita karikâpan uttama,manuṣya tuwi sāwakanya yan atön mara mara hiniḍĕp kadaŋ kadaŋ,kunaŋ saŋ agawe laranta paramāṙŧa nira sira ƀaṭāra śaṅkara,lukat ni kapalaŋ nikaŋ sukrĕta māṙgga ni kapalaŋ i denta dewatī*7:21:79*

priyanta riŋ anādijanma dadi mānuṣa lituhayu sūṙyyawaṅśaja,narendra raǥu rakwa mānak aniru prakaśita suƀagêŋ purāntara,Apañjy-aja đanuṙdđarânwam isi niŋ raǥunagara turuŋ smarātura,tuhun kita dine ƀaṭāra yugalanya muwaḥ akurĕnâsihê kita*7:22:80*

kunaŋ pwa siha ni ṅhulun ri kita tan kalawasana dadinta mānuṣa,Aṅālihana kapraƀun kita lawan saŋ aja suꝁa sarājya tuṅgalĕn,tuhun pamĕkasanta wīja sawijîrika kita maluyêŋ kadewatan,sĕkaṙ sumanasântakanta ya tikâmĕgatakĕna ri śāpa ni ṅhulun*7:23:81*

huwus pwa kita mantuk iŋ surapadânaku katĕka tĕkêŋ wwaluŋ tahun,samaṅkana narendra saŋ kawĕkas iŋ nagara muliha riŋ kadewatan,Apaṅgiha muwaḥ lawan kita tumĕmwakĕna ꝑala nikaŋ kadigjayan,mataŋnya pahayun manaḥta suꝁamāṙgga matĕmahana rājaputrikā*7:24:82*

nahan rasa ni de nirâmĕgati śāpa nira tĕhĕṙ ajaṙ satorasiḥ,ri mūla ni dadinya len tĕmahananya tinalataḥ irâgalaṙ taṅan,kunaŋ pwa wĕkasan hiḍĕpnya ri kaśāpa nika kadi wineḥ anugraha,Unĕŋnya matĕmaḥ luḥ adrĕs i kapö lara turida nikâtĕmaḥ taṅis*7:25:83*

<jagadđita>:8

^hāḥ saŋ mukṣa ri luḥku tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pasaṅgaman,maṅke pwâmbĕka niŋ prahāsana bisâṅhari hariḥ iŋ arĕs pinaṅkwakĕn,ṅūni n hyaŋ kita riŋ surālaya manĕḥta milu matĕmahan warāpsarī,maṅke pwâṅdadi rājaputra kita heṙ ṅhulun atĕmaha rājaputrikā*8:1:84*

hāḥ swāmiṅku dudut ṅhulun ri juraŋ iŋ lĕpihan alal aṅölakĕn laṅö,hĕmban riŋ wwat aśokapādapa tĕṅaḥku pagamĕlana luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,suŋsuŋ riŋ maṅunĕŋ galuḥ lulut unĕṅku ri kita kaka tan wĕnaŋ kinas,riŋ paṇḍan haḍaṅĕn ṅhulun lumaku śoka laku laku ṭikâhawan puḍak*8:2:85*

nāhan ṅrĕs ṅrĕs i samba sambat ika kāsihan alal apasaḥ lawan priya,tan siḥ niŋ wiđi moǥa tan patuluṅan karaṇa nika manĕmwakĕn lara,de niŋ gyānya tumĕmwa janma saŋ aniṅgalakĕn iriya riŋ kadewatan,Amwit matya manĕmbaḥ iŋ dwijawarânĕhĕṙ aṅusapi luḥnya riŋ sabuk*8:3:86*

<jagadnāŧa>:9 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^huwus praṇata ƀakti tan paśaraṇāśraya mati lumaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,humuŋ taṅis i sundarī nikaŋ alas hinariwuwu ni śabda niŋ gaguŋ,rĕrĕb kusumasāri tan papĕgatan kĕtug i tĕḍun iŋ eṙttalîŋ juraŋ,luŋ iŋ gaḍuŋ aṅindracāpa humaḍaŋ hawana nika madadya mānuṣa*9:1:87*

hyaŋ agni hana riŋ śarīra mijil aṅgĕsĕṅi śawa nikâgilaŋ gilaŋ,kasidđyan ira saŋ dwijaṙṣi gumawe dilaḥ ika karaṇanya n ujwala,bukuṙ pamiḍaran ndatan milu gĕsĕŋ kadi jalada rinĕṅgan iŋ kilat,samantaji paḍĕm tuhun hana kukusnya kari sakukus iŋ damaṙ pĕjaḥ*9:2:88*

hayunya milu ƀasmiƀūta tĕka riŋ gĕluŋ ahawuk amiṇḍa riŋ kukus,lumöŋ wa nikaŋ asŧi mātra kadi śeṣa ni luru ni matanya yan wulat,baṅun tura turaḥ nikaŋ sipat ikaŋ latu latu tumibā paḍâhirĕŋ,hilaŋ siniriṙ iŋ samīraṇa hawunya tumuluy anarīra riŋ hrĕbuk*9:3:89*

<jagadđita>:10 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ hyaŋ niŋ suraloka tan pahamĕṅan namu namu pĕjaḥ iŋ pamañcanan,sūkṣmâṅjanma marêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī sira ta pinakasāri niŋ sarāt,putrī śrī kraŧakeśikeśwara nĕhĕṙ hayu nira kadi ṅūni n apsarī,ꝁyāti śrîndumatī panaṅgaḥ i sira n pamuꝁa kadi śaśaṅka pūṙṇnama*10:1:90*

lwīṙ iŋ swapna wijil nirâdƀuta karĕṅwan i wali nira riŋ kadewatan,rĕmrĕm taŋ daśadeśa de ni sahab iŋ jaladakusuma muṅgu riŋ tawaŋ,lĕŋlĕŋ de ni gĕrĕḥnya ṣaṭpada maliwran apupul irikaŋ limut hrĕbuk,sumyuk taŋ mađupuṣpawaṙṣa maduluṙ jaya jaya ri jayā nrĕpātmajā*10:2:91*

ṅūni n tuṅgal anak nareśwara lawö manaḥ ira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā,ndātan pembuḥ ikaŋ suꝁê sira baṅun bañu humidĕŋ aṅanti riŋ ranu,maṅke n pembuḥ anak nirâhayu sinamƀawa maṅadĕha lakṣmi niŋ purī,Embuḥ göŋ kadi sāgara rwab amĕpĕk suꝁa nira ri wijil nrĕpātmajā*10:3:92*

rakryan saŋ pinakeña rakwa kulawaṅśa wĕka wĕka kadaŋ kadaŋ haji,Aśrī waṙṇna nirâraras kadi saroja kinĕlabakĕn iŋ ṙyyak iŋ bañu,de niŋ mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki saƀāwa nira tĕka hirĕŋ kineriṅan,suswan bāhwan agasyak aṅhalĕpakĕn wruḥ iŋ aṅinakanê tuhan tuhan*10:4:93*

lāwan towi nirâhalĕp marĕka hadyana kunaŋ asawaŋ priyambada,ndan paṙṇnaḥ kaka de nirêña nira karwa sira paḍa suśīla wīṙyyawan,kāliḥ kāliḥ irâṅharis haris anuswani rahina wĕṅî suputrikā,saṅkêŋ swaṙgga hulun tuhâṅgĕḥ ira ṅūni ri hana nira riŋ kadewatan*10:5:94*

wwaŋ ri jro juru niŋ mĕṅĕs pinarĕk iŋ wagĕd amirit i hatwik iŋ manis,sakwan selwan atūt manaḥnya kalawan kabayan iŋ arĕjêŋ kaguṇḍikan,tuṅgal riŋ katĕkāsihan lawan ikaŋ pinuji pinakagusti riŋ raras,rūm rakryan nrĕpaputrikā mawa hayunya tuhu ratu ni raśmi niŋ prajā*10:6:95*

strī māwak caturaṅga saƀya tan aŧāni panagara tĕkâhawan raŧa,prāyâpāmbĕkan aśwasañcari lakunya wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ liman,nistanya n wiparīta rūpa nika tan kasaḥ i pada narendraputrikā,himpĕṙ peka minantryakĕn huwus aƀūṣaṇa hinalĕpakĕn yayâhala*10:7:96*

rakryan rājasutânwam eṅgal atuhâṅiṅĕt iṅĕtakĕn aṅdĕlö tawaŋ,Aṅliŋliŋ kinahaṙṣan iŋ kaka kakâmwaṅi sira rinĕbut pinaṅkwakĕn,kahyun hyun kumurĕb kurĕb kumĕdal asriŋ aniru niru putra niŋ pĕñu,wahw-âhuntw-aputiḥ katon sĕḍĕŋ irâsĕmu guyu baṅun aṅhĕmū mĕnur*10:8:97*

solaḥ ƀāwa nirâmaṅun siḥ aṅĕwaḥ bapa bapa juga de nirâṅucap,yan paṅjaṅkaḥ aṅaṅguḥ aṅguhi gumoḥ lumaris asĕmu lĕmbu kanyakā,mogâhyaŋ sira yan maluṅguḥ ararĕm tumiru tiru paluṅguḥ iŋ gaṇa,yan sore mulat iŋ wulan wruḥ awawā wulan anuduhi wimba niŋ wulan*10:9:98*

Endaḥ budđi nikaŋ waneḥ mamitaṅis mitaṅis i sira haṙṣa riŋ taṅis,Eṅgal mary-anaṅis pinakpak amanis wulat ira sinawe pinaṅkwakĕn,len tekaŋ harĕp iŋ halâhala halan mamalaku hala hāsyakāraṇa,maṅkin tībra raras narendratanayâhayu ri huwus ira n paweḥ ala*10:10:99*

Anwam tapwan apâsarik hayu nirân inaṅĕtan apupuk ri wunbunan,tan paṅde hala tambĕḥ iŋ hayu bajaŋ bajaŋ ira mata niŋ lawak bulu,pantĕs yan pagĕlaŋ lawe wĕnaŋ i kāla nira kapĕjahan rare bajaŋ,tambā niŋ sĕgu tuŋtuŋ iŋ sĕrĕḥ aṅimbuhi manis ira yan hanê rahi*10:11:100*

ndi nyū danta paḍā mĕne n lĕwiha yan marĕk i sira sĕḍĕŋ pinaṅkwakĕn,lāwan ketaka dūra n aṅhiriba nista nika n inuparĕṅgan iŋ ṭikā,sakweḥ niŋ kusumâwĕnĕs pinakataṇḍiŋ ira wawaŋ alum sakêŋ taṅan,maṅgĕḥ de niŋ anuswanî sira dudū lawan anak anakan sinuswakĕn*10:12:101*

Eṅgal wruḥ tinitaḥ bisâtaratayan wĕgig aṅadĕg adĕg wawaŋ tibā,guywan wruḥ makukuk bayan tinañakĕn kahanan ira bisâtukup mata,sorêsuk malĕbū lĕbū cala kinon ahuwusana ya saṅkan iŋ taṅis,haṙṣânon gigirĕn sirâṅgyat anĕpak bisu bisu nĕhĕṙ aṅgigiṙ gigir*10:13:102*

dudw-aṅkĕn wĕṅi de nira n wruḥ aṅucap mari bisu bisu saŋsayâbĕnĕr,sāmpun rakwa sirâpupak pinakapūṙwwaka nira n aṅajî munīśwara,prajña wruḥ ri kalīṅa niŋ pada kadi wruḥ alawas anulus wicakṣaṇa,Eṅgal paŧya ri kaprayogan i rusit niŋ aji kadi tĕmaḥ saraswatī*10:14:103*

Umwat śīǥra tuwuḥ nirâhayu sawaŋ salaga niŋ asanâṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,tapwan wruḥ riŋ iraŋ dahat kalukaran tapiḥ awuda wudâgĕlaŋ gĕlaŋ,tan pendaḥ lĕṅĕŋ iŋ wuluḥ gaḍiŋ i kāla ni pamilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,mambĕt mađya nirâwĕlū buṅaḥ i waṙṇna nika kadi giliŋ giliŋ kuñit*10:15:104*

niṙwā tan paguṇa ŋ pupuṙ pinakapahyas ira tĕwas aweḥ kram iŋ muꝁa,dūrâṅhaywana tan padon sipat irâṅlĕtuhi ri hĕniŋ iŋ matâbiru,lāwan taŋ paṅĕluk lĕṅĕn wiꝑala yeka karaṇa ni halis nira n tikĕl,wyaṙŧâŋ tūlahanânukĕṙ nukĕri tan wuruŋ amaṅunakĕn srĕt iŋ susu*10:16:105*

sumraŋ sraŋ mata wahw-atön ri lĕṅĕŋ iŋ gĕrĕḥ aṅirim irim lawan riris,Aṅlūd ry-ambĕk ira n rimaŋ taṅis ikaŋ ƀramara kalilipĕn saḍĕk hrĕbuk,yan sore ri huwus nirâhawu hawu wruḥ amawa kalaṅön irêŋ natar,Aṅhĕmban karas esi ƀāṣa pinakānak anakan ira tan saḥ iŋ tanaḥ*10:17:106*

piṇḍa dwādaśawaṙṣa kāla ni wijil nira rumara rara n hanê dalĕm,yan paṅhyas hyasi moǥa tan kawanĕhan tiniru tiru sade nirâṅhyasi,sotan ta ṅhyaŋ iŋ indraloka kapana n tan apĕnĕda tĕmaḥnya mānuṣa,lakṣmī niŋ nagarâhulap mulat i rūpa nira n ahayu katwaŋ iŋ tulis*10:18:107*

miṅkil tapwan agöŋ payođara nirâṅlĕwihi buṅaḥ i tuŋtuŋ iŋ gaḍiŋ,hyaŋ hiŋ tāman aṅiṇḍarat sĕmu ni rūpa nira n ahayu muṅgu riŋ taman,tistis lālana tan hanâṅiriṅakĕn laku nira kadi tan tuhan tuhan,molaḥ sumpiŋ irâsanâlum awĕnĕs baṅun awĕdi ri luñcip iŋ mata*10:19:108*

paṅrāt niŋ kalaṅön tinurwakĕn irêŋ watu karaŋ aṅilo wway iŋ ranu,tan śoƀā humiriŋ lumaḥ makakaraŋ hulu lĕṅĕn ira mūṙcꞓitâṅligā,paṇḍan raṅkaŋ aṅöbi tan panisi mātra ri sira n apulaŋ lawan hrĕbuk,Amrĕm karwa karas lĕṅĕŋ kadi ṭikā piniturun inamĕṙ sakêŋ puḍak*10:20:109*

maṅkin maṙmma narendra māsiḥ anĕkāni samaṅinakanê manaḥ nira,budđi śrī parameśwarī suꝁa makānak i sira samanaḥ nirênariḥ,maṅke n tan hana wahw-atakwan ahiḍĕp nrĕpati tĕka sirâṅhĕmū guyu,maṅgĕḥ budđi nirâjajaṙ lawan anak nira baṅun aṅabehi jīwita*10:21:110*

saŋ ƀojânak irâtuhâpagĕḥ ikaŋ guṇa ri sira paṅawruḥ iŋ ratu,sākṣāt prāṇawa Īśwara nrĕpati kāsiḥ ira sira suśīla nītimān,Aṅhiŋ rakwa pakö nareśwara ri ƀūmi nira sira sadā janapriya,maṅgĕḥ rowaŋ irâṅadĕg ri hiḍĕp iŋ mulat i suꝁa nira n paḍâpagĕḥ*10:22:111*

ndan griŋ saŋ praƀu saŋsayâbwat atĕlĕb maṅinak inaki tan tulus waras,tĕṅrān iŋ hurip iŋ śarīra paḍa rūkṣa mawaraḥ i tĕkā nikaŋ pati,yekā hetu nirâṅutus marĕka riŋ dwijawara rĕṣi śꜽwa sogata,mwaŋ mantrī winĕkas wĕkas nira n anak nira sumiliha ratwa haywa len*10:23:112*

sakweḥ saŋ winĕkas wĕkas paḍa tĕñuḥ twas ira kahĕnĕṅan mulat juga,de niŋ duḥka tumon i kāsy-asiḥ i saŋ kawĕkas ira dumeḥ sirâsiha,mojaṙ mātra pĕgat pĕgat wĕkasan amriḥ asayut amĕlas mĕlas harĕp,luḥ lāwan sĕkĕl iŋ taṅis duluṙ i de nira sumahuṙ i śabda saŋ praƀu*10:24:113*

he nāŧaṅku huwus kapaṅku wacana nrĕpati rasa nirâwĕkas wĕkas,An saŋ ƀoja gumantya ratwakĕna yadyapi pĕjaha mĕne nareśwara,ndan lwiṙ wyaṙŧa ḍawuḥ ni śabda naranāŧa ri sama marĕk aṅlawad lawad,Āpan ṅhiŋ sira keṅĕ keṅĕt alawas kumalilirana kapraƀun haji*10:25:114*

śaktin de naranāŧa haywa lĕsu saŋ praƀu tahapana wedya kinkinĕn,śrī dewîndumatī katoliha katon uwuḥ uwuha nira n katiṅgala,mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja sirânwam aṙdđa kapalaŋ wĕkasakĕna narendra riŋ prajā,ndān amriḥ mriha saŋ praƀu syapa parāśrayana sama marĕk mĕne n kari*10:26:115*

nāhan liŋ sama maṅlawad lawad i saŋ praƀu lara nira membuḥ aṅlare,wahw-âṅlumpuhi saŋsayâmaṅĕti roga nira wawaŋ alum sirâwĕnĕs,tan polaḥ sira tan kĕḍap ṅuni ṅuni n paṅucapa sira kewalâturū,ṅhiŋ maṅguḥ kalawan miṅĕl sahuṙ ira n tinaña tañan i de nirâlara*10:27:116*

satya śrī parameśwarī tan awĕdîŋ pati tumuta ri līna saŋ praƀu,ndan dewîndumatī tinoliḥ ira kāsy-asiha nira mĕne n katiṅgala,mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja paḍânwam anwam anaṅis paḍa wihikan i tībra saŋ praƀu,kāliḥ kāliḥ irâpupul tinaṅisan pinĕkul ira nĕhĕṙ sinuṅkĕman*10:28:117*

Ꜽ ƀojaṅku wĕkaṅku haywa tan asiḥ kita bapa riy arinta kāsihan,putrīṅkw-indumatīṅku ƀaktya ri kakanta kita sarika samƀawâsiha,Anwam kāri tuhanku deṅku kawĕkas riŋ iña lawan uwâmalaṙ tuha,himpĕṙ hantiga niŋ manuk taḍahasiḥ sy-anaku tinuwawākĕn iŋ waneḥ*10:29:118*

wuṅsw-amwīta bibinta matya tumutê kapati saŋ ahulun ṅhulun tuhan,lwâmbĕk māsku saŋ aprihêŋ ƀuwana sĕmbahĕn iŋ amawa rāt kitânaku,Ꜽ putrîndumatīṅku māsku t ahurup tapiḥ alaḥ ibu kenku kenakĕn,soŋsoṅaṅkwa tapiḥta karwana lawan haji lĕpasa mamukṣa mukṣana*10:30:119*

sĕmbaḥ ni ṅhulun alpađaṙmma ri padadwaya paramawiśeṣapaṇḍita,pun dewîndumatī kayatnakĕna de wiwuđapati bapebwa māsiha,mwaŋ saŋ ƀoja muwaḥ wuruk wurukĕn iŋ nagara palaṙ aniṙwwa saŋ praƀu,waṙṣājñāna parâđipaṇḍita dumadyakĕna kawijayanya riŋ prajā*10:31:120*

nāhan liŋ parameśwarī tucapa saŋ praƀu kasiḥ arĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,saŋ hyaŋ jīwa hanê gulū nira lawan kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira saŋsayâsamun,sāmpun kāku pasāra sāra ni waraḥ yatiwara rinĕgĕp nareśwara,tan simpaŋ kadi de nirâṅayatakĕn panaḥ aṅĕnani de nirâṅhiḍĕp*10:32:121*

trĕṣṇābanđana riŋ śarīra pinĕgat nira manaḥ ira kewalâhĕniŋ,sadyotkranti linakṣyakĕn pataṅananya tumutupana simpaŋ iŋ hĕnū,lāwan mantra nikā ndatan dwa sira saŋ praƀu wiƀu riŋ awak wawaŋ mĕsat,kewalyâśraya sūkṣma māri kahiḍĕp mamarĕṅi śiwamāṙgga dug mĕṅā*10:33:122*

sāmpun māti nareśwarâtri sakaḍatwan anaṅisi pĕjaḥ nirâlara,śrī dewîndumatī muwaḥ tinaṅisan kapati lumay awak nirâwĕnĕs,mādan śrī parameśwarī marĕk anĕmbaḥ i śawa haji satya sādara,mājaṙ yan sira milwa matya pawaraḥ nira karaṇa ni luḥ niŋ aṅrĕṅö*10:34:123*

he nāŧaṅku nihan ṅhulun praṇata ƀakti tumuta saparanta tan saha,yadyastun kita dewatâŧawa manuṣya huluna pakĕnaṅkwa de haji,putrī putra rarā sĕḍĕŋ mĕrĕ mĕrĕḥ kaŧamapi tan ikā katoliha,patrĕmta praƀu yeki haṇḍĕmana ni ṅhulun amaḥ aku suŋsuŋ iŋ hĕnū*10:35:124*

nā liŋ śrī parameśwarī nĕhĕṙ apatrĕm amĕkasi hurip sirâsĕgu,himpĕṙ waṙṣa tibā nikaŋ luḥ i widaṙbƀanagara humilī mawaḥ wahan,sambat sambat ikaŋ sarājya gumĕrĕḥ kadi kĕtĕṙ i gĕrĕḥ niŋ ampuhan,tawwan riŋ kusumâṅjraḥ iŋ masa kapat paḍa ni taṅis ikā n rinĕṅwakĕn*10:36:125*

prāpta ŋ truḥ kadi sĕmbu sĕmbuṙ i jajâṅawara ri gĕmuḥ iŋ payođara,waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ apiṇḍa pupuk i rahi keṅgutan halis,polaḥ niŋ kilat iŋ tawaŋ kadi kĕḍap niŋ asamaya kapaṅgihêŋ taman,his hīs niŋ bañu muṅgu riŋ tarĕtĕpan kadi luḥ iŋ anaṅis pinaṅkwakĕn*10:37:126*

muṅgw-iŋ maṇḍyusa kāli kāliḥ ira moǥa kadi kinasut iŋ pasaṅgaman,keṅĕṙ mātra gulū narendramahiṣī kadi cala cala tan panūt kinol,piṅgiṙ niŋ kanin iŋ jajâsĕmu miraḥ kadi karagĕt i tuŋtuŋ iŋ kuku,rāhĕn siñjaŋ ira n lume miṅay awaṙṇna wahu kawawa de nareśwara*10:38:127*

śrī dewîndumatī lĕwĕs lara nira n panaṅis asidĕhâṅure gĕluŋ,mambĕt mađya nirâṅgaluṅgaŋ araras tĕṅaḥ ira sumawe ri saŋ pĕjaḥ,tan kewran lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ wijil i luḥ nira tan inusapan hanê muꝁa,sambat sambat irâṅrĕmĕk hati rasanya karaṇa ni taṅis niŋ aṅrĕṅö*10:39:128*

<jagadnāŧa>:11 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^Ahā bibi haji ndi siḥta winaliṅku ta kita tulusâsihê ṅhulun,muwaḥ bapa haji ndi siḥta palakunkwa tulusa ni wĕlasta ri ṅhulun,Ujaṙtta kita ṅūni kāsihana niŋ jagat anaku sadā pakāśrayan,jagat karika māsihêry-aku kita pwa paḍa tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn*11:1:129*

praƀuṅku kita kāliḥ ĕndi parananta pawuṅu sakarĕŋ waraḥ ṅhulun,yan iŋ śiwapadâŧawêŋ haripadâŧawa lĕpasa kunaŋ sakêrikā,ṅhulun tumuturâpa don iŋ ahurip wiꝑala yan apasaḥ lawan kita,patiṅku hawanaṅkwa muṅsiṙ i padanta bapa tañakĕnêŋ kadewatan*11:2:130*

pulaḥta humĕnĕŋ diṅaryan asagaṙ ndi kari culu culuḥta ri ṅhulun,nihan ṅhulun anakta paṅkwakĕn aḍâtiśaya bapa kita n huwus pĕjaḥ,prayojana ni deṅkw-asambat akusā baribinana kita n paḍâturū,palaṙ palaṙ awuṅwa de ni panaṅisku nĕhĕṙ ajara māsku cĕp tuhan*11:3:131*

nihan tĕtĕlakĕn hatiṅku bibi muṅgaḥ akĕsĕl ahĕnĕk tĕkê jaja,muwaḥ priḥ i mataṅku tīsana rahup rahupana bibi bawwa bawwana,pilī piliṅan i ṅhulun dumadak aṅhĕlu pupukana tulya tulyana,guluṅku kadi meḥ kahötana rasanya n anaṅis i patinta sĕmburĕn*11:4:132*

ri kāla ni huripta ṅūni bibi sāhasa kita sahasâṅabĕt ṅhulun,hasiḥ bapa hajî ṅhulun tĕka sirânuluŋ aṅusapi luḥ mamaṅkwakĕn,mataŋ ya bibi maḥ palu ṅhulun alaḥ pawuṅu sakaharĕp ṅhulun habĕt,ndya sī yan anuluŋ muwaḥ bapa hajî ṅhulun atĕhĕṙ ataṅguhê kita*11:5:133*

syapêka śaraṇāśrayaṅkwa ri pĕjaḥta bapa haji nihan dudut ṅhulun,Apan kaka turuŋ wĕnaŋ śaraṇa ni ṅhulun apituwin anwam iŋ wayaḥ,kadaŋ kadaŋ adoḥ sirâsiḥ alĕbâmihutaṅanana sī kadi ṅhulun,mataŋ yan anakanta riŋ suruwayan ṅhulun alaḥ alapĕn maran pĕjaḥ*11:6:134*

Aḍā hyaŋ aparan ta koŋ wiđi ṅaranmu tan awĕlas adĕṅky-anon suꝁa,bapaṅku sira māti demu mapa doṣa nira huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,lawan bibi tumūt prasidđa tika ko muwaḥ amĕjahi tan pakāraṇa,mataŋ ya wĕtu ko rwa sānak aku patyani saha bala demu hĕntyakĕn*11:7:135*

<jagadđita>:12 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^nāhan sambat irânaṅis kaḍĕḍĕtan lara hati nira tan wĕnaŋ kinöl,simsim wāhu hilaŋ maṇiknya kalĕbū paḍa paḍa nira niṣpraƀâkucĕm,dady-âteja katonan iŋ rahina tan parawi wĕṅi tiniṅgal iŋ wulan,saṅkê rūpa nirâsawaŋ karĕbahan gunuŋ alara ri līna saŋ praƀu*12:1:136*

paṅde niŋ wiđi tan wĕnaŋ winađa tiṅhalana kasiḥ arĕp suputrikā,kāry-anwam ri pĕjaḥ nareśwara samaṇḍyusa sira kalawan nareśwarī,de niŋ duḥka kĕdö sirâmalaku milwa maṅatigana maṇḍyusê dalĕm,patrĕm wahw-inunus nirênayatakĕn ri jaja kaka kakâkrak aṅrĕbut*12:2:137*

maṅkin ǥūṙṇnita śabda niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis wĕdi kaluputanêŋ nrĕpātmajā,Āpan budđi nirâṅhuwus huwus apakṣa pĕjaha tumutê nareśwara,göŋ trĕṣṇâsiḥ arāma rena kapĕgan kapati pati sirâlarânaṅis,drāk sidđânĕmu duḥka niŋ dadi manuṣya paṅawaśa ni śāpa saŋ rĕṣi*12:3:138*

saŋ ƀoja prihati n tumon kasiḥ arĕp ny-awak ira kari de nareśwara,kady-agriŋ sira de ni duḥka nira tan saḥ anaṅis i dagan narāđipa,Āśāƀūta marambĕhan wĕtu ni luḥ nira mulat i narendrakanyakā,maṙmmâmaṅku pĕgat pĕgat sapitutuṙ nira tuna tuna de nikaŋ taṅis*12:4:139*

rakryan haywa wiraṅrwaŋ induŋ ĕnĕbĕn ta pamanas i laranta tīsakĕn,riŋ swaṙggasŧa narendra sāmpun atuhâpituwi huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,pakṣa kṣatriya rāka rakryan apagĕḥ wĕnaṅa śaraṇa rakryan iŋ hayu,ṅhiŋ yan māti kakanta mamriḥ iŋ ayun kita pĕjaha tumūta ri ṅhulun*12:5:140*

haywâśâlara duḥka yan bapa haji mwaŋ ibu haji pĕjaḥ sirâdulur,yāwat janma ṅaranya tan hana tuwuḥ watu kaluputa saṅka riŋ pati,tan pendaḥ kadi cakra niŋ raŧa tĕka ŋ dadi niyata midĕṙ puriḥ nika,saṅkêŋ mrĕtyu tĕka ṅhurip kunĕŋ ikaŋ pati niyata mijil sakêŋ hurip*12:6:141*

māyākāra hanêŋ crĕmin paḍa nikaŋ dadi sahana hananya tan sŧiti,himpĕṙ pādapa tan wuruŋ manirarâmĕkasi tuha tuwuḥnya tan lanā,tiṅkaḥ niŋ hurip iŋ manuṣya juti tattwa nika tan alawas wawaŋ hilaŋ,kintw-îkaŋ pati jāti tattwa nika tan kṣaṇika pinakađaṙmma niŋ dadi*12:7:142*

Eman ṅwaŋ lumĕkas mamet pati sakêŋ lumĕkasa ri kapetan iŋ hurip,pöŋpöṅĕn ta huripta yogya dadahanta makahuluna de munīśwara,Āpan yan wruḥ i ƀeda saŋ rwa kalawan wruha ri pasamudāya niŋ tiga,Icꞓā nora kasaṅśayêŋ hala lawan hayu niyata luput sakêrika*12:8:143*

<wisaṙjjita>:13 
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 20

^kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hayu nikaŋ hayu yan gawayĕn,ri wruḥ i saŋ rwa ƀineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn,kumwa kunaŋ liṅa rakryan apa hala nikaŋ hala yan gawayĕn,ri wruḥ i saŋ rwa ƀineda lawan i sira saŋ tri tinuṅgalakĕn*13:1:144*

siṅgiḥ ujaṙtta ri saŋ krĕtasamaya wiśeṣa paṅawruḥ ira,kweḥ nira riŋ nagarêŋ acala paḍa tikā pinakoṅgwan ira,ndin rakĕta ŋ suꝁaduḥka ri sira satatâbrata tan palabuḥ,lokaparāśraya kāraṇa nira magawe hayu tan wipaŧa*13:2:145*

saŋ wruḥ i saŋ wĕkas iŋ samaya winuni de paramādiguru,kewala śudđa manaḥ nira linĕtu lĕtuḥ kapanâlĕtuha,wāhyaśarīra pinucꞓa nira ri tĕka niŋ pati tan ginĕgö,jñāna wiśeṣa śarīra nira taya śarīra nirêŋ wĕkasan*13:3:146*

wwaŋ magawe hayu yan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hayu,tan dadi tan luput iŋ hayu hayu ni gawe nika tan wiꝑala,wwaŋ magawe hala yan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hala,tan dadi tan luput iŋ hala hala ni gawe nika tan wiꝑala*13:4:147*

wwaŋ magawe hayu tan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hayu,tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhayu hayu ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ,wwaŋ magawe hala tan wruḥ i sira saŋ amukti gawenya hala,tan dadi tan tumĕmu ṅhala hala ni gawenya tumūt maṅiriŋ*13:5:148*

saŋ wiku gūḋa nihan wulatana mamaṅan tĕḍa riŋ pahĕhan,tan tĕḍa tan śuci ta pwa sahana hana niŋ pinaṅan liŋ ira,hetu nirâmbĕk alokika winulatan ajrĕm apiṇḍa kasop,śudđa nikaŋ pratipatti makalarapan uttama niŋ samaya*13:6:149*

māsku mataŋnyan ikaŋ hayu gawayakĕnanta sĕḍĕŋ mahurip,paṇḍita towi yayā sira maṅulahakĕn brata tan kaluṣa,budđy-ahĕniŋ brata yoga tapa taki takinta maran kawaśa,gĕgwana rakryan anĕmwakĕna wara waraḥ paramādiguru*13:7:150*

<girisa>:14 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^Anĕmu nĕmu kĕtêkā saŋ sāmpun krĕtasamaya,wihikan i rasa saŋ hyaŋ tattwajñāna kalĕpasĕn,tan uliḥ uliḥ iŋ aṅdoḥ saṅkêŋ pāda muniwara,Uliḥ iŋ asaṅu tasyan ƀaktîŋ paṇḍita matuha*14:1:151*

Aṅinak inaka taŋ wwaŋ yāwat jñāna pinakadon,syapa ta sira mamaṅgiḥ tattwajñāna dudu gawe,hana satata masewā tan byaktanya pinihanan,sukrĕta juga maṅinte lāwan duṣkrĕta maṅiriŋ*14:2:152*

hana sira guruputrânak niŋ paṇḍita nagara,sahana nira ta rakwâdrĕwya ŋ jñāna pakagurun,taha tan ika panidđan wet niŋ paṇḍita matuha,Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ tattwêŋ uṅgwana rahayu*14:3:153*

Anak iŋ apirak akweḥ ṅūnî nwamnya paḍa suꝁa,sahana nika ta rakwânirw-akweḥ apirak ika,taha tan ika panidđan wet niŋ śreṣṫa panariman,Amilihi juga saŋ hyaŋ śrī tan siŋ kahanan ira*14:4:154*

kita yayi sĕḍĕŋ anwam priḥ saŋ hyaŋ rasa kawikun,pira karika musuḥ niŋ wikw-aṅhiŋ nĕm ikaŋ akas,Alahakĕn i dalĕm twas pet siŋ soṅgwan ika raraḥ,Alaha pĕjaha rakryan yêki swaṙgga ṅaran ika*14:5:155*

<basantatilaka>:15 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^nā de nirâwara waraḥ ri narendraputrī,tapwan tĕtĕs tinuna sanđi nikaŋ prayoga,Anwam suśīla guṇamanta krĕtopadeśa,saṅkê paṅajyan ira kawruḥ irâđiguhya*15:1:156*

śrī putrikā kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕŋ tumuṅkul,sāmpun ƀinasmi śawa saŋ praƀu de munīndra,muṅgw-î taman sira cinaṇḍi lawan sudewī,sampūṙṇna bapra nira ratna mahāpraƀāwa*15:2:157*

saŋ ƀoja sāmpun aṅadĕg ri widaṙbƀarājya,swasŧā saƀūmi nira ƀakty-anukūla sāđu,mawwat paḍâmarahakĕn ri suꝁanya rakwa,Anwam muwaḥ nrĕpati liŋnya muwaḥ manĕmbaḥ*15:3:158*

sāmpun sirâyugala ratna wiśeṣaputrī,rājāṅkurâwilĕt ikaŋ pakurĕn sawanđu,soluṙ lulut sahati lĕŋlĕŋ aluŋluṅan kuŋ,saśrī sakĕmbaŋ alaṅö sakurā sawīja*15:4:159*

kaywan ragas paḍa nikaŋ nagarî widaṙbƀa,riŋ wrĕdđarūpa haji dewata lahru sākṣāt,maṅke n prasidđa kadi kaywan aron akĕmbaŋ,śrī ƀoja maṅdani sirânwam apiṇḍa rĕŋrĕŋ*15:5:160*

wet niŋ krĕtā ri paṅadĕg haji nora duṣṭa,rāmya ṅhĕnū tĕgal ayun tĕka riŋ wanādri,wāni ŋ wwaŋ aṅhaliwatîriya tuṅga tuṅgal,Aṅhiŋ gaḍuŋ luŋ ika maṅhabĕt asriŋ oliḥ*15:6:161*

mantrī nirâtuha tuha dwija śꜽwa bodđa,kāsiḥ kapaṙccaya narendra wĕnaŋ marê jro,prajñêṅgitajña ginulaŋ halu riŋ wiweka,sojaṙ niŋ āgama tinūt nira tan wimāṙgga*15:7:162*

söḥ śāla đaṙmma kuṭi kīṙtti narendra riŋ rāt,wwaŋ śreṣṫi đaṙmma ginawe nira sāri sāri,wwaŋ duṣṭa moǥa kapitūt milu đaṙmmabudđi,solaḥ swaƀāwa haji tan dadi tan tinūtnya*15:8:163*

śrī ƀoja sāmpun apagĕḥ siniwîŋ kaḍatwan,Okĕṙ tumiṅhal i saŋ indumatī hanê jro,Āpan samāsa niŋ akaṙmma wayaḥ nirâgöŋ,Aṅhiŋ swayĕmbarakĕnêṅĕt iṅĕt narendra*15:9:164*

nā de nirâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt kalawan sudewī,sāmpun wināhyakĕn irê kulawanđu ri jro,riŋ saṙwwasidđi tuwin amrĕtayoga tĕmbe,höman hajînarahakĕn para taṇḍa mantrī*15:10:165*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:16 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^Eñjiŋ śrîndumatī kinon marĕka kāliḥ saŋ sunandâṅiriŋ,lāgy-âmūṙṇnama mopawāsa ya ta maṅde suṅkawā niŋ hati,tistis meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu lumampaḥ tan kwa de niŋ harip,mukṣa lwīṙ amarāśrayê muꝁa nira śrī niŋ wulan tan lumöŋ*16:1:166*

sāmpun prāpta sirê dalĕm praṇata maṙmmâtwaŋ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu,lāwan śrī parameśwarī sira sinambaḥ māsiḥ aṅliŋ rĕsĕp,Om rakryan pada nīlakaṇṫa kinaƀaktyantâstu dīṙgǥāyuṣa,swasŧā tuṅgalĕn iŋ manuṅgali jagat māskw-îbu nā liŋ nira*16:2:167*

mojaṙ saŋ praƀu māsku tan tugĕta niŋ twastân inundaŋ mami,rākanta prihati n harĕp mamituhê māsku ndan ewĕḥ juga,saŋ ratw-âsiha len sasamƀawa muwaḥ yekī pinet ni ṅhulun,kady-amrat mrati mās juga ṅwaŋ amagantākĕn puriḥ niŋ dadi*16:3:168*

yāwat đaṙmma ṅaranya riŋ dadi manuṣyâwās hiwĕḥ yan pinet,lwiṙ sūkṣmā maganal ƀaṭāra gumawe tiṅkaḥnya yan maṅkana,yadyastun jalu jalw-ameta sawawanyêŋ janma haywâsali,byaktêwĕḥ niki kimpunaḥ kita yan iŋ strī strī n mameta priya*16:4:169*

saŋkṣepanya kita swayĕmbarakĕnaṅkwânugrahaṅkwê kita,sakweḥ saŋ ratu hundaṅĕn pilihanantâsiŋ sayogyê hati,yadyan hyaŋ palakunta māsku yugalantâmriḥ mrihaṅkwâṅhyaṅa,Aṅhiŋ yan hyaŋ anaṅga kahyuna hade tan pāwak ewĕḥ pinet*16:5:170*

nâjñā saŋ praƀu yogya paṅkwakĕna de saŋ mās maṇik niŋ purī,Āpan māsa nira n prapañca saputĕn riŋ rāga de hyaŋ smara,tan wruḥ riŋ sahurâwiraŋ mata sira n paṅyogyanê saŋ praƀu,tan maṅguḥ sira tan miṅĕl kadi liṅiṙ mās aṙcca paṅhyaŋ hyaṅan*16:6:171*

tan saṅkêŋ awalepa kāraṇa nira n lwiṙ tuhwa monabrata,kepwan budđi nirâtĕgĕg maṅucap agyā gyān harĕp mantuka,wahw-âdandan anĕmbahê nrĕpati mojaṙ saŋ sunandâṅjawil,Om yan Om huwusĕn huwus liṅa ni māskw-âlaḥ tuhan mājara*16:7:172*

tan kewö pitutuṙnya de nrĕpasutā mantuk sirêŋ pamrĕman,strī strī mājaṙ ajaṙ gumanti humatuṙ prāptêñjiŋ akweḥ marĕk,moliḥ tīṙŧa binuṅbuṅan winalun iŋ handoŋ sakêŋ paṙwwata,maṅde śudđa ri budđi saŋ praƀu suꝁā sāmpun sirâcāmana*16:8:173*

<puṣpacāpa>:17 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 20

^prāsāda sꝑaṭikâlaṅö ri tĕṅaḥ iŋ nūsâraras pañcuranya,strī stry-âmaṅku puḍak winimba makaranya lwiṙ lĕṅĕŋ de ni kuŋnya,kady-ahyun n-amahaywa luṅsuṙ i tapiḥnya n maṅligā yan hana wwaŋ,lāgy-ânaṅga suśūnya saṅka ri pacuṙ niŋ wwꜽ ya tâṅde ṅĕliḥnya*17:1:174*

ri prāsāda hanâṙcca ratna ri dalĕm ndān aṙdđanārīśwarâhyaŋ,wimba śrī naranāŧa dewata lawan dewī nirârok śarīra,ṅkā saŋ ƀoja maṅaṙccana pratidinâṅaƀyāsa ri swasŧa niŋ rāt,kady-âmakpak aṅastwakĕn ri jayaśatrwa śrī narendra n pamūjā*17:2:175*

saŋ ƀoja wruḥ i tattwa niŋ japasamāđi n đāraṇa đyānapūṙwwa,mwaŋ tiṅkaḥ niŋ adehaśudđi pinakānuṣṫāna yan recakādi,sāmpun kālap ulaḥ dwijeśwara mamūjā paŧya riŋ brahmamantra,saŋ hyaŋ kūṭarahasyamantra jinapākĕn de nirâtūt gaṇitri*17:3:176*

tatkāla nrĕpati n paṅuccaraṇakĕn mantra stutî saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,tan polaḥ wiṣayâṅhiḍĕp ri sira saṅyogānta riŋ yogya yogan,maṅgā tan lĕpara ŋ japastawa sĕḍĕŋ niŋ jñāna n enak tĕtĕpnya,simpaŋ niŋ hati yeki kāraṇa nirânaṅhāra saŋ hyaŋ śiwātma*17:4:177*

<girisa>:18 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^ri huwus ira mamūjā līlā śudđa manaḥ ira,Aṅusapi muꝁa saśrī de niŋ candana karakĕt,mijil aṅinaŋ aṅicꞓā riŋ wwꜽ niŋ ranu maṅilo,nĕhĕṙ anisigi dantê tuŋtuŋ niŋ gagaŋ inapi*18:1:178*

tucapa ta para mantrī śꜽwa brāhmaṇa sugata,parĕŋ apupul asewa ṅkānê jro paḍa humatur,nrĕpati sira maluṅguḥ riŋ siṅhāsana kanaka,Aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i sidđā niŋ kāṙyya n gawayakĕna*18:2:179*

<jagadđita>:19 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^ndin kāṙyyêwĕha riŋ wicakṣaṇa sujanma lituhayu kawi priyambada,ƀaktîŋ hyaŋ praƀu śakti đꜽṙyya saha wānđawa saha bala kośawāhana,yadyan sāgara tambakĕn satakĕnâŧawa wukiṙ alihĕn ratākĕna,byaktâwās kawaśanya de nira saŋ uttamapuruṣa wiśeṣa riŋ jagat*19:1:180*

śrī ƀoja pwa sira n prasidđa guṇamanta saꝑala sira ƀūmipālaka,prajñā śāstrawit iṅgita wruḥ iŋ apālapan aṅinaki budđi niŋ marĕk,Akweḥ drĕwya nirâprameya kadi sāgara papupulan iŋ wway iŋ nadī,wany-ânindita riŋ parākrama yan iŋ naya kadi ƀagawān wrĕhaspati*19:2:181*

maṅke pwa n hana rājakāṙyya gawayĕn kakaratala tĕkap nareśwara,śrī dewîndumatī swayĕmbarakĕnâmiliha ratu sasamƀawê sira,sāmpun saŋ praƀu motusan maminaṅê para ratu samayogya hundaṅĕn,lāwan saŋ haja milwa winwitakĕn iŋ nrĕpati raǥu katon tĕkā nira*19:3:182*

sāmpun höman irêrikā ta para taṇḍa sama sama samâṅharĕp gawe,sorêsuk gumĕrĕḥ makakrĕtug abaṇḍuŋ asahuran aganti loṙ kidul,len taŋ wwaŋ maṅusuŋ lakaṙ lakaṙ ikā winaca wuhaya de nikaŋ mulat,Akweḥ wwaŋ ka gĕrāḥ arĕp mulata wāhu mĕtu sinurakan muliḥ pacĕḥ*19:4:183*

Abwat hajyan ikaŋ humuŋ saha garantuŋ atabĕ tabĕhan paḍâsĕlur,Agyā lagy-aṅuhuḥ sirê harĕp alaḥ laku laku liŋ ikaŋ hanê wuri,tuṅgul paṅharĕp osik akrĕp asinaŋ kumuliliŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,lwiṙ guntuṙ kamarĕkrĕkĕn kayu pĕtuŋ priŋ asalĕsĕk agĕṇṭaḥ iŋ lĕbuḥ*19:5:184*

Ewĕṙ nora lĕgâŋ apaṇḍay anulis para lukis asipĕt mwaŋ aṅjahit,sakweḥ niŋ ginĕlaṙ wruhâṅanam anam wruḥ i suruhan ikā siliḥ tuluŋ,solaḥ niŋ tama tan hanâtaña ṅaranya huwus adu kabeḥ dinadyakĕn,paprāsan winaṅun paḍâcarita paṙwwa piniturun atuṅgalan kaŧā*19:6:185*

<widyutkara>:20 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 25

^Embuḥ ƀūṣaṇa niŋ tĕkĕn wuwuŋ apūṙwwa karacanan ikā tĕkêŋ pamanisan,lāwan tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ paṅastryanan apaṙppat ahalĕp akilā paḍâhayu hayu,de niŋ mās pinakopacāra sinisik pĕñu pinakawuwuŋnya kumram asinaŋ,lwiṙ digdāha riŋ astapaṙwwata sĕnö nika murub apadĕlwan iŋ kṣititala*20:1:186*

Aśrī rāmya ni de nirâmahayu rājya kaliliran apūṙwwa kādƀuta dahat,miṅgaṙ bapra nikê dalĕm watu hitĕm kuṭa nikaŋ i yawā lumaṅkuŋ ahirĕŋ,kulwan wetan agopurâtiśaya loṙ kidul agupura piṇḍa maṙppat aruhur,krĕṣṇākāra paḍâṅlunaŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukus i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ darâwrĕg aputiḥ*20:2:187*

<jagadđita>:21 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^luṅhā ŋ wrĕtta ri kāṙyya saŋ praƀu paḍâdƀuta sahana nikaŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,wwaŋ wwaŋ pora ḍusun ḍusun paḍa harĕp wihikana mulatêŋ swayambara,tan samwas raray aṅhwan iŋ tĕgal atakwan i tĕka ni gawe nareśwara,salwiṙ niŋ baṇijêŋ pĕkĕn taliṅa lintaḥ anaḍaḥ ucapan gawe nika*21:1:188*

sāmpun prāpta samotusan humatuṙ iŋ nrĕpati sĕḍĕŋ irân hanêŋ saƀā,Enak budđi narendra de ni panuwal para ratu rasa tan wuruŋ tĕkā,lumrā ŋ wrĕtta tĕkê dalĕm ri ḍatĕṅâṙyya raǥusuta marêŋ swayambara,twas niŋ strī sakaḍatwan aṅdadak aluŋ turida paḍa rumūpakê sira*21:2:189*

strī strī haṙṣa pinöm pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara ri pamihaŋnya riŋ yayaḥ,tan haṙṣêŋ kawi rakwa rena nika monaguṇa pisaniṅūn tumiṅhala,ndan rakwêki hinuṙnya matya saka riŋ tuluyakĕna susatya riŋ priya,liŋnya n kewala tan hinanti ni papaṅgiha nika pĕjahêŋ panambaṅan*21:3:190*

tapwan māri taṅis taṅisnya n inalap hinaturakĕn i jöŋ suputrikā,wrā niŋ roma maṅekadeśa ri piliŋ piliṅan ika baṅun pameṙ i luḥ,Enak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥnya mamalaṙ malaṙ i pada narendraputrikā,Āpan swāmi nikā karĕṅwan i parĕknya ri saŋ aja tĕwĕk nikâpasaḥ*21:4:191*

Antuk saŋ priya maṅdawākĕn inalĕm para kawi sumĕnāha riŋ kajaŋ,yeki n rakwa kinonya kady-aṅucapâmaḥ aku tuhan alap waca ṅhulun,moǥa nyan ya kinonakĕn wacan ikā ri pamaca nika maṅdadak lumuḥ,swāminyâdadi pustakânuturakĕn hiḍĕp ika pinapagnya riŋ taṅis*21:5:192*

ṅūnî kāla nika n turuŋ marĕk i jöŋ nira ṅaran ika ken mađūdakā,saŋ mambaŋ mađusūdana priya nikā kawi taruṇa marĕk ri jöŋ haji,wiđy-âmiđyani kāraṇanya wirahênalapan alara luḥnya tan pĕgat,ndaḥ rakryan jayawaspa teki wĕkasan ṅaran ika satĕwĕk nikā marĕk*21:6:193*

<Aƀikrĕti>:22 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 25

^para praƀu kaḍaṅhanan turida rāga nira sinaput iŋ smarâmulaṅuni,huwus katĕka kuŋ nirâhawan ujaṙ tuhun amĕlas arĕp riniptakĕn ira,lawan punagi kesy-anambaha ri jöŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā hana hyuna nira,Akiŋkiŋ aṅalap kasoṙ paḍa tan apraƀu sahana nirârĕbut kahulunan*22:1:194*

wawaŋ nrĕpatiputrikā rinĕbut iŋ hiḍĕp inaṅĕn aṅĕn raras raras ira,hanan kahiḍĕp iŋ mađubrata rĕṅiḥ rĕṅiha nira n arĕs kapaṅkwa harasĕn,lĕyĕp hayu nira n linaṅwakĕn amūṙtti kakawin inapus wineḥ amanisa,hanê hati kinubđa kady-apĕga kāraṇa nira mijil iŋ puḍak dadi ṭikā*22:2:195*

Adandan asĕnāha sañjata para praƀu ḍatĕṅa marê widaṙbƀanagara,lanâṅiṅĕt iṅĕt ri pahyasan irâṅinakana ri manaḥ narendratanayā,hanâṅdadak anat śarīra manahap nahap aharĕp alantasa n winulatan,paḍâṅalap alap sipat jĕnu mĕnuŋ hawu karaṇa suputrikā n aharĕpa*22:3:196*

muwaḥ saŋ aja sāmpun aṙppat akire lumarisa makamaṅgala dwijawara,sahasraśatakoṭi wīra winiđi nrĕpati tumuta śakti sāmpun ayaśa,pĕnuḥ sahana niŋ lĕbuḥ tĕkap i sañjata nika kumaluŋ pinañjĕṙ aṅadĕg,Ikaŋ nagara denya kady-akalaṅan wihaga saŋ aja moliha praƀusutā*22:4:197*

mijil sira śinaṅꝁapāṇyan i karaŋ ni patiga niŋ aśoka wahw-asalaga,Ikaŋ ƀramara haṙṣa riŋ kusuma muṅgw-i taṅan ira marâṅisĕp tan awĕliŋ,laki stry-aliwĕran hañaṙ hañaṙ apaṅgiḥ aduluṙ akaraŋ karaŋ sĕkaṙ arūm,katampwan i kucuṙ nikaŋ wway atawiŋ tawiŋ i lawĕ lawö nikaŋ sarasija*22:5:198*

I sāmpun i kaśaṅꝁapāṇyan ira mañjiŋ i dalĕm aduluṙ lawan dwijawara,Anambaḥ aṅusap ri jöŋ nrĕpati mamwit i ḍatĕṅa nirêŋ widaṙbƀanagara,sinuṅsuŋ iŋ ujaṙ prahāsana nĕhĕṙ jumaya jaya jayā nirê paran ira,Ahum hanaku saŋ pakolihĕn i tiṅhal iŋ ahayu dumĕlwa jalwa rasika*22:6:199*

kunaŋ pawĕkasaṅkwa haywa ta bapaṅku tan apĕnĕd iŋ ambĕk iŋ para paran,rare mara kita ndatan raraya de niŋ amawa manaḥ atwaṅêŋ wwaŋ atuha,Inuttama đanuṙdđarânaku taŧāpi tan ika paṅayāya riŋ kadi kita,Ikaŋ guṇa ya tan paraṅkĕpana maryada rahayu lawö hananya kapalaŋ*22:7:200*

Ikaŋ sakahawan ri ƀūmi ni bapaṅku pahayu kita rakṣakâṅanumata,sapawwat ika hantusākĕna sasamƀawa haturakĕnanya māsku tariman,Ujaṙku pituhunta haywa kita sāhasa maṅalapa wastu mūlya tinĕṅĕt,prasidđa kadaŋ iŋ jagat kita dumadyakĕna suꝁa nikā mataŋnya pahayu*22:8:201*

pamitran alawas rĕsĕp karaṇa niŋ wĕnaŋ aṅalapa wastu tan pamalaku,yan iŋ wiṣayarāmajātaka puriḥnya karaṇa niŋ anĕmwa mās pirak ika,karāsikaguṇan ya kāraṇa niŋ oliha raras i manaḥ niŋ adyaḥ araras,kaśaktin aƀimāna kāraṇa niŋ aṅraraḥ aṅalapa rājya niŋ ripukula*22:9:202*

sirat sirat i de narendra raǥu mojaṙ amanis amađaṙmmakĕn ri saŋ aja,minuṣṭi pinakādidewa hiniḍĕp rasa nika kinayogyakĕn pinituhu,putus niŋ ađamā tan ahyuna rumĕṅwakĕna ri pitutuṙ nirâhayu dahat,ya kāraṇa narendraputra makacāmana rarab i lĕbū ni jöŋ narapati*22:10:203*

ri sāmpun ira mamwit iŋ nrĕpati saṙwwi laku nira marê narendramahiṣī,hanâṅhaḍaŋ aweḥ sĕrĕḥ saha taṅis wagĕd ahayu hinĕmban iŋ kaka kaka,kataṅgamaŋ aweḥ sĕpaḥ nrĕpatiputra nĕhĕṙ amuhun amriḥ aṅhari hari,tapiḥ saŋ araras pininta nira mūlya basahan ira raṇḍi paṅhurup ira*22:11:204*

byatīta ri huwus nirâṅucap ucap tĕka sira ri taman narendramahiṣī,lĕṅĕŋ kadi kadewatan halĕp ikâpan ajuraŋ awukiṙ mapājaṙ ajaran,maeṙttali pinañcuran jinalatuṇḍa tinalaga ri soṙnya kādƀuta dahat,Ikaŋ kaka kakânwam adyus anĕṅaḥ lawan anak anakanya ketaka miṅiŋ*22:12:205*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ>:23 
– – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^kalpadruma taruwara pārijāta winaṅun bwat asana sakapat,Aƀrâsinaŋ asĕmu sakêŋ kadewatan ululnya kanaka pinahat,jinriṅjriŋ iŋ anak anakan maṇik cinaturaṅga lumarap amiraḥ,mās jaṅga katiraḥ awilĕt pralĕmba nika riŋ tarĕtĕpan alaṅö*23:1:206*

ṅkānā nrĕpatisuta marĕk ri rena nira sādara satiru tirun,Amwit lumarisa ḍatĕṅêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī bibi nira wihikan,maṙmmâsiḥ awĕlas asĕgĕḥ mamakpak amapag riŋ ucapan amanis,niṙwiǥna kita bapa jayêŋ swayambara sadâṅalahakĕna ratu*23:2:207*

rakryān aṅinaṅa tanayaṅku māsku mapa hetu niŋ awak akuru,Agriŋ karika kita lawan waneḥ brata kunaŋ karaṇa niŋ awĕnĕs,haywânaku kaluṣa kitâhyun iŋ kajayaśatrwan anuta ri harĕp,Akweḥ ꝑala nika kaki saṙwwawiǥna niyatanya hilaŋ alaradan*23:3:208*

ndan rakwa kadamĕlan ikaŋ swayambara kahop riŋ anakĕbi rara,sakweḥ para ratu pininaŋ ya teka pilihĕn sakaharĕp alapĕn,de ni ṅhulun ahiḍĕp i budđi saŋ rara kapan harĕpa riŋ atuha,ṅhiŋ kahyuna nika ratu cakrawaṙttitanayâguṇa kawi taruṇa*23:4:209*

rakryan pwa saꝑala wĕka cakrawaṙtti tuwi śakti wihikan aṅaji,siṅhākrĕti tuhu tuhu siṅhaputra wĕnaŋ uṅsirĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,byaktânaku mamĕnaṅa riŋ swayambarasaƀâṅalahakĕna ratu,tan sĕṅgahĕn aṅalĕm anak syapêka kadi māsku lituhayu wani*23:5:210*

<jagadđita>:24 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^tatkālê paṅucap narendramahiṣī tucapa ta para ratnakanyakā,Osik tan pakawanwan agyaŋ i ḍatĕŋ saŋ aja kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,tan pātmā kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn kalukaran gĕluŋ asidĕha tan hanâṅucap,kady-âhöm turidanya n osaḥ akĕcap lwiṙ anicipi manis nrĕpātmaja*24:1:211*

wwantĕn lwiṙ śaśiwimba wāhu mijil aṅḍaḍari hayu nikânwam iŋ wayaḥ,Aṅgöŋ mabrata śuklapakṣa nika paṅlwaŋ i manaḥ ika tan wĕnaŋ licin,rāganya n dadakan tumaṅgal i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasuta kadi tambwaŋ iŋ wulan,krĕṣṇākāra tĕṅaḥnya de ni tapak iŋ suḥ asĕmu sĕmu rāhw-añumbana*24:2:212*

len taŋ lwiṙ pranitâdagaŋ kira kiranya sumikĕpa wĕkas nrĕpātmaja,kapraŋ rwêpu kataṇḍĕgan turida tan patahĕnan aṅagĕm pralāpita,toḥ toḥ nyân iŋ agĕgwan ambĕk apagĕḥ mapa tiki n alaḥ aṅgĕgö smara,Aṅlampwâṅusirê padadwaya nirân panikĕlakĕna tuṙ humaṇḍĕma*24:3:213*

strī saŋsāra sarāga mohita sawaŋ wana gahana kalahrwan iŋ kapat,trāsa twasnya kakiŋkiṅan ginĕsĕṅan pinarawaśa tinunwan iŋ smara,norânīsi manaḥnya kewala panasbaran alisuḥ aṅölakĕn lara,maṅke pwa n karĕṅö gĕrĕḥ saŋ aja mañjiŋ aluŋ asĕmi kuŋ nikâsĕwö*24:4:214*

Endaḥ budđi nikaŋ waneḥ tĕkap ikâmawa turida luput linakṣaṇan,muṅkuṙ tan huniṅê ḍatĕŋ saŋ aja mañjiŋ asila ri harĕp nareśwarī,ndan denyâhyas apahyasan dudu dudū hiniraṅakĕn ikê nrĕpātmaja,sūkṣmākāra ni raśmi raśmi ni wulatnya n araras apadĕlwan iŋ crĕmin*24:5:215*

kanyā rwaŋ siki rāmya kāliḥ aṅisapwakĕn anak anakanya ketaka,tuṅgal mājaṙ i putra putran ika māsku saŋ aja sira rakwa maṅkata,ndan haywâkilayū tuhanku niyata ṅhulun inucap ujaṙ nikâkalib,maṙmmanyâpasaḥ ambĕk eṅgal apadudwan aṅuwahi pamitran aṅdadak*24:6:216*

strī strī sukṣĕka wahw-agātra turidanya mijil i wijil iŋ payođara,tan saḥ riŋ salukat gawe nrĕpatiputra sinalukatakĕnya tan humuŋ,ramyârūm karĕṅö manisnya sinameni pamawan ika riṅraŋ iŋ hati,tan samwas ginarut garutnya hiniḍĕpnya saŋ aja sahasâṅisapwakĕn*24:7:217*

sakweḥ niŋ kumĕmit prapañca ni hatinya kumĕkĕsi taṅisnya riŋ karas,Āpan budđi narendraputra kadi tan tulusa duga dugâṅhalimbaṅa,ƀakty-ânĕmbaḥ i jöŋ ni rena nira mĕṅgĕp amanis agawe wulat maliŋ,luṅhā tan pracurânĕhĕṙ nĕhĕrakĕn manaḥ iŋ ahayu kāri sukṣĕka*24:8:218*

<Aƀikrĕti>:25 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 25

^mijil saŋ aja kādƀutâƀinawa rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ apan paḍâhyaŋ ahalĕp,Ikaŋ gaja raŧâśwa sañjata saƀūṣaṇa nika dumilaḥ kasĕnwan aruṇa,sumaṅgraha humerakĕn wiđi nira n lumarisa kumisik pasaṅǥa niŋ ujar,baṅun jalada tan pakāla gumĕrĕḥ ri taya niŋ aṅin aṅḍapuṙ saha kilat*25:1:219*

payuŋ payuṅan iŋ lĕbuḥ kadi sĕkaṙ sinawuŋ apan anekawaṙṇna sumĕkar,Ikaŋ paṅuṅaṅan huwus winalunan wĕḍihan inuparĕṅga riŋ tulis ĕmās,rarânwam inĕgĕḥ parĕŋ mijil amaṅguŋ asĕmu sĕmu lakṣmi niŋ masa kapat,paḍâlal asĕnāha tiṅhal amanis wulatakĕna ri raśmi raśmi saŋ aja*25:2:220*

hanêŋ gupura tan wawaŋ sira lumampaḥ ataña ri gĕnĕp ni sañjata nira,samâsila hanêŋ lĕmaḥ muni manuk marahakĕn i wijilnya tan hana kari,sirêŋ palukayan kinon ira kumona ri para juru yan lumakwa rumuhun,samaṅkana sira n lumampaḥ aḍarat harĕp iŋ ulaḥ awās yayanyan ahalĕp*25:3:221*

ri lampaḥ ira ǥūṙṇnita ŋ paḍahi paṅharĕp ira kumisik maṅeṙttali tibā,saru swara nikâbaruŋ binaruṅan tabĕ tabĕhan agĕnturan kadi gĕrĕḥ,humandaru tibā gubaṙ kumĕtug asriŋ aniru kĕtug iŋ hudan wahu ḍawuḥ,Arūm uni ni ǥaṇṭa niŋ liman aṅuṅkaŋ asahuran i paṅhrik iŋ kuda bisir*25:4:222*

dwijāti rĕṣi śꜽwa bodđa śuci sojaṙ ira maṅaƀiwāda muṅgu ri harĕp,yaŧākrama paḍâdarâhalĕp agöŋ i wĕtĕŋ ira lawan huwan riŋ atuha,lumampaḥ alaris malaḥ ya tan arampaka ri sadawatā nikaŋ lĕbuḥ agöŋ,humuŋ tĕkap ira n paṅuccaraṇa mantra kadi mađukarâṅisis humaliwat*25:5:223*

kĕliŋ wani wanîŋ usāna pamarakṣa nira mamawa ƀindiwāla palaga,baṅun rinawisan wĕhaŋnya kalawan ḍaḍa nika paḍa wok tĕkêŋ suku wulun,hibĕk tatu rujit rujit kadi tinambalan awak ika waṙṇna bĕntaṙ inawĕt,Agöŋ paḍa kaƀīma ƀīma kadi dānawa muꝁa muꝁa dꜽtya piṇḍa cawiri*25:6:224*

Ikaŋ marĕk i jöŋ narendratanayânwam aguṇa paḍa daṙśśanīya taruṇa,titik nagara nora tan wruha n anak wĕsi haji tuwi mūlya kawwaṅan ika,watĕk madana maṅdadi wwaŋ ujaṙ iŋ mulat i lituhayunya n ahyaŋ araras,kunaŋ saŋ aja kāmadewa sakalânurun ucapan ikaŋ kapūhan i sira*25:7:225*

samaṅkana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan haṅu haṅun arĕbut mulat ri saŋ aja,hanan kadi harĕp siliḥ galaha riŋ susu manĕwĕka riŋ naꝁâkas aluṅid,paḍâkira kirâkĕkĕs mata maliŋ maliŋ aṅiriṅi kāladeśa sumilib,katon kadi siliḥ praṅêŋ halis arĕṅw-inayat ayatakĕnya maṅkin araras*25:8:226*

Ikāŋ amawa pawwahan lituhayu prakaśita kawi mambaŋ uttama rare,hañaṙ tĕka sakêŋ widaṙbƀanagarī layat inalapan aṅhañaŋ hañaṅakĕn,rarānya kawĕkas pinañjiṅakĕn iŋ nagara marĕk i jöŋ narendratanayā,ya kāraṇa ni luḥnya mantĕn amalaṙ malaṙ i saŋ aja molihê sira hĕlĕm*25:9:227*

manis ni kakawinya mūla ni papaṅgiḥ ika lawan ikaŋ rinudđa winalat,pinet pĕjahanâsĕnötan i kadaŋnya winuni karaṇanya yan lĕpas adoḥ,paḍâpalarasan lawan jaruman amriḥ aṅaliḥ ahawan wĕṅîŋ awa wulan,tinūt i paṅaran ṅaranya kawidoṣa wĕkasan i ḍatĕŋnya riŋ nrĕpasuta*25:10:228*

ya tīka tan adoḥ ginĕgwan ira bāhu nika winisikan tinakwanan ira,syapêka paḍa saŋ swayĕmbarakĕna prakaśita pinakādi niŋ wwaŋ ahayu,Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ bwat indrawanitâhyas ika pahawasĕn ta ya n sama hirib,kĕcapnya n aṅĕsaḥ miṅĕl ya pawaraḥnya ri saŋ aja wawaŋ rĕmĕk hati nira*25:11:229*

hanâṅuṅaŋ anuṅga nuṅgal aṅisapwakĕn anak anakanya ketaka miṅiŋ,mahâṅjĕlagakĕn hayunya makapaṅhaḍa buṅaḥ i muꝁanya tan patalutuḥ,ri kāla saŋ ajâṅinaŋ winulatanya ri wulat ira löṙ matanya lumiriŋ,baṅun hañaṙ anūt harĕp sĕpaḥ awĕdy-aṅucapa tumiliŋ miṅe kadi cala*25:12:230*

rarânwam akire wulat dudu dudū saŋ aṅĕsaḥ i kisapwan iŋ kaka kaka,tupis tupis i de nirâṅĕnahakĕn manaḥ ira tumibê narendratanaya,wagĕd wagĕd aniṙwwa niṙwakĕn i de nira gamĕl inamĕṙ nirê taṅan ira,tĕkāsiḥ atabĕḥ sĕrĕḥ saha pucaŋ nika dalihan irâṅawe ri saŋ aja*25:13:231*

I soṙ niŋ asanâsĕkaṙ hana sirâṅuṅaŋ araras aliṇḍuṅan kaka kaka,ṅĕliḥ ṅĕliḥ iŋ ekacitta ri narendrasuta ṅĕliḥ irâhuyaŋ pinĕpĕtan,sawaŋ sawaŋ i denirâmawa wulat wulat iŋ asamayâwĕdi n katĕṅĕra,mulat pwa saŋ ajâṅdadak sira miṅe sĕmu niŋ awarahê katĕmwana nira*25:14:232*

muwaḥ wwaya sirâhalĕp rara sujanma pinawulaṅakĕn hanêŋ paṅuṅaṅan,gaḍiŋ pinakaputra putran ira tan saḥ inarĕk arĕkan sakê nrĕpasuta,ya teka tumurun hinĕmban iŋ iñâmawa sĕrĕḥ arĕnaḥ marĕk ri saŋ aja,bapâṅinaṅa rakwa liŋ ra bibi liŋ nikaŋ aṅujarakĕn waśâsĕmu guyu*25:15:233*

pratāpa naranāŧaputra kumutug pracalita kadi paṙwwatâgni dumilaḥ,Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ baṅun kusuma sālas anĕḍĕŋ ika kāri tan papĕgatan,manaḥnya ginĕsĕŋ tĕkêŋ turida rāga nika paḍa hilaŋ syuḥ aṅdadi hawu,ya teka hinañutnya riŋ nrĕpatiputra sakala sira pöḥ niŋ aṙṇnawa mađu*25:16:234*

manis niŋ ucapan kaka dyaḥ ari liŋnya sinĕpuhan i raśmi niŋ wulat arūm,ya teka kinabehan iŋ wwaŋ aṅuṅaŋ mrĕdu lalita rasanya rāgakaraṇa,raras raras i denya miṅgĕk aṅĕnāni n aṅucap api tan wruhĕn hana mulat,halisnya minahānya molaḥ amaṅun gĕt unĕŋ arĕṅu maṅlare ri saŋ aja*25:17:235*

<Indrabajra>:26 
– – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 11

^strī stry-âṅucap sojaṙ ikā yinuktyan,liŋnyê narendrātmaja mūḋabudđi,Akweḥ sira ṅke nagarī ry-ayođyā,sāmantaputrī paḍa yogya-yogyan*26:1:236*

yadyan tĕkā dlāha sirê widaṙbƀa,tan suŋsuṅĕn riŋ kakawin wilāpa,tan kewwa riŋ rāga tĕkap suputrī,ƀagnapratijñā mulihêraŋ eraŋ*26:2:237*

nāhan wuwusnyê naranāŧaputra,ndan rakwa paṙṇnaḥ jaruman gatinya,wwantĕn suputrī paṅadunya yogya,maṙmmanya duḥkê saŋ aja n tan ahyun*26:3:238*

paṙṇnaḥ kakanyâsrak atuṅga yôjar,Antĕn hade denta tĕkôjaṙ apyak,putrī paran tan harĕpê tuhanku,hyaŋ niŋ purī towi yayā sirâhyun*26:4:239*

maṅko n marê śrī naranāŧa ƀoja,Ambĕk nira śrîndumatī pakādin,ǥārâpan atyanta wiśeṣaputrī,sāmantaputrī sira tā maṅadyaḥ*26:5:240*

nāhan sahuṙnyê paṅucap ny-arinya,ƀāwanya miṅgĕk tumikĕl halisnya,koŋ aṅdĕlö solaḥ ikā n asĕṅhit,göŋ krođa sojaṙ nika kaṙṇnaśūla*26:6:241*

wwantĕn kili wrĕdđa sahuṙ nirâtwaŋ,sajñêbu ni ṅwaŋ kṣama ta ṅhulun dyaḥ,budđinta kewalya sumorakĕn saŋ,sāmantaputrîndumatī wiśeṣa*26:7:242*

tan soṙ sirêŋ janma karājaputryan,riŋ wīṙyya siṅgiḥ sira tan paḍâḍaḥ,ndan yogya ǥārâpa hiwaŋ nirêbu,mūlya n minūlyan krama niŋ dadi wwaŋ*26:8:243*

nāhan sahuṙ saŋ wiku wrĕdđarūpa,mĕṅgĕp pratuhw-âsĕmu pakṣapāta,milw-âhadenî sira yan lumampaḥ,rowaŋ nirâgoṣṫi wulatnya hewa*26:9:244*

<nawahaṙṣa>:27 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^tucapa ŋ wwaŋ i paṅguŋ ika kadi wayaŋ jinajaṙ kinudaŋ,sakunaŋ kunaŋ iŋ taliṅa larap i hintĕn ika n kumĕñar,hana tâṅadĕg an hayu nika kahiḍĕp kadi modahita,I kasiṅkab i kenya hana kadi gibaḥ winuluŋ sinurat*27:1:245*

paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ sahana niŋ aṅuṅaŋ mawagĕd wagĕdan,Amanis manisan mata nĕhĕṙ araṅin raṅinan paṅawak,Arupit rupitan susu nĕhĕṙ alĕmĕs lĕmĕsan luṅayan,sira saŋ sinajinya saŋ aja juga nora muwaḥ kinire*27:2:246*

nrĕpaputra sĕḍĕŋ sapawulatan aweḥ lĕṅĕṅêŋ aṅuṅaŋ,tadanantara meḥ lĕpasa laku nirā wĕkas iŋ nagara,Amanis kadi tan pĕgata wulat irê salawaŋ salawaŋ,Amalaṙ hana niŋ wwaŋ ahaliṅana kori mĕṅā sasisiḥ*27:3:247*

Araras rinasan patĕmu nira wulat rasa tan lĕpara,kalawan saŋ akūŋ alawas i sira kady-awarĕg warĕgan,Apatūtan unĕŋ kasiḥ arĕp inatīta tiniṅgalakĕn,I layat nira kāri saŋ ahayu wulatnya tinambaŋ ira*27:4:248*

nda Atīta sira n kajĕnĕkan akurĕn wulat esy-akadi,Asalin wiṣaya n lĕpas i muꝁa nikaŋ lĕbuḥ iŋ nagara,kuṭi śāla lumaṅkuŋ i tĕpi niŋ ayun tirisanya pĕnuḥ,panĕḍĕŋ ni wuṅūnya mamituturi rāga nirêŋ aṅuṅaŋ*27:5:249*

kadi waḥ surasinđu bala saŋ aja kātatakut gumuruḥ,raŧa rĕṅga padāti kadi parahu söḥ aduluṙ humilī,gajaḥ aṅgala ǥūṙṇnita piraŋ iwu kady-asibū gumuluŋ,sagĕḍaŋ kahilī gaḍiŋ ika tulalenya lumintaḥ awās*27:6:250*

paḍa ƀakti hĕnū nira sakalihatan paḍa tan humĕnĕŋ,walahaṙnya lawan pahatan asaji mīna sayub cumaḍaŋ,Amapag waṅi niŋ kusuma winawa niŋ pawana mrik arūm,ƀramarâsĕmu maṅhaturakĕn i gawenya kiduŋ ri sira*27:7:251*

kadi maṇḍala rāmya ni papupul ikaŋ kayu kayw-asĕkar,waṅunanya wuṅū sĕḍĕŋ asinaŋ añaṇḍi minerw-aruhur,humilī wulakanya paḍa caluṅanêka katon humaḍaŋ,hulu kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕpĕrakĕn ri narendrasuta*27:8:252*

patapan kĕna rāga kayu manis ikā sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,Amapag mata jāti ni mata ni wuluḥ nika tan wriŋ iraŋ,Aḍahĕm haḍawanya rumara rara haṙṣaja denya mulat,pajajaṙ ni pabañwan ika kapahiriŋ milu kady-aṅaraŋ*27:9:253*

<girisa>:28 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^saŋ aja sira kaṅelan muṅgaḥ riŋ raŧa wĕkasan,saŋ agajaḥ aturaṅgânuṅgaŋ saƀya ciha ciha,mwaŋ agiliṅan arampak wwaŋ sāmānya tan ahalĕp,saŋ aḍarat alarêraŋ kagrĕk grĕk magarawalan*28:1:254*

nrĕpasuta lĕpas eṅgal prāptêŋ ŧāni kuluwutan,satĕka tĕka ni lampaḥ niŋ wadwânamun adulur,I harĕp i wuri lumrânĕṅkw-âyun manasa nasar,hawan arupĕk inambaḥ membuḥ lwā kadi tinĕpa*28:2:255*

wukiṙ ajajaṙ ahaṇḍap haṇḍap śūnya maṅililan,kadi kukusan amuñjuŋ puñcaknyâṙṇnĕb inululan,hana talaga riŋ agra ndan wwꜽnyâhaṅĕt ahasin,pinara paran iŋ adyus baṙyyan landĕp awukiran*28:3:256*

suku suku nika duṙggâtyantêwĕḥ nika pinaran,pinĕga tinĕpa de niŋ molaḥ ṅūni riŋ alawas,sahaja maliwat i jro ṅkân līlâmĕkasi parab,dadali nika laki strī prāptânambĕṙ asahuran*28:4:257*

lura luraḥ aparĕk lwaḥ guŋguŋ wwꜽnya ḍinawuhan,papupulan ikaŋ aṅhwan ramyâḍöm aṅariŋ ariŋ,paḍa marĕk adum uṅgwan yan wwaŋ śreṣṫi humaliwat,Asila sila ri piṅgiṙ niŋ māṙggâmalaku sĕrĕḥ*28:5:258*

Umaḥ atiśaya denyâporaŋ mĕṅgĕp aṅililan,wwaŋ ika paḍa humöt riŋ budđy-âlumbuŋ alit alit,tĕka ri sapi nikâlit norâkral kral amĕḍusi,talaga nika jugâlwâṅlaṅhuy laṅhuyakĕn agöŋ*28:6:259*

hana ta baṅun amet wwaŋ doṣa n krūra lĕkas ikā,Amawa tali lawan kris pamraŋ mraŋnya habalaṅan,sapi nika sinikĕpnyâṅrĕñcal maṅlawan agalak,ri huwus ika katalyan keṇḍit dinwal iŋ aṅulaŋ*28:7:260*

nrĕpatisuta kaluṅhâdoḥ śīǥra n saha śakaṭa,karaṇa nira n araryan mwaŋ sakweḥ ni bala nira,Amarĕki pĕkĕn alwā ŧāny-âgöŋ pakulĕmana,pira ta puluḥ i dūwanyâkweḥ söḥ paḍa winĕgil*28:8:261*

saŋ aja kadi hanê jro rājyâpan sira kinĕmit,sahana hana nikaŋ saṙwwāstra lwiṙ pinakapagĕr,raŧa turaga tiniṅkaḥ baprâṅrakṣa sana sini,makagupura halĕp niŋ mātaṅgâruhuṙ ajajar*28:9:262*

tucapa para kadūwan tuṣṭa n paṅhinĕpan ira,sahana hana ri deśanyâneka ŋ paḍa pamapag,nrĕpasuta sira muṅguḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,sama humatuṙ aṅantî soṙ niŋ wāṇḍira magĕlar*28:10:263*

wiku haji jĕnĕk aṅheṙ iŋ śūnyâlawas amarāt,wruḥ aṅaji sira santoṣâṅdo dohi narapati,nĕhĕṙ amarahi sāmpun wrĕdđâṅgöŋ ulaḥ alaṅö,Atuha tuha kadi brĕm santĕn kāku manis ira*28:11:264*

sira ta marĕk aluṅguḥ milw-iŋ dāyaka humatur,kinasĕgĕhan apan wruḥ ṅūnîŋ rājya sira kabeḥ,Apituwi paḍa rowaŋ rowaŋ niŋ maṅikĕt ikĕt,muꝁa niŋ aṅucap aśrī de niŋ mojaṙ akakawin*28:12:265*

kṣamakĕna bapa pawwat niŋ grāmyâđama kaluṣa,padapa hima lawan centĕn mepâlpa lihatana,sama duwĕga ri rakryan yan twak haywa hali halin,pinakabañu bañu ṅke ṅhiŋ yan len juga yan ikā*28:13:266*

wulatana kakudeśanyâŧānî gĕgĕṙ asĕpi,ya tuna tuna sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ tĕkwan tan hana dinadak,palapat alas agaryaŋ gaṙyyaŋ tan sawĕgilana,linĕṅĕṅakĕn iŋ ambĕk maṙmmanya n rĕsĕp alaṅö*28:14:267*

Aluru wahu kalahrwan kaywanya n śrawaṇamasa,Asĕpa humuraŋ awyaŋ rurwan ronya kapawanan,Analukati tĕlā wwad niŋ saṙwwatrĕṇa riŋ ayun,pĕjaḥ amĕkasi kiŋkiŋ luŋ niŋ jaṅga kapanasan*28:15:268*

tĕwĕk i ragas i kaywanya n karwâraras alaṅö,tĕṅaḥ i tal ika mambĕt mambĕt kāṅinan aṅĕliḥ,manis i lahaŋ ikâṅhiŋ panraŋ nraŋ wulat amanis,tiniru tiru niŋ ahyas ronyâṙjjâpataḥ akiris*28:16:269*

sĕḍĕŋ iŋ asujimāsâtyantêŋ kaṣṭa gatarasa,karikil ika kumĕṇḍĕŋ tūt māṙggâmacĕki suku,saha panas i hĕnunyâdoḥ wwe nora pinalaku,tuhun amuhara ramyā sakweḥ niŋ wwaŋ ika jĕnĕk*28:17:270*

jalada kadi pĕtĕŋ yan tĕmbe niŋ kapat alaṅö,jawuḥ amĕkasakĕn rĕm riŋ kaywan hañaṙ asĕmi,wahu mari panaṅis niŋ kālaṅkyaŋ suꝁa sumayab,Asiga kadi tinambaŋ wahw-înantukan agiraŋ*28:18:271*

trĕṇa taru paḍa mĕltik wījanya n masa kalima,wawaŋ aluru kapiṅrĕs tūt māṙggâṅĕliḥ alume,linaran i kĕñaṙ iŋ wꜽ yan luṅhā ŋ rĕmĕŋ anisiḥ,kadi pamanas i kuŋ niŋ kanyā dūra n atĕlĕba*28:19:272*

hañaṙ abañu tĕgalnya n kānĕm tapwan acarĕcĕḥ,kadi sinipatan apriḥ māṙgganyâracĕk abĕnĕr,turaḥ i wĕrĕḥ ikaŋ waṙṣâsat kāri kasarakat,Asĕmu pupuṙ areḥ tūt piṅgiṙ niŋ halis inamĕr*28:20:273*

brata nika ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ māǥâdyus rahina wĕṅi,jawuḥ aṅapitu tan pāntyâdrĕs maṅkin akĕcĕhan,Aṅura ṅuraṅi teja hyaŋ candrâṙkka kaginĕman,suꝁa salabuḥ ikaŋ luṅlūṅan māri kapiṅĕliḥ*28:21:274*

lĕbug i palĕmahanyâjro riŋ ꝑālguna puraci,patuna tunahan iŋ lĕmbw-âsaŋsiŋ tahi papuṅĕn,dwijawara sira baṙyyan rĕŋrĕŋ moǥa humaliwat,sumĕpĕṙ anasi pöhan maṙmmanya n śuci wĕkasan*28:22:275*

masa kasaṅa tĕka traŋ ndan mātrânĕlani jawuḥ,ya karaṇa ni latĕknyâtiṅgaṙ wahw-asat anisiḥ,sapapikatana göṅĕn tĕmbe niŋ manuk agalak,tuhun asĕpi hĕnūnya lwīṙ agriŋ paḍa caciṅĕn*28:23:276*

kusuma sahana māywan yan wꜽśāꝁa paḍa wijaḥ,sĕkaṙ iŋ asana kantun kady-ahyun kalarakĕna,paṅirim irim ikaŋ waṙṣâheṙ weḥ ayu ḍumawuḥ,kadi jaruman aṅinte rāgânīs amawa taṅis*28:24:277*

muwaḥ asĕkaṙ alasnya jyeṣṫâmiṅrwani sahapit,tuhun aṅuraṅi rurwan de niŋ waṙṣa wahu muliḥ,tura turaḥ i gĕrĕḥnyâgupyan meḥ amĕkasana,tuna tuna kadi pamwit niŋ haṙṣâmĕkasi taṅis*28:25:278*

Analahasa laṅönyêŋ āṣāđâṅlarani kawi,paḍa gumigil aṅinkin tiṅhalnyâniliṅi tawaŋ,kamaḍiḍiṅĕn aṅepw-î roganyâṅgĕgĕs aṅĕsaḥ,kadi kahapit aṅunṅun muṅgw-iŋ śūnya kakilatan*28:26:279*

nahan ucapan ira mpuṅkw-aṅde haṙṣa ri saŋ aja,wĕṅi mara sakamantyan prāptâneka taḍaḥ ira,dwijawara sira māliḥ muṅgw-iŋ bwat halu tĕpi lor,para wiku juga kāry-âgoṣṫi mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya*28:27:280*

paḍahi marĕk agupyan śabdanyâmanis inamĕr,kadi paṅucap ucap niŋ muṅgw-i jro jinĕm akule,Apituwi sinamenîŋ gīta śrī nrĕpatanaya,rasa nika winiwekâneka ŋ pālapan amanis*28:28:281*

tucapa bala nirâkweḥ ƀāwanya n paṅinum inum,Aṅigĕl aṅiduŋ asraŋ twaknyâkweḥ kadi humilī,paḍahi nika gumĕntĕṙ sinraŋ niŋ tabĕ tabĕhan,kadi baribina saŋ hyaŋ riŋ swaṙggâtukupa kapö*28:29:282*
