^luṅhā ŋ māsa piliḥ tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi tiḍĕm sahana niŋ aṅinum paḍâturū,tistis nora mumik tuhun saŋ aja tan mrĕm amaṅu maṅu tan kĕnêŋ turū,Aṅhiŋ rāmya rinĕṅwakĕn panalimuṙ nalimuṙ ira ri kiŋkiŋ iŋ hati,gĕṇḍiŋ walyan arūm swaranya karĕṅö sawĕṅi kiniduṅan kiduŋ buwun*29:1:283*

loṙ wetan pamalantĕnan kaparĕk iŋ lwaḥ adalĕm asamīpa paṅdyunan,wwaŋnyâwuṅw-amasaŋ damaṙ wruḥ i masanya n amalu malu meḥ tibā ṅĕnĕm,tan paśrī swara niŋ palu dyun asarag tĕwas amaribini ŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,Endaḥ mwaŋ palu wastra rāmya kadi de niŋ amalu daluwaŋ rinĕṅwakĕn*29:2:284*

Aṅdyun karwa rabinya tan padiwasâwiḍiṅan awurahan siliḥ cacad,nitya ŋ śabda paḍêṅgal asrak amalĕs hinalan uliḥ ikâgawe ǥaṭa,strīnyâmet parihāra tan wĕdi kadūṣana n ahala gawe nikā paṭa,kahyun hyun kadi śꜽwa sogata mapaṅǥaṭapaṭa juga hetu niŋ humuŋ*29:3:285*

sakweḥ niŋ baṇijêŋ tĕpas paḍa sumambutakĕn i sagawe nikâlawas,norâpĕk paḍa loƀa lāƀa kaharĕpnya n akuṭa kaṭikan paḍâdamar,saṅkĕp dwalnya huwus ratĕŋ paḍa sumaṅgraha wijila niki n marêŋ pĕkĕn,Asyaŋ syaŋ karĕṅö humuŋ saṅa saṅanya sĕmu niŋ aharĕp katumbasa*29:4:286*

Eñjiŋ wāhu huwus ḍawuḥ pitu muni ŋ paḍahi baṅun akon adandana,sakweḥ niŋ prajurit paḍâmuṅu ri paṅhawin ika kamĕnanya maṅkata,Aṙdđêñjiŋ pwa hiḍĕpnya tĕkwan apuyĕŋ ya ta karaṇa nikâturū muwaḥ,ṅhiŋ maṅkat saŋ ajâkĕmul kĕmul alañciṅan aṅarahakĕn sakêŋ raŧa*29:5:287*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ ri sira marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,prajñā tan kasilib ri tiṅkaḥ iŋ asewaka maṅinakanêŋ tuhan tuhan,wruḥ riŋ yogya kahĕnwa de nira tinūt sapawaraḥ ika rāmya tūt gĕgĕr,yekā rakwa hĕnūnya ṅūni n aṅaliḥ saha jaruman ikâmĕgat gunuŋ*29:6:288*

śūnyâporaŋ ikaŋ gĕgĕṙ hana guhā rĕbaḥ adalĕm arĕs twas iŋ mulat,tan pātmā ŋ aṅuṅaŋ hanan kadi hanâṅduhuṅakĕna tĕkā sakêŋ wuri,tistis nora marâṅlĕṅĕŋ ri pataninya paḍa kadi sinaṅgan iŋ kawi,ṅhiŋ raṅrö gumĕrĕḥ tinūb niŋ aṅin adrĕs aniru gĕrĕḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat*29:7:289*

ṅkānê lĕmbaḥ ikâlaṅö pamaḍĕkan wwaŋ ika wija wijaḥ paḍâṅayar,lumrâkweḥ aputiḥ wuyaḥnya kasawuṙ sumarasaḥ anamaṙ wway iŋ jawuḥ,Awrā tampĕṙ ikâgĕlaṙ kasarakat sarakat asĕmu sāri niŋ puḍak,haṙṣâmbĕk saŋ aja n tĕkâwuya wuyaḥ mata tuwin aharip kadînusap*29:8:290*

tambak tambak akaṇḍa loṙ kidul i pomahan ika kadi piṇḍa niŋ sawaḥ,wwaŋnyârampak amet wĕlut kadi pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ aṅurit katiṅhalan,pakṣinyâgĕŋ agĕŋ humuŋ kadi kĕbo paṅulaḥ awurahan siliḥ buru,yan kawrĕg paḍa möṙ gumĕntĕṙ anamaṙ gĕrĕḥ iŋ adurugan paḍâwĕrö*29:9:291*

Aƀrā lwiṙ sĕkaṙ iŋ laṅit braja katon pamĕwĕḥ i supit iŋ sahiŋ sahiŋ,Aṅjraḥ tan kahanan lĕwas pasuŋ ikâsira sira kadi kĕmbaŋ iŋ karaŋ,lwiṙ luŋ niŋ katiraḥ miraḥ ni suṅut iŋ huraŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ marêŋ lumut,tūt māṙggâharĕmis pĕjaḥ kadi mĕnuṙ saka salawĕ lawö sumamburat*29:10:292*

<basantatilaka>:30 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^sāmpun lĕpas raŧa narendrasutâpan adrĕs,saŋ brāhmaṇê wuri lawan rĕṣi śꜽwa bodđa,Agyā paḍânututi tan hana kāry-araryan,muṅgw-iŋ gajâśwa raŧa masraŋ alumba lumba*30:1:293*

lwaḥ naṙmmadā katĕmu de naranāŧaputra,saŋ brāhmaṇâsaƀa saƀā ri ya sāri sāri,Atyanta niṙmmala paṅawruhanê śucinya,maṙmmanya n uttama wijilnya sakêŋ śaśāṅka*30:2:294*

söḥ puṣpa laywan iŋ atīṙŧa hanê hĕnīnya,kuntul paḍâṅadĕg adĕg ri pacaṙ pacaṙnya,līlā ḍarā ri kalakānya wijaḥ paḍâdyus,Akweḥ mayūra maṅigĕl ri pasiṙ pasiṙnya*30:3:295*

ṅkāna n pararyan arahup naranāŧaputra,muṅgw-iŋ Aśoka sira tan mari śokacitta,nyū danta medi ri manaḥ nira keṅin eṅin,kāṅgĕk sirânĕmu puḍak maṅuḍoḍa riŋ wwꜽ*30:4:296*

nya ŋ cakrawāka paḍa rāmya mahimya himyan,ṅkānê saroruha wĕkasnya lawan priyanya,manda swaranya karĕṅö nira tan sꝑuṭârūm,winrĕg nirâpa ta kalīṅa ni de nirâmrĕg*30:5:297*

haṅśâputiḥ ri tĕṅaḥ adyus aṅumbaŋ umbaŋ,kombak tinūb iŋ aṅin adrĕs aṅiṅgĕk iṅgĕk,mogâraras raras arūm karĕṅö swaranya,kady-âwaraḥ yan alaṅö ri hananya riŋ wwꜽ*30:6:298*

wadwā nirâduluṙ i piṅgiṙ aḍanta ḍanta,Akweḥ lĕpas paḍa kahañjuṙ adoḥ lakunya,maṅsul muwaḥ saha padāti tinuṇḍa pājar,Āpan kinonakĕn aṅantya makuwwa kuwwa*30:7:299*

śīǥrâgawe grĕhalatā mrik arūm sĕkaṙnya,norâkawö paḍa wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅwan,Andul wuṅū mwaŋ asanâṅjraḥ i piṅgiṙ iŋ lwaḥ,ramyâlaṅö pinarĕkanya hanan pamaṅguŋ*30:8:300*

ndaḥ riŋ samantaji hanâdƀuta mūṙtti niŋ hyaŋ,mātaṅgarūpa pinakāṙggaḍa riŋ wanādri,siṅhâṅḍapuṙ wĕdi manambaḥ arĕs tumon ya,Ꜽrāwaṇânurun ujaṙ niŋ anaṙkka naṙkka*30:9:301*

ri lwaḥ saƀānya sĕḍĕŋ adyus ahilya hilyan,nora ŋ ƀayêriya putus wuhayâluṅâṅlwaŋ,Aṅlaṅhuy adrĕs anamaṙ gajamīna mĕtta,himpĕṙ karaŋ liman i kāla nikâṅalimpuŋ*30:10:302*

Ambö ni meda ni gajaḥ naranāŧaputra,sākṣāt inambuŋ ika hetu nika ƀramanta,Abyūran iŋ lwaḥ alĕtuḥ kakĕbuṙ bañunya,wit niŋ saroja kadahut kalawan sĕkaṙnya*30:11:303*

mĕntas pwa yâṅadĕg aṅuṅgul i tīra niŋ lwaḥ,gaṅgĕŋ lawan sarasijâṅhibĕki ry-awaknya,mĕttâwĕrö nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ aǥaṇṭa kambaŋ,Aƀrā katiṅhalan ikā kadi nāgapuṣpa*30:12:304*

meww-îwu saṅꝁya ni gajaḥ naranāŧaputra,ndātan pamaṙppati ri göŋnya lawan guṇanya,Awrĕg sakê taṅan alaḥ ḍyam api n rinukrak,Āpan swaƀāwa niŋ alit juga ta n tinaṅgĕl*30:13:305*

strī strī paḍâṅhili lawan raray anwam anwam,Adrĕs lakunya karikil kawĕdinya ṅūni,maṅke n tĕkêŋ ƀaya sukĕt rwi yayān inambaḥ,wet niŋ takut pati susup susupîŋ alas göŋ*30:14:306*

Akweḥ marêŋ tahĕn anuṅtuŋ amet upāya,watw-înuluṙnya sagĕnuk sawaluḥ salumpaŋ,tĕṇḍas nikaŋ liman awās tinujunya tan len,tog toṙ ndatan dwa katibān dan ikaŋ śilā syuḥ*30:15:307*

krođa ŋ liman mata nikâṅdrĕŋ anon wwaŋ akweḥ,riŋ kāywan aṅhabalaŋ iŋ kayu kayw-aganti,yeka n tumandaŋ aṅayuḥ paŋ agöŋ katuṅkul,syāk pok rĕbaḥ ri walakaŋnya baṅun rinĕṅgan*30:16:308*

wadwā nrĕpātmaja masĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,sārâkusāra śaraṇāśraya wāni riŋ praŋ,krūrâkihal kihal agöŋ karawalya timbul,śūrabratâsira siran paḍa tan dadi jriḥ*30:17:309*

yekâṅlawan paḍa marĕk pinupul sĕmutnya,kweḥnyâpramāṇa satasik ya ta paṅhaḍanya,Ambĕk nikaŋ gaja mamatyana nora wāni,göŋnyâprameya sagunuŋ ya ta paṅgajaḥnya*30:18:310*

māsö hanêŋ raŧa narendrasutâṅagĕm hrū,laṅkap hanê kiwa huwus pinasaŋ talinya,sāmpun minantran inayat saha hastiśikṣā,saṙ cĕb tibâṅĕnani kumƀa nikaŋ gajendra*30:19:311*

sāmpun kĕnâmriḥ aṅusī pulihan tumandaŋ,ndan saṙwwasanđi ni śarīra nikâgraḥ aṅrĕs,yeka n paṅohan aṅadĕg mati tan pasāra,goṙ ƀoḥ tibā kadi śilādri rĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*30:20:312*

waṅkenya sakṣaṇa hananya kadîŋ paṅipyan,teja prakīṙṇna dumilaḥ tĕka tan pasaṅkan,widyāđarâhalĕp adĕṇḍa hanê tĕṅaḥnya,Utpatti niŋ dwirada māti mahāpraƀāwa*30:21:313*

kalpadruma mrik inalapnya pamuṙṣitanya,lwiṙ puṣpawaṙṣa tumibê naranāŧaputra,Āścaṙyya budđi nira sādara de nirâṅliŋ,hyaŋ hyaŋ paran kari kita syapa tā ṅaranta*30:22:314*

<waṅśasŧa>:31 
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = 12

^kĕnoḥ patakwanta ri tiṅkaḥ i ṅhulun,ṅhulun kasaṅꝁya n maṅaran priyambada,swaputra saŋ citraraŧa prakāśita,sirâdiganđaṙwwapatî kadewatan*31:1:315*

ṅhulun sakêŋ swaṙgga wiśāta lālana,Anuṅga nuṅgal mahas iŋ wanāntara,tĕkêŋ pasiṙ tan hana tan kalaŋlaṅan,laṅö niŋ ambĕk saparan tinūtakĕn*31:2:316*

<basantatilaka>:32 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^ṅke naṙmmadā ṅhulun acaṅkrama sāri sāri,kañcit kapaṅgiḥ aṅadĕg ƀagawān pataṅga,pakṣâdyusâpatĕlĕsan tumuluy marêŋ lwaḥ,moǥa ṅhulun tumurun aṅruhurî sirâdyus*32:1:317*

göŋ krođa wākcala sira n panibāni śāpa,Oyuḥ gajaḥ tĕmahanamwa maran mari hyaŋ,ṅke tôṅgwanamwa tan adoḥ ya sakêrikiŋ lwaḥ,nāhan wĕkas ni paṅucap nira kaṙṇnaśūla*32:2:318*

tan miŧya ri ṅhulun ikaŋ gajamĕttarūpa,byaktân asaṇḍuta ŋ ujaṙ yan anĕṅgaḥ alwā,saṅkêŋ amaṅgiḥ i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,tapwan śināpa tumuluy matĕmaḥ gajendra*32:3:319*

An maṅkana bwat i wuyuŋ ƀagawān pataṅga,kāruṇya budđi nira riŋ wĕkasan sirâsiḥ,Āpan ṅhulun marĕk anĕmbaḥ apinta kāsiḥ,maṅhyaŋ ry-anugraha nirê rikaŋ antaśāpa*32:4:320*

mojaṙ sirâsĕmu manis tĕkap iŋ tumiṅhal,Om haywa saṅśaya ri sidđa niŋ antaśāpa,tan lupta yan tĕka hĕlĕm saŋ ajâhawan ṅke,tuŋtuŋ ni sañjata nikā hawananta mantuk*32:5:321*

sāmpun sirâmĕkasakĕn wacanântaśāpa,luṅhā sira ṅhulun aṅanti humeṙ tĕkanta,sowenta tan tĕka ya kāraṇa niŋ ƀramanta,mĕttâwĕrö pira piraŋ tahunĕn byamoha*32:6:322*

maṅke n ḍatĕŋ kita sahâśwa sahasra saṅꝁya,ṅke naṙmmadâwija wijaḥ sawatĕk watĕkta,mātĕṅga papraŋ aṅiriŋ paḍa sāra śūra,mawrĕg rĕbaḥ binuru ni ṅhulun iŋ paḍöman*32:7:323*

Aṅhiŋ kitâmanaḥ anuṅsuŋ iŋ astra tīkṣṇa,syuḥ kumƀa ni ṅhulun ikā tinut iŋ paratra,ndātan paniṣꝑala wawaŋ maluyâdadi hyaŋ,sākṣāt kitâmrĕta wijil nikaŋ antaśāpa*32:8:324*

Atyanta göŋ ni hutaŋ i ṅhulun apramāṇa,saṅmohana ŋ pamalĕsê kita diwyaśāstra,ganđaṙwwaśāstra pinajöŋ hyaŋ asañjatêka,jñānanta maṅlĕpasakĕn saha mantra sidđi*32:9:325*

Atyanta yogya yan ajinta ya kawruhanta,kārāđananya saha mantra sahêndikanya,pöŋpöŋ ṅhulun wruḥ i wĕkas ni rusit rusitnya,śaktinya kawruhan anambĕhanê guṇanta*32:10:326*

ndātan pamatyani guṇanya yadin guṇanta,śatrw-âđamâpituwi tan mati denya mūṙcꞓa,moǥâturū sahana niŋ ripu tan wri rātnya,nistanya maṅkana yayā kita yan jayêŋ praŋ*32:11:327*

he saŋ priyambada kita n paṅutus paṅajya,moǥâwiraŋ hulun apan gumawe laranta,ṅūnî sĕḍĕŋta matĕmaḥ gajamattarūpa,tan len ṅhulun kaṅaranan karaṇanta māti*32:12:328*

hā hāḥ hade saŋ aja denta manaṅgaḥ eraŋ,An sāhasâmĕjahi ri ṅhulunĕn gajendra,Āpan prasidđa kita maṅhwatakĕn kajanman,Atyanta göŋ i hutaŋ i ṅhulunĕn maluy hyaŋ*32:13:329*

yadyan saƀūṙ ƀuwaḥ ikaŋ guṇa kawruhanta,tātan sadoṣa yan atambĕha wīṙyya saswaḥ,ndā maṅkanā kita n aṅajya wimohanāstra,taṅgap nihan hila hila ŋ tumulak paweweḥ*32:14:330*

An saŋ priyambada kĕdö maṅutus maṅajya,mary-âwiraŋ saŋ aja sāmpun atiṅkaḥ uṅgwan,loṙ saŋ priyambada kidul saŋ ajâtalaṅkup,saṅmohanênaji nirêṅgal apan widagđa*32:15:331*

sanđinya kāku saha śakti ni dewatanya,saṅyoga niŋ śarawara mwaŋ ikā tujunya,sāmpun tama stuti nikā saha kūṭamantra,saṅhāramantra paḍa kawruḥ ira praƀeda*32:16:332*

wruḥ saŋ priyambada ri haṙṣa narendraputra,An pembuḥ astra śara sūkṣma mahāpraƀāwa,tiṅkaḥ niŋ apraŋ inucap nira moǥa jambat,Amwit sirâsĕmu manis baśa de niŋ ojar*32:17:333*

he mitra mantuka kakanta lumarya maṅke,sidđā ŋ prayojana kita n ḍatĕṅêŋ widaṙbƀa,nāhan wuwus nira nĕhĕṙ maṅagĕm sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,luṅhâhawan gagana mĕltuk apan sira hyaŋ*32:18:334*

<jagadđita>:33 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^sāmpun prāpta sirêŋ surālaya wicitraraŧa paḍa suꝁa n tumon sira,ndan saŋ kāri kamānuṣan hĕla hĕlâṅucap ucap i sĕḍĕŋ nirâpupul,nistanya n tama de nirâṅaji taŧāpi salahasa ri saŋ priyambada,yan tĕṅhā kadi tan tumuṅkula sawet ni karakĕtan irâṅdĕlö tawaŋ*33:1:335*

sanđyākāla pasaŋ damaṙ nrĕpatiputra manaḍaḥ i huwus nirâjapa,Eñjiŋ pūṙwwaka saŋ priyambada ginoṣṫi nira mahuwusan tĕṅaḥ wĕṅi,wahw-amrĕm tumuluy tinaṅhi sira maṅkat asalĕsĕk i tīra niŋ nadī,gĕntĕṙ ni grit ikaŋ raŧâmĕkarakĕn kucup iŋ asana rāmya tūt hĕnū*33:2:336*

Eñjiŋ kāla nira n tĕkêŋ pasiṙ alasnya pĕtĕŋ asĕmu śeṣa niŋ wĕṅi,lwiṙ haṙṣā gaganâsĕgĕḥ pawulatanya gĕrĕḥ ika kadi priyambada,moǥâśrī kumĕḍap kilatnya nĕhĕṙ aṅluru luru kadi medi maṅdu lor,kady-ânĕmbahakĕn sĕkaṙ niŋ asanânisi huyaŋ i riris nikâṅdadak*33:3:337*

mambö sāgara rāmya niŋ laṅit awaṙṇna tali hurut urutnya tan pĕgat,kālaṅkyaŋnya baṅun jukuŋ niŋ amayaŋ lĕyĕp i lari nikâmaḍĕm ḍarat,kuntul möṙ kadi tuṇḍan iŋ banawa kāri tan ilu kajahat lanâlayar,saŋ hyaŋ candra baṅun bahitra ḍatĕŋ iŋ kulĕm amawa śaśā marê jawa*33:4:338*

meǥa lwiṙ karaŋ iŋ laṅit kadi wĕrĕḥ limut ika ri sare nikâputiḥ,wahw-âmīt i kuwuŋ kuwuŋnya sawaneḥ karĕrĕban akucĕm pĕgat pĕgat,gĕntĕṙnyâwurahan humuŋ kadi katunwan i larap i kilat nikā murub,runtuḥ piṅgiṙ ikâtĕmaḥ jawuḥ anūtakĕn aṅin alaṅö tibânisiḥ*33:5:339*

rāmya lwiṙ siluman karaŋ ri muꝁa niŋ muhara paḍa paḍâṅhapit bañu,Alwā tiṅkaḥ i meꝁalanya ri tĕṅaḥ paṅadĕg adĕgan iŋ marâṅlĕṅĕŋ,karwânuṅgul apāntaran sapaṅuhuḥ kadi gupura śiwak sakêŋ adoḥ,lwiṙ hambal sꝑaṭikâŋ alun turunan iŋ kawi pĕjaḥ atuhâṅhañut laṅö*33:6:340*

priṅgâhrit tĕpi niŋ samudra kadi paṅhinĕpan i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ labuḥ kapat,lwiṙ prāsāda pukaḥ karaŋ ni paraṅanya hana kadi siluŋluŋ iŋ kawi,Ꜽṙttambaŋnya baṅun wwit iŋ truḥ asĕwö kilat awilĕt alūŋ awaṅkawa,lumrâwaṙṇna rĕṅit kukusnya sinawat sawat inidĕran iŋ guruṇḍaya*33:7:341*

miṅgut piṇḍa nikaŋ karaŋ liman anuṅkuli paraṅan i piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik,lwiṙ molaḥ tulale nikâmijilakĕn bañu kadi paṅanak niŋ eṙttali,kahyun hyun kumucuṙ parĕŋ rwa tumĕḍun lĕṅĕŋ aṅĕnani tiṅhas iŋ karaŋ,rĕmpū syuḥ Amĕniṙ mĕniṙ kadi tinapyan iŋ aṅin aputiḥ sumamburat*33:8:342*

paṇḍan māti lĕṅĕŋ sumuṇḍay akaraŋ hulu karaŋ i sare nikaŋ pasir,sakweḥ niŋ ƀramarânaṅis paḍa sumuṅkĕm aṅarĕki sĕkaṙ huwus lĕwas,dinyūs iŋ truḥ i saṅhub iŋ jalađi saŋsaya lĕṅĕŋ arurub rurub limut,hemanyânwam arūm puḍak nika tumūt pĕjaḥ i turuŋ ikâtulis ṭikā*33:9:343*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:34

^nyū dantâsĕpi tuṅga tuṅgal aṅadĕg muṅgw-î rĕṅat niŋ trĕbis,lĕŋlĕŋnya n hana riŋ pasiṙ siliḥ awe lāwan ṙyyak iŋ sāgara,tan wruḥ yan tinulis parab sahana niŋ wwaḥnyâkĕmul nīrada,de niŋ laṅw-anaput katuṅkul i laṅö niŋ nūsa mukṣa n rĕrĕb*34:1:344*

<śiꝁariṇī>:35 
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 17

^mahantĕn sāk riñcuŋ lĕṅĕŋ i tĕpi niŋ sāgara lĕyĕp,palambaŋnyâkweḥ nora wĕnaṅa wacan śīṙṇna lamukĕn,tulisnyânuṅgal wikw-acĕpuḥ atalaṅkup katuruhan,tumuṅkul ƀāwanyâḍĕku ḍĕkuḥ apiṇḍânasi hatĕp*35:1:345*

Ikaŋ prāsāda syuḥ karahan apa tekâmarikala,tibê piṅgiṙ niŋ sāgara kasiḥ arĕp hyaŋ gaṇapati,katampwan de niŋ ṙyyak mata nira kumĕmbĕŋ kadi lumuḥ,mulat kady-ahyun wuṅwakĕna sira yan kāla hasila*35:2:346*

karaŋ sawwaŋ muṅgw-iŋ jalađi mapa mūlanya ta kunaŋ,wilĕt niŋ meǥa ry-âwak ika sagibaḥ tan pinahuwus,winaswās kady-ânabraṅa sĕmu nikâṅlaṅhwiy anĕṅaḥ,baṅun ƀrāntâmaṅgiḥ pasiṙ aharĕp aṅlimbaṅa laṅö*35:3:347*

<girisa>:36 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^banawa kajahat iŋ lod biṅkas de niŋ alun agöŋ,tihaŋ ika gumalaṅgaŋ muṅgw-iŋ tuṇḍan ika marĕk,kadi ta pamĕkulanya n māsiḥ tan wĕnaŋ apasaḥ,sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ līṅanya n wruḥ aṅucapa*36:1:348*

wukiṙ anak anĕlat riŋ wwꜽ niŋ sāgara ri tĕṅaḥ,kadi sakadaṅa lāwan wwaŋ mūṙcꞓā kawi pasisi,sĕmu sĕmu nika sānak lāwan ṙyyak jĕnĕk aharas,pili piliḥ abapenduŋ truḥ truḥ māṙgga nika lĕṅĕŋ*36:2:349*

layaṙ iŋ amayaŋ akweḥ ṅkānê soṙnya humaliwat,karahan aburu maṙmmanya n kedĕṙ nĕhĕṙ awĕlaḥ,đwatala rayuŋ ikânraŋ lumrā söḥ paṅanan ika,bañak aṅidĕri nūsā kāraŋnya n midĕṙ alaṅö*36:3:350*

patani kadi jamuṙ syuŋ rūpanyâmanis atulis,kalimutan i siluk niŋ groŋ groŋ iŋ paraṅan arĕs,kakawin ika palambaŋ riŋ lambaŋ cinacahakĕn,cĕcĕk ika hana tan saḥ muny-asriŋ baṅun amaca*36:4:351*

<jagadđita>:37 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^māry-âmet lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ nrĕpatiputra lumaris ahawan gunuŋ gunuŋ,Ambö niŋ pakis ĕṇḍaḥ iŋ walahaṙ aṅlĕwihi waṅi ni ganđa niŋ pupur,moǥârūm sirarā nikaŋ kayu ragas kadi hulĕs apulaŋ lawan burat,sakweḥ niŋ kahalintaṅan rumimaŋ ambĕk ira winulatan paḍâlaṅö*37:1:352*

paṇḍan suṇḍay asoŋ latāṅkura paranti para kawi mahas lanâpikat,paŋ niŋ campaka śudđi guṇḍik aṅilo ri harĕp ika maṅuṅkul uṅkuli,luṅlūṅanya tikĕl tikĕl katitihan papikatan agĕnĕt hibĕk hĕlar,tan śoƀa ŋ kitiran jaraḥ pili piliḥ luput alara kasambĕt iŋ habĕt*37:2:353*

wwantĕn rāmya kadewagurwan aṅuṅaŋ jalađi kadi kalaṅwan iŋ tulis,saŋ muṅgw-îriya tan wĕnaŋ lumaganîndriya nira kawĕnaŋ binañcana,paṅliṅgāna sawaŋ sawaŋ ni hayu nîdĕman ira sĕmu niŋ warāpsarī,kady-âṅanti ri sāmpunanya n apatūtan aniliba marêŋ surālaya*37:3:354*

ṅkānêŋ bwat halu sāk durenya kahanan nrĕpatanaya tumiṅhal iŋ tulis,heman waṙṇna nikâsamun katuruhan lutuṙ asamun inambaḥ iŋ cĕcĕk,ṅhiŋ dewī kawĕkas lawan kili paḍâṅadĕg adĕg abĕbĕd bĕbĕd hati,kady-âminta tumūta rūpa nika budđi saŋ aja hiḍĕpan kamānuṣan*37:4:355*

ṅkānê rĕmbaṅan iŋ juraŋ mpu tapa rāmya mamuluku katuṅku tuṅkulan,wuṅkal kedĕran aṅjĕlag sadĕdĕg iŋ sapi kaparĕk i piṅgiṙ iŋ galĕŋ,lĕmbunyân ahĕle hĕli n palayanan pawulatan ika de nikaŋ watu,Asrak waṅsulan iŋ kiyâtrĕt alaṅö lĕṅĕŋ araras aniṙwwa niṙwakĕn*37:5:356*

nyāsa lwiṙ minahā gunuŋ pinakapājaran aṅadĕg i mađya niŋ juraŋ,lwīṙ apwī kumukus miraḥ ni kayu teja nika kasaputan himâputiḥ,wwꜽ saṅkêŋ paraṅan ya kadrĕsan aṅin kadi siniramakĕn sumamburat,saŋ wrĕdđaṙṣi katon iŋ agra sawaŋ aṙcca lamukĕn alaṅö kasaṅhuban*37:6:357*

siṅgiḥ kottaman iŋ wanāśrama saƀā saŋ ataki taki niṣparigraha,kaywanyâwruḥ acandanâpriḥ atĕṅö jawa huwi kusumâṅjraḥ iŋ talun,kālaṅkyaŋnya lĕyĕp wiśāta baṅun ahyun atapa riŋ aṅin huwus lĕpas,saŋ hyaŋ lek sumĕnö prakāśa śuci śukla pinakasuluḥ iŋ hanêŋ wukir*37:7:358*

tan saḥ riŋ daluwaŋ kukap nika subadđa sĕkaṙ ikaŋ uluṙ paḍâjaṭā,wrenyâṅalwaŋ ikaŋ warāha wana tan parabi suꝁa manambi riŋ tahĕn,mwaŋ saṙppâtapa tāpan abrata lanâṅaluṣa puyuḥ ikâkipū kipū,niṙđūma ŋ balĕman lumöŋ barĕbĕk iŋ kayu pinaṅan ika n hanêŋ alas*37:8:359*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ>:38 
– – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^budđi nrĕpatisuta jĕnĕk ya kāraṇa nirâṅrĕwĕŋ alas akulĕm,sakweḥ nira saŋ ajaṙ ajaṙ marĕk saha kilaŋ hinaturakĕn ira,ramyâṅucap i sakaharĕp nirêŋ ꝑala nikaŋ tapa ginawayakĕn,Eñjiŋ sira tumurun atūt alas wahu tinoṙ pinakapatalĕsan*38:1:360*

deśâsĕpi hawan ira kālasan sipi kaniṣṫa nika gatarasa,Aṅluḥ wwaŋ ika pinanasan ḍinaṇḍa sinipat layat apalarasan,Akweḥ pahutaṅan i sawaḥ gaganya paḍa tan hana maṅinak inak,lumbuŋnya kasiḥ arĕp aninya ya n milu katuṅkĕb alawas aṅariŋ*38:2:361*

Akweḥ wray anusup anukĕt nukĕt baṅun amet kayu parĕŋ adulur,ḍaŋḍaŋnya lumĕkas aṅatĕṙ sĕsĕḥ kaṅĕlihan sawaŋ aṅipil ipil,pakṣinya palatuk amaduŋ maduŋ kahiḍĕpanya n amahayu kuwuŋ,wwaḥ niŋ kamalagi tumatiŋ katon kadi caluk niŋ anutu nutuhi*38:3:362*

kācāṙyyan alawas inatīta śīṙṇna pamicāran ika katuruhan,riñcuŋ saka nika sasisiḥ siliḥ jaga murantak aṅĕmuki parab,norâkṣara kakawin i paṅlarinya paḍa tan hana katĕmu lĕbur,ṅhiŋ candana kasirat agātra mātra ri tawiŋnya kari kadi panu*38:4:363*

jöŋ niŋ giri gahana kadewagurwan ahalĕp lura luraḥ arĕnĕb,strī strī dwijakula śuci śudđa saŋ pinakamaṅgala niŋ anaruka,tūs niŋ wulakan aṅali mekalanya śatapattra nika mĕkaṙ arūm,sakweḥ niŋ amaṅan i lumutnya rakwa cinacad puru puru katalu*38:5:364*

<śiꝁariṇī>:39 
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 17

^byatītan meḥ prāptêŋ nagara saŋ ajâṅel bala nira,Araryan ṅkānê jro kuṭi katĕmu sakweḥ para wiku,tinamwī tamwī riŋ sĕḍĕṅan amanis de nira mulat,Apan prāya ŋ wastw-alpa maṅinaki yan riŋ sĕḍĕŋ aṅel*39:1:365*

wiwakṣan sakweḥ saŋ para ratu hinundaŋ paḍa tĕka,paḍâkuṇḍaŋ gĕṇḍiŋ gumĕrĕḥ asĕluṙ tan papĕgatan,tuwin paṅhrik niŋ tuṅgaṅan asahuran lāgi karĕṅö,Ikaŋ sattwâlöŋ śabda nika baṅun asyaŋ syaŋ aṅuhuḥ*39:2:366*

kaḍatwan saŋ ƀojâtiśaya mara göŋnyâparamita,yayâhöt maṅke kāṙyya nira ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ para ratu,pĕnuḥ tamwī tamwî sahana para taṇḍâlana ṅiwö,tĕkêŋ māṙggâgöŋ nora pinakapahidwan paḍa hibĕk*39:3:367*

Ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ sāgara kahibĕkan wwaŋ kadi bañu,karaŋ mātaṅgâkāra ni liman ikâneka majajar,baṅun ṙyyak polaḥ niŋ đwaja kagurilap kadrĕsan aṅin,curik wahwas patrĕm lumarap asĕmu praŋ praŋ agalak*39:4:368*

sanistanya n tan waspada wiṣaya niŋ śabda karĕṅö,tĕkap niŋ gĕṇḍiŋ mwaŋ grĕbĕg i laku niŋ wwaŋ mapapagan,yayâtaḥ wrĕtta śrī raǥusuta karĕṅw-an sira tĕka,wulat herĕn taŋ wwaŋ sanagara paḍâlaḥ rĕṅĕ rĕṅön*39:5:369*

lumampaḥ saŋ ƀojâmapag i saŋ ajâpan sira tĕka,kasuŋsuŋ riŋ māṙggâṅucap ucap aluṅguḥ paḍa suꝁa,parĕŋ maṅkat ramyâduluṙ iniriŋ iŋ wwaŋ sanagara,Ikaŋ rājya lwiṙ bĕntara muꝁa nikân aṙdđa marupĕk*39:6:370*

Umaḥ niŋ taṇḍâgöŋ pinakapasĕnāhê nrĕpasuta,kulĕm saŋ hyaŋ sanđyā diwasa niŋ amūjâjapa japa,tĕka ŋ pamyāpārê sira wijil ikaŋ sāgara wukir,ndatan waṙṇnan tiṅkaḥ ni panaḍaḥ irâkweḥ cinarita*39:7:371*

<jagadđita>:40 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^tiṅkaḥ śrîndumatī n kapiŋ tiga nira n piniḍuḍuk i dalĕm kaŧākĕna,Akweḥ pañcabale ri wiṅkiṅan ikaŋ pamiḍuḍukan i soṙ huwus hibĕk,de niŋ strī paḍa hinyasan cumurigênunus awak ika waṙṇna sañjata,byaktâkūṅa kalĕṅgakêŋ panulisan puḍak ikaŋ anulad raras nika*40:1:372*

twas niŋ meǥa dinadyakĕn waṅunan uttama pinahuwus iŋ labuḥ kapat,tumpaŋ pitw-aruhuṙ sinaptaƀuwanâparimita kalaṅönya riŋ tawaŋ,truḥ truḥ mwaŋ larap iŋ kilat hatĕp ikā karaṇa nika lanâkuwuŋ kuwuŋ,gĕntĕṙnyâṅdadi kumbaŋ edran anaṅis hana lĕṅĕŋ aṅurambat iŋ tĕtö*40:2:373*

ṙyyak niŋ tīṙŧa sinrĕṣṭi wastra tinulis pinakatiba tibān linaṅwakĕn,tustus niŋ maṇi sūṙyyakānta dumilaḥ rahina wĕṅi dinadyakĕn damar,kĕmbaŋ niŋ cirapattra kalpatarupuṣpa sadĕdĕg aṅadĕg tigaŋ siki,māyā niŋ wulan iŋ samudra mađu śudđa saꝑala ginawe laṅit laṅit*40:3:374*

byaktâbyakta nikaŋ tulis wuwuḥ i kādƀuta nika tulis iŋ huwus tama,yan kĕmbaŋ kadi mambwa rūmnya kadi molaha winilĕt i luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,mwaŋ yan wwaŋ wwaṅan aṙjja kady-aṅucapâsĕmu sĕmu guyu de nikā mulat,wimba hyaŋ smara śudđi de niŋ anulis lwiṙ amanaha manaḥ nrĕpātmajā*40:4:375*

ṅkā tôṅgwan nṛpatiputrikā piniḍuḍuk tuhu tuhu sira janma dewatī,tan sāmānya mahāpraƀāwa tĕka riŋ kaka kaka kadi dewakanyakā,Aśrī pahyas ira bwat indrawanitâmuwuhi halĕp ira n hanêŋ saƀā,ḍaŋ saṅǥâguñĕpan ƀaṭāra karikâṅrakĕt ujaṙ ira yan tumon sira*40:5:376*

sakweḥ kweḥ nira saŋ kadaŋ haji huwus kili marĕk atatā paḍâtuha,mambö paṙwwata pājaran halĕp i de nira humalĕpakĕn suputrikā,Endaḥ mwaŋ sira saŋ rare hañaṙ ataṅkil ahayu hayu wahw-ameꝁala,mambö maṇḍala riŋ saƀā paṅuparĕṅga ni halĕp ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā*40:6:377*

strī strī wāhu cumampakâsĕmu hijo pamulu nika pinantĕs iŋ saƀā,sampiṙnyêŋ jaja tan paniṣꝑala hananya muwuhi halĕp iŋ wulaŋ tatur,tuṅgal denya mawâmbĕk abwat atuhan ri parĕk ika ri jöŋ nrĕpātmajā,lwiṙ dewī humatuṙ sakêŋ surapadânrahakĕna halĕp iŋ surālaya*40:7:378*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ>:41 
– – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^praḥ praḥ nrĕpawaraduhitā ri guṇḍik ira len i kaka kaka nira,yan wruḥ wruḥ agamĕl aṅiduŋ lawan wruḥ aṅawat ya linĕṅĕnan ira,Embuḥ pwa guṇa nika siniṅhĕlan kinaluṅan ya kinalĕwihakĕn,sāmpun pwa ya kawi paḍa kāku siŋ guṇa samaṅkana ya kinarahan*41:1:379*

sakweḥnya paḍa marĕk anaṇḍaŋ anwam araras rara rahayu wagĕd,saƀyâmanis aṅucap ikāŋ asiṅhĕl akaluŋ wahu kawi kakawin,ndan rwaŋ puluḥ ikaŋ akaraḥ jitākṣara wicakṣaṇa naṭakagiṇa,ṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayaluḥ ikaŋ inuttamâsisik ĕmās maṇi nĕhĕṙ amawa*41:2:380*

<jagadđita>:42 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^prāpta ŋ rātri yayan katon hayu ni waṙṇna nira ri wijil iŋ niśākara,hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ mađumāsa rūpa nira yan kasaṅa kasapuluḥ tiniṅhalan,maṅke n māsa kapat hyaŋ iŋ masa kapat kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ mulat,cañco strī liṅa niŋ tumon sira mĕne n huwus atĕmu lawan nrĕpātmaja*42:1:381*

lumrâmintaŋ ahöm ri bāhu lumarap jĕnu nira kanakâṅhulap hulap,Embuḥ söŋ ni tutup gĕluŋ nira murub maṇik ika kadi motaṙ otaran,de niŋ kostuƀa nīla kādƀuta sĕkaṙ taji nira sumĕnö kapañjutan,Ūṙṇnā śudđa huwus hanêŋ rahi nirâsĕmu paṅawaka tĕṅran iŋ hurip*42:2:382*

ndin ṅgānya ŋ wwaŋ anĕmwa rūpa kadi rūpa nira n ahayu rājaputrikā,wwaŋ riŋ rājya yayan kapūhan aṅalĕm ri sira kadi hañaṙ hañaṙ mulat,Aśrī waṙṇna nira n tuhan saꝑala yogya n adĕgakĕna ratwa niŋ tulis,tan samwas lawaŋ iŋ kaḍatwan inucap milu milu kawĕṅān tiniṅhalan*42:3:383*

paṅkun mesya ṭikā kayogyan i wĕtis nira damarana teja niŋ wulan,pantĕs yan makasumpiṅĕn kikirĕn iŋ kuku kuku nira kosapêŋ laṭi,reꝁan riŋ kakawin wilāpa kahalĕp ni susu nira parantya niŋ parab,tan sāhêŋ ratu śakti kenaka ni soca nira yan ikĕtĕn sĕkaṙ taji*42:4:384*

Ekĕl roma nirâraras kadi katona rumaraba sakêŋ gĕluŋ lukar,Akweḥ mahyun aṅuḍwa de nira yan ahyas anisigi wajâṅhĕmū guyu,yogyâsaṅkan aṅin dumadyakĕna polaḥ i tikĕl i halis nira n cala,byaktâgatgat ataṅhya taṅhya manaḥ iŋ mulat i muꝁa nira n pasaŋ damar*42:5:385*

ndin putry-âhayu hayw-amaṅpaṅa hayunya ri hayu nira n ahyas aṅḍiri,sakweḥ niŋ wwaŋ ahadyan akryan asawaŋ hinayu marĕk i jöŋ nirâlawas,pahyas niŋ para pora maṅhiribi pahyas ira hinayu cihna niŋ manūt,Ekacꞓattra raras raras nira paṅöban iŋ ahayu sujanmakanyakā*42:6:386*

sakweḥ saŋ ratu tan wĕnaŋ sahasa kewala humĕnĕŋ aṅantyakĕn pariḥ,Aṅlampū sumĕsĕl śarīra nira tan wĕnaŋ anĕkani senakê hati,mogânaṅgĕl arĕs rumĕṅwakĕn i kādƀuta ni hayu narendraputrikā,mawwat rāga wilāpa cihna niŋ akūŋ alaḥ alĕḥ akirim kirim ṭikā*42:7:387*

Akweḥ pahyas irârĕbut kahulunan kahiḍĕpan ira de nikaŋ marĕk,rorw-aŋ campaka rāmya māyun ayunan ri jaja nira n amaṅya maṅyani,lāwan pādapa tan wĕnaŋ saḥ i sirâmĕpĕti gaway ika n sĕḥ iŋ gĕluŋ,tañjuŋ muṅgw-i kapö nira n mrik inaṅit marĕk araras anulya nulyani*42:8:388*

prāptôliḥ kalaṅön ikāŋ asana rāmya pinakakalasā nirâturū,mwaŋ roṇḍonya tinap rinūpaka tilam sinalinan i sĕḍĕŋ nikâluñut,maṅgā sĕmpalĕn aṅkĕn eñjiŋ alapĕn humatura śayanā nira n rimaŋ,swaṙgga n māti kakiŋkiṅan huwus akīṙtty-amihutaṅi laṅö ri jöŋ nira*42:9:389*

moliḥ waṙṣa sipat nirârahat i solaḥ ika tĕka hirĕŋ hanê mata,kālanya n kahĕmū sĕpaḥ nira baṅun pinakaliḍaḥ ira n hanê tutuk,kāsiḥ kāsiḥ irâlawas karika puṇḍutan ira kasĕlap hanê hati,ṅhiŋ kĕṇḍit nira mās tumūt i parahasyan ira wahu marĕk sinanmata*42:10:390*

tambe rakwa sira n swayambarakĕnâmiliha sakaharĕp nira praƀu,ndān ambĕk nira kewalâwiraŋ i līṅa niŋ umulat anĕṅgahâhaṅan,Āpan tan hana ṅūni kewala sirâmuṅari pinakakabwatan hañar,yekā hetu nirâwiweka kalawan kaka kaka wihikan riŋ iṅgita*42:11:391*

ndātan kaṙkkaśa de nirâṅucap ucap ri pasĕluṙ iŋ ujaṙ sirâṅucap,ndi ŋ paṙwwa ndi kitâṅrĕṅö n hana kadi ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā,yadyastun hana maṅkanā niyata ta pwa wiraŋ ika kadîraŋ i ṅhulun,saŋkṣepanya huwus katon wiđi nareśwara dinuluṙ i tan siḥ iŋ wiđi*42:12:392*

Āpan kenaka niŋ kadi ṅhulun aṅanti ri kaka haji yan sirâsiha,heṙ herĕn palarĕn hanâsiha ƀaṭāra tumĕkakĕna đaṙmma ni ṅhulun,prāptânomaha yogya liŋ nrĕpati samƀawa kaharĕpa ni ṅhulun muwaḥ,yadyastun layata ṅhulun pi tawanĕn ry-uƀaya haji paran kasaṅśaya*42:13:393*

lāwan yan hana ratw-anomaha marā ta sira humaturê nareśwara,ndātan kahyuna ni ṅhulun sira tuhun kaka haji sira kewalâharĕp,haywâmiđyani ta pwa siḥ siha nirâmawarĕṅĕha ri budđya ni ṅhulun,ndak ton duḥka nikaŋ kinĕdwakĕn apaṅgiha wiꝑala yan tan paḍâharĕp*42:14:394*

yan kāṅĕn suꝁa niŋ licin dumadak ahyun adaluwaṅa haṙṣa riŋ jamaŋ,denya n kilya rarā makāśraya nareśwara kumĕmita kāla niŋ rare,yan wrĕdđâjara đaṙmma riŋ giriwanâmagĕhakĕna ri đaṙmma saŋ wiku,rāmya ŋ waŋ guru loka saṙwwa tĕka yan lumaku laku rinampak iŋ kili*42:15:395*

maṅke pwa n ḍumawuḥ wiđi nrĕpati tan pamawarĕṅĕḥ i budđi ni ṅhulun,ṅwaŋ dūra n wĕnaṅâjñalaṅǥana tuhun rasa pĕjaha tibêŋ paluṅguhan,Ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp kalīṅa ni manaḥ nira yan aharĕp iŋ swayambara,maṅgâṅdadya limut ṅhulun ri wiraŋ i ṅhulun amiliha jalwa riŋ saƀā*42:16:396*

<nawahaṙṣa>:43 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^tuhan i ṅhulun akṣamakĕna paṅucap ni manĕḥta rĕṅön,wiđi saŋ praƀu samƀawa kĕkĕsakĕnê hati yogya dahat,dumadak pwa hade n katĕkana rinasan ri manaḥta tuhan,pira haywa nikâṅucapa n ahala yan hiniḍĕp mahala*43:1:397*

pituhun wiđi saŋ praƀu tuhan anipis kawiraŋta hade,paḍa wāhu ḍatĕŋ sahana hana nikaŋ pariwāra marĕk,Amahuṙ hurakĕn ri para ratu pinetnya sirêŋ wĕgilĕn,sira saŋ kinabehan inalĕm ika rĕṅwakĕnanta tuhan*43:2:398*

<jagadđita>:44 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ nāŧêŋ magađa praƀāwa nira tan patĕpi kadi laṅit maṅambara,lwiṙ widyāđara daṙśśanīya pakatonan i bala nira śūra dug siṅī,Ahyaŋ solaḥ irâmanis kawadi de nira lituhayu tan pasiŋsiṅan,sākṣāt indra sakêŋ surālaya kaweni tumuta mijilêŋ swayambara*44:1:399*

krūrākāra saŋ aṅganāŧa sanirukti sira yan aruhuṙ sulakṣaṇa,saƀyâmbĕk nira tan rinakwa sira yan praƀu lituhayu sādarâṅucap,śakty-ânindya mahāpraƀāwa kumutug bala nira paḍa śūra suśrama,tan pendaḥ kadi saŋ hyaŋ agni mijil amralayakĕna rumampaka ŋ jagat*44:2:400*

siṅhâmbĕk saŋ awantināŧa kadi saŋ yama guṇa nira lokapālaka,norâđaṙmma ṅaranya rakwa yan i ƀūmi nira paḍa suꝁâgawe hayu,söḥ wadwā nira piṇḍa kiṅkarabalâmawa curiga gadāyuđâpupul,sākṣāt mrĕtyu curik nirâkas aluṅid baṅun aṅayam ayam parāṅmuꝁa*44:3:401*

tan pendaḥ baruṇânurun saŋ anupāđipati suyaśa ƀūmipālaka,himpĕṙ sāgara kāṅinan bala nirâṅrwabi nagara hibĕk tĕkê dalĕm,tĕkwan lwiṙ nira riŋ raṅin đwaja wĕlaŋ wĕlaŋ aputiḥ arok lawan hirĕŋ,rāhu mwaŋ śaśiwimba rūpa nika kāraṇa ni musuḥ irâtabĕḥ titir*44:4:402*

<sragđara>:45 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^siŋ solaḥ saŋ susenā pracalita kadi saŋ bāyu riŋ budđi madrĕs,wadwā wadwā riŋ ambĕk lituhayu katĕṅĕṙ yan prawīrâpriḥ iŋ praŋ,himpĕṙ seḍuŋ karĕsrĕs bala nira kumisik lwiṙ gĕlap holiḥ asriŋ,byakta syūha ŋ musuḥ de nira n asĕmu hudan sañjatâwoṙ halisyus*45:1:403*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgadâtyanta sugiḥ ira hibĕk mās maṇik rājayogya,līlâcum somya saŋ wꜽśrawana paḍa nira n ǥorarūpâdawâgöŋ,norânaṇḍaŋ yatan mās bala nira satĕgal kāla niŋ hanyan aṅjraḥ,sakweḥ niŋ śatru śīṙṇnâkuniṅa wulat ikā de nirâpan waḥ iŋ mās*45:2:404*

Aśrī saŋ pāṇḍya śudđākrĕti nira satirun paṇḍitânwam widagđa,tan kāsy-asiḥ tuhun tan harĕp iŋ ulaḥ agasyak yayan sopacāra,saŋ hyāŋ īśāna sākṣāt paḍa nira n ahalĕp riŋ saƀā nora tan wruḥ,Atyantêŋ yoga kawruḥ nira karaṇa nira n katwaŋ iŋ śatru śakti*45:3:405*

wwantĕn saṅkêry-ayođyā lituhayu dahatĕn rājaputrâdwitīya,ndan rakwânak mahārāja raǥu saŋ aja saṅjñā nirêŋ rāt prakāśa,saŋ saptāđikrĕtâtyanta halĕp ira kabeḥ soṙ kagöṅan pratāpa,himpĕṙ candrâkucĕm tan wani mulat i narendrātmaja lwiṙ hyaŋ aṙkka*45:4:406*

saŋ hyaŋ brahmâgawe rūpa nira kadi paran riŋ raras māṙ manisnya,yadyan ganđaṙwwa widyāđara niyata nikâsora riŋ rūpa kāliḥ,Aṅhiŋ hyaŋ kāma saŋ samƀawa mapaga raras rūm nirêŋ maṙttyaloka,sāmpun pwâṅāśrayê citta nira masuruhan rāga kuŋ don irâṅher*45:5:407*

ndān ambĕk ni ṅhulun ṅhiŋ sira juga kadĕlö n kāptya rakryan suputrī,Anwam pūṙṇnêŋ paṅawruḥ lituhayu taruṇâpālapan kṣatriyāṅśa,jaṅgâṅuṅsiṙ kapat rāmya nira winulatan dlāha yadyan patĕmwa,Āpan tuṅgal sirêŋ rūm kadi wulan aṅilo wimba niŋ candrakānta*45:6:408*

<wisaṙjjita>:46 
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 20

^nāhan ujaṙnya paḍâsĕluṙ awara waraḥ kinatuṅgalakĕn,söŋ i manaḥnya katon sĕmu sĕmu niŋ akuŋ ri narendrasuta,ṅhiŋ kakĕna priḥ ikā sira wiṣaya ni goṣṫi nika n paṅucap,rūpa nira sŧiti ri twas ika sinamudāya lawan turida*46:1:409*

śrîndumatī suꝁa māṙ hati nira rumĕṅö ry-ucapanya rĕsĕp,yan tan awĕdya sirêŋ wwaŋ atuha hana budđi nirâmĕpĕra,rāga nirê saŋ ajâwĕtu taṅis inamĕṙ wĕdi kawruhana,liŋ nira moǥa lumuḥ yan aharip araras parihāra nira*46:2:410*

mojaṙ ikaŋ rinahasyan ira wacana liŋnya rĕṅön ta tuhan,saŋ ratu tan hana tan lituhayu kadi dewata rakwa sira,ndan paḍa soṙ sira de saŋ aja saꝑala putra narendra raǥu,hīṅan ira n sira yogya kaharĕpana digjaya rūpa nira*46:3:411*

śrîndumatī kĕna rāga tuhun api hade kadi tan malara,de nira mojaṙ apet silib amarani lokika budđi nira,haywa wawaŋ pinisiṅgiḥ ujaṙ ika tuhun hiḍĕpĕn sakarĕŋ,Āpan ikaŋ dadi janma sakaharĕp ikā kaka moǥa dudū*46:4:412*

nista nikân apadudwan ibu kaharĕp iŋ dadi janma kabeḥ,yan kinatuṅgalakĕn ndya tika hala nikā tuhanĕn pituhun,māsku mataŋnya kakūṅana saŋ aja tuwin wwaŋ anakta sira,haywa kĕdö liŋ ira ndan asĕmu sĕmu haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ gumuyu*46:5:413*

ndaḥ paḍa bindaṙ ikaŋ marĕk i sira kapeṅin ajalwa muwaḥ,moǥa girahyasĕn ambĕk ika katanĕhan turidâṅlarani,Asyaŋ i rowaŋ ikâṅucap ucapa kinonya marĕk marĕka,liŋnya nihan sanu saŋ ratu pili pilihan dumĕn i ṅwaŋ ari*46:6:414*

wwaŋ wwaŋ ahadwan agatgat anagu nagu mĕṅgĕp atĕṅw-ahĕniŋ,ƀāwa nika n kĕna rāga hanan asidĕhâlupa tan paṅinaŋ,wyaṙŧa sĕrĕḥnya hanê taṅan inagĕm agĕm tuhu tuhw-alaṅö,ƀrānta rumūpaka saŋ suṅana sĕrĕḥ asūṅa sĕpaḥ ri waja*46:7:415*

len taŋ agoṣṫi ri gīta saŋ aja ginawenya hañaṙ katĕka,dudw-aṅalĕm ri palambaŋ ira mamaranî manis iŋ paṅikĕt,śrîndumatī kawĕlad hati nira rumĕṅö ri rasanya lĕṅĕŋ,lwiṙ jaruman saŋ ajâmisiki hiḍĕp irâsriŋ akon mijila*46:8:416*

saŋ wwaŋ inuttama sāmpun adaluwaŋ adoḥ sira riŋ wiṣaya,milw-atuhâmbĕk irârarĕm arĕja suśīla lanâsiḍakĕp,tan rĕṅu tan lumiriŋ duga duga pakatonan i tiṅhal ira,yan paṅucap sira tan paṅucap ucapa len saka riŋ kawikun*46:9:417*

strī sĕḍĕŋ iŋ wiṣayânwam ahaṅan apasabraṅan ambĕk ika,mwaŋ sira saŋ wiku wrĕdđa marĕk aṅipi nāga milĕt ri sira,yan wulat aṅdu matanya dinuluṙ i halisnya tikĕl minahā,maṙmma manisnya paḍâṅucapakĕn i kahaṙṣa nikā karĕṅö*46:10:418*

<nawahaṙṣa>:47 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^wiku rājya kawi wruḥ aṅaji kaharĕpku siwiṅkwa sanu,kakawinya palaṙ piguṇana ri parĕknya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,Ulaḥ iŋ paḍa kāsy-asiḥ aṅapi laṅö hiḍĕpĕṅkwa suꝁa,kĕmulaṅkwa jajanya taṅan ika saput saputaṅkwa susu*47:1:419*

Agaḍuḥ kawi kāpti mami sanu wĕnaŋ pasaƀā pawukir,wijil iŋ pihutaŋ pawadal inani rowaŋ ikânuꝁani,kalawan kalaṅönya wĕnaŋ anigakĕn manaḥ iŋ prihatin,yadin aṅlĕṅĕṅâdulura maṅusirê trĕbis iŋ paraṅan*47:2:420*

Atitiḥ kaharĕp mami sanu wĕka niŋ pihutaŋ hutaṅan,wruha têŋ kakawin kiduŋ ulaḥ ulaḥ iŋ wahu wāhu kawi,saparanya pamaṅkwakĕna lĕpihan amriḥ ameta laṅö,sumĕpĕṙ sĕpĕrêŋ papihutaṅan i saṇḍiŋ ikaŋ pasisi*47:3:421*

kaharĕpkw-alawas ṅhiŋ abasana wicakṣaṇa riŋ kalaṅön,niyatârarasĕn marĕk anigi nigî pamabaṙnya tapiḥ,paṅapusnya hatiṅku laris i paṅawaknya katon adadar,prawalanya marêŋ papasaṅan ika ta n kaharĕpku sanu*47:4:422*

puhawaŋ wahu wahw-amrĕti mrĕti katönku siwiṅku sanu,turidaṅku kaḍaṇḍa n alawas aharĕp wwatĕn iŋ banawa,Aputĕk hati niŋ kasarapuŋ alaṅö mulat iŋ pasisi,kaputĕṙ hati ni ṅhulun alal aharĕp tumutêŋ alayar*47:5:423*

Anak iŋ prajurit mĕtu pajurit ikaŋ kaharĕpku sanu,lĕwu rāmya niki n katĕkana lurugan ri huwuskw-atĕmu,hawinĕṅkwa curiknya saha raṅin ikā payuṅaṅkwa tumūt,tan arĕs yak umilwa sĕḍĕṅa nika keṇḍita riŋ palagan*47:6:424*

<girisa>:48 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^ya ta tĕmahana tiṅluṙ denya n śꜽwa sira siwin,Ikaŋ apalaran anwam wruḥ têŋ śāstra wiku haji,lilu tumakula lampūn dan yan paṇḍita nagara,Atuha tuha bagañjiŋ byaktâṅhöbi yan inusir*48:1:425*

kunaŋ amuhara kiŋkiŋ yan bot swan sipi mararas,wiku miraḥ aguṇâśrī maṅgĕḥ wikwa narapati,sira ta siwin aharyan santoṣâmalara dĕmak,palumutana yan anwam yan wrĕdđâpuput anadi*48:2:426*

taha sanu yan i rantĕntâṅhiŋ tyāga juga siwin,sipi raras iŋ ataṇḍaŋ deśâdoḥ mahas alaṅö,lĕwu suꝁa niŋ akarwan soŋsoŋ yan jamaŋ anipis,pakararas ika paṅkun gantin mwaŋ palu daluwaŋ*48:3:427*

tuhu marika wuwusta ndan son moǥa salaḥ ile,tĕka turida kĕna priḥ de saŋ brāhmaṇa siniwi,mulat iŋ awĕka mambaŋ prajñā prāya jitasaƀā,ṅhiŋ amuhara wiraṅroŋ heman đūṙtta cala nika*48:4:428*

kunaŋ amuwuhi rāgī riŋ twas ni ṅhulun alawas,wĕka wĕka capaŋ apriḥ riŋ praŋ wāni panagara,Aṅawayuha saliŋ liŋnya n sāmpun ṅwaŋ apatutan,Ikaŋ ujaṙ ibu rakryan kady-asyaŋ maṅiṅin iṅin*48:5:429*

nahan ucapan ikaŋ strī tĕmbenyânĕmu turida,tan awuni ri manaḥnya n ƀrāntâkuŋ managu nagu,hana ta titiṙ anambut wehan milw-aṅucap ucap,mawara waraḥ i rumrūm niŋ sāminya tan awiraŋ*48:6:430*

<jagadnāŧa>:49 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^rare mĕrĕ mĕrĕḥ pajātyan agĕlo winara warahan iŋ pasaṅgaman,mapaŋ kumĕtĕṙ aṅgamĕl susu taṅanya saha kĕtĕ kĕtĕg sumamburat,Uliḥ niŋ amuruk muruk tinaṅanan ri pataṅanan i sanđi niŋ prĕman,huwus pwa ya tamâharĕp wayuha tan rĕṇa kadi manaḥ iŋ tamêŋ aji*49:1:431*

dudū sanu lawan huwus pracacaḥ asriŋ arabi siniwi priyambada,huwus tama karāsikanya kadi waḥ mađu rasa nika riŋ giṇâmanis,Amakpak aṅucap tuhan tinikĕlan halis i sĕḍĕŋ ikâṅgamĕl tapiḥ,baṅun pĕjaha riŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan ṅwaŋ i paṅamĕṙ ikâṅalap hati*49:2:432*

Ikaŋ kawi ñamut laṅönya rinasan saha kakawin araśmi riŋ tilam,Ikaŋ jariji moǥa kelu ginamĕlnya kinuku hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp tanaḥ,lanânipati pet manis kawawa kelu kadi lĕkas ikânulis karas,kiduŋnya panurū nurūnya sahajâṅgamĕli susu nĕhĕṙ kinaṅsyakĕn*49:3:433*

prawīra siniwi priyambada tuhun kawatĕk ulaḥ ika n wanîŋ raṇa,Añumbu kadi de nika n paṅalawaŋ raṅin i sĕḍĕŋ ika n paṅolakĕn,Anaṅtaŋ amapag wulat nĕhĕṙ aminta linawanan anūt mamaṅkwakĕn,marêŋ susu taṅanya moǥa hiniḍĕp nika ḍuka ḍuka niŋ curik siṅī*49:4:434*

lawan lawanan i ṅhulun wiku miraḥ lituhayu pinakesi niŋ kuṭi,manisnya kadi poḥ apādapa tiki n mamaragi gula gaṇṭi dug siṅī,liriŋnya pinarantyan i ṅhulun iŋ ambyan iŋ umaḥ i sĕḍĕŋ nikânasi,dudū swara nikê karinya karĕṅö panamaya nika yan parê ṅhulun*49:5:435*

<jagadđita>:50 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^nāhan de nika goṣṫi senak i manaḥnya panalimuṙ ikâharip mata,tan tuṅgal rumĕṅö ry-ujaṙnya hana hewa hana sĕmu pacĕḥ mĕṅĕn mĕṅĕn,strī kryan kryan paḍa mūla mūla rabi niŋ kawi muwaḥ aṅucap samaṅkana,tan doṣâsiŋ ujaṙnya moǥa minanis manisan ika tinuṅtuṅan laṅö*50:1:436*

rakryan kenaka niŋ manuṣya sararā wĕrĕ wĕrĕha yayan papaṅgiha,Ambĕk nāgarika wruhâṅikĕta ƀāṣa sakurasa sawīja riŋ laṅö,yan pāywan kakawin maṅaṙwwana wilaḥ kakawin ika palambaŋ iŋ yaśa,yekā kāma ratī ṅaranya n araras paḍa kawi sawawânak iŋ maṅö*50:2:437*

luṅhâṅdoha marêŋ pasiṙ kahalĕpanya n amarĕṅana māsa kāṙttika,sakwan selwan ahimya himyana manumpaka ri walakaŋ iŋ karaŋ liman,ramyâtuntunanêŋ hĕnī ri surud iŋ rwab i tĕpi tĕpi saŋsayâḍake,līlâmeta huraŋ tanaḥ nĕhĕṙ asumpiŋ asaṅu saṅu saṅwa niŋ maṅö*50:3:438*

ndak ton haṙṣa nika n parambakana riŋ bañu tuna tuna mombak ombakan,kāliḥ kāliḥ ikâduluṙ paḍa girahyasĕn anĕmu laṅö lĕyĕp dahat,strīnyâmiṅkasakĕn tapiḥ jĕnĕk amet uwuṙ uwuṙ agĕlaṙ marêŋ tĕpi,byaktâlūma kaköma riŋ bañu hasin wĕtis ika panahā nikaŋ mulat*50:4:439*

rūpanya n mahasêŋ pasiṙ kadi katona mahasa ri samudra niŋ tulis,Āpan de ni lĕyĕp lĕyĕp ni patĕmunya kadi tasik awoṙ lawan laṅit,yadyastun yan aṅumbaṅêŋ jalađi kawruhan i pamilĕt iŋ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,sākṣāt dewata dewatī mahas ahas lĕṅĕŋ aṭika ṭikan sakêŋ tawaŋ*50:5:440*

budđinya n wahu wahw-acaṅkrama marêŋ pasisi wahu mahas lawan priya,maṅgā n tan muliha n panon paduluṙ iŋ layaṙ asĕmu matuntunan taṅan,soliḥnya n pakaraŋ karaŋ winawanan taṅan ulaḥ ulaḥ iŋ hañaṙ hañar,Apwī niŋ hiliran ya sāđana nikâkĕla kĕlana ri piṅgiṙ iŋ tasik*50:6:441*

piṅgiṙ niŋ paraṅan gihā watu sumoŋ pinakapasaji riŋ marâṅlĕṅĕŋ,priṅgârĕs tinataṙ hĕnū nika sumĕṅka tumurun atupis rĕṅat rĕṅat,paṙṇnaḥ loṙ maṅuṅaŋ tasik muꝁa nikā dunuṅan i kĕñaṙ iŋ niśākara,ṅkāna n paṅhinĕpâmaḍaŋ wulana yadyan aharipa suꝁa n paḍâmrĕma*50:7:442*

tĕkwan pwêki n anak wĕsi nrĕpati kawwaṅan ika wĕka niŋ sinanmata,yadyastun kilalan tĕkap saŋ ahulun pawĕkasakĕna riŋ marêŋ pasir,byakta n mantuka moliḥ oliḥ alaṅö haturakĕna ri jöŋ nareśwara,cihnanya n kawi karwa kāsiḥ ika wāhu wihikan asaƀā saƀâmasir*50:8:443*

nāhan wastu ni denya mojaṙ api doḥ ndan aƀimata nikê suputrikā,śrī dewîndumatī huwus wruḥ iŋ apa n kasiliba riŋ ujaṙ samaṅkana,kālap budđi nirêniriŋ winawa riŋ lĕṅĕŋ amasiṙ ahimya himyana,ndan mogâpi hade sahuṙ nira paṅawruhana panalimuṙ manaḥ rimaŋ*50:9:444*

siṅgiḥ ṅgānya wuwusta rāmya ŋ akurĕn sarara wĕrĕ wĕrĕḥ paḍâraras,luṅhâsaṅwa karas tanaḥnya mahasêŋ pasiṙ aduluṙ ahimya himyana,tan waŋ mātra kasiṅya mātra manaḥ i ṅhulun irikaŋ ulaḥ samaṅkana,ndak ton kewran ikaŋ giṇâniwi taṅeḥ mamaḍana raras iŋ wujaŋ wujaŋ*50:10:445*

tĕkwan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅhulun ataṇḍaṅa pasisi huwus tama ṅhulun,pora wwaŋ nika tan wruḥ iŋ puruṣaƀeda hiliran amukĕt hanâmayaŋ,moǥêraŋ ṅwaŋ isin maṅambila karaŋ karaṅan i pasurak niŋ ampuhan,Aṅhiŋ ṙyyaknya maṅaṅkul aṅkul ajajaṙ baṅun asĕgĕḥ anĕmbaḥ iŋ maṅö*50:11:446*

Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ wukiṙ tĕka rĕsĕp mwaŋ aṅalĕwihakĕn sakêŋ pasir,de niŋ kweḥ nira paṇḍitâtapa ri paṙśśwa nika kumuliliŋ tĕkê ruhur,yadyastun ṅwaŋ atiṅgalêŋ nagara wikwa rara maṅusirê munīśwara,rāmya ŋ pakṣa wukiṙ yayan ku n aṅuṅaŋ ry-aƀimata saŋ apakṣa sāgara*50:12:447*

wöṅîŋ māsa kapat ṅhulun milu ri jöŋ nrĕpati mahas ahas mariŋ wukir,saŋ hyaŋ lek i surup hyaŋ aṙkka mijil aṅḍaḍari kadi maṅumbaŋ iŋ pasir,tūban mwaŋ gĕrĕḥ iŋ patĕṙ tan asarag đwani nika lalitânurū nurū,Eñjiŋ meḥ tumibā ŋ ḍawuḥ pitu samaṅkana mawuṅu tinaṅhi niŋ cucur*50:13:448*

Aƀrā kaywan ikaŋ wukiṙ wijaḥ arūm kadi pinisalinan sĕkaṙ miṅiŋ,len taŋ saṙwwalatâwilĕt samaṙ arok baṅun ahurupa luṅgu luṅguhan,sakweḥ niŋ kayu mās lawan kayu puriŋ paḍa paḍa masuṅut wĕlas harĕp,ṅkānê piṅgiṙ ikaŋ juraŋ pĕtuŋ ikā paḍa kadi pinituŋtuṅan limut*50:14:449*

sore ry-ampĕḥ ikaŋ jawuḥ kari gĕrĕḥnya muni pinakarāmya niŋ wukir,lāwan meǥa marantayan tura turaḥnya siniriṙ iŋ aṅin pĕgat pĕgat,miṅsoṙ miṇḍuhuṙ aṅlayaŋ kadi dinĕmwan añawĕli kukus carik carik,himpĕṙ siñjaŋ iŋ apsarī kasarakat ri laris ika sakê pamañcanan*50:15:450*

saŋkṣepanya katon kasoṙ i lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasisi tĕkap i rāmya niŋ wukir,tĕkwan wiǥna niŋ aṅlĕṅĕŋ mahasa riŋ pasisi tarahan aṅhaḍaŋ haḍaŋ,śudđa ŋ paṙwwata nityaśâsĕmu kadewatan i hana saŋ ugrapaṇḍita,ndak gañjaṙ kita yan kitântuka tasik mamaḍana kapawitran iŋ wukir*50:16:451*

<śiꝁariṇī>:51 
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 17

^taham rakryan di ŋ paṙwwata lĕwiha saṅkêŋ jalaniđi,Anūsâpaṇḍan raṅkaŋ apasiṙ asaṅhub saha kilat,muwaḥ tan pāntyāntyâmpuhan ika baṅun kāṙttika sadā,manuknyâliwran yan wahu mari jawuḥ lwiṙ laru laru*51:1:452*

kumĕmbaŋ tuñjuŋ kāṅinan uwuṙ uwuṙnyâṅjraḥ aputiḥ,layaṙ niŋ baṇyāgânutakĕn aṅin aṅdoḥ kadi limut,lĕṅĕŋ ṙyyaknya n sanđyâmiraḥ asĕmu meǥânisik iwak,laṅit suṅsaŋ lwiṙnya n maśaśađaramāyā makalaṅan*51:2:453*

ƀaṭārī śrī pöḥ niŋ jalađi pinutĕṙ lāwan amrĕta,muwaḥ catrâśwâtyanta riŋ aṅuparĕṅgê halĕp ira,tuwin hyaŋ wiṣṇu swāmi nira jĕnĕk i jro jalaniđi,mataŋnyan mūlya ŋ sāgara karaṇa niŋ paṙwwata sinor*51:3:454*

tuhan putrī tan kemĕṅan iŋ ucapan yogya sahura,huwus wruḥ rakwê tiṅkaḥ iŋ acala len kṣīrajalađi,Apan yan mūḋā budđi nira pisaniṅw-ânĕmu sahur,kunaŋ pwâpan prajñā sira sumahuṙ apyak saha guyu*51:4:455*

ndatan moli n hyaŋ śrī winijilakĕn iŋ kṣīrajalađi,parĕŋ lāwan catrāśwa kapat ira tekîkaŋ amrĕta,Apaṅgiḥ mwaŋ hyaŋ wiṣṇu hana riŋ anantāsana sadā,ya hetunya n soṙ liŋta ŋ acala tĕkap niŋ jalaniđi*51:5:456*

kaka ndi n sora ŋ paṙwwata tĕkap i rūm niŋ jalaniđi,Apan lwiṙ wruḥ riŋ swaṙgga ŋ aṅahasi puñcak niŋ acala,paran saṅkan saŋ hyaŋ rawi gati niŋ astodayagiri,Umādewī sākṣāt mara sira sinaṅguḥ girisutā*51:6:457*

sirâtekā duṙggā ṅaran ira kasaṅꝁyêŋ triƀuwana,wĕkas niŋ strī sidđi syapa ta sira dewī kadi sira,huwus limpad riŋ kāṣṭaguṇan atiduṙgga n tiru tirun,kunaŋ tâpan riŋ bimba ya sira n awās kottaman ira*51:7:458*

ƀaṭāra hyaŋ rudra pwa siniwi nirâtūt siliḥ asiḥ,Apaṅgiḥ ṅkānêŋ meru sira paḍa sidđapraƀu wiƀu,mataŋnyan nora hyaŋ kadi sira mahāsidđi dahatĕn,Anādi n riŋ liṅgodƀawacarita pamyaktana kaka*51:8:459*

sirâtekā tūtĕnkwa lumĕwihakĕn riŋ mahiđara,sakê sakweḥ niŋ sāgara mapa ta sī madwa karika,sahuṙ haywâsowe kaka rasa rasâpan kita bisa,tuhankw-ibw-amwītâlaha tuhu wuwustâhayu dahat*51:9:460*

<jagadđita>:52 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^nāhan de nira goṣṫi rāmya tadanantara rahina huwus ḍawuḥ pitu,sakweḥ niŋ paricārikâṅiriṅa sāmpun anarima dadaṙ paḍâsalin,lāwan saŋ wwaŋ inuttamâhayu sujanma paḍa sira marĕk sumaṅgraha,śrī dewîndumatī sirâṅadĕg awaṙṇna ratu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ ṭikâṅaraŋ*52:1:461*

strī stry-ânekawiśeṣa pakṣa ḍatĕṅêŋ paṅuṅaṅan aduluṙ hanêŋ lĕbuḥ,Ahyaŋ waṙṇna nika n hinĕmban araras pinayuṅan iniriŋ ƀinūṣaṇan,sakweḥ niŋ kapapag lumiṅsiṙ awĕdîŋ wwaŋ ahalĕp akĕmul ya riŋ wĕṅi,pañ̈ñjut sañjata len garantuŋ i harĕp prakaṭa baṅun akon sumiṅgaha*52:2:462*

Eñjiŋ rāmya tiniṅhalan sahana niŋ paṅuṅaṅan atatâkatap katap,de niŋ pañjut awaṙṇna wintaŋ anulaṙ wĕdi karahinanânusup nusup,mrik ganđanya huwus kinasturi miṅiŋ rinacana tinulis linaṅwakĕn,wwaŋnyâpiṇḍa surāpsarī saha wimāna wahu tĕka sakêŋ surālaya*52:3:463*

wastrâƀrā pinakapralamba hana riŋ walikuwaŋ anamaṙ kuwuŋ kuwuŋ,kram niŋ cawli kukus baṅun truḥ anisiḥ pinakapaṅuparĕṅga niŋ hatĕp,himpĕṙ nīrada citrameǥa nika riŋ haḍa pinakatawiŋ tawiŋ marar,luṅsiṙ baŋ pinakoluṙ oluṙ i pucak pucak ika kadi luṅgaḥ iŋ kilat*52:4:464*

saśrī waṙṇna nikaŋ payuŋ payuṅan akrĕp asĕmu sĕmu paṅjraḥ iŋ jamur,Akweḥ waṙṇna nikā hanan dadu hanan prĕcik asira siran paḍâṅadĕg,de niŋ kweḥ nira saŋ wĕnaŋ paḍa katon kawĕnaŋ ira mijil samaṅkana,len taŋ biṙyyan amet sĕkaṙ niŋ asanâniru niru halĕp iŋ payuŋ kuniŋ*52:5:465*

saŋ hyaŋ sūṙyya mijil kamantyan abuṅaḥ pawulatan i saƀā nikaŋ kuwu,wwaŋnya lwiṙ jaladâkĕmul kilat asoŋ hima sahana hananya riŋ lĕbuḥ,de niŋ kweḥnya lawan praƀā ni sasinaṇḍaŋ ika lumarap aṅhulap hulap,śaṅꝁa mwaŋ tarayan mrĕdaṅga kumisik mamaji taliṅa niŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö*52:6:466*

wwaŋ wwaŋ ŧāni paḍâduluṙ wahu tĕkâṅibĕki nagara len hanêŋ hĕnū,tĕkwan riŋ sakurĕn hanânak ika pat lima marĕk amilĕt milĕt laku,strīnyâṅĕmban anuntun āmĕtĕŋ apan maṅĕliḥ ika manamby-anuswani,Aprakprākan apan hilaŋ sasiki lūd kakutil awurahan siliḥ daliḥ*52:7:467*

len têkaŋ kaki kaky-amet putu nikā hilaŋ i sĕḍĕŋ ikā siliḥ sĕḍĕk,liŋ niŋ strīnya mahâkas ī kita harĕp mulata kita nininya riŋ waneḥ,Āpan de ni Uninta lāgi ta kitâmupuḥ i sĕḍĕŋ ikâṅucap kaki,Iḥ dūrânaṅisâku yan kita midoṣana pĕjahana sĕṅgahĕn bahud*52:8:468*

strī strī wrĕdđa huwus tĕkêŋ kabuyutan milu milu mulat iŋ swayĕmbara,Aṅhĕmban raray anwam akrak anaṅis winaliŋ ika putunya rakwa ya,mojaṙ swāmi nikā nini syapiku hāpa ya kaki taha tan putunta ya,hā hāḥ tiṅgalakĕn hade nini tĕwas kita kabrĕkĕkĕ duḥka kabwatan*52:9:469*

nāhan liŋ nika hāsyakāraṇa sapolaḥ ika tucapa saŋ para praƀu,ginyākĕn ḍatĕṅêrikaŋ pagĕlaran paḍa mijila kabeḥ sirêŋ lĕbuḥ,wīṙyyā wīṙyyan amĕtwakĕn hati nirêrikaŋ aṅinakanê wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,muntab lwiṙ ni halĕp nirâṅarab arab sama sama kadi bahni kāṅinan*52:10:470*

maṅkat śrī magađeśwarâtri gumuruḥ paḍahi nira karĕṅw-agĕnturan,sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ kapūhan i halĕp nira paḍa mapipit pipit muꝁa,kady-âṅaṙwwani sumpiŋ endaḥ araras pinatihakĕn ika n paḍâṅuṅaŋ,tuṅgal waṙṇna nikâbuṅaḥ kadi wulan sasiki pinarawĕñca niŋ smara*52:11:471*

Aśrī waṙṇna saŋ aṅganāŧa sawatĕk watĕk ira mapupul paḍâhalĕp,himpĕṙ sāgara lakwa lakwan ira rāmya tan asĕpi kapiŋ rwa niŋ laku,tĕkwan rūpa nirâsĕḍĕp tan ahañaŋ huwus amuyahi ri twas iŋ rimaŋ,tan tuṅgal stry-aṅaraŋ tumon sira manaḥnya kalara lara karwaban laṅö*52:12:472*

lwiṙ guntuṙ saŋ awantināŧa tĕka gumrĕbĕg ahalĕp anuṅgaŋ iŋ raŧa,himpĕṙ truḥ sumaput lĕbū nira mĕlĕk pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍa mrĕm apĕpĕt mĕpĕti muꝁa ri tuŋtuŋ iŋ sabuk,Agraḥ rūpa nikaŋ kaḍatwan i kĕtug ni paḍahi nira mapratiđwani*52:13:473*

<sragđara>:53

^liṇḍū lwiṙ saŋ hanūpāđipati manaḥ ikaŋ strī mulat ƀrāntacitta,miṅgut miṅgut halisnyârĕṅu rĕṅu kadi tan wwaŋnya kewalya mūṙcꞓā,katrag santĕnya kegū hati nika kagiwaŋ sāri sāri prapañca,kady-ânumbak jajanya n pasidĕha tĕka riñcuŋ tĕṅaḥnyâṅgaluṅgaŋ*53:1:474*

wānîŋ praŋ saŋ susenā laku nira lumurug kesyan ambĕk nirâkras,wadwā wadwān dĕlit niŋ tahu rinĕbut i rūm niŋ mulat riŋ paniñjon,siṅhākārêŋ saƀā yogya wulatana kasaṅꝁya n đanurwedaśāstra,sakweḥ niŋ stry-âmapag tiṅhal ira paḍa kĕnêŋ rāga tībra byamoha*53:2:475*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgadâkweḥ asĕmu gunuŋ ĕmās katraṅan kāla sanđyā,de niŋ siṅhĕl kaluŋ mwaŋ karaḥ atip apipit paṅharĕp niŋ lumampaḥ,tan pendaḥ puṣpa sālas dadaṙ i bala nirârūm apan saṙwwawastra,gĕṇḍiŋ tan kaṙkkaśâlwan ƀramara kahiḍĕpanyâṅisĕp saṙwwasāri*53:3:476*

saŋ pāṇḍyâpiṇḍa dewâlaku laku tuwi saŋ paṅruhun paṇḍitâkweḥ,tātan pendaḥ sakêŋ budđapada sahana saŋ bodđapakṣâmpak ampak,śꜽwaṙṣy-âwaṙṇna saṅkêŋ śiwapada paḍa sāmpun pĕnuḥ riŋ paṅawruḥ,sakweḥ saŋ brāhmaṇâpūṙwwa pawulatan ira lwiṙ sakêŋ brahmaloka*53:4:477*

<jagadđita>:54

^maṅkat śrī naranāŧaputra kadi kāṙttika wahu tĕka de nira n laku,luḥ niŋ strī kĕna rāga riŋ paṅuṅaṅan kadi riris inusap sakê muꝁa,tiṅhalnyâdu baṅun kilat lumarap aṅluru luru ri huwus nikaŋ jawuḥ,sambat sambat ikā ginūḋa kadi mĕtwa marĕṅana kalaṅwan iŋ patĕr*54:1:478*

liŋnyê twasnya ƀaṭāra manmaŧa manĕḥta kawĕlas arĕp aṅhiḍĕp lara,kiŋkiŋ rāga tĕkânaput prihati māṙ pinuhara nika tan wĕnaŋ kinas,maṅke kāla nikaŋ swayambara tĕkâmarupuhi sahasâṅrĕmĕk hati,Aṅgyat lwiṙ hudan adrĕs iŋ katiga tan pakakaraṇa karĕṅwan iŋ gĕrĕḥ*54:2:479*

t asy-âsiḥ siha saŋ hyaŋ i ṅhulun alaḥ sĕpĕrakĕna nareśwarātmaja,syūhĕn denta manaḥ nirêŋ lulut unĕŋ kĕtĕrakĕna nĕhĕṙ tĕkākĕna,Āpan tan hana len sakê sira pakāśrayan awĕlasa riŋ griŋ i ṅhulun,tambā rāga siroṣađa prihati jampi turida pinakāmrĕtêŋ rimaŋ*54:3:480*

yadyan laṅǥana tan panūta manaḥ i ṅhulun i sĕḍĕŋ ira n pamaṅkwakĕn,ndak ton kĕdwa nirânukūlakĕna tan kawaśa hinudanan wulat maliŋ,Āpan siṅha sirêŋ rahasya niyatârĕp arĕpan i tan olya kaprĕma,byaktâṅrampasa ken dunuŋ susu kayuḥ tĕṅaḥ anĕkani senakê hati*54:4:481*

<Aƀikrĕti>:55

^nahan liŋ ika ri twas epu wihikan ri manaḥ ika yatan sakāra dahatĕn,ya kāraṇa nikâwuyuŋ ri taliṅanya tĕka rĕṅĕ rĕṅön i wrĕtta saŋ aja,halisnya pinisitnya tan duga duga n paṅujiwat i sĕḍĕŋ nira n umaliwat,matanya dinaliḥnya duṙjjana hĕnū nira mara ri hatinya tan pamali luḥ*55:1:482*

<jagadnāŧa>:56 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^taṅeḥ yan ucapĕn laranya tali niŋ carita waluyanôcapĕn muwaḥ,para praƀu huwus tĕkêŋ pagĕlaran mapupul asĕmu hetwa niŋ laya,Apan gumuruḥ apratiđwani surak ni bala nira ya tâmaṅun ƀaya,baṅun hana katona digjaya katona pĕjaha rĕbutĕn salaḥ siki*56:1:483*

Atuṅgalan umaḥ bwat indranagarâjajaṙ asĕmu kaḍatwan iŋ tawaŋ,para praƀu mahāpraƀāwa sawaŋ aṙcca maṇik inululan hanêŋ saƀā,paḍâsira siran pratāpa kadi tan hana lĕwiha sakê halĕp nira,tĕka pwa saŋ ajâkucĕm sira baṅun śaśađara matĕmaḥ kunaŋ kunaŋ*56:2:484*

syapêka tan awĕdya riŋ kadi sirâguṇa wĕka niŋ amĕdyakĕn ratu,Awaṙṇna mađumāsa kāṙttika piniṇḍa piniturun adadya mānuṣa,Ikaŋ wwaŋ aharĕp wruhê sira humuŋ sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,katon pwa sira denya rĕp wĕdi kumĕl humĕnĕŋ asĕmu sinyukan bañu*56:3:485*

rare saŋ aja śakti pustaka lĕṅĕn raǥuwĕka wani kawy-anuṅgali,Ikaŋ guṇa hanê sirâgaṇita riŋ kapana kawaśa taṙkka niŋ mulat,prasidđa sira sūtra niŋ karawiwaṅśan amagĕhakĕn āgamêŋ prajā,rusit niŋ aji ta pwa rūpa nira tan hana ratu wĕnaŋ aṅdĕlö dĕlö*56:4:486*

<jagadđita>:57

^sāmpun prāpta sirêŋ saƀā pinakamaṅgala ni halĕp ikaŋ swayambara,śrī dewîndumatī sirênarahakĕn mijila wahu huwus ƀinūṣaṇan,muṅgw-iŋ ḍampa sirâpĕgâṅĕnĕb ĕnĕb kĕtĕ kĕtĕg ira māṙ sumamburat,saśry-âwaṙṇna tulis ḍinampan awĕnĕs wĕnĕs asĕmu rakĕt kapañjutan*57:1:487*

Endaḥ ḍampa nirâpĕnĕd kinajaṅan kusumaśara tinap linaṅwakĕn,ronyêndrāyuđa puṣpacāpa pikulanya mamuꝁa muꝁa nāga campaka,mās tuṅgal nika puṣpaliṅga niŋ aṅaṙccana ri pada ƀaṭāra manmaŧa,nāgākāra surat suratnya tinĕtĕs ni luḥ iŋ akuŋ amaṅkwakĕn ṭikā*57:2:488*

Ācārī kalawan karaṇḍan ira saŋ pinituhu ri tatā samâṅiriŋ,sāmpun muṅgw-i harĕp sirâhalĕp acum nĕhĕṙ aṅarahakĕn lumampaha,kĕṇḍaŋ goŋ muni t aṅkat aṅkat atĕrĕḥ đwani nika karĕṅö sakê yawa,sakweḥ niŋ maṅuṅaŋ paḍâṅĕnĕb ĕnĕb raras i hati nika n tumiṅhala*57:3:489*

maṅkat śrīndumatī garantuŋ ira muny-asĕmu gula ǥināṣa riŋ waja,rūm niŋ paṅlima muṅgu riŋ śrigaḍiŋ iŋ masa kalima tinū hanêŋ kapö,Aṅlaṅwākĕn awaṙṇna kāṙttika pamatnya gumuruḥ araras rinĕṅwakĕn,lwiṙ tūban kumusuḥ karĕṅwan i panĕmpuḥ ika kadi panĕmpuḥ iŋ jawuḥ*57:4:490*

<sragđara>:58

^rakryan putrī mijil kāƀinawa halĕp irâpūṙwwa saṅkêŋ kaḍatwan,Aṅlīlâwās katon ƀūṣaṇa nira kumĕñaṙ lwiṙ panoliḥ hyaŋ aṙkka,Aṅheṙ riŋ gopurâṅrĕgrĕg i pasalĕsĕk iŋ paṅharĕp söḥ marampak,sākṣāt saŋ hyaŋ wulan wāhu mĕtu riŋ udayādrîniriŋ niŋ grahâkweḥ*58:1:491*

mogâhyaŋ de nirâmet hayu mamulaṅunî budđi niŋ wwaŋ tumiṅhal,hyaŋ śrī liŋnyê sirâṅiṇḍarat aharĕp ametâśrayêŋ maṙttyaloka,len tekaŋ wwaŋ sumĕṅgaḥ ratiḥ i sira sakêŋ swaṙgga lāwan surastrī,ƀrantânĕṅgaḥ dwicandrâduluṙ i payuŋ irâtyanta śudđa rwa sādĕg*58:2:492*

<jagadđita>:59

^menmen rwaŋ siki wāhu rāgawaśa muṅgw-i harĕp ira marĕk manimbaṅi,hyaŋ niŋ gīta tĕkânurun kahiḍĕpanya ḍatĕŋ iniriŋ iŋ tabaŋ tabaŋ,siṅhĕlnyâṙjja lawan sawitnya katiraḥ wĕlas arĕp awilĕt lawan gaḍuŋ,tan pendaḥ kadi nāgapāśa pamanaḥ niŋ atanu karaṇanya lĕŋlĕŋa*59:1:493*

nyū dantâkuniŋ aṅhapit gula gula lwiṙ ikaŋ amawa pawwahan gaḍiŋ,tapwan wāla dahat rwa sādĕg abĕbĕd niyata kahirisan twas iŋ mulat,tĕṅgĕknyâluŋ apiṇḍa kāṅinana polaḥ ika n asĕmu buṅkaḥ iŋ pupus,Aṅhiŋ dyaḥ jayawaspa paṅhulu manisnya n anilihi mamaṅku pawwahan*59:2:494*

tan hawwan gati saŋ rarâhawu hawu wwaŋ ahayu tinuras raras nika,lūd ƀasmāṅkura laṇḍa rakwa sira saŋ tuha tuha nika yan sakêŋ bibi,solaḥ seṅĕṙ ikâhaṅan gĕsĕŋ i pāmbĕkan ika tĕkap iŋ smarānala,yogyā kuṇḍaṅa niŋ manunwani pamiṅgiṙ amĕnĕma kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ*59:3:495*

mopiḥ wahw-amayaŋ mayaŋ ri hati niŋ mulat anĕku nĕku pralāpita,tapwan rañca hatinya kewala walĕlwan amagĕhakĕn iŋ kakanyakān,kāsĕṅkanya piliḥ pucaŋ pucaṅan iŋ smara rumimaṅa budđi niŋ kawi,yogya n raṅkulĕn iŋ wanîŋ raṇa tĕṅaḥnya pasuṅakĕna sĕmba sĕmbahan*59:4:496*

tapwan wrĕdđa dahat sirêña nira lāwan uwa nira paḍâkurug miraḥ,Ekĕl roma nirâsĕlat huwan ikaŋ hayu tumalawuṅan turuŋ lĕwas,luñcip niŋ kuku pantĕs aṅgrĕmusa lagy-aṅuluŋ uluṅi rāga niŋ mulat,Edran tiṅhal irêŋ saƀā baṅun anambĕra hinayamakĕn titik maṅö*59:5:497*

putrī niŋ kryan anak wĕsi nrĕpati rakwa kaka kaka nirânwam iŋ wayaḥ,pantĕs tan pamikārakĕn hayu rĕṅunya muwuhi raras iŋ matâmanis,lwiṙ hyaŋ hyaŋ tĕka tan hinundaŋ anurun sahana nika paḍâwulaŋ tatur,kram niŋ sampiṙ i bāhu mās inapi molaḥ asĕmu hĕlaranya n aṅlayaŋ*59:6:498*

<jagadnāŧa>:60 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^Ikaŋ mamawa kaṇḍi kaṇḍi rara wahw-agĕluŋ ahayu poṣađan lulut,lumut lumut ikaŋ payođara wĕnaŋ paṅuwata sĕḍĕŋ iŋ jajâhĕnĕk,pupuṙ nika wĕnaŋ paṅoṣađa pilĕg niŋ iruŋ apan arūm sakêŋ kapur,lukaṙ karika kenya muꝁya pinakādi paṅuwata ri rāga niŋ rimaŋ*60:1:499*

wagĕd wagĕd ikāŋ añāmarani waṙgga pasisi salĕmaḥ lawan wukir,sawaṙgga kalawan wulan muꝁa nikā kalĕṅĕṅan ika mitra niŋ cucur,tĕṅaḥnya wahu wanwa riŋ jriŋ aṅĕliḥ wahu waśa riŋ aśokapādapa,sasīma kalawan mayūra gĕluṅanya wĕka niŋ asanâkadaŋ patĕr*60:2:500*

kunaŋ saŋ apahidwan eṅas ahaṅan pawulatan i manaḥnya riŋ saƀā,sĕkaṙ nika pinintakāsihakĕn iŋ kawi huwus aṅikĕt hañaṙ tĕka,kisapwakĕna riŋ prawīra kahalĕp nika suṅana sĕpaḥ sakê waja,kayogyan i laṭinya yan kadi duḥ iŋ wwaḥ ika sĕsĕpĕn iŋ priyâtalĕḥ*60:3:501*

Anak wĕsi narendra rakwa rasikā saŋ amawa curigâraras dahat,Aroma maṅunĕŋ galuḥ kahiḍĕpanya n apaṅawaka patrĕm uttama,Ikaŋ wwaŋ araṅin wineḥ curiga kadga sinĕpuhan apan wagĕd waśi,wajanya mamiraḥ tĕkê gusi gusinya halis ika tĕkâmraŋ iŋ mulat*60:4:502*

Ikaŋ wwaŋ aṅagĕm curik pinakapaṅruhun aduluṙ arĕs twas iŋ mulat,Asiṅhĕl akaluŋ krĕtāṙŧa riŋ ayun pinakapaṅisi niŋ wanîŋ raṇa,surakṣaka kaƀīnna ƀīnna baṅun antaka mapupul ahöm aṅiṇḍarat,winaswas asipattra sālas asĕwö krĕtala curiga tomarâluṅid*60:5:503*

<jagadđita>:61 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^wwaŋ wwaŋ kasturi sāri niŋ kusuma rūpa saŋ aṅiriŋ inuttamâhayu,meww-iww-âtap awaṙṇna kuntul aṅusī pasisi kakilatan hanêŋ tawaŋ,yadyastun tulisĕn samaṅkana pirâwig awiga nika yan hanêŋ yaśa,ṅhiŋ ganya n drawanĕn manisnya niyatanya tumuluy atĕmaḥ tasik mađu*61:1:504*

laslāsan wruḥ iŋ iṅgitâṅinakanêŋ mulat ahayu puji n pakawwaṅan,yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ cala calârĕṅu rĕṅu sahajâpuput guyu,nistanya n kadi pāwak iŋ mađu manisnya raras ika kadi ṅrĕs iŋ hati,tan paṅgintiṙ i rūm nirâsĕmu jamuṙ hapa hapa marĕk iŋ jamuṙ wulan*61:2:505*

denyâṅlaṅkahakĕn sukunya kadi tan lĕpasa tĕkap i lon ikaŋ laku,mĕñcuḥ mĕñcuḥ aṅambĕk ambĕki pupūnya hana bĕnĕṙ adĕgnya pet ulaḥ,kahyun hyun laris iŋ wĕtis tan alaris laku nika minahā hinerakĕn,Aṅjiŋjiŋ sasisiḥ mĕluk tuṙ ika mātra wagĕd aniru lampaḥ iŋ tulis*61:3:506*

strī strī saƀya wicakṣaṇânagara nora kakuraŋ ika pantĕs iŋ saƀā,kady-ânaṇḍuṅakĕn rwi de nika lumampaḥ arĕṅu sahajâṅhĕmū guyu,Eñjuḥ prāya nika n wulat riŋ aṅuṅaŋ tan ahulap atawĕŋ tawĕŋ taṅan,tan pendaḥ salukat jajaṙ gĕluŋ ikā lukaṙ i jaja tinumbakan susu*61:4:507*

kady-aṅrakṣa hayunya rūpa nika de ni galak i pamatanya yan wulat,hrū nîruŋnya lanā katon amatitis pamarayaŋ i halisnya lot mayat,waṙṇnākāra nikaŋ wajâkrĕp asinaŋ gusi gusi nika kesisan laṭi,Ahrit wit ni suśūnya tĕkwan aluṅid paḍa paḍa kadi suṅga niŋ jaja*61:5:508*

<suwaṅśapattra>:62 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 18

^tucapa tikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan wagĕd aṅucap ucap,liŋ ika suputrikā pinakaratna winuni ri dalĕm,saŋ aja sujanma mās kinĕmit iŋ nagara wahu tĕka,saꝑala sira n humambanakĕnê narapatiduhitā*62:1:509*

nrĕpatanayā katon wĕdi nira n mulat i para ratu,yadin alupa ŋ śarīra sira mūṙcꞓita lumaya kawĕs,hulĕsana tan bawaŋ jasunanê sĕḍĕŋ ira kapati,niyata sirâṅliliṙ saŋ aja saṇḍiṅakĕna ri jaja*62:2:510*

narapatiputrikā n gĕluṅa niŋ wwaŋ anaṅis i ṭikā,saŋ aja paṅisya mon sira wirāga sadaka pasaji,Aŧawa yadin padadyana sipat narapatitanayā,nrĕpasuta de nira n gagaṅa mon pusuḥ usapa mata*62:3:511*

sĕkara niŋ aṅhiḍĕp smara kunaŋ narapatitanaya,saꝑala n apallawâmbĕt i tĕṅaḥ narapatiduhitā,nrĕpawaraputrikā n sĕkara de nira kumuda paḍa,saŋ aja niśākarā nira maran patĕmu paḍa lĕṅĕŋ*62:4:512*

para ratu tan padon pisaniṅū sira kaharĕpana,tuhu sira śakti wāni paḍa tan hana kakuraŋ ira,ndan atiśaya praƀāwa saŋ ajâdƀuta kagiri giri,Asana lawan wuṅū paḍa nira ndya ta hurĕn i rika*62:5:513*

nahan ucapanya yan dinuluran rĕṅu saha kujiwat,waja nika tan wĕnaŋ winuni keṅis amuhara raras,wĕkasan anagwa nagwakĕn i rowaŋ ika ri saŋ aja,cinalukakĕn mahâpicala haṙṣa riŋ ujaṙ ajuwĕt*62:6:514*

hana ta muwaḥ sira kryan apupul pupul ahayu raras,walu walu saŋ lumaḥ ry-anu patibrata lumaku wiku,paṅawaśa niŋ nwam iŋ wayaḥ agatgat asalaha jamaŋ,hana sĕmu niŋ manaḥ maru marun mulat i nrĕpasuta*62:7:515*

hana wahu wahw-anūt karakĕtan siliḥ asiḥ akurĕn,nrĕpaduhitā kahewa nika mĕṅgĕp aṅalĕm aṅupĕt,tuhu tuhu yan latā paḍa ni budđi nika kadi nadī,cumulu culuḥ priyanya pamawanya lulut i saŋ aja*62:8:516*

rara ri widaṙbƀarājya makamuꝁya nrĕpatitanayā,paḍa kĕna rāga rāga nika tībra lumuŋ aṅalayan,humañutakĕn lulut lulut unĕŋnya mara ri saŋ aja,bisa sira tan tĕñuḥ rinĕbut iŋ turida sanagara*62:9:517*

<jagadđita>:63 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^Osik budđi nikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,sāmpun prāpta ri mađya niŋ pagĕlaran para ratu kĕna rāga de nira,Akweḥ ƀāwa nira n wimūṙcꞓita hanan maṅuwahi makuṭa ndatan tulus,dudw-âƀāwaka kady-aweḥ sĕpaḥ aƀāwaka kadi tinĕwĕk miṅe midĕm*63:1:518*

len taŋ tībra lulut nirê nrĕpasutā humiḍĕp awak irâṅisapwakĕn,de niŋ rāgawaśâmarājaya tĕkâmulaṅuni ya tinūtnya yan rimaŋ,ṅhiŋ kāmīrasa lot ginoṣṫi nira rāmya lawan ikaŋ amaṅku pawwahan,mogâṅde tutuṙ iŋ gula drawa karĕṅwan i wacana nirânamaṙ juruḥ*63:2:519*

Ambĕk ni ṅhulun iŋ rarâhayu lawan lituhayu sawawân apaṅgiha,ndan maṙmmanya n atĕmwa dūta lĕpihan pirĕsĕpakĕna riŋ pralāpita,Āpan tan hana raśmi niŋ winaraŋ iŋ wwaŋ atuha tuna de nikâlaṅö,ṅhiŋ ganđaṙwwawiwāha rāmya katigâmawa sĕrĕḥ amisāta riŋ pasir*63:3:520*

luṅhâhĕmbana putra putran ika gantin arĕk arĕkanêŋ pararyanan,liṅlīṅĕn kisapun kudaŋ kudaṅĕn iŋ kakawin uliḥ iŋ aṅdadak dadak,yadyan māliha riŋ wukiṙ sipi laṅönya winulatan awikwa wikwana,Aṅhiŋ gīta panĕmba nĕmbaha nika n huwus inuƀaya mantukêŋ bibi*63:4:521*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:64 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^nāhan liŋ nira n aṅlipuṙ lipurakĕn kiŋkiŋ nirê twas nira,kāsiḥ kāsiḥ irâṅlawan lawani goṣṫy âpan huwus wruḥ kawi,wwaŋ śrĕṅgāra wicakṣaṇâṅrahati sojaṙnyân asiḥ saŋ praƀu,pet pet haṙṣa sahuṙnya rāgakaraṇa wruḥ riŋ kasöṅan smara*64:1:522*

yan kanyā ri hiḍĕp patik haji hade kahyūnanâpan raray,tonĕn de nrĕpati ndya taŋ mađukarā hānê kucup niŋ sĕkar,lāwan yan lĕwasa ŋ rarâpa pakĕnanyâpan lĕwas riŋ raras,paṅliṅganya sĕkaṙ lĕwas pisaniṅū kumbaŋ marâṅambuṅa*64:2:523*

saŋkṣepanya sĕḍĕŋ rarā bwatana kiŋkiŋ hundaṅĕn riŋ ṭikā,maṅgĕḥ de niŋ aṅolakĕn tĕṅaḥ ikā sāmpun pinaṅkw-âṅliga,kady-aṅgān i sĕkaṙ nikāŋ asana yan mĕmbaŋ katampwan riris,ṅkāna ŋ ṣaṭpada miwya yan ƀramara saṅjñānya n jĕnĕk tan midĕr*64:3:524*

nāhan denya n apet sahuṙ mĕtu rarasnya n pāwak iŋ rāsika,tambā niŋ rimaŋ aṅlawaŋ lawaṅi kuŋ pet rāga denyâṅucap,lwiṙ truḥ niŋ mađumāsa kāraṇa ni kiŋkiŋ śrī narendrâsĕwö,mambö ken lukaṙ iŋ tilam sahuṙ irâtuŋtuŋ rum iŋ saṅgama*64:4:525*

<jagadđita>:65 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^kanyā liŋta hade kahaṙṣana paḍanya salaga kapana n kakūṅana,kuŋ jaṅgâṅalayan taŧāpi kapana n pamilĕta raras iŋ rara n lĕwas,drĕṣṭāntanya sĕkaṙ lĕwas riŋ apa rakwa wulatana mĕne n kasumpiṅa,kiŋkiŋ tībra yan iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara rarasnya paḍa paḍa lawan jraḥ iŋ sĕkar*65:1:526*

yêkā têka hade paṅawruhana campaka salaga nika n kinahyunan,yadyan sumpiṅa niŋ maṅālihi hulĕs lĕwu raras ika yan pagantyana,mambö rūmnya hanêŋ karaŋ hulu taṅan turaḥ ika rumĕsĕp tĕkê hati,haṙyyan tan hana haṙṣa ni ṅwaŋ i sĕkaṙnya puru puru rĕmĕk katiṇḍihan*65:2:527*

yan laywan pakasumpiṅĕn hana rarasnya tuhun asĕpi solaḥ iŋ lĕwas,tĕkwan rakwa ꝑalanya moǥa pinalaywan asiŋ amupu luṅsuran sĕkar,denya n mantĕna rūmnya yan pakirim iŋ wwaŋ ahayu panuwal nikā ṭikā,Ambönya n huwus aṅharas pipi ya târĕk arĕkana waṅinya kuṇḍaṅĕn*65:3:528*

mwaŋ yan strī hucapĕn rarasnya paḍa ta pwa kaharĕpana tan tayākĕna,rūmrūm niŋ rara kanyakā kadi saroruha kumuḍu mijil sakêŋ bañu,himpĕṙ paṅkaja karyakan wahu mĕkaṙ pamĕwĕḥ i raras iŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara,tan pendaḥ śatapattra wāhu lĕwas iŋ talaga hayu nikaŋ rara n lĕwas*65:4:529*

kanyā ta pwa wiśeṣa riŋ pawaraṅan raras ika marumaḥ lawan riris,Antuk niŋ maṅalap kasoṙ karaṇa niŋ tinarima marĕkâṅaras pipi,riŋ paṅkwan winaraḥ riŋ akṣara manaḥ wahu tama wahu wanwa koluyan,Āŋ aḥ wus kaka liŋnya moǥa kawatĕk ri sĕḍĕŋ ika kinewalânukĕr*65:5:530*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ maṅaṙwwani hĕnū rumasa rasana rāmya niŋ kapat,byaktâlona lakunya sotan ika tan tahu mahas ahas aṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,tapwan wanwa dahat tuhun rĕṅu nikâmarahakĕn i harĕpnya hĕmbanĕn,suṇḍaŋ suṇḍaṅĕn iŋ tĕgal payuṅanâsana hari harin iŋ pararyanan*65:6:531*

tan gyā gyākĕna de nikā lumaku mon karirisana ri mađya niŋ tĕgal,yan paṅdöla paran kunaŋ wĕnaŋ akona pituhun ika yan lumampaha,solaḥnyêriṅanâpa tan wuruṅa luḥnya patulaka nikā yadin kĕdön,ṅhiŋ gānya nya lumampaha n hana gĕrĕḥ maṅarahakĕna kāla niŋ rĕmĕŋ*65:7:532*

ndan yan rāmya nikaŋ sĕḍĕŋ rara kapiŋ rwa niŋ arabi rĕsĕp twas iŋ mulat,kas kas pādapa kāṅinan kas i tĕṅaḥnya kinayuḥ aṅĕliḥ wawaŋ tumūt,mwaŋ twasnyâṅasanâṅrĕṅö patĕṙ adan mĕkara hinudanan karāsikan,kady-amrĕm kalawan puḍak ṅwaŋ aṅisapwakĕn arisi kanin ragĕt ragĕt*65:8:533*

yadyan rowaṅa niŋ lumampaḥ anukū sapara paran iŋ aṅraraḥ musuḥ,śođâta pwa hayunya nora kakuraŋnya mata waja nikā paḍânulus,mambö wīra raras rarasnya tĕkap iŋ hañaŋ aṅiriŋ akālihan tapiḥ,pantĕs pantĕs anuṅgaṅêŋ śakaṭa pamrĕgakĕna kahalĕpnya riŋ hĕnu*65:9:534*

Aśrī raśmi nikaŋ rarā tuha kapiŋ tiga niŋ arabi mon kapiŋ pata,prāyâsiḥ wilaja n kinolakĕn anaṅgap i waja nika yan wineḥ sĕpaḥ,dūrâṅrĕṅwana yan kisapwakĕna riŋ śayana pisaniṅūn apaṅgila,Eṅgal wanwa wisik pisan kadi sadoṣa ginupi tumuluy kataṅgama*65:10:535*

yogya n rowaṅa niŋ licin wanawasânusupa ri pasamūha niŋ sĕkar,kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa niŋ mahas mahas atīṙŧa riŋ acala mahārakā gaḍuŋ,līlânaṇḍaṅa walkalâjaṙ ajarânalawaha jawuḥ iŋ labuḥ kapat,śrī rājādayitā pi yogya ta ṅaranya n aduluṙ anusup lawan ratu*65:11:536*

nāhan de nira nāŧa mojaṙ apadudwan ulaḥ ulaḥ ira n paḍâlulut,budđi śrī naranāŧaputra milu rañca ri wulat ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,mūṙcꞓâpan wahu wahw-anon rakĕt aṅiṇḍarat anĕmu ṭikā tĕkâlulut,paŋ niŋ kūŋ asĕwö wilāpa kakawin tinama tama nirê dalĕm hati*65:12:537*

rakryan ṅke kahananku māsku mapa hetu niŋ asĕmu wiwal salaḥ wulat,Ahyun suŋsuṅĕn i ṅhulun karika māsku karaṇa niŋ arĕṅwa pet ulaḥ,Om om haywa miṅe nihan ṅhulun amaṅkwakĕna ri kita milw-aḍampana,taṅgap māsku sĕpaḥku sāmpun amiraḥ rumĕsĕpakĕna rāga ni ṅhulun*65:13:538*

dyaḥ saŋ sāgara katruhan luḥ apasiṙ panĕpi saŋ ahĕnī hĕnī pupur,muṅgw-î jro hati kuŋta māsku kapana n rwaba sumapatanê kuŋ i ṅhulun,Ambĕk ni ṅhulun amriḥ aṅlayari tan wĕdi kajahata kombakan halis,swaṙggâku n karĕmêŋ tĕṅaḥta suꝁa kaprĕma kapaguta riŋ karaŋ susu*65:14:539*

rakryan saŋ mađu niŋ kaḍatwan uliḥ iŋ hyaŋ amituruni sāri niŋ sĕkar,lwiṙ tawwan pakatonan iŋ kaka kakâṅrubuŋ ahayu paḍâṅisis wĕtis,de niŋ hyunku tumon manista n agĕlaŋ gupura maṇi duwĕg pakolihĕn,ndak lampū pĕtĕŋ iŋ mulat sakahananta ri dalĕm ibu rohĕn i ṅhulun*65:15:540*

<sragđara>:66 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^ndaḥ nāhan liŋ narendrātmaja ri hati nirâpan sira ƀrāntacitta,rakryan putrī marê śrī magađapati pĕnuḥ wwaŋ manonton marê jro,Awrĕg de saŋ sunandā kadi lanaŋ aṅusī sāhasânĕmbuŋ iŋ hwī,ramyâwelā katon riŋ wĕkasan aṅililan śrī suputrī tinonton*66:1:541*

<jagadđita>:67 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^mojaṙ śrī magađāđipê nrĕpasutā nihan ibu marĕkâkisapwana,socaṅkw-îbu lawan matanta sakadaŋ paḍa paḍa dadi niŋ gula drawa,Atyantêbu hayunta tan patatalan tuhu tuhu n awatāra niŋ ratiḥ,heman māsku yatan papaṅgiha lawan ṅhulun apan awatāra niŋ smara*67:1:542*

wruḥ ku n tan hana sanmatanta hana duṣṭa marĕki ri kitâmadohakĕn,tonton denta matanta mĕṅgĕp amanis dumadak arĕṅu yan tumon ṅhulun,paṅron wimba nikuŋ halista n abĕnĕṙ kuṭila milu ri tuŋtuŋ iŋ hiḍĕp,tan saṅkêŋ hana doṣa kimburu manaḥta tĕka wiwal apeda ri ṅhulun*67:2:543*

rakryan janma ni janma ni ṅhulun adadyana ratu tumutêŋ swayambara,ndan rakryan ta muwaḥ swayambarakĕnâmiliha ratu ri mađya niŋ saƀā,denya n tan kinasanmatanta palalun sinalahasa ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,rāmya ṅwaŋ pinagantakĕn tulusa tan tulusa tuwi yayâpuput raras*67:3:544*

nāhan de magađeśwarâṅucap arūm amalaṙ i sahura nrĕpātmajā,śrī dewîndumatī tan eṅĕḥ apa tan hana manaḥ ira keṅĕrê sira,maṙmma śrī naranāŧa mantĕn aṅucap tĕhĕṙ amaḍĕm ikaŋ smarê hati,wruḥ ri wyaṙŧa ni kuŋ nirê nrĕpasutā n kadi wiꝑala niŋ ahyun iŋ tulis*67:4:545*

<sragđara>:68 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^ndaḥ mojaṙ saŋ sunandā ri narapatisutā liŋnya tiṅhal tuhanku,nāhan ta śrī mahārāja magađapati saŋ yogya petĕn siwinta,yadyastun sidđa rakryan sasisihana hulĕs dlāha lāwan narendra,sakweḥ niŋ strī hanê jro nagara niyata tan sāha saṅkê padanta*68:1:546*

<jagadđita>:69 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^sugyan tan wruha māsku yan śrī magađeśwara sira maṅaran parantapa,sāmpun śīṙṇna musuḥ nirâwrĕg i kaḍatwan ika mati ri mađya niŋ raṇa,Aṅhiŋ pat lima śeṣa niŋ karahatan paḍa kawĕkas anūt marê sira,saŋkṣepanya yaŧāṙtta māsku sira yan prakaśita maṅaran parantapa*69:1:547*

yan riŋ wīṙyya lawan guṇa syapa sirâṅlĕwihana sira yan paḍa praƀu,waḥ riŋ mās maṇik uttama ndya ŋ adagaŋ lumĕwihana sira n đaneśwara,sāmpun pūṙṇna kadānaśūran ira kaprakaśita tĕka riŋ purāntara,ṅhiŋ putrī kakuraŋ ni ǥāra nira hetu niŋ aṅadu ri māskw-aṅĕdwakĕn*69:2:548*

wwantĕn deśa lĕṅĕŋ ri puṣpapura ƀūmi nrĕpati pasamūhan iŋ kawi,luḥ niŋ strī kĕna rāga rakwa talaganya pinarigi ri laywan iŋ gĕluŋ,sambatnya n panaṅis ya tâṅdadi mađubrata hana dadi cātakêŋ tawaŋ,mambö rūm ni muꝁanya sāmpun atĕmaḥ kumuda mĕkaṙ i tambwaŋ iŋ wulan*69:3:549*

ṅkā tênduŋ parananta māmĕŋ amĕŋ an huwus atĕmu lawan nareśwara,ƀuktin siḥ nira denta rāmya niŋ atuntunan aduluṙ akālihan payuŋ,yêkā wīṙyya ṅaranya riŋ kadi kitâhayu pinuji yan amriḥ iŋ priya,ramyâṅaṙwwana ḍampa riŋ para paran sipi wanĕḥ iŋ akālihan tilam*69:4:550*

<sragđara>:70 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandâmanis araras arūm de nikâkon atĕmwa,sāmpun kājaṙ pratāpa nrĕpati lawan ikaŋ wīṙyya sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ,ndātan mlecꞓā suputrī n inucapan aṅucap len sakê saŋ narendra,mogâsuṅsut mĕne n ahyuna kinĕdĕ kĕdö kewalâdoḥ riŋ ambĕk*70:1:551*

<jagadđita>:71 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^śrī dewîndumatī katon sĕmu ni budđi nira n alalisê nareśwara,Āpan tan hana raśmi raśmi ni wulat nira pinarĕkakĕn wawaŋ miṅe,yêkā hetu nira n kinon aṅalihâmwita rumuhun anĕmbahê sira,mambĕt mađya nirâṅgaluṅgaŋ i panĕmbaḥ ira kadi panĕmbaḥ iŋ tulis*71:1:552*

ry-aṅkat śrī nrĕpaputrikā śrī magađeśwara kawĕlas arĕp kamānuṣan,mary-âteja sĕpaḥ nirâsĕpa sigit sigitan ira tibâkusêŋ lĕmaḥ,tan śoƀâkilayū wulat nira sĕkaṙ nira maṅaway awe hanêŋ kapö,trĕṣṇā kūŋ ira tan katoliḥ inatīta nĕhĕṙ inilagan yayan tumūt*71:2:553*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:72 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^śrī dewîndumatī lumampaḥ aṅĕliḥ prāptê saŋ aṅgāđipa,ndātan wany-asaƀâhaliŋ haliṅan iŋ ceṭī paḍâkweḥ marĕk,tan saḥ dyaḥ jayawaspa lot linihaṅan bāhunya karwâwiḍaŋ,Āpan kāsiḥ irâlawas tuwin arūm tan soṙ dahat riŋ hayu*72:1:554*

<jagadđita>:73 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^Agyā ŋ budđi saŋ aṅganāŧa ri ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā marê sira,mojaṙ tan panahânĕkākĕn i lulut lulut ira ri nareśwarātmajā,ṅke rakryan mapa hetu niŋ kadi wiwal mulat ariris apakṣa maṅsula,hāḥ wāliṅku tĕkâkisapwana kita n tĕka dumadak adoḥ tĕka ŋ tamuy*73:1:555*

Antĕnku n tuna kapwa siḥta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,māskw-induŋ ndi wĕkas ni kuŋta palakuṅkwa hurupĕn i lara priḥ i ṅhulun,rāganta mwaŋ unĕṅku denya n ahurup tali paṅuwata kiŋkiŋ i ṅhulun,wet niŋ tan hana sanmatanta palarĕṅkwa karika karaṇanta tan sahur*73:2:556*

dyaḥ saŋ haṙṣa piniṇḍa ratnawanitâṅaraṅa karaṇa niŋ lanā lulut,saŋ kiŋkiŋ ginawe rarâhayu sujanma karaṇa niŋ akuŋ tumon kita,saŋ rāgānala maṅdadi wwaŋ amanas manasi hati kita n kinonĕṅan,saŋ rĕs maṅdadi janma rājaduhitâmuhara wĕdi niŋ ahyunê kita*73:3:557*

nāhan de nira mojaṙ aṅrĕṣi hatîniṅĕt iṅĕt apa tan kinahyunan,heman wīṙyya nira mwaŋ uttama ni kapraƀun ira suyaśâdƀutêŋ jagat,riŋ rūpâsĕmu rūpa niŋ smara sawaṙgga lawan asana riŋ labuḥ kapat,tan kewö wiꝑalaprayāsa hana tan pinakadi kadi kambaŋ iŋ caru*73:4:558*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:74 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^mantĕn śrī naranāŧa mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunandâṅucap,liŋnya dyaḥku harĕp kita wruha ri pāwak niŋ gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat,nāhan māsku saŋ aṅganāŧa pahawās gĕntĕṙ madadyan ratu,yogyâtĕmwa lawan kitā kita tĕmaḥ niŋ cātakâmet jawuḥ*74:1:559*

ṅkānê rājya saŋ aṅganāŧa wĕkas iŋ ramyê huwus niŋ laga,ry-antuk saŋ praƀu maṅlurug saha bala lwiṙ waḥ sakêŋ paṙwwata,gĕntĕṙ niŋ grit ikaŋ raŧânĕmahakĕn kuŋ ni wwaŋ iŋ kāṙttika,luḥ niŋ strī kahañaŋ ri līna ni ratunyâṅde paḍĕt niŋ lĕbū*74:2:560*

ndan heman tuna rājalakṣmi satĕwĕknya n rājya niṙdewatī,hetu śrī naranāŧa tan sŧiti pijĕṙ luṅhā madewāśraya,de niŋ hyūn ira n aṅhyaṅa ŋ nagara moǥa n kewĕhan tan hana,ṅhiŋ rakryan pakarājalakṣmi nira maṙmmā de nirâṅundaṅa*74:3:561*

rakryan yan hana sanmatanta ri sirânambāna kiŋkiŋ nira,ndak pinta nya sĕkaṙ tajinta pamahugya mwaŋ sĕrĕḥ riŋ kajaŋ,taṅgap denta mĕne sĕpaḥ nira katon heman yatan suŋsuṅĕn,nya ŋ siṅhāsana karwananta pakisapwan māskw-i paṅkwan haji*74:4:562*

nāhan denya n aṅĕdwakĕn nrĕpasutâhyun waspadê saŋ praƀu,mogâcūm ararĕm wulat nira sinuṅsuŋ riŋ wulat löṙ miṅe,ndan dūrâhyuna kewalâwĕdi kumöl ambĕk nirâṅdoḥ arĕs,yan tiṅhal kadi tiṅhal iŋ mulat iŋ aṙccâṅheṙ iŋ uṅgwan ƀaya*74:5:563*

māliḥ śrîndumatī riniṅriŋ inariḥ de saŋ sunandâmawa,Āśāƀūta saŋ aṅganāŧa ri layad dewī nĕhĕṙ tan waluy,de niŋ ƀrānta nirâṅikĕt rasa palambaŋ paṅlipuṙ luḥ pinöm,ṅkānê watwan ikaŋ salö panulisan maṙmmā rasanyâmanis*74:6:564*

rakryan saŋ maliŋ iŋ matâmatik i rūpaṅkw-âṅĕḍap yan wulat,kālap denta manaḥku mĕṅgĕp amanis rūpanta duṣṭêŋ hati,mukṣa twaskw-i sĕḍĕŋta mūṙ syapa ta len saṅkê kitâṅambila,Eman māsku tuhan tuhan maliŋ atimpuḥ duṙyyaśakṣatriya*74:7:565*

rakryan haywa kita pramāda ri surup niŋ lek mĕne riŋ wĕṅi,prāptâmora kakanta haywa kita tan yatnā ry-awaktêŋ jinĕm,sāk niŋ ken awanaṅkwa mañjiŋ i parāhasyanta riŋ pamrĕman,maṅgā matya matâku pökana kukuṅku n paṅguhā riŋ pupū*74:8:566*

<jagadnāŧa>:75

^nahan rasa ni de nirâhyun amaliŋ maliṅana ri raras suputrikā,Agöŋ suꝁa nira n tibā manaḥ i saŋ katuduḥ arusita pwa riŋ manaḥ,ri kāpusan ikaŋ smarâpunagi yan waluyana sira de nrĕpātmajā,lumakwa mapasaŋ pasaŋ wuyaha yan muliḥ iriŋ iriṅĕn marê dalĕm*75:1:567*

Atīta sira saŋ narendra maṅaraŋ tucapa sira narendrakanyakā,sinuṇḍaŋ inamĕṙ kininkin aṅĕliḥ rasa tumayuṅa kabwatan raras,tuwin manaḥ ira n prapañca kumĕtĕṙ hati nira mulat iŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,baṅun lumaku ri wwat ewĕḥ alĕyö maṅamĕṙ amĕṙ i de nira n laku*75:2:568*

sahaṙṣa saŋ awantināŧa ri ḍatĕŋ saŋ ahayu pinakahyaŋ iŋ saƀā,hanan pasiḍakĕp hanan pasidĕhâṅuraḥ ariḥ ulaḥ iŋ girahyasĕn,waḥ iŋ kapitu tan pahī wĕtu ni rāga nira ri naranāŧaputrikā,pĕnuḥ maṅarape tĕkêŋ kaka kakânwam atuha sinarambahan lulut*75:3:569*

I maṅkana ni de nira n karakĕtan turida sinaput iŋ manoƀawa,tan enak aṅinaŋ tan enak aṅucap humĕnĕŋ apĕga ta n sayâwĕnĕs,sawet i pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,ya kāraṇa nirâṅucap tan awiraŋ sumĕgĕ sĕgĕḥ i saŋ nrĕpātmajā*75:4:570*

<jagadđita>:76

^rakryan ƀāgya kita n ḍatĕŋ nihan aluṅguha yayi ri kisapwan i ṅhulun,mās lāwan maṇik uttamâṙjja humaḍaŋ pakĕna nika panumbasê kita,yadyan kapraƀun i ṅhulun suṅakĕnaṅkwa ri kita yayi yan kitâharĕp,yan praŋ yan kakawin panĕkwa ni kakanta ri kita yayi yan n-apaṅgiha*76:1:571*

yan riŋ kāṙttikamāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕŋ amĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅĕn i ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kakawinku riŋ yaśa,yan māsâsujimāsa rāmya masa ni ṅhulun amĕnĕm i rājya niŋ musuḥ,kuṇḍaŋ kuṇḍaṅa ni ṅhulun kita mulat mulata ri kawaninku riŋ raṇa*76:2:572*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:77

^nāhan de naranāŧa mojaṙ araras mambö laṅö niŋ jinĕm,siṅgiḥ yan pracacaḥ karas waśa ri tuŋtuŋ niŋ tanaḥ riŋ kapö,siŋ soṅkab ni tutuk nirâwĕtu laṅö kāmīrasâpet manis,pöḥ niŋ haṙṣa pinöm atūt guru laǥunyâṙjjâṅĕnoḥ lambaṅa*77:1:573*

saŋ katwaŋ niŋ awaṙṇna campaka tumiṅhal sakṣaṇê saŋ praƀu,ceṣṭākāra nirênariḥ winulatan de saŋ sunandâtaña,māskw-induŋ mapa budđi rakryan i narendra n swāmya rakryan sira,yogyâpan kadi mūla tuṅgal apasaḥ maṅke n tĕmaḥ mānuṣa*77:2:574*

<Upendrabajra>:78 
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 11

^yadin kitâtĕmwa lawan narendra,ry-awantideśâtiśayêŋ suƀikṣa,wwaŋ uttama wwaŋnya kawîṅgitajña,pacaṅkramānanta pasiṙ wukiṙnya*78:1:575*

gunuŋ mahākāla ṅaranya rāmya,kapunpunan de saŋ awantināŧa,I pāṙśwa pāṙśwanya patīṙŧa tīṙŧan,pĕnuḥ dwijaṙṣy-âjaṙ ajaṙ tan imbā*78:2:576*

saƀā ƀaṭārêśwara nityakāla,śiwāmƀa sakweḥ ni bañunya śudđa,kulĕm pwa saŋ hyaŋ tuwi krĕṣṇapakṣa,yayâpaḍaŋ de nikaŋ aṙdđacandra*78:3:577*

paran tatan rāmya nikā parāna,pamenanê kāla nikaŋ basanta,Ikaŋ larâgöŋ mala niŋ śarīra,Awās hilaŋ māry-aṅaweśa denya*78:4:578*

<sragđara>:79

^tāman saŋ nāŧa tan popama halĕp ika sāmpun prakāśâdwitīya,piṅgiṙ niŋ lwaḥ srĕp ātis ny-aṅin ika humaras ganđa niŋ paṅkaja mrik,sākṣāt swaṙggātmakâpan sahana hana nikaŋ kĕmbaŋ aṅjraḥ paḍârūm,heman yan lena saṅkê kita śaraṇa ni kādewatanya n pinūjā*79:1:579*

nāhan de saŋ sunandâmirĕsĕpakĕn i saŋ yogya kaṙmmā sudewī,ndān ambĕk śrī suputrī miṅay atimĕs adoḥ tan hana ŋ rāga mātra,sāmpun wruḥ saŋ sunandā karaṇa nika n akon muṅsirê saŋ pratīpa,Asrĕt lampaḥ nirâlon laku laku jaladânūtakĕn mārutâlon*79:2:580*

ndan saŋ kāry-âṅaraŋ sis kawĕlas arĕp irâmeri luḥ tan tinoliḥ,baṙyyan tiṅhal ri dewī sira rasa pĕjahâpan rĕmĕk twas nira syuḥ,limbe limbe sudewī kadi maṅaway akon milwa ri śrī narendra,wet niŋ ƀrāntâṅikĕt ƀāṣa ri saruṅan ikaŋ patrĕm aṅrĕs rasanya*79:3:581*

<jagadnāŧa>:80

^ṅhulun yaśana rāga māsku pakađaṙmman ĕnahana raras niŋ aṅrĕṅiḥ,hayunta makawāṇḍiranya ya paṅöbana para paranaṅkwa yan rimaŋ,prasĕnta ri dalĕm jinĕm titisananta luḥ i lukaṙ i kenta riŋ tilam,susunta pakasāđananta kalawan pipi katiga tĕṅaḥ maran lĕpas*80:1:582*

<sragđara>:81

^nāhan de śrī narendrânĕmahakĕn i lulut kuŋ nirâwak wilāpa,yêkī tan saḥ ri paṅkwan winaca tiniliṅan koŋ rinĕṅwan winaswās,Adrĕs luḥ śrī narendrâṅrasani rasa nikâpan katuhwan rasanya,yogyâṅantyêŋ mahantĕn wacan iŋ alaradan kālapan ratnakanyā*81:1:583*

rakryan putrī huwus māliḥ asĕmu paṅaliḥ niŋ sĕkaṙ sālas aṅjraḥ,kweḥ niŋ guṇḍik nira mwaŋ kaka kaka rumarâṅasturi mrik waṅinya,lagy-âtaṅkis humuŋ hambuluṅan i tali kenyânamaṙ ṣaṭpada strī,haṙṣâmbĕk saŋ pratīpâmapag iŋ ujaṙ arūm tustus iŋ laṅwa laṅwan*81:2:584*

<krĕti>:82

^Ibu t asy-asiḥ kita kadaŋ kadaṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ i ṅhulun rimaŋ,kita yogya mitra kulabanđw-amarasana ri rāga ni ṅhulun,pakawaṙgga ni ṅhulun i paṅkwan asisihana raśmi niŋ prĕman,Arĕnaḥ manahkw-aṅaku sānak iri kita patĕmwan iŋ jaja*82:1:585*

pakĕnaṅkwa yan marĕk i māskw-amibikana laṭinta riŋ waja,lumut iŋ payođara huwus kakiṅan usapanaṅkwa riŋ jaja,Iruŋ i ṅhulun panutulaṅkwa luḥ i pipi ri pamriḥ iŋ sipat,lukaṙ iŋ tapiḥ salinanaṅkwa karatala mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*82:2:586*

<sragđara>:83

^ndaḥ yêki n liŋ narendrârasa mijila sakêŋ ƀāṣa lāwan palambaŋ,sotan ta ŋ sāri niŋ rāga piturun i laṅö niŋ kawi ƀrāntacitta,tan paṅgintiṙ manis niŋ tĕbu sawukiṙ apan tan patuŋtuŋ manisnya,maṙmmânyuḥ prāṇa rūmnyâsĕmu paṅucapan iŋ wahw-amaṅkw-âṅdudut ken*83:1:587*

rakryan putrī mulat riŋ nrĕpati kadi wulat niŋ ṭikā riŋ wilāpa,mojaṙ ta dyaḥ sunandā wwaya ta sira siwin śakty-asaṅjñā pratīpa,sākṣāt swaṙggânurun rūpa ni nagara nira ry-ânupa ꝁyāti riŋ rāt,kumbaŋ kĕmbaŋ papaṅgiḥta kadi patĕmu niŋ kāṙttika mwaŋ basanta*83:2:588*

<jagadnāŧa>:84 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ aṙjjuna sahasrabāhu riŋ usāna sira siniwi śakti nītimān,prakāśa sira saŋ daśānana musuḥ nira huwus ayaśâmatī musuḥ,taŧāpi kaparājayêŋ raṇa huwus hinuripan alawas pinañjara,hana pwa sira saŋ pratīpa sira rakwa wĕka nira suśīla digjaya*84:1:589*

paran pwa wĕkas uṅsirĕnta paḍa wastu kita wĕka niŋ uttamapraƀu,para praƀu kapan paḍâsira lawan sira tĕwas amilĕt milĕt wulat,Ameta kita len muwaḥ tĕwas aṅel midĕṙ ibu kapana n pamaṅgiha,mataŋnya sira sĕṅgahĕnta kaka yogya sira manuwalêŋ ujaṙ yayi*84:2:590*

<śiꝁariṇī>:85 
⏑ – – | – – – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 17

^yadin sidđā rakryan sasisihana rūm niŋ siliḥ asiḥ,Awās rakryan glānâhuyaŋ apupul i jro pakasutan,hana lwaḥ ramyâlwā prakaśita si rewā ṅaran ika,kitâdyūsa ṅkānêsuḥ isuhana lāwan saŋ ahulun*85:1:591*

raras niŋ karwa swāmi paran ika rakwâṅlĕwihana,marā riŋ tāman tan hana marĕka līlā ṅwaŋ aṅĕnĕs,yadin madyūsêŋ lwaḥ talaga wulakan śūnya kasĕnĕt,wĕnaŋ sāmbĕk niŋ swāmi tariman apan tan hana mulat*85:2:592*

kalīṅanyâlaḥ māsku marĕka nihan dak parĕkakĕn,paran maṙmmantâsuṅsut arĕṅu miṅe tan pamituhu,paṅantî paṅkwan saŋ praƀu hila hila ŋ duḥka siwuhĕn,Apan māskw-âpet pet hayu pahayu budđinta ri sira*85:3:593*

<sragđara>:86 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^nāhan liŋ saŋ sunandâmirĕsĕpakĕn i tiṅkaḥ narāṙyya pratīpa,paŧya wruḥ sopapattîṅgita nikaŋ ucap akrĕp kĕna priḥ narendra,yâṅde tan saṅśayê twas nira ri ḍatĕṅa rakryan suputrî kisapwan,kady-aṅhyaŋ motusan wallaƀa mamagĕhakĕn tan wuruŋ niŋ swakāṙyya*86:1:594*

rakryan putrī miṅe tan wawarĕṅĕḥ apa tan trĕpti rakwê narendra,saŋ nāŧa wruḥ sira n tan kinaharĕpan ikaŋ budđi maṅkin prapañca,Āśāƀūtânulis ketaka rasa kakawin pöḥ nikaŋ rāga tībra,tambā niŋ keraṅan tan winadal i liḍaḥ iŋ kāma nāhan rasanya*86:2:595*

<nawahaṙṣa>:87 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^Ibu tan paꝑala pwa ŋ amalaṙ i hayunta sĕḍĕŋta rare,syapa māsku kadi ṅhulun aṅurati rāga lawan turida,katunan lĕpihan kita kinirimakĕnku karaskw-i kita,tĕka riŋ kararan pwa kita mapa tiki n sahajâpi lupa*87:1:596*

sĕḍĕŋ iŋ pabĕlaḥ turida kinĕkĕsanku kitêŋ lĕpihan,makasāđana kuṅkw-aṅiṅĕt iṅĕt i rūmta lanā n pinalar,Aṅadĕg pwa kitêŋ puḍak araras inastwakĕn iŋ ƀramara,winaliṅku kitâŋ liṅa puji puji yan ratu niŋ kusuma*87:2:597*

saŋ apiṇḍa wukiṙ ṅhulun ajaṙ ajarê kita muṅgwa sadā,tarukāṅkw-i hayunta pamiṣayana rāga sĕḍĕṅkw-alulut,licinêŋ śayanâkw-anusupa ri hulĕsta suganđa miṅiŋ,sipi māsku suꝁaṅku katuruna ri soṙ i tĕṅaḥta rari*87:3:598*

<sragđara>:88 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^nāhan de śrī narendrâkakawina maṅani twas nirê jro drawâṅras,ndātan tiṅhal muwaḥ riŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā kewalêraŋ tumuṅkul,māry-âśāƀūta sāmpun pinĕgat ira lulut kuŋ nirê śrī suputrī,hetunya n tan wijil luḥ nira pamaḍĕm irêŋ rāgabahnî dalĕm twas*88:1:599*

sāmpun māliḥ sudewī kasusu laku nirâṅĕñcuḥ ĕñcuḥ kaṅelan,ndan tiṅhal saŋ susenâṅiriṅakĕn aṅamĕṙ tan wĕnaŋ sāḥ amaṇḍĕŋ,kady-âdandan kisapwan yan alihan asilâhyūn amaṅkwê sudewī,haṙṣâgyā gyān anuṅsuŋ riŋ ujaṙ akakawin lwiṙ katonêŋ palambaŋ*88:2:600*

<jagadđita>:89
