^rakryan saŋ pinunagyakĕnku śaraṇāśraya tumuluṅa kiŋkiŋ i ṅhulun,Aṅlū māsku kisapwan i ṅhulun aluṅguha kita yayi haywa saṅśaya,t asy-âsiḥ kita māsihê kawi guṇaṅku palaṙ amalĕsêŋ karāsikan,lambā kapraƀun i ṅhulun kita rumaṅkĕpana saꝑala yogya tuṅgalĕn*89:1:601*

maṅke n prāpta ni māsku tambay iŋ anon wwaŋ ahayu kadi dewakanyakā,yan riŋ śūnya katĕmwananta saha ƀūṣaṇa maṅĕnĕsa tan parowaṅa,byaktânĕṅgaha dewatī kalĕmahan ṅhulun iri kita dūra saṅśayā,Āpan de ni hayunta yogya kita māsku panadinakĕna n pinaṅkwakĕn*89:2:602*

paṅkwankw-îbu paranti niŋ wwaŋ anukĕṙ nukĕṙ aṅĕsaḥ ĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,śīṙṇna syuḥ lĕṅĕn i ṅhulun pinakarantunan i kuku niŋ epu tan panūt,tan pamwas jaja ni ṅhulun wahu waras linawad i panĕpak niŋ aṅrĕṅiḥ,lagy-emö pipi ni ṅhulun saƀa saƀā ni waja niŋ anulak wineḥ sĕpaḥ*89:3:603*

<sragđara>:90 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^sojaṙ saŋ nāŧa kady-âṅalapana kasusuk niŋ kĕnêŋ rāgapāśa,kady-ânambāna kiŋkiŋ niŋ amalaku suwal kewĕhan kāladeśa,sākṣāt sambat niŋ onĕŋ kinirimakĕn apet pet manis de ni kuŋnya,mambö rūm niŋ katurwan winuṅu ni jarumanyânĕkākĕn wilāpa*90:1:604*

tatkāla śrī suputrī sapawulatan aṅantî harĕp saŋ susenā,tan kantun saŋ sunandā marĕk ataña tĕhĕṙ sopacārâtalaṅkup,rakryan sāmpun kita wruḥ ri narapati mapâmbĕkta māsku n patĕmwa,Āpan saŋ nāŧa sākṣāt madana midĕṙ amet hyaŋ ratī riŋ kaḍatwan*90:2:605*

yadyastun māsku sidđâṅhaturakĕna hayuntêŋ kisapwan narendra,ṅkānêŋ gĕṅgā kitâmena mahas ahasa riŋ nūsa śūnyê tĕṅaḥnya,mwaŋ yan rakryan marêŋ wrĕndawana taman irânopamêŋ laṅwa laṅwan,Akweḥ ƀuktinta ramyâmarĕkana yamunā lālanâkuwwa kuwwa*90:3:606*

rakryan putrī tan eṅĕḥ sira kinĕdĕ kĕdö yan paniwyê narendra,siṅgiḥ rakwa n rarā suṇṭi masĕmu lĕṅa suṇṭy-âkalis de nirâmbĕk,ndan budđi śrī susenā kadi pulut atĕguḥ tan lumeṙ de nirâhyun,saŋkṣepanya ndi tan sidđa kapalikĕtana śrī suputrî narendra*90:4:607*

luṅhā lampaḥ sudewī narapati kawĕkas keraṅan tan tinoliḥ,kady-agriŋ nora rakwâṅinaki laṅu laṅun yan mulat riŋ sĕrĕḥ wwaḥ,rakryan putrī jugânuṅgayap i hati nirâtyanta riŋ priṅga wiṣṭi,maṅkin ƀrāntâṅikĕt ƀāṣa panalimuṙ irê tībra niŋ rāga tikṣṇa*90:5:608*

<jagadđita>:91

^dyaḥ maḥ luṅsuran i ṅhulun pasuṅa ni ṅhulun iri kita māsku taṅgapĕn,siñjaŋ siñjaṅa rakryan iŋ paṅaraṅan ri huwus iŋ anulis pralāpita,göŋ ny-âsiḥku ri māsku yogya suwalĕn ṅhulun amalaku luṅsuran tapiḥ,donyêbū pinakātmarakṣa n amĕrĕnkw-abasahana tĕhĕṙ pamera luḥ*91:1:609*

rakryan saŋ hinarĕp harĕpku śaraṇāśraya mulata ri rāga ni ṅhulun,tan sênuṅsiṙ adoḥ manaḥta salawasku tĕka ri kita moǥa tan liniŋ,ṅhiŋ gānyā hana kāsihanta ḍatu ḍatwa kahulunana tan sahê kita,yêkī pañjiṅanaṅkwa nitya saparan ṅhulun aṅucap ucap lawan kita*91:2:610*

nāhan ƀāṣa nira n tiniṅgalakĕn iŋ paṅaraṅan i layat suputrikā,mantĕn duḥka nirâsamun turida rāga ni manaḥ ira tan tinūtakĕn,śrī hemāṅgada kabwatan kuŋ i ḍatĕŋ nrĕpawaraduhitā marê sira,wwāgan moǥa gumanty-amukti lara rāga niyata sira tan kinahyunan*91:3:611*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:92

^śrī dewîndumatī ḍatĕŋ sira ri saŋ sāmpun kaciry-an smara,Ewĕḥ tan kahiḍĕp harĕp nira lawan tan hyūn irê saŋ praƀu,ndān eman wĕkasan kataṙkkan i kalis ny-ambĕk nira n tan rimaŋ,Aṅhiŋ piŋ rwa mulat kapiŋ rwa sahajâtuŋtuŋ tikĕl niŋ halis*92:1:612*

sāmpun waspada doḥ i rāga nira tan tuṅgal panononana,suṅsut suṅsut ira n kinon marĕka len tiṅhal nirâṅrĕṅwani,Ākārêṅgita niŋ manaḥ saha wijil niŋ śabda norâkadi,Ahyun kawruhana n tan ahyun ika kaprajñān irâpet wiwal*92:2:613*

tan wruḥ śrī naranāŧa yan tan aharĕp rakryan suputrî sira,Aṅgĕṅgöŋ kamadan trĕṇāṅkura hiḍĕp saŋ nāŧa riŋ wwaŋ kabeḥ,hamham paṙccaya de ni rūpa nira tĕkwan śakti wānîŋ raṇa,kĕdw-âkuŋ makasoŋ larônĕŋ ira yan pojaṙ waśâkon marā*92:3:614*

<jagadđita>:93 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ sākṣāt smarakanyakā saŋ anarīra ri hati saŋ amiṇḍa riŋ hiḍĕp,budđiṅkw-âlal aṅantyakĕn siha ni māskw-ahuyaŋ ajaruman pralāpita,maṅke pwā tĕka tan wawaŋ marĕk awaṙṇna kĕna guṇa miṅe kitâriris,rakryan haywa kakanta māsku sinaranta kalalaḥ ibu rāga ni ṅhulun*93:1:615*

saṇḍaŋ ƀakta samotusankw-apuyĕŋ an layat alisuḥ amet rarâhayu,ndātan poliḥ aṅel aṅulwan aṅawetan aṅidĕri kaḍatwan iŋ musuḥ,maṅke pwa n hana māskw-arūm pakawayaŋ wayaṅĕn amĕrĕn iŋ pasaṅgaman,tan pātmā rasa kaprĕman saśayanânĕkĕnakĕna śarīra ni ṅhulun*93:2:616*

nāhan de naranāŧa mojaṙ awuyuŋ sira wĕkasan adoḥ suputrikā,śrī putrī katibān ujaṙ haji tan eṅĕḥ apuji sira yan tuhan tuhan,Ājñālaṅǥana yogya daṇḍan apa tan hana sahuṙ ira pakṣa māliha,simbantĕn haji molihâmiđi balik sira kawiđi dinaṇḍa niŋ smara*93:3:617*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:94 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^sakweḥ saŋ marĕk uttamottama wiwal munduṙ paḍâmid miṅe,Aṅheman ri narendra yan sira tan antuk śrī suputrī mulat,mwaŋ strī strī paricārikā paḍa humuŋ maṅyogyanî saŋ praƀu,ḍyam têkî wĕkasan tuhun hana mulat yan saŋ sunandâṅucap*94:1:618*

rakryan tiṅhalanâtpada nrĕpati sākṣāt ṣaṭpadâmet sĕkar,maṅheṙ heṙ i dalĕm taman makapaṅanty-antyan kucup niŋ mĕnur,maṅke n mūṙ aṅaliḥ cumuṇḍuk i widaṙbƀâpakṣa tan mantuka,Āpan maṙmma nira n ḍatĕŋ kita karĕṅw-an paṅjraḥ iŋ campaka*94:2:619*

śrī hemāṅgada laṅwa laṅwan asana ndātan mĕkaṙ kābunan,saŋsāra kṣaya saŋsayâluru lume de niŋ smarāꝁyâpanas,heman māsku kucup ni budđi nira yan tan sanmatan kāsihan,ṅhiŋ gānya n mĕkara n kitâṅlawada māskw-âpan gĕrĕḥ niŋ kapat*94:3:620*

wwantĕn rājya nirê kaliṅga kita yogya hyaŋ hyaṅanyâhalĕp,tĕkwan paṙśśwa nikaŋ mahendragiri hetunya n kadîndrālaya,gĕntĕṙ ny-ampuhan iŋ mahodađi karĕṅw-âgĕnturan tan pĕgat,Aṅhiŋ donya mamuṅwa saŋ praƀu lawan māsku n katurwān apöm*94:4:621*

rakryan tan kasasaṙ hayunta kawawê saŋ nāŧa hemāṅgada,Āpan budđi nirâbĕnĕṙ tan arusit wruḥ ry-ambĕk iŋ dug rimaŋ,hĕnwanta n marĕkê kisapwan ira kewalya ṅhulun tan saha,yêkī don i manĕḥta mājara ri māṙgganta n suꝁâsaṅgama*94:5:622*

Aṅhiŋ yogya siwinta tan patatalan trus tuñjuŋ iŋ kapraƀun,prajñā wany-anulus bisâṅaji đanurwedâđika wruḥ nira,yan riŋ kīṙtty-aniwāṙyya śudđa hana soṙ niŋ candrawimbâkucĕm,tustus niŋ ratu śakti digjaya sĕkaṙ tajy-aṅkuran kṣatriya*94:6:623*

nāhan de niŋ amet manis niŋ aṅucap mambö juruḥ kābunan,Antuk niŋ maṅalap manis ni kakawin saŋ wrĕḍđa wrĕdđîŋ laṅö,ndātan paṅgarit aṙdđa tan rĕsĕp i budđi śrī narendrātmajā,luṅhā wruḥ tumuluy sira n kinĕḍapan de saŋ sunandâṅaliḥ*94:7:624*

śrī hemāṅgada kāri keraṅan akiŋkiŋ tan wĕnaŋ sāhasa,maṅgâmora makilya kilyana tumūtê śrī narendrātmajā,saŋ hyaŋ manmaŧa duṣṭa tan rwa tĕlu pat rowaŋ nirâśâlara,yêkī hetu nirâṅikĕt rasa wilāpâṅras rasanyê hati*94:8:625*

<sragđara>:95

^maṅko pwântĕnku dentâmbĕk atiśaya dahat kewalâṅgöŋ kaputryan,budđintâpyak madêŋ haṙṣa tan akuŋ iŋ akuŋ saŋsayâpy-âwalepa,dentâweḥ rāga tan popama kadi ginawe lĕŋlĕŋâku n tumiṅhal,māyā muṅgw-iŋ crĕmin lwiṙtta riŋ apa wĕnaṅaṅkwâṅisapwê tuwuḥta*95:1:626*

saŋ lwīṙ aṙccâṅaraŋ byakta pan ulaha ni māskw-i ṅhulun yan pamaṅkwa,saŋ lwiṙ dewî tulis tan wuruṅa kasarikâku n marê pamrĕmanta,saŋ lwiṙ wwe niŋ samudrâṅaraṅakĕn i manaḥku n surud siḥta māsku,saŋ tuŋtuŋ ni rwi niŋ ketaka kari kacarik twaskw-i luṅhānta maṅko*95:2:627*

<basantatilaka>:96 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^nāhan manis ni paṅikĕt nira rāgacihna,śrĕṅgāra rāsika pinöm atĕmaḥ wilāpa,muṅgw-î dalĕm hati ginūḋa raras rarasnya,pinrāṙŧanākĕn ira mĕtwa mĕne n papaṅgiḥ*96:1:628*

saŋ lwiṙ hyaŋ iŋ jalada kāṅinan iŋ basanta,ndātan panis nisi huyaŋ ni manaḥ niŋ onĕŋ,luṅhā lawan riris i budđi nirê narendra,saŋ nāŧa kāri tĕlĕs i drĕs i luḥ nirâṅdyus*96:2:629*

byātīta saŋ praƀu narendrasutā wiwakṣan,dolāyamāna ri turuŋ ni manaḥ nirêsi,luṅhâmiliḥ miliḥ i jalwa nirê narendra,himpĕṙ sĕkaṙ midĕṙ amet ƀramarê kuwuŋnya*96:3:630*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ sira ri sanmuꝁa saŋ narendra,śrī pāṇḍya haṙṣa kadi tan rāt ira n tumiṅhal,runtuḥ lĕbuṙ manaḥ irâsĕmu rāgabahni,lwiṙ mās hanêŋ muṣa wawaŋ drawa de niŋ apwī*96:4:631*

saŋ pāṇḍya siṅhapuruṣākrĕti rāgaśatru,śrī putrikâciri wĕdi n para riŋ paḍöman,söḥ budđi sattwa naranāŧa paḍâwrĕg awri,keṇḍit manaḥ nira lawan kuŋ irê dalĕm twas*96:5:632*

sāmpun pĕtĕŋ twas ira söḥ turidâṅaweśa,Aṅhiŋ hineṙ siliḥ asiḥ naranāŧaputrī,Āpan katon muꝁa nirâsĕmu śītaraśmi,yêkī nimitta nira mojaṙ amanwa manwa*96:6:633*

<jagadđita>:97

^ṅke siṅhāsana māskw-aluṅguha paran karaṇa niŋ aṅadĕg baṅun wiwal,rākantâlawas aṅrĕṅö ri hayu rakryan ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun ḍatĕŋ,tĕkwan śrī naranāŧa ƀoja maṅutus ḍatĕṅa ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,nāhan taŋ karas esi ƀāṣa pahulaṅkwa ri kita yayi hantusākĕna*97:1:634*

wruḥ ku n tan paṅĕnoha kuṅku ri kitâpan ahayu sakadaŋ lawan ratiḥ,tuṅgal rakwa rarasta riŋ muꝁa lawan rĕsĕp i raras i māsku riŋ pupū,rāgaṅkw-îbu hanêŋ tĕṅaḥta kapipis lara turida kinölwa riŋ susu,lampūn kaprĕma riŋ pasaṅgaman i paṅhapit i wĕtis i māsku ri ṅhulun*97:2:635*

<basantatilaka>:98 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^sojaṙ narāđipati tan palawan manisnya,maṅgiṣṭa śiṣṭa mari śiṣṭa sinorakĕnya,lwiṙ tan mađu ŋ mađu tinaṇḍiṅakĕn yayān sor,lambā manis manis ikaŋ gula tan panaṅkĕp*98:1:636*

śrī putrikā sira mulat ri harĕp narendra,ndātan kapūhan apa tan hana paṅgaritnya,mogâkalis manaḥ irâsĕmu tan panaṅgĕl,kady-adwa tiṅhal ira kewala tan papiṅrwa*98:2:637*

do doḥ i budđi nira niścaya saŋ sunandā,śrī pāṇḍya tiṅhal ira kady-aṅutus maṅĕdwa,ndan saŋ kinon ira bisâṅupacāra śabda,mojaṙ tuhun pali palin ya tĕkapnya mojar*98:3:638*

<jagadđita>:99 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^nāhan śrī naranāŧa pāṇḍya sira yogya paṅayatan i māsku riŋ hayu,heman rūmta yatan pagĕgwan i manis manis ira n aṅisapw-aṅolakĕn,Aṅhiŋ samƀawa rakwaṅöbana huyaŋta saꝑala parĕkĕnta riŋ tilam,siŋ sojaṙ haji yan rahasya rasan iŋ śayana kĕmitananta cupwana*99:1:639*

yadyastun kita māsku n âmĕŋ amĕṅêŋ tuha rawa kalawan nareśwara,byaktânaṅśaya cakrawāka dadi mānuṣa maṭika ṭikan mariŋ ḍarat,mwaŋ yan karwa narendra māsku mahasêŋ pasisi mĕgila riŋ wwaŋ iŋ pasir,byaktânĕṅgaha dèwa niŋ miŧuna rāśi mĕtu harĕp ahimya himyana*99:2:640*

Atyantêŋ kalaṅön lĕyĕp winulatan patĕmu ni lĕṅĕŋ iŋ pasiṙ wukir,ndan dūrâmaḍanê laṅö ni patĕmunta matĕmu kalawan nareśwara,yadyāpin paḍa riŋ laṅö pisaniṅū kadi rarasa ni māskw-asaṅgama,ṅhiŋ gānyâmaḍanê rarasta raras iŋ rati madana n akālihan hulĕs*99:3:641*

<mālinī>:100 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 15

^nahan ucapan ikâpet pet manis tan pamandi,kadi rĕsĕpa rasanyê budđi rakryan suputrī,kunaŋ apa tan ikâṅde haṙṣa riŋ haṙṣa niŋ len,wiꝑala kadi manis niŋ twak yan iŋ madyasakta*100:1:642*

narapatitanayâṅliḥ tan sahuṙ lwiṙ tulis mās,rĕṅu nira paṅadeśan yan tan aṅgâmituhwa,kalalu laku nirâṅdoḥ mūṙ lawan saŋ sunandā,nrĕpati kawĕkas ākuŋ śīǥra māwak wilāpa*100:2:643*

<jagadđita>:101 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^rakryan saŋ kĕna rāga tībra kaka rakryan aṅuwatana haywa saṅśaya,hrū saŋ hyaŋ madanê hatinta dahutĕṅkwa bĕbĕdĕn i taṅanku hĕmbana,ṅhiŋ jampyanta karāsikanku n amĕkul garĕgĕtĕn amijĕt mijĕt susu,romantâjumĕn i ṅhulun sadakanaṅkwa n anĕsĕpi laṭinta riŋ tilam*101:1:644*

kocap māsku wicakṣaṇôṇḍahagi yogya panagara bisâmaṅun lulut,ṅke ta dyaḥ mata ni ṅhulun sipatananta pĕnĕdĕn usapanta riŋ pusuḥ,yan kālanta pinaṅkwakĕn wwaya jajaṅku rari siku sikunta yan cala,kuŋta mwaŋ turidaṅku pādwakĕna māsku patitisana luḥ maran rapĕt*101:2:645*

<jagadnāŧa>:102 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^nahan tĕmahan iŋ prapañca ni manaḥ nrĕpati wahu lipuṙ linaṅwakĕn,hanâmbĕk ira mantukâmruda tuhun mawaraha rumuhun ri saŋ praƀu,katon ujara niŋ mulat ri sira tan pamahayu kadi budđi niŋ rare,ya hetu nira tan wawaŋ muliḥ aṅantyakĕn i huwusa niŋ swayambara*102:1:646*

byatīta ri sĕḍĕŋ nira n mari rimaŋ tucapa sahana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ saƀā,manaḥnya paḍa pakṣapāta ri narendrasuta tan aharĕp ri saŋ praƀu,paḍâsraŋ aṅucap ry-uliḥ nrĕpasutā wruḥ i harĕpa nirêri saŋ haja,Alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikanâṅgĕtĕm asahuran atry-aṅadwakĕn*102:2:647*

<jagadđita>:103 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^rāga śrī naranāŧaputra masĕwö kadi kayu ragas iŋ labuḥ kapat,Osik budđi nirê ḍatĕŋ nrĕpasutā winaliŋ ira tĕkâkisapwana,Agyâweha sĕpaḥ sakê waja siliḥ suwala guyu panaṙkka niŋ mulat,bwat śrĕṅgāra dahat panāntwa nira maṙmma rasa nika rĕsĕp rinĕṅwakĕn*103:1:648*

ṅke rakryan pakisapwan onĕŋ alawas ṅhulun ibu saŋ apiṇḍa nīrada,saŋ saṅhub ni lulutku saŋ patĕṙ i kuṅku kilat i pĕtĕŋ i twas i ṅhulun,saŋ rĕm niŋ turidâṅalaḥ siḥ apuput huyaŋ amĕkasakĕn putĕk hati,saŋ truḥ truḥ ni laṅöṅku mukṣa hiniḍĕp kinisapu sahajâtĕmaḥ riris*103:2:649*

donkw-aṅlitlita roma rakryan anapak napaka hayu ni māsku riŋ tilam,Āpan tan hana len pramāṇa ri rarasta n aṅaraŋ aṅisapwakĕn puḍak,māskw-induŋ huniṅan ṅhulun ri manis iŋ mata sarasija kābunan mađu,suŋsuŋ rāga tĕṅaḥ puriḥta kalawan pipi taḍaha ni luḥta pintanĕn*103:3:650*

paṅkwankw-îbu wĕtĕḥ turuŋ pinakapaṅrĕṅihan iŋ aṅĕsaḥ pinaṅkwakĕn,tapwan kāni lĕṅĕnku de ni kuku niŋ hinari hari miṅe kinolakĕn,mwaŋ tapwan katĕpak jajaṅku kalawan pipi tĕkap iŋ arĕs kinewala,ṅhiŋ rakryan karaṇanya n emwa ragĕta mwaŋ anuluṅa manĕmbu nĕmbura*103:4:651*

<wisaṙjjita>:104

^ṅke saŋ apiṇḍa nirātmaka tinĕmahakĕn maṇi rājasutā,tan hana ṅūni dĕlāha kadi kita sujanma suśīla wagĕd,saŋ dadi janma sakêŋ taya taya kadi rakryan arūm anulus,māsku śaśāṅkawimāna karika kita maṅdadi maṙmma dahat*104:1:652*

Aṅgriṅi simbali rakryan amarasana moǥa tĕkâṅlarani,dyaḥku nihan tuluṅĕn ṅhulun uwatana kāraṇa niŋ warasa,griŋ kĕna rāga laraṅkw-aṅinak inaki mĕṅgĕp atīs apanas,māsku mataŋ yan akaṙ pipi guliga tĕṅaḥ palakun ri kita*104:2:653*

<jagadđita>:105

^nāhan de saŋ ajâṅucap mĕtu raras ni kataruṇan irâṅhiḍĕp smara,mambö turwan i paṅkwan aṅharas i paṅlawad iŋ ahayu riŋ pasaṅgaman,kady-aṅrĕṅwa rĕṅiḥ lawan paṅĕsaḥ iŋ kinisapu rasa niŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,śrī dewîndumatī pwa muṣṭi niŋ akuŋ kapana sira n aṅiṣṭya mintara*105:1:654*

<jagadnāŧa>:106

^Ujaṙ saŋ aja waṙṇna waṙṣa tumibânĕkarakĕn asanâṅrĕṅö gĕrĕḥ,Aśoka ḍinĕḍĕṙ sawaŋ nrĕpasutā wahu kasiram alūŋ apādapa,wawaŋ sĕkaṙ irânĕḍĕŋ ƀramara tan hana wani mara kewalâtilar,Apan saŋ aja rakwa tan wuruŋ aṅol aṅarĕkana mĕne n pamaṅkwakĕn*106:1:655*

narendratanayâwĕnĕs mulat i rūpa saŋ aja wawaŋ agriŋ aṅlayuŋ,kasambĕt i manis manis ni luṅid iŋ mata sarasija keṅgutan halis,huwus wruḥ i manis nira n kasarik iŋ lituhayu suƀagêŋ swayĕmbara,ya kāraṇa nirâharĕp marĕka paṅkun uwat uwatanêŋ sĕpaḥ sarik*106:2:656*

sawet ni pamanas nikaŋ madanabahni ri hati nira maṅkin aṅlare,tinaṙkka nira rājaputra dadi niŋ smara saŋ aja marêŋ swayĕmbara,muwaḥ saŋ aja saŋsayânaha nahā mulat i hayu narendraputrikā,ratiḥ karika sinwayĕmbarakĕn iŋ madananagara liŋ nirê hati*106:3:657*

sipat nrĕpasutā lutuṙ kadi humeṙ i paṅusapa nareśwarātmaja,gĕluŋ nira baṅun harĕp suruyanê jariji nrĕpatiputra yan lukar,Aṅrĕs kadi harĕp kadĕmwanana de saŋ aja mata nirâṅdadak lumuḥ,paniṅsĕt i tapiḥ nirâsĕmu harĕp lukarana ni taṅan nrĕpātmaja*106:4:658*

waja nrĕpatiputra kātara rarasnya tĕka ta mamusuḥ yan iŋ laṭi,Alal kĕtĕ kĕtĕg nirêŋ jaja lumiṇḍihana jaja narendraputrikā,Asaṅgraha naꝁâluṅid taṅan irâmiraḥ aharĕp adun lawan susu,tĕkêruŋ ira tan pakāla kumĕsut sĕmu sĕmu niŋ asĕṅhit iŋ pipi*106:5:659*

<jagadđita>:107 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa tan saḥ i narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,lāwan dyaḥ jayawaspa kāsiḥ ika tan saḥ i pada naranāŧaputrikā,ndan rakwênalapan sĕḍĕŋnya n ahañaŋ tinut ika mapasaḥ madum tuhan,tĕmbenya n sapatiṅhalan paḍa lumuḥ kawĕlas arĕp aluŋluṅan taṅis*107:1:660*

saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa mājaṙ i narendratanaya nĕhĕṙ aṅhĕmū taṅis,rakryan honya manĕḥta tiṅhalana pun marika makaṅaran mađūdakā,pun muṅgw-î hiriṅan marĕk linihaṅan wagĕd araras amaṅku pawwahan,Aṅhiŋ pun juga tan wĕnaŋ mulat awaṙṇna lara mata n aṅölakĕn taṅis*107:2:661*

yadyastun nrĕpaputrikā mara mĕne humaturakĕna rūm nirê kita,rakryan tan wĕnaŋ edihê sira yadin sira tumĕṅĕta pun mađūdakā,dūra n đāraka riŋ lara smara manĕḥta pinasahakĕn iŋ tuhan tuhan,ṅhiŋ maty-âṅaraṅê daganta bapa tan panĕmu kahulunan sadā marĕk*107:3:662*

mwaŋ yan śrîndumatī tan aptya ri tuhanku muliha sira tan panoliha,suṅsut śrī naranāŧa rakwa ri manĕḥta bapa maṅulanĕḥ turuŋ lipur,byaktâṅgĕgwana sĕmpalĕn manĕḥta bāpa kita tan awĕlas maṅaryakĕn,mātîŋ māti kināladeśa kadi kambaŋ iŋ asana sinĕmpal iŋ kapat*107:4:663*

nāhan liŋnya nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul anaṅis tucapa ta panaṅis mađūdakā,hāḥ rakryan kadi riŋ paṅipyan ahurip takari manĕ manĕḥta tiṅhali,nāhan pun mađusūdanâmwaṅi narendrasuta marĕk amaṅku pawwahan,kĕmbĕŋ kĕmbĕŋ i luḥ nipun marahakĕn siḥ ipun arabi tan wĕnaŋ muliḥ*107:5:664*

maṅke ry-antuk ipun tumūt ri naranāŧatanaya baṅun aṅhuwus huwus,tan lot ṅgānya pun aṅhiḍĕp turida rāga kadi wuruṅa matya monĕṅa,yêkā hetu nipun tĕkâhañutan aṅlalu pĕjahana de nareśwara,Aṅhiŋ luḥ ni manĕḥta kahyuna nipun rurubakĕna lawan ṅrĕs iŋ taṅis*107:6:665*

Ājñā śrī naranāŧa ṅūni ḍumawuḥ ri para panĕpi riŋ pasiṙ wukir,An pun patyana tūt tlasĕn haḍaṅĕn iŋ hawan i hawan ipun marêŋ musuḥ,maṅke n tan hana patya patyana sadoṣa nipun i sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayambara,pun ṅgānyêka dumeḥ pun ahyuna mulat mulata juga sawet ny-unĕŋ nipun*107:7:666*

hāḥ rakryan siha rakryan iŋ manĕ manĕḥ ṅhulun ibu pituhun ṅhulun tuhan,nāhan śrī naranāŧaputra pakisapwan ibu ri sira haywa tâwihaŋ,Āpan yan tuna kūŋ i māsku ri sirâpa ta hamĕṅana ni ṅhulun mĕne,tan wanđyā mati karwa pun mađu manĕḥta tuhan i huwus iŋ swayambara*107:8:667*

maṙmmā de jayawaspa mojaṙ ataṅis tĕka hirĕŋ i narendrakanyakā,pantĕs pantĕs apolahan marĕk atakwan i manaḥ ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā,siŋ solaḥnya wagĕd hanan pamisusal misusal api calâṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,kĕdw-âkon marĕkâkisapwana nĕhĕṙ mulat arĕṅu waśâṅdĕlö mata*107:9:668*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:108

^sāmpun dyaḥ jayawaspa mojaṙ irikā ta dyaḥ sunandâṅucap,rakryan tiṅhalananta māsku saŋ ajâtyantêŋ halĕp riŋ saƀā,putra śrī raǥu potrakê haji dilīpâṅhiŋ kadaṅtâparĕk,śudđakṣatriya sūṙyyawaṅśa taruṇâṅhiŋ śakti maṅke n raray*108:1:669*

waswāsĕnta halĕp nirâṅdaśaguṇê rūm niŋ tulis mās tatur,waṙṇnākāra nirâmarājaya ri waṙṇnākāra niŋ campaka,muṅgw-î pāda nirâlawan miraḥ i kĕmbaŋ niŋ tawā kedĕkan,Aṅhiŋ ketaka lot pinaṅkwakĕn ira n lwiṙnya n wĕtistâlaris*108:2:670*

tan sāhêŋ śarapuṣpa kenaka nirâpan lwiṙ smarâṅiṇḍarat,mwaŋ maṅgĕgwana puṣpacāpa ri kiwa n paṅde raras niŋ mulat,pantĕs muṅgwa ri citta niŋ rara sujanma n sūkṣma tan pāwaka,yogyâmaṅkwa ri māskw-apan paḍa lawan dewī ratiḥ riŋ hayu*108:3:671*

nāhan raśmi nikāŋ ujaṙ tĕka rĕsĕp ri twas narendrātmajā,sāmpun waspada kuŋ nirê saŋ aja maṙmma dyaḥ sunandā suꝁa,ndan mogâṅjrum apet prahelika laṅö siṅgiḥ juga n strī kawi,denyâṅjrum rasa guywa guywan araras ndātan tĕke jro hati*108:4:672*

<jagadđita>:109

^rakryan tan sasiwinta māsku sira de ni karakĕtan irâṅurĕn laṅö,riŋ tāman sira menduŋ enduṅan aśoka mĕkaṙ inarĕkan pinaṅkwakĕn,Aṅkĕn māsa kapat mahas mahas adoḥ sahaja majamahan karas tanaḥ,praŋ praŋ ciṇḍaga ketakī pracacaḥ akṣara salawas irâsiḥ iŋ ṭikā*109:1:673*

rakryan maṅsula māsku saŋ ratu kabeḥ muwaḥ ibu parananta waswasĕn,piŋ pat piŋ lima waspadākĕna raras nira waluyana haywa saṅśaya,yadyastun sira nora kāptya ni manaḥta muwaḥ uwahana ŋ swayambara,ṅkā ta dyaḥ t-aduluṙ pahuṙ hurakĕnanta sira lamakananta mantuka*109:2:674*

nāhan denya n amet prahelika laṅö rasa kakawin anambyakĕn manis,ndan simbantĕn adoha budđi nira maṅkin arumaḥ apulaŋ lawan smara,tan wruḥ ry-ambĕk irê narendrasuta yan sira winarahakĕn marêŋ laṅö,tan pendaḥ lara koluran turida rāga nira ri saŋ ajâwuwuḥ laṅö*109:3:675*

ndān ambĕk saŋ ajânahā sira ri budđya narapatisutā n tan ahyuna,Āpan tan huniṅê halĕp niŋ asĕkaṙ taji wĕdi mulatêŋ ajoŋ kuniŋ,tan hep hepĕn aniwya riŋ kadi sirâpi puji sinahuran patik haji,riŋ siṅhāsana saŋ katiṅgal aṅaraŋ paḍa lĕṅĕŋ aṅikĕt pralāpita*109:4:676*

Aṅlampū saŋ ajânahĕn turida māry-amalaṙ i harĕpā suputrikā,Āpan tan ratu liŋ nirêry-awak ira praƀu tuwi sira tan kinahyunan,Enak riŋ wĕkasan manaḥ nira harĕp harĕpĕn amĕnaṅêŋ swayambara,molaḥ bāhu nirê tĕṅĕn marahakĕn ri pamĕnaṅa nirêŋ swayambara*109:5:677*

ṅkā n jātismara putrikâtutuṙ i rūpa saŋ aja ri sĕḍĕŋ nirâpsara,riŋ swaṙgga n pakurĕn lawan sira tuhun kapalaŋ alaŋ i tan siḥ iŋ wiđi,maṅke pwa n paḍa janma mānuṣa sirâtutuṙ i siliḥ asiḥ nirâlawas,wruḥ meraŋ kadi tan priyâpriya ri kāla nira n atĕmu riŋ surālaya*109:6:678*

kāla śrîndumatī kapāśa tĕkap iŋ lara turida ḍinaṇḍan iŋ smara,rāgâṅaṇḍĕhi sāhasâmarĕpĕki twas ira rasa kapatya riŋ saƀā,yekā hetu nira n harĕp marĕka riŋ nrĕpatanaya palaṙ sirâsiha,Āpan yogya pakāśrayan saꝑala paṅgajaha maḍĕmana ŋ smarānala*109:7:679*

ratnânopama candrasūṙyyaja kaluŋ kaluŋ ira naranāŧaputrikā,yêka n pawwat irê narendrasuta rāgapahula sumĕnö marê muꝁa,Embuḥ teja nikā sĕḍĕŋnya kinaluŋ kaluṅakĕn ira riŋ nrĕpātmaja,lwiṙ dewī ratiḥ aṅhyasi smara sira n paṅamĕṙ aṅĕnakĕn kaluŋ kaluŋ*109:8:680*

<jagadnāŧa>:110

^nrĕpātmaja mulat ry-awak nira suꝁâmbĕk ira n amĕnaŋ iŋ swayambara,paḍâṅrahati cakṣuṙ ādi nira moliḥ i turida narendraputrikā,tĕkê muꝁa nirâpriḥ oliḥ inusap hariṅĕt ira tumus tĕkê jaja,ginañjaṙ ira riŋ sĕrĕḥ waja nirâsĕmu sĕmu guyu saƀya riŋ saƀā*110:1:681*

para praƀu sirâlarâlaḥ arĕbut ri turida naranāŧaputrikā,paḍânĕsĕl awak nirâlaraŋ anaṇḍaŋ inucap ira duṙyyaśapraƀu,gĕluŋ nira rusak mure n inalapan makuṭa nira katon paḍâkucĕm,tiḍĕm waja nirâsamun mari lumöŋ hinilan ira sĕrĕḥ mĕṅĕs mĕṅĕs*110:2:682*

<girisa>:111 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^hĕnĕṅakĕna narendra śrī putrī sira caritan,muliḥ aṅalihi ḍampâwās de niŋ mulat i sira,paḍa suꝁa paḍa haṙṣânĕmwākĕn kaharĕp ira,patĕmu nira winaswās dewī dèwa piniturun*111:1:683*

kaka kaka nira mantĕn denyâpet wulat amanis,Akusikan apĕgâpriḥ yan lampaḥ paḍa balisaḥ,siliḥ usap i muꝁâpan rūkṣa glāna hariṅĕtĕn,wuwuḥ i hayu nikâṅhiŋ tiṅhalnyârĕṅu n ahuyaŋ*111:2:684*

paḍahi paḍa gumĕntĕṙ muny-asraŋ sraṅan i harĕp,grĕbĕg i laku nikaŋ wwaŋ sāmānyâṅiriŋ adulur,ri harĕp i wuri lumrā sakweḥ niŋ para pajurit,saha curiga karĕsrĕs maṅrakṣê nrĕpatanaya*111:3:685*

ri tĕka nira maluṅguḥ riŋ paṙyyaṅka maṇimaya,kaka kaka para guṇḍik muṅgw-î soṙ paḍa humarĕp,kadi talaga patīṙŧan sakweḥ niŋ marĕk apupul,nrĕpasuta nrĕpaputrī tan pendaḥ kumuda mĕkar*111:4:686*

tucapa ta para taṇḍa n tan sŧity-âkuṭa kaṭikan,pijĕṙ aṅarahakĕn wwaŋ siŋ yogyâṅatĕṙ atĕra,hana sira wiku wrĕdđācārī motus atawura,Amilihi śuƀasaṅjñā mwaŋ saŋ wruḥ wruḥ atawura*111:5:687*

sĕḍĕŋ atawuṙ ahosan ginyākĕn sira huwusa,curiŋ amarĕṅi ǥaṇṭârūm lālitya tan asarag,paḍahi niŋ atawuṙ śabdanyâraśmi puja pujān,mahuwusan i huwus niŋ pañcabrahma kinĕnakĕn*111:6:688*

tĕlas ika ginuwantĕn śudđa ŋ mūla patawuran,śarawa kalaśa lāwan śrāntimrĕt paḍa sumaji,ǥaṭa kanaka wawan tīṙŧâtiṅkaḥ marĕk atatā,paḍa hana pinalaṅkan salwiṙ niŋ saji humaḍaŋ*111:7:689*

huwus asaji pari rwaŋ saṅǥâṙppat saha pipisan,pasikĕpan ika tan saḥ soṅgwan mwaŋ hapit ajajar,saŋ aja sira maluṅguḥ ṅkāna mwaŋ nrĕpaduhitā,sĕmu ni manaḥ irêraŋ yan tuṅkul baṅun aṅurit*111:8:690*

wiđi nrĕpati paṅajyan dewī maṅdyusa ri sira,nrĕpatanaya lawan śrī dewī śudđa manaḥ ira,ndan i huwus ira dinyus dyus pahyas nira kumĕñar,kadi salaga kalahrwan mĕmbaŋ wāhu kajawuhan*111:9:691*

nrĕpawaraduhitâdan siñjaŋ wāhu sinalinan,tapiḥ ira katutuṅkul maṅde tuṅkula saŋ aja,dumadak amuharâśrī siŋ dodot nrĕpatanaya,siliḥ asiha nirâṅhiŋ don iŋ wastra siliḥ asiḥ*111:10:692*

Aŧa ri huwus irâhyas prāpta mpuṅkw-aṅarahakĕn,sira tumuluy adandan sakweḥ niŋ marĕk aṅiriŋ,I lari nira cumuṇḍuk riŋ dewagrĕha madulur,dwijawara sira masyaŋ tan sāhê hiriṅan ira*111:11:693*

huwus ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ tapwan wanwa siliḥ asiḥ,siniwikaraṇa de saŋ paṇḍya brāhmaṇa matuha,saŋ amawa kuśapāśâṅgyākĕn mādĕga ri sira,kadi mĕbĕda sira n tan sāhâtĕmwa siliḥ asiḥ*111:12:694*

ri sĕḍĕŋ ira tinuntun de saŋ brāhmaṇa ri harĕp,kumuliliṅi ƀaṭārâgni mwaŋ kāsiḥ ira tumūt,dwijawara paḍa saśrī masraŋ weda nira humuŋ,Aƀinawa kadi kumbaŋ moliḥ kĕmbaŋ iŋ asana*111:13:695*

hyaŋ anala suꝁa haṙṣa n ton saŋ rwâṅidĕri sira,dilaḥ ira paṅadeśan tan suṇḍe malad aṅadĕg,nrĕpawaraduhitâgyaŋ mogânoliḥ i saŋ aja,sĕmu ni wulat irâjaṙ yan piŋ sapta sira midĕr*111:14:696*

muwaḥ ajajaṙ aluṅguḥ kāliḥ kāliḥ ira marĕk,kĕtĕṙ i taṅan ira n wahw-âpāṇigraha rumaras,paḍa parĕŋ anibākĕn pūṙṇnāhūti saha samit,śiwa sakala ƀaṭārâgni n sākṣī niŋ awiwaha*111:15:697*

<waṅśasŧa>:112 
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏓ = 12

^huwus mamūjā ri ƀaṭāra pāwaka,parĕŋ sirânĕmbaḥ inastwakĕn jaya,lawan sawīja n siniwi n jayêŋ raṇa,muwaḥ pratiṣṫênaƀiwāda śāśwata*112:1:698*

śinaṅꝁapāṇyan sira de mahādwija,muwaḥ mahāpaṇḍita śꜽwa sogata,maśaṅꝁapāṇî sira len mahāguru,huwus wineḥ uttamadāna de haji*112:2:699*

mijil suputrī kalawan nrĕpātmaja,paḍâpatĕmwan wulat esi manmaŧa,harĕp gumuywa nrĕpaputrikâwiraŋ,tumuṅku tuṅkul matukup tukup tutuk*112:3:700*

marĕk wruḥ ī tiṅkaḥ ikaŋ pasaṅgrahan,hatĕp nikaŋ ḍampa wineḥ sumiṅhita,narendraputrâṅgĕnĕṅî suputrikā,parĕŋ manuṅgaŋ wĕkasan paḍâraras*112:4:701*

sĕkaṙ taji śrī naranāŧaputrikā,tiliŋ kagiṅgaŋ kalawan tutup gĕluŋ,narendraputrâmahajĕŋ sakê wuri,Anĕmwakĕn leśya suꝁâṅharas pipi*112:5:702*

Alakwa lakwan paripūṙṇna riŋ halĕp,tabaŋ tabaŋ rāmya karĕṅw-awaṅsulan,kiduŋ kinaṅsyan murawanya tan humuŋ,lalitya tan kaṙkkaśa saŋsayâraras*112:6:703*

mrĕdaṅga sāmpun sumĕneha paṅruhun,hanâtĕkap len sinameni riŋ kiduŋ,ṇḍĕk ĕṇḍĕkan prāya ni de nikā muni,lĕṅĕŋ karĕṅw-âsĕmu paṅgyat iŋ jawuḥ*112:7:704*

payuŋ putiḥ rwa-rwa manimbaṅî sira,parĕŋ lumampaḥ tan adoḥ paḍâṅadĕg,pujut lawan jĕṅgi rarâmawâhirĕŋ,baṅun graha rwa rwa paḍâṅgayaṙ wulan*112:8:705*

<girisa>:113 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^ri huwus ira tĕkêŋ paprāsan bwat suranagara,sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ ƀakty-âṅañjali ri sira,pasaji ri sira hampyal dantâśrī sira n apupul,kadi surapati saṅkêŋ swaṙgga mwaŋ suramahiṣī*113:1:706*

tucapa halĕp ikaŋ paprāsan dug sira winaraŋ,kadi humarasa wimba hyaŋ candrāṙkka winulatan,tĕka riŋ alun alun söḥ luṅsiṙ baŋ hinatĕpakĕn,paḍa kadi gunuŋ āpuy muntab de niŋ aṅin adrĕs*113:2:707*

rasa bubula tĕṅaḥ niŋ rājyâpan paḍa gumĕrĕḥ,para ratu saha gĕṇḍiŋ goŋ rojeḥ tabĕ tabĕhan,Apituwi para taṇḍâsraṅsāṅan midĕṙ aritan,saha paḍahi gumĕntĕṙ lagy-atry-âsurak aṅawat*113:3:708*

para widu sĕḍĕŋ aywan saŋ taṅkil hyaŋ acarita,paḍa gumuyu kapūhan sakweḥ niŋ widu binisa,hana kawatĕk ujaṙnya n guyw-âwaṙṇna macarita,Uḍuḥ uḍuḥ uḍuḥ āḥ āḥ hā hā hāḥ bisa dahatĕn*113:4:709*

sahana niŋ abañol denyâṅguywākĕna puraci,Aṅigĕl igĕl agĕŋ göṅan koṇṭol paḍa mĕtĕtĕŋ,wĕlu sakĕbĕḥ agasyak ndan mogâwĕdi wĕkasan,kaguyu guyu kagöman yan prāpta ŋ wĕlu sabaṭaŋ*113:5:710*

pirus amirusi menmen denyâmet pacĕḥ acĕmĕḥ,rabi nika bisa pantĕs denyâƀāwaka maṅĕyĕḥ,laki nika mulat aṅdrĕŋ kahyun hyūn aṅuṅas uṅas,kadi wĕḍus anut añjyan yan tĕṅhā tĕka muriṅis*113:6:711*

Ikaŋ amacaṅaḥ oliḥ guyw-apriḥ paḍa sinurak,tĕkap ika nini niny-elik maswāmi wĕrĕ wĕrĕḥ,paḍa bisa ŋ awayaŋ wwaŋ denyâṅguywakĕn atarik,pacĕḥ ika kaki kaky-akrak ginyat muliḥ akusa*113:7:712*

sahana nika pinaṅguŋ tūt padw-âƀinawa katon,paḍa gumuruḥ awantus sakweḥ niŋ guyu gumĕtĕr,bari bari kapacĕḥ niŋ wwaŋ ŧāni n gumuyu kĕkĕl,patĕmu ni pasurak niŋ wwaŋ kady-ampuhan apagut*113:8:713*

Atali tali kakulwan loṙnyârĕṅgiṅan ajajar,rasa ḍawuha tĕkapnya n lumpat lumpat api tibā,milu milu para raṇḍânonton dan paḍa gigirĕn,paḍa sinurak i lumpatnya n kālaḥ paḍa kawalik*113:9:714*

Amĕnuhi nagara ŋ wwaŋ ŧāny-akweḥ madulu dulur,winijilakĕn ikâsiŋ saṇḍaŋ saṇḍaṅan ika mās,wijaḥ amĕli ḍaḍaŋ saṅgiŋ calwan saha kurupuk,Anak ika suꝁa de niŋ tumpi mwaŋ gaja gajahan*113:10:715*

hana sira wiku saṅkêŋ haryāhâlĕpiṙ acĕpuḥ,kasutapan ira maṅde kweḥ niŋ śiṣya paḍa marĕk,tuhun ulaḥ ira pĕñcul siŋ siŋ ƀāwa nira kiṭuŋ,siŋ ucapan ira baṅsit yêkī śabda nira rĕṅön*113:11:716*

ra tapa laki kapūhan wahw-ânon nagarasaƀā,Aƀinawa mulat iŋ ƀogâtyantâmuhara suꝁa,kalĕwi lĕwiḥ ikaŋ kory-alwâgöŋ gupura nikā,nrĕpati tĕka salumbuŋ riṅgi ṅgānya tiniwikan*113:12:717*

nahan ucapan ira wwantĕn têkā titiṙ ataña,paḍa karika ŋ ujaṙ köto mwaŋ kori hayu nipun,kalawan ujaṙ anĕṅgaḥ kāri mwaŋ kari liŋ ikā,sira sumahuṙ agampil mruḥ mruḥ maṅhawag aṅucap*113:13:718*

kṣamakĕna bapa dentâtakwan yogya tan ahala,tumañakĕn ikanaŋ kori mwaŋ kori pariƀaṣa,paḍa bapa wĕnaŋ aṅgon yan tuṅgal taliṅa gajaḥ,kalawan ujaṙ adigra mwaŋ tan padriga rahayu*113:14:719*

nahan ujaṙ ira baṅsit baṅsit tan ya cala nira,sahana hana nikaŋ wwaŋ ŧāny-atwaŋ mulati sira,tapa tapa nira pĕñcul wwaŋ wwaŋ sākṣara maṅucap,milu milu ta ya baṅsit ndan twaŋnyê sira liŋ ikā*113:15:720*

hĕnĕṅakĕna saŋ aṅdon tontonan sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg,waluyana caritan śrī putrī mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya,ndan i huwus ira pinrasprās mantuk mara ri dalĕm,gĕrĕḥ ikaŋ arĕbut prasprāsan maṅgyat adadakan*113:16:721*

kunaŋ ikaŋ arĕbut penī penī hana ri ruhur,Uliḥ ika paḍa mūlyâpan wastrâhayu saꝑala,binĕbĕdakĕn ikâkweḥ len muṅgw-iŋ cĕṅĕl i gulū,hilaŋ i cĕṅĕl ikê soṙ mwaŋ dodot nika karĕbut*113:17:722*

nda tucapa para nāŧân sāmpun kewwan ira kabeḥ,paḍa mamaluyakĕn mās lāwan wastra pamisalin,saha manis iŋ ujaṙ ndan liśya n pawwata pahula,muliḥ i huwus irâmwit duḥkâsĕṅhit i saŋ aja*113:18:723*

muwaḥ ucapakĕna śrī putrī mwaŋ nrĕpatanaya,saŋ amaraŋ i sira strī strī wrĕdđā pitu ŋ abuyut,tuwi kadaŋ ira tan len riŋ sajñâhayu manulus,Atuha tuha tinuṅgal sakweḥ niŋ marĕk i sira*113:19:724*

^bwat kāmeśwara ratna nīla winaṅun grĕha linaraṅan iŋ huwus praƀu,lwiṙ padmâsana siṅha rūpa ni sakanya kumĕñaṙ abirū paḍâkiris,kasraŋ de ni sĕnö nikaŋ kanaka paṅhatĕp apituwi söḥ mađubrata,sākṣāt rātri winĕtwan iŋ wulan awā linĕṅĕṅakĕn i śabda niŋ cucur*114:1:725*

ṅkā dewī winaraŋ lawan saŋ aja māṙ hati nira rumaras paḍâwĕnĕs,ry-antuk saŋ mamaraŋ maraŋ ri sira kāri sira kadi mađubratâsana,maṅke pwa n tumĕmu ŋ prayojana ni rāga nira malawas aṅhiḍĕp smara,kady-âṅipy-aṅisapwakĕn wulan awâmbĕk ira n aṅisapu nrĕpātmajā*114:2:726*

śrī dewîndumatī miṅe tan anumoda ri palaku ŋ asiḥ nrĕpātmaja,heman luḥ nira maṅlĕtuḥ lĕtuhi soca nira kadi saroja kābunan,moǥanya pwa mayat mayat halis irârĕṅu rĕṅu kaharas wawaŋ tikĕl,tan pātmā kinisapwakĕn twas ira tan pajajamuga rĕmĕk sakê taṅan*114:3:727*

^lĕŋlĕŋ niŋ lod lĕyĕp niŋ wukiṙ inayu papaṅgiḥ nirârok piniṇḍa,kālaṅkyaŋ mwaŋ rĕrĕb waṙṇna nira kadi liraŋ kāmukan saṅhub awrā,himpĕṙ saŋ hyaŋ śaśī kĕmbaṙ apupul akĕmul truḥ truḥ iŋ kāla sanđyā,dewī dewâṙdđanārīśwara patĕmu nira lwiṙ ṭikâkarwa karwan*115:1:728*

saŋ kady-ânaṅga māry-âtanu mijil atĕmaḥ rājaputrâdwitīya,maṙmmâpet siḥ tan imbâmĕkul aṅamĕṙ amĕṙ cumbu cumbw-âṅalap sor,sotan ta ŋ wwaŋ riris kāṅinan apĕnĕd arūm paṅhilaŋ rāgabahni,pömpöman rāsika lwiṙ nira paliḍaḥ iŋ elik miṅe riŋ kisapwan*115:2:729*

mambö sub niŋ smarâṅde huyaŋ i hati nirâwaṙṣiḥ apriḥ rasanya,sumyuk taŋ rāgawaṙṣâṅapitu makĕcĕhan lagy-awantö raras twas,Atruḥ truḥ haṙṣacittâmarupuhi turidâwaḥ wahan sanmatâgöŋ,trĕṣṇâṅumbaŋ lawan siḥ manis iŋ ujaṙ arūm saŋsayâdrĕs hilīnya*115:3:730*

^saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ ni laṅöku māwak aśarīra mĕtu ri paṅaweśa niŋ smara,lwiṙ dewī sakalânurun bĕsuṙ i rāmya niŋ amĕŋ amĕŋ iŋ surālaya,lakṣmī niŋ nagarī turuŋ matĕmahan karika kita wiśāta lālana,saŋ sākṣāt pratimâṅaraŋ hulun anugrahana tariman aṅharas pipi*116:1:731*

ṅūnî kāla nikaŋ swayambara mijil kita kadi wijil iŋ niśākara,sakweḥ saŋ pininaŋ praƀāwa nira söḥ murub aṅabaṙ abaṙ tĕkêŋ laṅit,rākantânwam alĕk taŧāpi kita haṙṣa tan aharĕp i wīṙyya saŋ praƀu,göŋ niŋ priḥku lawan siḥ iŋ hyaŋ aṅiriŋ ri ḍawuḥ i turidanta ri ṅhulun*116:2:732*

maṅke muṅgaḥ apöm waliṅku ta kataṅgamaṅakĕna pamaṅku ni ṅhulun,seṅĕṙku n dinĕlö ndatan tinarimâṅusapi hariṅĕt i wwit iŋ susu,dentâhyun kadi guywa guywan iŋ apa n rĕsĕpa pisaniṅū tĕkê hati,siŋ solaḥku sinikwakĕnta tinĕpak hana tinama rare pinīḍana*116:3:733*

nāhan de nrĕpaputra haṙṣa maṅĕnākĕn ucapan amanis priyambada,Aṅluṅlūṅi laṅö hanan pakakawin kakawin aṅarĕki nrĕpātmajā,mogâtön aṅusap jajâṅĕluk ĕluk lĕṅĕn araras amaṭya maṭyani,pet pet rāga mamanwa manwa mamĕpĕṙ mĕpĕṙ ataña ri mūlya niŋ tapiḥ*116:4:734*

^śrîndumatī kakĕnan wiṣa niŋ ujaṙ arūm sumusuk ri hati,ndan kadi tan huniṅā pawulatan ira moǥa mahâpi hade,rwā ŋ katahā n uduhĕn brituha wilaja hetu nirâpi tulak,rāga nirâṅulanĕḥ tuhun awĕdi kawĕs riŋ ulaḥ kawawa*117:1:735*

maṙmma nirâwri lanâkiput awĕdi kasiṅkaba siñjaŋ ira,tan huniṅan tinañan lara ni wĕtu ni luḥ nira niṣkaraṇa,nora waneḥ paran iŋ manaḥ apĕga kumöl winisik wisikan,ṅhiŋ panamantara ri sru saŋ aja winiweka nirê twas ira*117:2:736*

sāma paran wĕnaṅânulaka ri pamĕkulnya tan eraŋ amĕl,dāna paran ta kunaŋ wĕnaŋ anuculanê paṅagĕmnya tapiḥ,ƀeda paran wĕnaṅanya kumawaśakĕna bwat i rāga nira,daṇḍa jugênaka liŋ nira nĕhĕṙ anĕpak jaja sāhasika*117:3:737*

kāla nira n panĕpak taṅan ira kadi pādapa molaḥ alon,mambĕt ikaŋ luṅayan kadi lurus iŋ aśoka tinūb niŋ aṅin,tiṅhal irârĕṅu moǥa kadi sarasijê tĕka niŋ ƀramara,suṅsut irê nrĕpaputra hana kadi gula drawa de niŋ ĕbun*117:4:738*

^Ꜽ koŋ ƀrānta kasop i luḥ niŋ aṅaraŋ kasarik i laṭi niŋ wineḥ sĕpaḥ,lĕŋlĕŋ denta mulat piliḥ winawa niŋ turida sinaput iŋ hyaŋ iŋ ṭikā,rūm niŋ śabda mameka sambĕt i gĕluŋ kari kita pati jumput jumputi,dentâṅol midĕṙ iŋ tĕṅaḥ kapana yan warasa kadi panumpal iŋ smara*118:1:739*

siṅgiḥ ƀrānta kakanta māsku mapa don iŋ aṅasag inawenta lĕŋlĕŋa,twaskw-apriḥ binĕbĕdta riŋ tali gĕluŋ cinucuk i luṅid iŋ matâluru,mogâṅde wulaṅun manista rinasan tuhu tuhu n agĕlaŋ gĕlaŋ kuniŋ,ṅhiŋ yan rakryan aṅastwa riŋ luḥ uwatanya marasana ri rāga ni ṅhulun*118:2:740*

pintĕn māsku wuyuŋta tan hana waneḥ pinalaṙ asiha sanmatêŋ akuŋ,cĕp tênduŋ taha tan taṅis kaharĕp i ṅhulun aṅisapu jöŋta sewaka,luhtâdrĕs humilī pasuŋta karikā taham ibu tan ikā prayojana,Aṅhiŋ prāṙŧana moǥa sidđa katĕkāna siliḥ usapa luḥ lawan kita*118:3:741*

Intaṙ haywa marĕk paran karika donta paran iku kināṙyya niŋ marĕk,tan siḥ rāga nimitta niŋ taṅis adoḥ tiki kakĕnana kapriyambadan,lāwan tan suꝁa hetu niŋ luḥ aṅasapta ri mata tuwi tan gawe gawe,luḥ luḥ duḥka luḥ i ṅhulun taṅi taṅis prihati karaṇa niŋ lanânaṅis*118:4:742*

nāhan de nrĕpaputrikânulak i sāhasa saŋ aja saranta riŋ prĕman,tan paṅde wĕdi riŋ kĕdö marĕk aṅol nĕhĕṙ aṅarĕki de nirâṅucap,maṅkin haṙṣa rinĕṅwan aṅlalu kasuṅsutana saŋ aja saŋsayâwawuḥ,śrī putrī sira kāpĕsan ri panulak nira jaja wĕkasan sirânaṅis*118:5:743*

<nawahaṙṣa>:119

^Adawa n panukĕṙ saŋ ahayu kadi tuhwa nĕhĕṙ miṅaya,Anaṅis kadi tan patĕmahana lulut pwa ri suṅsut ira,Aṅĕsaḥ kadi tan siliḥ asiha mĕne ri huwus niŋ ulaḥ,Anulak ri sĕpaḥ nrĕpasuta kadi tan pamalakwa hĕlĕm*119:1:744*

Atukup taliṅâwĕdi katĕkana rūm niŋ ujaṙ kinire,susu tan winĕḍaṙ wĕḍaṙ awĕdi kakukwa ragĕt ragĕta,Akĕmul kĕmul epu ri pĕpĕsa ni mađya nira n pinĕkul,Asaput muꝁa kady-awĕdi hilaṅa rūm nira kārĕkana*119:2:745*

nrĕpaputra mamaṭyakĕn i manis ira n gula rāga rinok,ratus iŋ mađupaṙkka sira guliga niŋ lara haṙṣa pinöm,rinĕbut pinakesi ni mata niŋ akuŋ ri dalĕm nagara,papa de nira tan paṅaraṅakĕna tan panibākĕna luḥ*119:3:746*

lĕṅĕŋ iŋ mađumāsakusuma pinakaswaśarīra nira,paḍaŋ iŋ wulan aṅrahinakĕn alaṅö pinakāmbĕk ira,lumĕkas pwa sirâṅhari hari kadi kāṙttika raśmi nira,mĕtu kady-asirat sirata maṇik ujaṙ nira maṙmma dahat*119:4:747*

^strī niŋ śꜽwa tan eraŋ eraŋ aṅigĕl kaguyu guyu wĕrö wĕrö dawā,tan haṙṣêŋ swara niŋ mrĕdaṅga salukat ṅuni ṅuni yan i gīta niŋ waneḥ,hetunya n paṅiduŋ wijil niŋ ajiyaḥ sahuli huliḥ ikâṅrĕṅö rĕṅö,sahtote praŧamā kiduŋnya n aṅawat midĕm aṅujiwat ambahan tayoḥ*130:1:782*

^yogya wuwusta tuhun ṅhulun aharĕp aṅuṅsira wīṙyya guṇa,ndātan adoha sakêŋ ibu parĕkĕn apan sira māsiḥ anak,göŋ i kaƀaktin iŋ apraƀu maṅipulu ri twas akon muliha,ṅhiŋ kita māsku rumaṅkĕpana kahulunankw-i narāṙyya raǥu*133:1:791*

yan muliha prihawak ṅhulun ibu kita kāṙyya ri jöŋ nrĕpati,tiṅhali kāsihan iŋ huwus akurĕn asiḥ mara tambaṅana,yan waluyâku muwaḥ ri kita pira piraŋ tahunĕn ḍatĕṅa,ṅhiŋ panaṅisku lawan kita linalu ri dūra nikaŋ palagan*133:2:792*

^priya kahiḍĕp ujaṙttârūm kady-âmrĕta kasirat,kunĕŋ amuhara kepwan ry-ambĕk ni ṅhulun alawas,ya tan asiha kitânaṅsārâpujya tinutakĕn,syapa ta taṅisanaṅkwa ṅhiŋ matyânaṅisi tawaŋ*134:1:794*

ya ta karaṇa niŋ aswī yan rakryan jĕnĕka siwin,Iwĕḥ iŋ aniwi maṅheṙ siḥ niŋ hyaŋ ya ta tinahā,Atilara kita luṅhâtiṅgal wanwa n alalisa,ṅhiŋ anaṅisana ri śrī ƀoja mwaŋ nrĕpamahiṣī*134:2:795*

taham ibu taha rakryan maṙmmâsiḥ ṅhulun atuhan,saꝑala pinakadewī tan wwaŋ len kadaŋ aparĕk,sapati sahuripa ṅwaŋ sakwan selwan adulura,kita pinakahuripku n sekaprāṇa siliḥ asiḥ*134:3:796*

manis i wacana rakryan sāmpun kagraha ri hati,pinakapaṅanumānan ry-ambĕkta n tulus asiha,sapara parana rakryan ƀaktyâkw-âṅiriṅi kita,yadin anadina lampūn matyâśânuku riŋ awak*134:4:797*

ṅhulun ibu wihikan yan budđyantâwĕlas asiha,Ika karaṇa niŋ aswī māsku n rowaṅa muliha,nrĕpati raǥu katon gyā gyā ny-ambĕk nira mulata,niyata papagĕn iŋ strī sāyođyā n kita ḍatĕṅa*134:5:798*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:135 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^sāmpun māyu wuwus nrĕpātmaja lawan dewī nira n maṅkata,ṅkānê wwit niŋ aśoka rambay anaḍaḥ prāpta ŋ madaṅgâṅhaḍĕp,luṅhā ŋ kāla huwus hyaŋ aṙkka sumurup sanđyā masĕŋsĕŋ miraḥ,mambö kasturi niŋ paturwan araras kady-âṅutus mañjiṅa*135:1:799*

Ambĕk niŋ paḍa haṙṣa sāmpun amatĕḥ riŋ rāga soluṙ lulut,trĕṣṇêŋ saṅgama tan kawaṙṣihan apöm māywan raras riŋ prĕman,yan līlā mijil iŋ nataṙ pinanasan de niŋ smarâṅras hati,Oṅsil tuŋtuŋ ikaŋ halis jaruman aṅgyākĕn marā riŋ tilam*135:2:800*

sāmpun muṅgaḥ aṅanti riŋ pasamayan saŋ hyaŋ hyaŋ iŋ pamrĕman,maṙmmâsiḥ paḍa de nirâṅĕnahi rāga wruḥ ri tuṅgal nira,A-rwa-rwan manaḍaḥ manis niŋ upadeśâtyanta riŋ rāsika,nora ŋ saṅśaya riŋ rahasya winĕḍaṙ kāgĕm rasanyê hati*135:3:801*

saŋ raśmînayu niŋ smarâṅucap ucap riŋ pamrĕman tan bĕsur,sekaprāṇa sapakṣa tan wĕnaŋ adoḥ māsiḥ sađaṙmmâdulur,prajñêŋ budđi siliḥ wikalpa ri rusit niŋ śabda kady-âcĕṅil,paṅliṅganya n anak sināđya nira masw-aswâmiƀāwêŋ tilam*135:4:802*

<jagadnāŧa>:136 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^I sāmpun iŋ ulaḥ kapintiga nikaŋ ǥaṭita kawalĕsan sirâturū,Ikaŋ hulĕs adoḥ sakê sira lanā kawadal alulunan marêŋ dagan,hanan pawuṅu sakṣaṇâlĕḥ akaraŋ hulu taṅan aharip suputrikā,tapiḥ nira huwus lukaṙ kasarakat kahurup i basahan nrĕpātmaja*136:1:803*

huwus kalalu de nirâmrĕm asuwe paḍa tan umik aṅel asaṅgama,Ikaŋ manuk anaṅhi riŋ ḍawuḥ ĕnĕm suꝁa muni maṅuyūyu riŋ taman,cucuṙ taḍahasiḥ swaranya kawĕlas harĕp anaṅis i paṅlwaŋ iŋ wulan,Ikaŋ mrak akakab munîŋ gupura lagy-amuṅu ri sira riŋ ḍawuḥ pitu*136:2:804*

paḍâsraŋ aṅajîŋ kulĕm sahana niŋ manuk anarawatâguṇêriya,parañjaṅan aṅanti riŋ gagana paŧya tumiru tiru śabda niŋ pĕkiŋ,I soṙnya hana caṅkiluŋ muni laki stry-asĕmu mamarahi ry-anak nikā,syapêka ta kunaŋ paṅajyan ika maṅhuwusakĕn ika yan bisâṅaji*136:3:805*

Awuṅw-ajajaṙ iŋ surambyan arahup nrĕpatanaya lawan suputrikā,Anĕṅgaḥ atis aṅharas harasakĕn susu saŋ ahayu maṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ,kataṅgamaŋ aṅolakĕn saŋ aja maṙmma maṅĕmuli nĕhĕṙ mamaṅkwakĕn,pupū nira kasiṅgahan hulĕs i polaḥ ira kasuluhan niśākara*136:4:806*

samaṅkana ni göŋ i rāga nira kāliḥ aṅisapu lawan mamaṅkwakĕn,taŧāpi sinamantaran manis i de nira ṅucap araras prahāsana,saŋ adyaḥ api hewa hewa tuhun ambĕk ira tumiliŋ iŋ karāsikan,nrĕpātmaja mañumbu ñumbu mamibik tapiḥ aharĕp i buṅkaḥ iŋ tĕṅaḥ*136:5:807*

ri luṅsuṙ i tapiḥ nirârukĕt ikaŋ luṅayan asĕmu luṅgaḥ iŋ gaḍuŋ,Ikaŋ gĕlaŋ ataṅkis iŋ wĕtis apiṇḍa mađukara marâhyun iŋ puḍak,payođara lanâpipit kadi wĕdinya kaharasa ri tuŋtuŋ iŋ kuku,Ikaŋ muꝁa sawaŋ wulan marĕk i wimba nira sĕḍĕŋ ira n sapamrĕman*136:6:808*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:137

^maṅkin wrĕdđi wijil ni rāsika nira n pa-rwa-rwan iŋ pamrĕman,nidrâcumbana ta pwa nitya ginawe maṅde suꝁê twas nira,söṙ mambö waṅi niŋ sĕkaṙ kadi mahā mañjiŋ mamuṅw-î sira,tan wruḥ yan rahinâpaḍaŋ paḍa mijil de niŋ hrĕbuk niŋ puḍak*137:1:809*

<jagadnāŧa>:138 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^samantaji mijil hyaŋ aṙkka kadi raktakumuda sumĕkaṙ sakêŋ bañu,wulan mari lumöŋ kagöṅan ahulap sumirĕp awĕdi tan wĕnaŋ mulat,tĕkêŋ grahagaṇânusup nusup arĕs karahinana humöt paḍâkucĕm,Ikaŋ wĕṅi huwus paḍĕm kadi hilaŋ pinĕjahan ira riŋ ḍawuḥ wwalu*138:1:810*

Ikaŋ ƀuwana kālapan wĕṅi baṅun jalađi karaŋ asat ḍasaṙ nika,katon awas ikaŋ gunuŋ kadi timiṅgila makatihalaŋ paḍâṅjĕlag,Urut saka satal kumĕṇḍĕŋ ajajaṙ paḍa paḍa kadi nāga maṅlayaŋ,muni ŋ jalada maṅrĕguŋ sagajamīna kasatan aṅuliŋ harĕp bañu*138:2:811*

<puṣpacāpa>:139 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 20

^ri wwit niŋ kayu pārijāta hana tīṙŧâlantaran wwad kucuṙnya,tūsanyânalagâjajaṙ watu karaŋnyâgroŋ rinoŋ pañcuranya,tampyak tampyakan iŋ wĕrĕḥ pamarigi lwiṙnya n patap de nikaŋ ṙyyak,wwꜽnyâƀrā kadi saṙwwawaṙṇna ri sĕḍĕŋ niŋ puṣpamāyā hanê jro*139:1:812*

ṅkā dewī marahup rahup sira yaŧālīlâṅuḍoḍâñawuk wwꜽ,tan saḥ śrī naranāŧaputra maṅĕmit lwiṙ kumbaŋ aṅrakṣa kĕmbaŋ,wruḥ riŋ cāmana pītrĕtaṙppaṇa satiṅkaḥ tiṅkaḥ iŋ tīṙŧayātra,mādĕg pūṙwwamuꝁâjajaṙ parĕŋ amūjâṅañjalî saŋ hyaŋ aṙkka*139:2:813*

<śāṙddūlawikrīḍita>:140 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | – – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^mantuk śīǥra marê dalĕm humatuṙ i śrī ƀoja riŋ pamrĕman,Akweḥ strī haji samƀramê tĕka nirâganty-âṅucap gaṙjjita,maṙmma śrī parameśwarī mulat anuṅsuŋ cumbu cumbw-âṅucap,Ī Ī śrī maṇik i ṅhulun sira ḍatĕŋ kāliḥ nihan liŋ nira*140:1:814*

śrī dewîndumatī parĕŋ sira manĕmbaḥ mwaŋ narāṙyyātmaja,riŋ lampit hana siṅhacaṙmma humaḍaŋ kāna n pratiṣṫârarĕm,saŋ nāŧa wruḥ i don ira n para wawaŋ śoka drawa twas nira,Amwit sādara sopacāra saŋ ajânĕmbaḥ ri jöŋ saŋ praƀu*140:2:815*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ>:141 
– – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^sĕmbaḥ niŋ aśaraṇa ri jöŋ narendra huniṅan parĕk i narapati,Amwīta muliha satatâṅriwĕg riwĕgi tan bĕsuṙ amaribini,tan sĕṅgahĕn akalis i pāda saŋ praƀu pasaŋ kuhira pinahayu,paṅgil wĕnaṅa dadaha riŋ raṇâṅharĕpa śatrukula yan iŋ ayun*141:1:816*

Om wruḥ ṅhulun ika mara hetu niŋ kahĕnĕṅan kapĕgan aṅucapa,māsiḥ ṅhulun iri kita moǥa tan wĕnaŋ asiḥ karaṇa niŋ asĕkĕl,maṅke n mulat iri kita tan palekan aṅĕḍap muliḥ analahasa,wahw-âpupul alal alawas tĕka pwa kita sakṣaṇa wawaŋ apasaḥ*141:2:817*

pintaṅkw-i kita bapa sihanta tan kapalaṅâmipila riŋ agati,saṅkan raray uwuḥ uwuḥ ūpamānĕn iŋ ulaḥ kasiḥ arĕp alawas,maṅke n marĕk iri kita sanmatan kawiguṇanya tan ucap ucapĕn,Aṅhiŋ pakadaṅan i bapaṅku tolihĕn i māsku laki pakatalin*141:3:818*

nwam ny-ambĕk ika mĕṅĕ mĕṅö kalotakĕna denta kajugulan ikā,tan wruḥnya riŋ aṅinakanê mulat pipili denta pituturi piṅit,saŋkṣepa nika kita waśa pramāṇa guṇadoṣa nika wawarĕṅöḥ,yadyastun iwĕŋ iwĕṅa riŋ hulun bapa manaḥnya palu palu waraḥ*141:4:819*

Atwaŋ saŋ aja sumahuṙ apraṇamya rumuhun saha manis iŋ ujar,Ājñā nrĕpati rasa nirâwĕkas wĕkas akon siliḥ asiha sadā,sāmpun karĕgĕp i hati de patik haji minuṣṭi maṅinaki hati,ṅhiŋ gānya n apasaha ri tan siḥ iŋ wiđi harĕp mulata riŋ alara*141:5:820*

Atyanta hĕla hĕla niŋ aṅrĕṅö wacana rakryan aṅinaki hati,niṙwiǥna kita bapa tĕkêŋ sināđya wĕnaŋ uṅsirĕn iŋ aśaraṇa,śānti dwijawara ri bapaṅku kesyana tumirw-a narapati raǥu,swasty-astu saha tanaya dāra māsku saŋ anĕmwa jayaꝑala sadā*141:6:821*

mwaŋ yan pawuwuha kita ǥāra pat lima sujanma wĕka wĕka ratu,tan doṣa tumĕkakĕna sāmbĕk iŋ wĕnaŋ amukti wiṣaya saꝑala,ndan haywa sira ta bapa kāri denta pakamaṅgala niŋ anakĕbi,yogya n kalĕwihakĕna tan paḍan ꝑala nikâṅurati kahulunan*141:7:822*

tĕmbe ŋ śuƀadiwasa bapaṅku maṅkata kakanta maṅatĕrakĕna,jyotīṣa paḍa tinañan i ṅhulun wiṅi ri kāla nira paḍa marĕk,Awyāhata pawaraḥ irâpadohan atukaṙ paḍa kamasĕṅĕrĕn,saŋ lekan aṅucap apagĕḥ tuwin binisa kāraṇa niŋ amituhu*141:8:823*

yêkī muwaḥ ucapakĕnê bapaṅku sahajâlupa kamituturĕn,dūmĕn sahana hana ni drĕwya drĕwya haji dewata tĕka tĕkanĕn,lāwan sahana hana nikaŋ rare kawula rakryan aṅalapa muwaḥ,yadyan jĕnĕka kita bapaṅku pālihĕn ikaŋ nagara kaliliran*141:9:824*

nāhan paṅucap ucap ira lwiṙ amrĕta hañaṙ mĕtu siniratakĕn,maṅdadyakĕn i suꝁa narendraputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā,kesyan rasa ni manis i de nirâṅucap arūm asĕmu gula siṅī,ƀeda mwaŋ ujaṙ amanis iŋ pralāpita namun rĕcĕpa rasa nikā*141:10:825*

kañcit paḍa tĕka maduluṙ sirêŋ pagaḍuhan marĕk i narapati,sakweḥ ni kĕmitan ika mās maṇik pirak ikā ya tinañakĕn ira,yêka n pamaca padadaran tĕlas pwa ya samaṅkana winijalakĕn,kasraḥ satĕṅaḥ i naranāŧaputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā*141:11:826*

nantĕn samĕgĕt aniga muꝁya sāra ginulaŋ halu makĕmitana,mwaŋ drĕwya pahula naranāŧa sojaṙ i narendra paḍa sinuṅakĕn,lāwan muwaḥ anĕkakĕnêry-ayođyanagarī tumuta ri saŋ aja,Āpan wĕnaŋ akun iŋ ulaḥ prayatna wĕka sāđu wĕka niŋ aniga*141:12:827*

dum dūman ira pira kunaŋ wilaŋnya kadi tan kawĕnaṅa wilaṅĕn,yadyan banawa saha bahitra dūra wĕnaṅâmwata niyata sarat,muṅgw-iŋ raŧa pira pira taŋ raŧêŋ nagara hĕnti paḍa hinibĕkan,wastrādi pinada pinadāti pādadara tan wuruŋ apan adadar*141:13:828*

ndātan caritan ulaḥ irânaḍaḥ ri huwus iŋ wwalu wahu ḍumawuḥ,tan saḥ Uwa nira kalawan sirêña nira muꝁya niŋ aṅiriṅakĕn,sāmpun praṇata sira paḍâṅadĕg muliḥ i pamrĕman ira ri dalĕm,sakweḥ ni hulun ira kinon madandana paḍâgarawalan ataña*141:14:829*

dewī sira maṅutus aniṅka niṅkaḥ i sadrĕwya nira pinahayu,norâhala hala kalasā tinon kinajaṅan winalunan ahalĕp,Akweḥ papiku pikul irâpupul kawula dāsa kaliliran ira,boṇḍan sajuru lawan ikaŋ pujut sajuru jĕṅgi sajuru humaḍaŋ*141:15:830*

wyāpāra sahana hana niŋ wwaŋ iŋ nagara tan hana maṅinak inak,kady-âsawuṅan asipĕt olaḥ olaḥ adamaṙ damaṙ amalaku duḥ,ceṭī rumara rara paḍâṅasū wija wijaḥ dudu taŋ amususi,siṅgoḥ ya humuŋ asahuran baṅun śakaṭa gumrit amuhara laṅö*141:16:831*

guṇḍik kaka kaka mawiweka pahyas ikaŋ endaha tan awanĕha,lagy-âminĕkĕti hayu tuṅgal ĕmbulana tan hana niŋ amihaṅa,ṅhiŋ raṇḍi dadaṙ ika kabeḥ kahaywakĕna don ika pinagĕhakĕn,denyâmahayu sipat ināptyakĕn pinakadaṙśśana tiniru tiru*141:17:832*

sāmpun ǥaṭita pitu tibā putiḥ timuṙ ikâwawa rahina mijil,Āƀā ni pawuṅu naranāŧaputra karĕṅö piliḥ anuculi ken,dewī kadi kahĕnĕkan asriŋ ambĕkan irâsahuran aṅĕsĕsan,Ākāra ni hĕnĕŋ ira meḥ tigaŋ paṅinaṅâwuṅu mijil adamu*141:18:833*

dewī sira pinahayu hinyasan pinahawās kadi maluya rarā,dūran wĕnaṅa paṅanumānanê huwus irâpriya luṅayan ira,lāwan mata waja nira tan wĕnaŋ pinakaliṅga ni pasawi nira,ṅhiŋ mājaṙ i huwus ira medĕman susu nirê kiwa kani kakuku*141:19:834*

<basantatilaka>:142 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^sāmpun sirâhyas asalin hima puṣpawaṙṣa,dodot narendrasuta rakwa kilat rinĕṅga,Āsĕṅka niŋ mulat i rūpa narendraputrī,putrī sakêŋ surapadânĕmu rājaputra*142:1:835*

prāsāda ratnamaya muṅgw-i dalĕm kaḍatwan,ḍaŋ hyaŋ purohita sirêniriŋ iŋ pamūjā,ǥaṇṭâlaṅö đwani nikā saha pūja pūjān,śaṅꝁa lwiṙ asyaŋ aṅuhuḥ ri narendraputra*142:2:836*

sāmpun ḍatĕŋ nrĕpatiputra lawan suputrī,ganđâkṣatādi humaḍaŋ kalawan niwedya,mañjiŋ sirê dalĕm aṅaṙppaṇakĕn pamūjā,Amwīt i wimba haji dewata ƀakty-anĕmbaḥ*142:3:837*

dewī sirâmĕkul i jöŋ nira saŋ hyaŋ aṙcca,Aṙṇnaḥ manaḥ nira sadâṅaku rāma rena,glānânaṅis kasiḥ arĕp twas ira wyamoha,sambat nirâmuhara luḥ pamĕlas harĕpnya*142:4:838*

Ꜽ rāma rena kita saŋ lumaḥ iŋ kaḍatwan,ṅūni n maṇusya kita karwa bapêbu liṅku,maṅke dadi hyaŋ inalĕmbana sāṙdđadeha,hā hāḥ yayā bapa hajîbu hajîki liṅku*142:5:839*

ndā t aṅrĕṅö bapa hajîbu hajî taṅisku,pamwitku tiṅhali sumambaḥ i pādukanta,Āḍā wĕkasku mulatî kita têki maṅke,rakṣan ṅhulun bapa hajîbu hajî paranku*142:6:840*

nāhan taṅis taṅis irâlara wāhu mantĕn,milw-ânaṅis nrĕpatiputra nĕhĕṙ tumuṅkul,lāwan hyaŋ aṙcca pakatonan irêpu winwit,de niŋ śiwāmƀa ri muꝁâsĕmu luḥ drawâdrĕs*142:7:841*

sāmpun mijil nrĕpatiputra lawan suputrī,prāptê narendra mahiṣī tumuluy sirâṅliŋ,kĕmbĕŋ ni luḥ nira panuṅsuŋ irê suputrī,de niŋ sĕkĕl sapaṅucap nira tan sꝑuṭâsrĕt*142:8:842*

māskw-îbu haywa kita tan praṇatā suƀakti,I swāmi rakryan apan uttamarājaputra,Āsiŋ sakahyun ira tūtakĕnanta māsku,yêkā patibrata ṅaranya pakabratanta*142:9:843*

mwaŋ haywa māsku paṅayāya karājaputryan,lāwan hayunta wiꝑala n pakapaṅhaḍanta,tan kweḥ ni māsta makapaṅgajahanta māsku,kakṣatriyanta maniwîbu pakātmarakṣa*142:10:844*

lāwan muwaḥ saŋ aja haywa bapaṅkw-atiṅgal,I śrī narendraduhitā paḍa wastu māsku,riŋ rūpa sampĕlaḥ awaṙṇna sĕkaṙ pināliḥ,prāṇanta tuṅgalakĕnanta maran tan imbā*142:11:845*

tan ketaka ŋ puḍak adoha ri ṣaṭpadanya,tan ṣaṭpada ŋ ƀramara sāha sakê puḍaknya,tan putrikā sarika yan taya rājaputra,tan rājaputra kita yan taya rājaputrī*142:12:846*

nā liŋ narendramahiṣī n panaṅis sumuṅkĕm,I śrī narendraduhitā pinĕkul siniṅsĕt,Akweḥ mulat kapitaṅis ri narendraputrī,Āpan wĕkas nira katon ri widaṙbƀarājya*142:13:847*

Embuḥ taṅis ri pataṅis taṅisan suputrī,de niŋ swawanđu nira söḥ atuluŋ bwat iŋ luḥ,prāptâmalandani pirak maṇi wastu mūlya,len taŋ sĕrĕḥ kinajaṅan saha modakādi*142:14:848*

<dođakawrĕtta>:143 
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏓ = 11

^śrī nrĕpaputra lawan nrĕpaputrī,Amwit anĕmbaḥ i jöŋ mahadewī,mary-ataṅis taṅisan paḍa līlā,śeṣa ni luḥ nira mātra kumĕmbĕŋ*143:1:849*

maṙmma dahat paṅucap mahadewī,Om bapa saŋ makapunpunana ŋ rāt,sora samāpta para praƀu denta,śrī raǥu māsku tirunta jayêŋ praŋ*143:2:850*

śrîndumatîbu huripku kitântĕn,moǥa katĕmwa suꝁanta dadi strī,rowaṅa rakryan ajâsisihan siḥ,tuṅgalĕn apriya riŋ nrĕpaputra*143:3:851*

sāmpun ira n paṅucap mahadewī,śrîndumatī kalawan nrĕpaputra,mādĕg inumbalan iŋ paricārī,maṅkat awaṙṇna śaśāṅka kameǥan*143:4:852*

kīṙṇna tikaŋ pamikul pikul akweḥ,denya lumampaḥ arampak apaṇṭa,nora jaruḥ wihikan ri duluṙnya,yogya katiṅhalanâpan atiṅkaḥ*143:5:853*

maṅkana taŋ raŧa nora kagiṇḍal,meww-iwu lampaḥ ikâdĕdĕṙ adrĕs,drĕwya narendrasutā winawanya,mās maṇi len rajatādi suwastra*143:6:854*

salwiṙ ikaŋ paḍahîŋ nagarâsraŋ,rāmya tĕkapnya hanan sinameni,len masarag makapaṅhaḍa göŋnya,lwiṙ kĕtug iŋ lĕwu denya gumĕntĕr*143:7:855*

śrîndumatī siwuhĕn sira luṅhā,de ni lulut nira riŋ nrĕpadewī,lūḥ ira tan pĕgat adrĕs awantu,śrī nrĕpaputra kaṅelan ameri*143:8:856*

muṅgw-irikaŋ kapiṅan sira kāliḥ,rāmya katonan irâpan awelā,lwiṙ kawĕlad twas ikaŋ wwaŋ aniñjo,ƀakti mamakpak aṅañjali māsiḥ*143:9:857*

maṙmma nira n mari sukṣĕka rañca,rūm saŋ ajâṅhari hary-aṅalap sor,mwaŋ jayawaspa wicakṣaṇa tan saḥ,māry-aputĕk sira rakwa tumon ya*143:10:858*

strī ri dalĕm nagarârĕja pantĕs,mātus atus paḍa maṙmma rarasnya,kocap anampikakĕn sĕkaṙ aṅjraḥ,milw-aṅiriŋ ri nareśwaraputrī*143:11:859*

kādƀuta lampaḥ iraŋ nrĕpaputrī,de ni halĕp para guṇḍik atiṅkaḥ,wastra nikā paḍa raṇḍi sapaṇṭa,lwiṙ kusumânĕḍĕŋ iŋ pratimāsa*143:12:860*

śrī naranāŧa tumūt saha mantrī,söḥ aṅiriŋ paḍa śūra wanîŋ praŋ,meww-iwu lakṣa sahasra kumĕṇḍĕŋ,lwiṙ paṅawak nikaŋ antaka sākṣāt*143:13:861*

śrī naranāŧasutā sira śoka,sis kamatolihĕn iŋ nrĕpadewī,wāhu lipuṙ tumuluy sira monaŋ,luḥ nira lāgi kumĕmbĕŋ asowe*143:14:862*

sāmpun ira n lĕpas iŋ kuṭa wetan,toliḥ ikaŋ nagarâsĕpi tistis,kaywan ikā manirâṅaway asriŋ,kady-aṅutus maluyê sira kāliḥ*143:15:863*

rāmya nikaŋ kahawan sawaḥ alwā,maṅdadi ƀasma daminya tinunwan,ṣaṭpada muṅgw-i sĕkaṙ ni wuruŋnya,lwiṙ kawi māsiḥ aǥāra daridra*143:16:864*

ndan sadawā ni hĕnū nira rāmya,sontĕn ikaŋ jawuḥ adrĕs asowe,śīǥra pucuk ni tĕkinya tumūwuḥ,waṙṇna nikā kadi campaka siṅsal*143:17:865*

<wisaṙjjita>:144 
– ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏓ = 20

^kīṙṇna katon wijil iŋ laru laru kumukus kadi tan lĕwasa,haṙṣa sirêña nira mwaŋ uwa nira riwönya katon aṅĕliḥ,mwaŋ para guṇḍik amupw-awurahan arĕbut paḍa budđi rare,śrîndumatī marĕk iŋ nrĕpasuta suꝁa haṙṣa sirâmawani*144:1:866*

hyaŋ rawi tumraŋ ikaŋ walaŋ aṅariŋ ariŋ makamūla ŋ atis,cumbw-i rabinya marĕk nĕhĕṙ aṅĕpĕṙ uninya karĕṅw-araras,strīnya kumöl inaras haras anarima solaḥ ulaḥ niŋ akuŋ,saŋ rwa mulat marĕn ahyun aṅalapa tumon i wilāsa nikā*144:2:867*

moǥa jĕnĕk sira de ni paṅaraman ikaŋ bañu wāhu ḍatĕŋ,katkat aliwran amet walaŋ asira siran kalawan dadali,Aṅlĕṅĕṅi twas irêka ta karaṇa nirâsrĕt alon lumaku,lālana lagy-anĕpĕṙ nĕpĕri sĕkaṙ arūm kadi mitra kadaŋ*144:3:868*

lampaḥ irâtut ayun tinutakĕn iŋ aṅin saha meǥa rĕmĕŋ,lwiṙ makadoṣa laṅö nira sahasa manĕmpal aśoka liman,hinrĕt i kĕmbaŋ ikaŋ gaḍuŋ anĕḍĕŋ analyani budđi nira,riŋ wĕkasan dinudut ni karas ira nimitta nira n lumaku*144:4:869*

lwaḥ laraṅan kahalintaṅan asat apirak pirakan gumĕlar,waḥ kayu mās ri tĕpinya salak apupul awwaḥ atöb anĕḍĕŋ,nista nika n sugiḥ iŋ kalĕṅĕṅan atĕṅö tuwi tan papaḍa,wwatnya katiṅgal adoḥ anĕmu maru hĕnū pamĕnĕṙ mĕnĕran*144:5:870*

piṅgiṙ ikaŋ pagagan harata hara hara n pamuraŋ muraṅan,luñcip ikaŋ rwi kulampis i pagĕṙ ika waṙṇna tanaḥ kinikir,wwaḥ ni saganya baṅun mata hañaṙ asipat pinuyuṙ puyuran,daŋdaṅan aṅgarit iŋ wĕtis aniru kuriñjĕm umuṅgw-i pipi*144:6:871*

sīma kawaṅśan alas juraŋ anasarakĕn sinĕpĕṙ sĕpĕran,saṅkawilanya mañaṇḍĕt i rusit i hĕnūnya lawan wadara,mĕṅgĕp arūm araras gaḍuŋ ika katĕkan tuha milw-amilĕt,budđi nikā wilut aṅduhuṅakĕn apituwy-aḍaḍap wwaŋ agöŋ*144:7:872*

<jagadnāŧa>:145 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^taṅeḥ yan ucapĕn kalaṅwan i hĕnū nira kadi nawanāṭya niŋ kawi,wimūṙcꞓa para guṇḍik aṅrĕṅi rĕṅiḥ para kaka kaka śoka kaṅlihan,katuhwan iŋ apa n tan apriha sukunya wahu lumaku lakw-adoḥ dahat,sirêña nira len uwā nira paḍâkĕsĕl awak ira muṅgu riŋ raŧa*145:1:873*

I tan wĕnaŋ ikā lumampaḥ awĕḍak suku binĕbĕd ikêŋ kajaṙ kajar,baṅun surawađū paḍâdarupa kady-anapaka gagana n tiniṅhalan,tuhun suꝁa manaḥnya riŋ wĕkasan eṅgal asĕmu guyu māri suṅkawa,Ikaŋ magiliṅan kajātaka paḍâmawa giliṅan inājña mamwata*145:2:874*

tigaŋ wĕṅi sirâṅinĕp nrĕpati mamwit i saŋ aja lawan nrĕpātmajā,I pāntaran ikaŋ wukiṙ hiṅan irâṅatĕrakĕn i nareśwarātmajā,maluy sira lawan gajâśwa raŧa tan hana hiḍĕp ira wanya wāđakā,narendratanayânaṅis nrĕpatiputra salahasa tumon kamānuṣan*145:3:875*

muwaḥ nrĕpatiputra maṅkat aṅusī pakulĕmana nira wwaŋ iŋ pasir,karaŋ karaṅan endaḥ endaḥ alaṅö hinaturakĕn ikā lawan sayub,paḍânrik aṅinum twak iŋ pasisi saŋ watĕk aja karuhun nrĕpātmaja,ƀaṭāra baruṇâṅaliḥ nagara rūpa nira wahu mijil sakêŋ tasik*145:4:876*

riŋ eñjiŋ i wijil hyaŋ aṙkka sira maṅkat aduluṙ ahawan gunuŋ gunuŋ,huwus tĕka sirêrikaŋ pĕkĕn agöŋ sĕḍĕŋ amĕpĕg ikaŋ wwaŋ iŋ pĕkĕn,Ikaŋ baṇija saṅśayânaha nahā ri patukara nareśwarātmaja,lawan sahana saŋ watĕk ratu kabeḥ rumĕbuta ri narendraputrikā*145:5:877*

mpu rāma humatuṙ marê saŋ aja sādara tĕkap ika mojaṙ aprĕgi,tuhanku bapa sugya tan wruha bapaṅku ri hana nira saŋ watĕk ratu,ry-uliḥ nira sakêŋ swayĕmbara paḍâpupul amarĕki deśa duṙggama,kunaŋ bapa panaṙkka naṙkka ni manĕḥta kadi rumĕbutê suputrikā*145:6:878*

putus mara lĕbā nikaŋ tĕgal ayun palapat alas alas gunuŋ gunuŋ,taŧāpi paḍa söḥ kinuwwan arupĕk wĕkasan asalĕsĕk tĕkêŋ juraŋ,dudū sawĕṅi saŋsayâwuwuḥ ikaŋ gaja raŧa saha sañjatâsinaŋ,mataŋnya bapa yatna yatna tuhan i ṅhulun apupula haywa wismrĕti*145:7:879*

nahan wuwus ikā nrĕpātmaja wawaŋ sumahuṙ asĕmu siṅha kātara,mpu rāma tak anāgatâkw-iriya yadyan awuwuha muwaḥ samaṅkana,muwaḥ yadin ameta dꜽtya saha dānawa pakaśaraṇanya riŋ raṇa,hade raǥusutâku tak sy-aja ṅaranya yak atakuta riŋ samaṅkana*145:8:880*

samantaji ḍatĕŋ hulun nrĕpatiputra sahana nikaŋ aṅruhun ruhun,kanin rujit awaknya maṅhaturakĕn śiraḥ apan arujit nĕhĕṙ murud,ya tâjaṙ i narendraputra saha cihna rĕsĕp i hati de nikâṅucap,Alap ta wus amaḥ nahan liŋ ikanaŋ wani wani karuhun nrĕpātmaja*145:9:881*

I sāmpun ira muṅgaḥ iŋ raŧa tumūt nrĕpawaraduhitā hanê wuri,pasaṅǥa ni surak watĕk raǥusutâmaji taliṅa nikaŋ wwaŋ aṅrĕṅö,linūd i kĕtug iŋ gubaṙ saha garantuŋ uni nika karĕṅw-aṅalw-alö,Ikaŋ wwaŋ apĕkĕn pĕkĕn gumuruḥ awrĕg inawaran i dūta niŋ musuḥ*145:10:882*

<meǥawitānā>:146 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏓ = 10

^tucapa ŋ kahawan paḍa yatna,wihikan ri manaḥ para nāŧa,sahasâṅrĕbutê nrĕpaputrī,saŋ aja prihĕn iŋ raṇamađya*146:1:883*

juru sāmya ḍatĕŋ paṅatagnya,I samāṅjuru len para duhwan,paḍa samƀrama maṙmma paḍâgya,Anabĕḥ kukulan makapĕṇṭok*146:2:884*

pamajânwam anaṇḍaŋ agasyak,wahu wahw-akurĕn paḍa māsiḥ,kamĕnanya lumakwa masaṇḍiŋ,hana budđi nikâmwit akāṙyya*146:3:885*

juru tuṅgul añumbw-i rabinya,Ibu puñcawali n pĕjaha ṅwaŋ,pĕraṅĕn ri jajaṅku kitântĕn,mila liŋ ni rabinya tan aṅgā*146:4:886*

widu milw-aharĕp tumutâpraŋ,wĕdi wĕdy-aṅabuk prawalanya,I hilaŋ ni galaḥnya salaḥ ṅgwan,tinañākĕn ikê pagaḍaynya*146:5:887*

saŋ ibu nya paran di galaḥku,hana riŋ paḍaṅan ya hikā ya,Aŋ usĕn laku t āsaḥ iri ŋ lwaḥ,mata maḥ laku he pira dohe*146:6:888*

ndi wahosku paran di wahosku,mbruta pet ndi pametana siŋ sī,syapa ta wruha takwanakĕn sī,Aḥ aḥ aḥ sy-apĕṅiŋ kadi wāni*146:7:889*

Alupâku paran pwa katiṅgal,ri sĕḍĕŋta siliḥ galaḥ oliḥ,kawĕkas ni wĕtis ni lawanta,si ḍulîka paṅenak uwanya*146:8:890*

Atutuṙ wĕkasan sy-aku maṅke,pañukilku hapū maḥ asaḥ ñen,mapa yan guruwindakĕnanta,paṅupaḥ tĕlu mās aḍug induŋ*146:9:891*

ndi juluk julukuṅku dalampat,hana riŋ lwaḥ anakta si maṅdyus,A dĕlit ny-anak iŋ wani riŋ praŋ,baribin pa ya tan tuhu hāḥ ñwak*146:10:892*

ndwa sĕrĕḥ ndi ta polihanaṅkwa,ndi pupuk ni hucu n kinaṅĕṅkwa,maḥ alap haḍug ību taluḥnya,ndwa kamal ḍiḍikan hibu rakryan*146:11:893*

laku t aṅkat amaḥ bĕkĕlanta,ndwa ta sī mapa liŋta malīya,ndwa ta sī mapa hāḥ hapi tan wruḥ,ndwa ta sī si putiḥ pisane wus*146:12:894*

ya tikā paṅucap si jarĕmpu,Aṅadĕg ya maṅundurakĕn wwaŋ,gumadā wĕsi têki galaḥnya,pinikulnya nĕhĕṙ mĕtu Ꜽg lĕs*146:13:895*

para sāmya paḍâprĕgi maṅkat,muni goŋnya lawan paḍahinya,saha sañjata söḥ ri tĕgalnya,papupulnya salakṣa sinākĕn*146:14:896*

tĕka śīǥra ri jöŋ nrĕpaputra,sira muṅgw-irikaŋ raŧa ratna,I katon ira denya madandan,humatuṙ saha tuṅgul anĕmbaḥ*146:15:897*

sĕmu haṙṣa sirê para sāmya,kadi wanwa tĕkap nira n aṅliŋ,Uƀayê panunasnya macatwa,paḍa maṅdaśamāsa catunya*146:16:898*

<sragđara>:147 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^śīǥrâdandan kinon de saŋ aja marĕka lumrā katon sañjatanya,Āpan prāpta ŋ musuḥ sāhasa waragaŋ ikā krūra tan paṅgalaŋ twas,sakweḥ niŋ śūra śūra ŋ watĕk aja kumutug söŋ ikaŋ krođabahni,gut gūtĕn tan panaṅgĕl trĕṇa hiḍĕp ira riŋ sañjatâkrĕp lumaṅkuŋ*147:1:899*

sakweḥ niŋ strī makādi nrĕpawaraduhitā muṅgu riŋ deśa duṙgga,mwaŋ salwiṙ niŋ raŧâmwat pahula haji lawan drĕwya rakryan suputrī,līlânon tan tinon śrī nrĕpawaraduhitā de nikaŋ kaywa kaywan,tĕkwan salwā nikaŋ papraṅana kalihatan koṅkulan tan pawiǥna*147:2:900*

mojaṙ saŋ mambaŋ iŋ śrī raǥusuta bapa haywâta tan yatna yatna,haywêcꞓâpan musuhtâṅdaśaguṇa ri wilaṅtêŋ mahāpadmasanꝁya,loṙ kulwan wetan akweḥ tumut i paṅuliliŋ niŋ gunuŋ söḥ lumaṅkuŋ,wadwāntâṅhiŋ wijilnya n paṅayat ayat i göŋ niŋ praƀāwanta riŋ praŋ*147:3:901*

ndā nāhan śrī mahārāja magađapati kady-ânĕṅaḥ riŋ samudra,Āpan sāmantarājâkĕmit i sira lawan rājaputra prawīra,ratnâyw-aywan lawan mās raŧa nira kumĕñaṙ katraṅan de hyaŋ aṙkka,śwetākārâhalĕp ꞓattra nira kadi halĕp niŋ wulan tan kameǥan*147:4:902*

paṙṇnaḥ kulwan saŋ aṅgāđipati kadi kilat niŋ truḥ iŋ kāla sanđyā,de niŋ saṙwwāstra muṅgw-î hiriṅan ira pĕtĕŋ lwiṙ hudan tan pameǥa,lāwan mātaṅga meww-îwu kadi gunuŋ apuy de ni rĕṅganya kumram,Aṅlīlânuṅgaŋ iŋ ratnaraŧa sira hanê wwit nikaŋ pārijāta*147:5:903*

nāhan taŋ bāṇa sālas kadi sinaliwaḥ iŋ campakâṅjraḥ sĕkaṙnya,Akweḥ wīrâṅrĕrĕb ṅkāna saha gaja turaṅgâwakîww-îwu lakṣa,honyê wwit niŋ susantĕn raŧa kanaka rinĕṅgan maṇī hīrabajra,Uṅgwan śry-âwantināŧâdƀuta bapa kadi digdāha niŋ kāla sanđyā*147:6:904*

ndaḥ nāhan śrī pratīpâṅadĕg amawa laras riŋ raŧâṅdandani hrū,Akweḥ wadwā nirâtumpuk awuwuḥ i harĕp maṅrĕgĕp sañjatanya,lwiṙ priŋ sālas galaḥ niŋ prajurit ira wahosnyânamaṙ meǥa mĕṇḍuŋ,maṅde rĕs niŋ tumiṅhal raṅin i bala nira n lwiṙ gĕlap tan pawaṙṣa*147:7:905*

lamban loṙ saŋ susenā saha bala kadi siṅhâsigâsiṅhanāda,salwiṙ niŋ sañjatâlas nira pinakaguhā rūpa niŋ hastirĕṅga,wyāǥrâṅjurw-âpupul tiṅkaḥ i bala nira muṅgw-î harĕp sāra śūra,budđinyâsiŋ musuḥ kewala dĕmakĕn ikā pawwatanyê narendra*147:8:906*

nā saŋ hemāṅgadâḍĕm sawatĕk ira kabeḥ riŋ kĕpuḥ rambay akrĕp,tan pendaḥ rākṣasa mwaŋ bala nira kadi dꜽtyâṅuhuḥ sāri sāri,solaḥnya n kādƀutâsañjata baḍama lawan laṇḍĕsanya n pamöki,Agyâmūkêŋ musuḥ sāsinĕsĕb ika turuŋ matya laṅgan ya raḥnya*147:9:907*

paṙṇnaḥ wetan walū mwaŋ karamayan aṅurambat marêŋ siṅkṣapâgöŋ,saŋ pāṇḍyâṅhöb karĕsrĕs kagiri giri baṅun rāja ƀūtâtirodra,wadwā pekâsĕmu preta hana kadi piśācâlapā raḥ paḍâṅhruk,Agyā gyān apraṅâgyâṅrujaka hati nikaŋ śūra sāmpun pinökan*147:10:908*

nā liŋ saŋ mambaŋ ojaṙ saŋ aja mijil ikaŋ budđi kakṣatriyāṅśan,siṅgiḥ kweḥ niŋ musuḥ liŋta kadi jalađi bahny-atrigañcâṅgaluntaŋ,ndātan waŋ mātra wĕdy-âku dan irika kabeḥ mon patambĕḥ samāna,siṅhâṅantî guhā byūha nika surupi wūk hĕntyakĕn hīnaśakti*147:11:909*

nāhan liŋ saŋ narāṙyyātmaja kadi sinaṅa twas nirâsĕṅhit apriḥ,tan saḥ saŋ mambaŋ āpan marĕk añamarani mwaŋ kawī ḍaṇḍanīti,siṅgiḥ yan putra niŋ śakti saŋ aja katĕṅĕṙ krūrasiṅhâwamāna,Agyâmūkêŋ musuḥ duṣṭa kamadan ika śīṙṇnan marapwan panĕmbaḥ*147:12:910*

sākṣāt hyaŋ niŋ đanurweda saŋ aja sakala n pāwak iŋ đaṙmmayudđa,raktākārâkiris wastra nira kilat i sub niŋ praŋ asriŋ larapnya,saṅkêŋ swaṙggânurun cāmara nira kumĕlab roma niŋ saṙwwakadga,saṅhub niŋ sañjatâḍĕm pinakapayuŋ irântuk niŋ aṅdaṇḍa śatru*147:13:911*

hyaŋ hyaŋ niŋ tuṅgaṅan sāraŧi nira wĕka niŋ sidđi sāmbĕknya sidđa,ratnênādyūta de hyaŋ rawi raŧa nira tan manda manda praƀānya,śudđākārâputiḥ roma ni kuda nira pöḥ niŋ praƀā niŋ śaśāṅka,rwaŋ lakṣa ŋ sūṙyyabadđađwaja nira piturun saŋ hyaŋ āditya sewu*147:14:912*

Akweḥ sāmantaputrâṅiriŋ i sira paḍâtuṅgalan saṙggacāpa,pantĕs lwiṙ hyaŋ hyaŋ iŋ sañjata tĕka rumaras māṙ twas iŋ śatru denya,sewu kweḥnyânwam anwam wruḥ akuda kudan iŋ papraṅan wīraputra,jihwā niŋ mrĕtyu sākṣāt đwaja nira dumilaḥ rājasiṅhâmarĕmpu*147:15:913*

wīra prajñā juru dyaḥ nira sama sama ganđaṙwwa denyâmawâmbĕk,Ilwêlwanyânwam anwam saṅaŋ iwu taruṇânaknya mantrī narendra,Apriḥ riŋ praŋ sujanmâraŧa raŧan apupul tan saḥ iŋ waṅśa sālas,wālāṙkkākāra sākṣāt lwiṙ ika n aruṇameǥa đwajanya pradīpta*147:16:914*

sakweḥ kweḥ niŋ rare jro wani hañaṙ anapuk sañjatâgyâmrihêŋ praŋ,rwaŋ lakṣa kweḥnya mĕttâṅuhuḥ aṅayam ayam śatru mwaŋ dèwa dꜽtya,Anwam wruḥ riŋ đanurweda juru nika huwus kāku siṅhanya riŋ praŋ,dewāṅgâneka tuṅgulnya saṅaŋ iwu kadîndrādi milwâmukêŋ praŋ*147:17:915*

Ambĕk niŋ dāsa śūrâpraṅa rumuhun apan kāsatan pwa ṅhatinya,mattā wīṙyyâṅuhuḥ göŋ ni kamanan ika riŋ praŋ murub tan pahīṅan,miṅsoṙ mĕntas mariŋ tuṅgaṅan apan ahuyaŋ kweḥnya sewwaṙwwudâḍĕm,mātaṅganyâpupul mwaŋ đwaja nika dumilaḥ citrameǥâkilat mās*147:18:916*

saŋ jurw-âjâbala rwaŋ prayuta pinakasenāpati prāṇa niŋ praŋ,kapwâdandan rukuḥ mās kawaca minaṇikan lwiṙ samudrāgni muntab,wadwâṅjurw-aprameyâraŧa sayuta gajaḥnyâtatā sewu lakṣa,lākâneka đwajanya n pracalita kadi bahnî sĕḍĕŋ niŋ yugānta*147:19:917*

mantrī rwaŋ lakṣa sāmpun ginĕlaṙ i hiriṅan bāhudaṇḍâṅgakāra,len tekaŋ pādarakṣa prakaṭa kadi tasik rwaŋ puluḥ duṙgga niŋ praŋ,Aṙppat muṅgw-î tĕṅaḥ śrī nrĕpasuta muꝁa niŋ siṅha śāṙddūla śakti,kady-âgastyâṅuyup sāgara wunuhan ikaŋ byūha sāmpun tiniṅkaḥ*147:20:918*

<wisaṙjjita>:148

^Aṙppat ikaŋ waragaŋ sahasa siliḥ usī paḍa nora wĕdi,siŋ sakasambut ikaŋ pinakagada gadānya paḍâmurulu,Umban aliwran arok rĕmĕk iŋ awaŋ awaŋ kapagut kawaluy,dukduk ikā kadi saṙppa pakan aṅin aneka hanêŋ gagana*148:1:919*

wwaŋ bahulâtuha milw-ajurit alara tĕṇḍas ikā ginutuk,Ꜽ putu liŋnya nihan laku walĕsi gutuk buru demu pisuḥ,ndi n wĕnaŋ aṅgutukâṅrahana tan uƀayâku putu prihawak,dwal putu demu palakwan i katigawĕlas tĕṅahê laku ta*148:2:920*

brāhmaṇa wany-apuliḥ galaḥ apupul aḍĕm pinurugnya rĕbaḥ,tan wruḥ aweda kuraŋ kuraŋ aji makapaṅhaḍa timbul ikā,kepwan ikaŋ musuḥ amraṅa paḍa wĕdi yan raḥ ikā mijila,ṅhiŋ pamĕdinya pulut pulutan ika ta hetu nikā malayū*148:3:921*

<basantatilaka>:149 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^nya ŋ sogatânwam ajurit kĕna tan dwa bĕntar,mojaṙ kutiknya ḍuḥ uḍuḥ pukulun laranya,yêka n mijil para cĕṅĕlnya nĕhĕṙ sinuṇḍaŋ,kadyaṅgan iŋ ǥaṭa rĕmĕk tika yan panaṇḍĕm*149:1:922*

śꜽwâpuliḥ kĕna pilis wulaṅun kajuṅkĕl,mitrânuluŋ mpu mapa teku manaḥta maṅko,Eṅĕt ṅhulun ri kita ƀāgya tasim yan eṅĕt,strī ni ṅhulun kita tulakṣaya ko hadêki*149:2:923*

nā liŋ nira mpu tucapa ŋ prajurit siliḥ praŋ,Ārok rinok awuṙ awuṙ paḍa tan wri rātnya,teg tog ḍaḍap nika bubul ginalaḥ tinaṅkis,ḍöhak musuḥnya sinuḍatnya pĕjaḥ kasoran*149:3:924*

gĕntöṙ i śabda ni gubaṙnya baṅun siliḥ prĕp,kady-âcakĕp đwani nikaŋ kukulan karĕsrĕs,kaṅsinya lāgi manaḥ ambĕk iŋ ajriḥ iŋ praŋ,moŋmoṅan aṅgyat anamaṙ macan asriŋ oliḥ*149:4:925*

wadwā nrĕpātmaja tumampuhakĕn gadānya,rwaŋ lakṣa tan kuraŋ asĕṅhit asiṅhanāda,Akweḥ tikĕl tikĕl igā ni lawanya rĕmpuḥ,Aṅrwaŋ pulūḥ uliḥ ikā ri patuṅgalanya*149:5:926*

wīrânapuk raṅin apiṇḍa sahasra wrĕnda,meww-îwu koṭi pagalaḥnya parĕŋ tumampuḥ,gĕk ǥoṙ rĕbaḥ wiꝑala siŋ kinayuḥnya runtuḥ,sawrĕnda māti ginalaḥ sawaneḥ pinökan*149:6:927*

sewwaṙwwudâmana manaḥ mwaŋ ikāŋ agaṇḍi,tandaŋnya tan dwa kinawĕdyan apan karĕsrĕs,hrūnyânrik iŋ gagana söḥ kadi meǥa mĕṇḍuŋ,saṙ cĕb tibâṅĕnani siŋ kĕna tan pasāra*149:7:928*

wadwā narendra malayū sawatĕk watĕknya,peka prawīra kĕna tan dwa yaya praŋ aṅrok,kombak linūd awalikan kumĕlab đwajanya,himpĕṙ nadī kinĕbuṙ iŋ gaja sewu lakṣa*149:8:929*

ƀātriṅśa lakṣa ŋ apuliḥ kalulun kawaṅsul,kālaḥ tibā siliḥ idĕk sinĕsĕb pinökan,rĕmpak tikĕl wiꝑala salwiṙ i sañjatanya,lwiṙ kaywa kaywan asipattra rĕbaḥ kaliṇḍwan*149:9:930*

wadwā nareśwara Inatyan irêŋ kasiṅhan,śakti prawīra parapök i musuḥ yan iŋ praŋ,yêkâpuliḥ tan awĕdî ripubāṇawaṙṣa,wany-ânusup tĕpĕt amūk makasoŋ ḍaḍapnya*149:10:931*

kagyat balā nrĕpatiputra maluy tinaṅkis,Akweḥ an amriha tawan tiki tan kagöman,mĕṅgĕp kadi jriḥ akikib malayū tan adrĕs,munduṙ yayā bala nareśwara duṙbbalâlwaŋ*149:11:932*

tan jriḥ bala nrĕpati đꜽṙyya sahâƀimāna,Apraŋ karuŋ paḍa tumiṅgalakĕn ḍaḍapnya,de niŋ siliḥ pĕḍĕk arok wĕkasan siliḥ prĕp,bĕk tĕg hĕhĕḥ kahĕnĕkan jriḥ ikaŋ lumumpat*149:12:933*

Awrâlayū bala narendrasutâwrĕg awrin,śakti prawīra kapana n kĕna pakṣa pakṣan,hamham tĕkâṅamaḥ amaḥ bala saŋ narendra,Apyak tĕkapnya n aṅucap tuhu siṅha riŋ praŋ*149:13:934*

Ꜽ koŋ watĕk raǥusuta priḥ awakmu maṅko,haywâpraŋ unduṙ aŧawā paṅaliḥ para ṅke,Āpan ya tan hana sihankwa ri kāsy-asihmu,kāton pĕjahmu pususĕṅkwa ri sañjataṅku*149:14:935*

nā liŋ nikâmutuŋ aṅĕmbuli tan panaṅgĕl,kweḥnyâprameya kadi sāgara tan papiṅgir,maṙmmanya wāni sahasâmraŋ amūk tumiṇḍiḥ,dukduk panaḥ kadi hudan ya ta paṅharĕpnya*149:15:936*

Aṅwehi sañjata humuŋ gumuruḥ suraknya,Aṅrok atambĕḥ i harĕp kumucup đwajanya,Akweḥ pĕjaḥ tan awĕdî pati maṅkin embuḥ,lwiṙ laṙwwa laṙwwan arĕbut damaṙ alwaŋ embuḥ*149:16:937*

krūrâpuliḥ bala narendrasutâmuk amriḥ,munduṙ bala nrĕpati śīǥra muwaḥ tumampuḥ,Enak siliḥ galaḥ apan paḍa wāni wāni,söḥ sāhasâṅuḍik uḍik praŋ ikā siliḥ sob*149:17:938*

Enak marâpraŋ arukĕt paḍa nora mundur,rwaŋ yojana ŋ paƀaratan paḍa söḥ gajâśwa,sāmpun rĕbaḥ wukiṙ anaknya watunya kabwaŋ,Akweḥ juraŋ mari juraŋ wĕkasan kahinya*149:18:939*

ṅkānê ruhuṙ gunuŋ ikaŋ praŋ arok siliḥ sob,Apraŋ sumĕṅka tumurun paḍa rota rodra,rĕp tan katon hanan awās tĕkap iŋ himâwrā,ramyâtulis praŋ ika konĕŋ unĕŋ tinonton*149:19:940*

brahmaṙṣi śewa sugatādi ri soṙ anonton,mwaŋ wwaŋ jriḥ iŋ raṇa huwus katuhan wayaḥnya,kweḥnyâtatânudiṅi haṙṣa nĕhĕṙ tumĕṅhā,Akrak paḍâtri gumuruḥ ri paṅadwakĕnya*149:20:941*

rīyūk rĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ rinĕbut sinökan,rīyūk rĕbaḥ muwaḥ alaḥ kasĕsöḥ ikaŋ lor,rīyūk rĕbaḥ muwaḥ ikaŋ kidul alwaŋ akweḥ,rīyūk rĕbaḥ pinĕgatan wĕdi wök ikaŋ lor*149:21:942*

Āḥ uḥ piraŋ juru muwaḥ saka loṙ tumandaŋ,rīyūk rĕbaḥ kidul alaḥ binurunya kagyat,kady-ânutuḥ kalapa denya mamöki tĕṇḍas,nā liŋ nikā hana ta len aṅutū kapūhan*149:22:943*

śīṙṇna ŋ samaṇḍala samaṇḍala konduran syuḥ,Awrĕg paḍâṅhili sira mpu tĕkêŋ kaninyan,Aprakprakan di ta kaki hyaŋ ujaṙ nini hyaŋ,putrī nikā kaburĕṅek burĕṅek tinaṅguŋ*149:23:944*

sāmpun tĕkê ruhuṙ iŋ agra muwaḥ paḍâwrĕg,wwaŋ wrĕdđa wrĕdđa guru niny-aṅuhuḥ sakê sor,pāran pinawrĕgakĕn ā mapa liŋ kaki hyaŋ,wikw-âñaruk wiṣaya rakwa nimitta niŋ wrĕg*149:24:945*

lāwan turun patapan ĕmbuli haywa mundur,Ambĕk ṅwaŋ iŋ kaguru ninyan alaḥ padandan,ṅwaŋ pwâtuhâlaḥ alaḥ ĕmpu buyut ta lampaḥ,nā liŋ nini mpu kabalik wĕdi wök kaki mpu*149:25:946*

wīrâpraŋ iŋ tĕgal ayun paḍa wāni wāni,kontab maṅontabakĕn amraŋ amūk añakra,kedĕṙ paḍâkuliliṅan gumuluŋ raŧanya,lwiṙ nāga moliḥ amĕbĕd gaja matta sālas*149:26:947*

Enak dahat praŋ ika kādƀuta riŋ triloka,Āpan katuhwan atĕwĕk tĕwĕkan paḍâkris,len taŋ siliḥ tujaḥ amatrĕm amajra maṅduk,bāhunya runtuḥ asakit trus aṅĕmbak ĕmbak*149:27:948*

sojaṙnya kātara nĕhĕṙ marahup rahup raḥ,hāmaḥ śiraḥ hurupa jīwamu haywa tâjriḥ,haywâdwa ƀoḥ ndya ta śiraḥ mata maḥ ndya jīwa,bwat kaprawīran iki tan dadi miŧyawāda*149:28:949*

nā liŋ nikā tucapa śabda ri de nikâpraŋ,pyak byuṙ kĕpuk kĕtĕlĕbuk kĕḍĕpĕk kĕtug tog,ceŋ has tĕhap tĕhap aḍuḥ gĕdĕbĕg ḍĕhak syok,caṙccab lĕbik bĕk aḍu göŋ gumĕcik gĕlĕmpöŋ*149:29:950*

nāhan taŋ ĕlwan asĕluṙ karĕṅö karĕsrĕs,maṅde ƀayānaka pasaṅǥa nikā gumĕntĕr,len taŋ mahātiśaya rodra paṅalw-alönya,wīrâṅgĕtĕm nĕhĕṙ aṅohan i meḥnya matya*149:30:951*

^śrī magađāđipa sāhasa mijil aƀimāna nirêŋ palagan,nāgamayāstra laras nira sĕḍĕŋ inayat ƀramita ŋ prĕŧiwī,göŋ swara niŋ tali de ny-aṅin ika kumusuḥ mĕtu kātatakut,hrū nika kādƀuta kātara gunuŋ ahĕlaṙ warakadga murub*150:1:952*

prajwalitāgni cucuknya kagiri giri đūma dilaḥnya murub,sek gumuruḥ paṅawaknya kumisik amĕgat jaladêŋ gagana,boṙ kumutug śara bajra saŋ aja kumĕtug lĕpas aṅdwiguṇa,teg tumibā ŋ wihagācala mati pinanaḥ makĕbĕt kĕbĕtan*150:2:953*

<jagadđita>:151

^muntab krođa saŋ aṅganāŧa kadi bahni maṅaraman i puñcak iŋ wukir,ṅkānê kūwara niŋ raŧâmahayu lañciṅan ira pinisit siniṅsĕtan,hrū lāwan laras adwitīya sinamāđy-amijilakĕna saṙwwasañjata,wuntw-îkaŋ gaganāntarāla tĕkap iŋ panaḥ atip atĕtĕl turuŋ tibā*151:1:954*

dewanyâwurahan tĕkâṅamaḥ amaḥ harĕp amususa riŋ nrĕpātmaja,lwiṙ meǥodaya māǥamāsa sumaput pĕtĕŋ alimunan aṅhudan hawu,saŋ hyaŋ bāywanala pracaṇḍa pamanaḥ nrĕpatanaya dumeḥ kawaṅsula,bĕk gĕk toṙ cĕrĕcĕb tibêŋ bala nareśwara makasulayaḥ kawaṅsulan*151:2:955*

śaktîŋ praŋ saŋ awantināŧa sira mrĕtyu sakala yan i mađya niŋ musuḥ,maṅgĕḥ budđi nirâpuliḥ nĕhĕṙ aṅakw-amĕjahana nareśwarātmaja,rāhasyântya nikaŋ kaśaktin inayat nira mĕtu ŋ ayuđâgnipaṙwwata,boṙ muṅgw-iŋ gaganāntarāla paḍa yatna bala saŋ aja kebĕkan panas*151:3:956*

tan kewran saŋ ajâpan adƀuta kaśaktin ira tumiru śakti saŋ raǥu,rĕp mārāđana pañcabāyu mĕtu kātaratara gumĕrĕḥ magĕnturan,kabwaŋ taŋ śara paṙwwatâgni kadi handaru sayuta dilaḥnya riŋ laṅit,ƀuṙ tog söŋ prĕkĕtĕk nahan swara nikâmĕkasi hurip i mađya niŋ tasik*151:4:957*

maṅsö sāhasa tan surud saŋ anupāđipati manaḥ ira n wanîŋ raṇa,paṅhrik niŋ kuda len grit iŋ raŧa karĕṅw-asĕluṙ i hiriṅan hanê harĕp,pakrak niŋ balasaṅǥa maṅgyat aṅasut ri bala saŋ aja wāni kāmbulan,teg tok lwiṙ garuḍâḍahĕm kĕtug ikaŋ gubaṙ asahuran apratiđwani*151:5:958*

sāmpunya n lumĕpas panaḥ saŋ anupāđipa kadi ruga ŋ aṇḍamaṇḍala,pātālasŧa samāpta nāga lĕkĕṙ iŋ ƀuwana rumĕbuti nrĕpātmaja,porot boṙ dumilaḥ mara ŋ wiṣa sinĕmburakĕn ika hanâtĕmaḥ kukus,byuṙ laṙ lĕs paḍa mukṣa de ni kuku saŋ garuḍa wahu minuṣṭi riŋ laras*151:6:959*

<sragđara>:152 
– – – | – ⏑ – | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – – | ⏑ – ⏓ = 21

^krođâmbĕk saŋ susenā saha bala sumaput kātarâsiṅhanāda,haṙṣa n ton saŋ narāṙyyātmaja pinakamusuḥ kewalânuṅga nuṅgal,hrū hrū śaktîŋ daṅū söḥ linĕpasakĕn irâtaṅkis akrak karĕsrĕs,Āpan pakṣy-âhĕlaṙ sañjata kadi garuḍâneka seww-aṙwwudâhöm*152:1:960*

sumyaŋ sumyak hĕlaṙnya n kinirigakĕn ikâǥāṣa muntab dilaḥnya,sumyuk tan kāwaran dṛĕṣṇya kadi dinukakĕn yan tumandaŋ sakêŋ doḥ,kāṇḍĕg katrĕn dinuk de saŋ aja linud irêŋ cakra puṅgĕl gulūnya,perat sok raḥnya saṅkêŋ ḍaḍa nika kawutaḥ mrĕm tibâdoḥ gumĕntĕr*152:2:961*

ṅhiŋ saŋ hemāṅgadâmriḥ mriḥ apuliḥ i luyuk saŋ susenā katampĕk,sāmpun kempun sinimpĕn bala saŋ aja paḍa krūra kedran kawuṅkus,syuḥ tan sārā sa hemāṅgada mati tinĕḍak bĕntaṙ alwaŋ salakṣa,kāry-aṅlīlā narendrâmanahakĕn irikaŋ sāgarâtyanta rodra*152:3:962*

śīǥra rwabnyâṅgaluntaŋ gaganacara lĕpas māmpuhan matrigañca,lĕmboranyâṅlayaŋ kāƀinawa kadi gunuŋ sewu māliḥ marampak,sumyūk adrĕs tumĕmpuḥ ri saŋ aja kawaluy de ni göŋ niŋ kaśaktin,mawrĕg luṅhâstra de hyaŋ baruṇasuta kaṛĕṣṇya n hilaŋ tan paśeṣa*152:4:963*

saŋ pāṇḍyâmaḥ gunuŋ sāhasa tĕka rumahab de ni göŋ niŋ kamānan,sākṣāt guntuṙ sakêŋ paṙwwata tumurun atūt lwaḥ juraŋ duṙggamâjro,mātaṅga mwaŋ raŧa lwiṙ watu gumuluŋ apan tan pararyan lakunya,krođâmĕṇṭaŋ laras saŋ praƀu mamanahakĕn bahni saṅkêŋ samudra*152:5:964*

lumrā riŋ dik widik teja nika saha panasnyâṅgĕsĕŋ saṙwwawrĕkṣa,sakweḥ niŋ meǥa mĕṇḍuŋ pinaṅan ika huwus hĕnti lāwan gĕlapnya,lwiṙ jihwānya ŋ mahāmrĕtyu dumilata narendrātmajâtyanta rodra,saŋ hyaŋ kālāgni muṅgw-î naraca saŋ aja maṙmmanya mātîŋ raṇāṅga*152:6:965*

<basantatilaka>:153 
– – ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 14

^saŋ pāṇḍya soṙ titiḥ alaḥ malayū tinaṅkis,wadwā nirâlara hilaŋ kahalâwrĕg alwaŋ,Āpan siliḥ praŋ arĕbut hawan ahrit ewĕḥ,wadwā nrĕpātmaja maluy sakarĕŋ mararyan*153:1:966*

saŋ saptarāja sumahab saha ƀrĕtyamantrī,sāmpun sirâṅhabĕtakĕn đwaja śīǥra maṅkat,saṙ sök prawīra gumuruḥ kadi sāgara rwab,lwiṙ siṅha sāṙwwuda paḍâkrak asiṅhanāda*153:2:967*

wīrâtyan iŋ wani hinatyan inĕṇḍĕm ĕṇḍĕm,Agyâpraŋ aṅgĕtĕm atön maṅusap lĕṅĕnya,mwaŋ saṙwwasañjata nikā milu haṙṣa riŋ praŋ,paṅliṅganâṅiṅis iṅis kumĕñaṙ wajanya*153:3:968*

hamham tĕkâmanaḥ añakra bubak sakāmbaḥ,rodrâmupak cĕṅĕl amūk arĕbut kasiṅhan,len taŋ paḍâpapatihan kuḍuwak paḍâkre,saṅhāra kātĕkan i rūpa nika n karĕsrĕs*153:4:969*

śūrâmĕrĕḥ kadi surat tĕkap iŋ kaśūran,kontanya kādƀuta sahasra kuwuŋ kuwuŋnya,Asraŋ kĕtug ni panutugnya ḍaḍap gumĕntĕr,himpĕṙ praƀāwa ni musuḥnya pĕjaḥ kapökan*153:5:970*

munduṙ bala nrĕpatiputra tinūt cinakra,Awrā rinampak inirup pinanaḥ ginaṇḍi,ndātan wĕdîŋ panaḥ atip kadi meǥa mĕṇḍuŋ,tahw-âhudan hudan i mađya niŋ astrawaṙṣa*153:6:971*

wadwā narāđipati sāhasa tan panaṅgĕl,śāṙddūla śakti pinakāgramuꝁêŋ kasiṅhan,mañjiŋ marêŋ pakĕkĕs iŋ wunuhan tĕkâmraŋ,tan sāra hĕnti satĕṅaḥ rinakut kadi bras*153:7:972*

kagyat winūk pinĕgatan tinalaṅkup awrĕg,tiṅgalnya sañjata raŧâśwa sahasra saṅꝁya,kedĕṙ gajaḥnya rinubuŋ dinudut śinūla,lwiṙ waṅkay iŋ walaŋ inīrakĕn iŋ sĕmut baŋ*153:8:973*

saŋ saptarāja kadi saptasamudra muntab,de niŋ kamānawiƀawan pinakaswaƀāwa,maṅsö sahâśwa raŧa wāhana meru tulya,Apwī sakêŋ panaḥ irôjwala mumbul umbul*153:9:974*

meǥodayâmaḍĕmi sakṣaṇa tan paśeṣa,saṅkê panaḥ nrĕpatiputra lawan halisyus,mĕtw-âmusus musus anūb raŧarĕṅga kabwaŋ,lāwan gĕlap makasulambĕṙ anambĕṙ aṅgyat*153:10:975*

saŋ saptarāja saha ƀrĕtya rĕbaḥ katampĕk,bĕntaṙ winūk saha gajâśwa raŧâlaḥ awrĕg,guntuṙ prawīra kumusuḥ katĕḍun marêŋ lwaḥ,himpĕṙ gunuŋ pituŋ atus rĕbaḥ iŋ samudra*153:11:976*

saŋ saptarāja kabĕlĕt wĕkasan sirâdan,rĕp sy-andakâwak aśarīra liman sawrĕnda,saṅkê panaḥ nira mijil tĕkap iŋ kasidđyan,wuntu ŋ naƀastala lawan prĕŧiwī kasĕṅkö*153:12:977*

śīǥrânurumbunuḥ amūk ri narendraputra,Atyadƀutâlimunan iŋ gaganāntarāla,mĕttâṅuliŋ kadi gunuŋ kumukūs umaṇḍĕm,saŋ saptarāja humuŋ atry-asurak gumĕntĕr*153:13:978*

de niŋ maṅadwakĕn apiṇḍa tĕkap niŋ apraŋ,Āḥ āḥ mati sy-aja mulat muliṅā kaṅelan,kedran kawuṅkus i tĕṅaḥ kalulun kapĕṇḍĕm,nā liŋ nirâṅgĕtĕm atön dan asiṅhanāda*153:14:979*

kāla nrĕpātmaja n inambulan iŋ gajendra,Eṅĕt sirâmanahakĕn śara hastiśikṣā,meww-îwu hĕnti mati śīǥra parĕŋ tumĕmpĕk,himpĕṙ namuk tinĕpak alwaŋ atambĕḥ akweḥ*153:15:980*

riŋ sakṣaṇa nrĕpatiputra kumöl ayoga,saŋ hyaŋ smarāntakaśarāgni mijil sakêŋ hrū,śīṙṇna ŋ gajaḥ ginĕsĕṅan paḍa ƀasmiƀūta,lumrā hawunya kumutug baṅun anđakāra*153:16:981*

krođâṅayat śarawarāgni narendraputra,Āpan musuḥ nira suđīra mahāpraƀāwa,maṅsö paḍâṅlĕpasakĕn śara nāgapāśa,tapwan tĕkâpan awilĕt pinĕgat nirêŋ hrū*153:17:982*

saŋ saptarāja paḍa śakti widagđa riŋ praŋ,wil krūra dꜽtya pamanaḥ nira sewu lakṣa,krođâmupul sĕmut amūk ri narendraputra,himpĕṙ grahâṅhibĕki rāt marĕbut śaśāṅka*153:18:983*

siṅhaprawīra saŋ ajâṅayat astra śakti,ḍaṅṣṭrā niŋ antaka minuṣṭi huwus minantran,dewātmakâmawa gadāyuđa mĕtw-arampak,mawrĕg pĕjaḥ siliḥ idĕk para dꜽtya mukṣa*153:19:984*

An maṅkana praŋ ira tan hana soṙ awantaḥ,maṅsö nrĕpātmaja lawan naranāŧa maṅsö,tĕmpuḥ ni sañjata nirâpagut ātirodra,himpĕṙ gunuŋ madu gumĕntĕṙ inadw-atĕmpuḥ*153:20:985*

liṇḍū bĕlaḥ ƀramita ƀūmi nikaŋ raṇāṅga,mwaŋ saptapaṙwwata kadînayun agraḥ olaḥ,pātāla sapta kadudut kagiriŋ kagiṅgaŋ,nya ŋ saptasāgara katumpĕk arok bañunya*153:21:986*

kweḥ niŋ pĕjaḥ saka salakṣa sahasra wrĕnda,len taŋ paḍâmĕkasi jīwa humūŋ aṅohan,meḥ matya maṅrĕguŋ ikaŋ gajaḥ asriŋ aṅgro,Abyūran iŋ ruđirasāgara kombakan ṙyyak*153:22:987*

mātaṅga len turaga nūsa nikâṅalimbuŋ,saṙwwāstra kaywan ika śīṙṇna marok đwajâkrĕp,ṅkāna ŋ prawīra marĕbut ꝑala niŋ kasiṅhan,wetnyâlĕyö kasidĕkuŋ sidĕkuŋ siliḥ praŋ*153:23:988*

ṅkānê pasiṙ pasiṙ ikā naranāŧaputra,Apraŋ lawan ratu kawīśwara riŋ palambaŋ,hrū muṅgw-i kaṙṇna nira piṇḍa tanaḥ kasumpiŋ,tapwan warĕg praŋ alaṅö lagi kombakan raḥ*153:24:989*

rudrāyuđāgni pinasaŋ naranāŧaputra,duṙggānalâdƀuta mijil pamanaḥ narendra,trus riŋ laṅit dilaḥ ikâsĕmu meǥa bahni,lumrâwilĕt latu latunya mahāsurâkrak*153:25:990*

prodƀūta kātara dahat patĕmunya kāliḥ,maṅkin tĕkê ruhuṙ aṅambara kaprahāran,saŋ hyaŋ śiwāṙkka kasuban pan asoṙ sirâgyaŋ,luṅhâhawan kuda lumiṅsiṙ adoḥ maṅulwan*153:26:991*

widyāđarī saha wimāna sumaṅgrahâkweḥ,muṅgw-î tawaŋ wruḥ irikaŋ wani wāni riŋ praŋ,dukduk hayunya sinahāyan iŋ ambĕk ahyaŋ,haṙṣâmapag ri para wīra pĕjaḥ kapökan*153:27:992*

sāmbĕk niŋ onĕŋ alawas tinĕkan rarasnya,kāmīrasâyam ayamanya sĕḍĕŋ ƀinukti,tan lot đumāraṇa panas nikaŋ agnibāṇa,luṅhā lawan priya nikā suꝁa rāmya māṙgga*153:28:993*

saptaṙṣi dewagaṇa guhyaka sidđa sidđa,Anrik hanêŋ gagana sāṙwwuda riŋ sapaṇṭa,göŋ niŋ praŋ adƀuta ya hetu nira n panonton,milw-âsurak nĕhĕṙ aṅadwakĕn akrak ahyā*153:29:994*

luṅhā muwaḥ kapanasan paḍa tan hanâṅher,saŋ nāradâsyaŋ aṅuhuḥ ri narendraputra,Ꜽ putra toḥ bapa wulat ndak apintakāsiḥ,hrūntâgni śakti paḍĕmĕnta sihanta ri hyaŋ*153:30:995*

mwaŋ paṅrĕṅökw-i kita yan pinakāntaśāpa,de saŋ priyambada sĕḍĕŋnya gajendrarūpa,kāruṇya māsiḥ amalĕs ri waluy nira hyaŋ,saṅmohanêkaŋ inajinta kĕnoḥ parīkṣan*153:31:996*

An maṅkanôjaṙ ira śīǥra narendraputra,mārāđanâmrĕta sinrĕṣṭi ri tuŋtuŋ iŋ hrū,sumyuk sakêŋ awaŋ awaŋ kadi riŋ paṅipyan,đwasta ŋ śarânala paḍĕm paḍa ƀasmiƀūta*153:32:997*

saŋ saptarāja paḍa śakti parĕŋ tumandaŋ,kapwâṅhudan hudani sañjata bāyubajra,Atyanta tan paṅupamê saŋ ajâpan anwam,muṅgw-iŋ raŧânudiṅi wākcapalâwalepa*153:33:998*

Ꜽ rājaputra mapa tâṅĕn aṅĕnmu maṅko,Āpan huwus wruḥ aku yan kapalaŋ manahmu,trĕṣṇan purihmu ri huripmw-apan anwam awri,nā pādukaṅku pakacāmana sambahĕmwa*153:34:999*

nāhan wuwus nrĕpati senaka ri twas apyak,pāruṣyaśabda mada tan wruḥ i śakti niŋ len,krođa nrĕpatmaja sumöŋ i muꝁa ŋ kamānan,saƀyâṅucap sahuṙ irâtĕhĕṙ aṅdĕdĕl twas*153:35:1000*

sanwam nwamaṅkwa n aku siṅhakula prawīra,tak nāgatêŋ atuha tiṅhali demu maṅko,sakweḥ ni sañjatamu tan hana paṅgaritnya,byakta n pacuṇḍaŋ i bapaṅku kabeḥ kabehmu*153:36:1001*

nā liŋ narendrasuta śakty-aṅayat warāstra,saṅmohana smrĕti nirêŋ kṣaṇa n ekacitta,nidrâṅaweśa sumaput ri lĕpas nikaŋ hrū,mrĕm saŋ watĕk ratu huwus kĕna tan pasāra*153:37:1002*

sāmānya peka rumuhun para taṇḍa mantrī,mātaṅga matta turagâṅrĕpa tan wri rātnya,mūṙcꞓâturū kadi tasik wwaŋ ikaŋ raṇāṅga,mombak raṅin gajaḥ aǥaṇṭa karaŋ liman ya*153:38:1003*

sāmpun jayêŋ raṇasaƀā naranāŧaputra,saŋ saptarāja kadi māti parĕŋ katurwan,tĕkwan huwus kacuriṅan raḥ i tuŋtuŋ iŋ hrū,yêkā siluŋluŋ ira yan kaparājayêŋ praŋ*153:39:1004*

saŋ hyaŋ sirâjaya jayêŋ gaganāntarāla,mwaŋ puṣpawaṙṣa tumibā kadi kasturi mrik,prīty-âdara nrĕpatiputra sināđukāra,sāmpun maṅañjali sahaṙṣa nĕhĕṙ tumĕṅhā*153:40:1005*
