^sāmpun byakta kacakrawaṙttyan i nrĕpātmaja ri huwus irâmarājaya,nora lwaŋ nira pūṙṇna maṅkana sasañjata nira kadi ṅūni dug siṅī,sakweḥ niŋ bala śūrasaṅǥa humatuṙ paḍa maṅarahakĕn lumampaha,maṅkat śrîndumatī lawan nrĕpatiputra paḍa suꝁa makālihan raŧa*154:1:1006*

tiṅkaḥ tiṅkaḥ i de nirâpraŋ inucap winarahakĕn irê suputrikā,mojaṙ śrîndumatī wagus kita kakâpa hamĕṅan ikanaŋ watĕk ratu,rakryan yêki panahkw-amuṅwakĕna tan dadi wiꝑala lĕpasnya riŋ musuḥ,saṅhārāstra wimohanāꝁya paṅalaḥ pinakakajayaśatrun i ṅhulun*154:2:1007*

nāhan liŋ nrĕpaputra rakwa tadanantara nrĕpati parĕŋ sirâwuṅu,mwaŋ mantrī saha ƀrĕtya wāhana turaṅga warurutĕn aṅob ariṅguṅan,Eraŋ de ni kahīnakāyan ira tucꞓa kacuriṅan alaḥ sirêŋ raṇa,ry-antuk saŋ praƀu tan kaŧākĕna kunĕŋ nrĕpasuta sira waṙṇnanĕn muwaḥ*154:3:1008*

sāmpun mintaṙ adoḥ laku nrĕpatiputra manĕmu haraṇān ḍusun ḍusun,piṅgiṙ piṅgiṙ ikaŋ hĕnū pakapasan pakalayaran apaṇṭa tan parok,Ewĕḥ tan satinūtakĕn rupit ikāŋ aṅiwa hana nĕṅĕn paḍâgĕnĕt,tan tuṅgal kasasaṙ humuŋ siliḥ uhuḥ kapasaḥ asahuran siliḥ taña*154:4:1009*

duṅhus niŋ palapat kahundul aruhuṙ kabuyutan alawas kinatwaṅan,pañcâṙṇnik winĕlaŋ sakanya pinakolul ika tawiŋ ikā hibĕk parab,wwaŋnyâkweḥ mapupul hanâṅiduṅakĕn ri gaway ira nareśwarātmaja,lantuŋ mambw-awaṅînasū nika ginanti saha caru sinaṅgaran hañar*154:5:1010*

ṅkānê soṙ talagâhĕniŋ hana buyut buyut iwak arĕbut walaŋ tibā,piṅgiṙnyênasaban paras hawan ikā siniku siku hinambalan watu,raṅrö kaywan ikā lawan kĕpuḥ agöŋ jaha wijaḥ asĕkaṙ lawan winöŋ,Akweḥ sĕñjaŋ ikâjajaṙ hana kawadwan ana kalanaṅan dinudwakĕn*154:6:1011*

meḥ meḥ rwaŋ puluhaŋ kulĕm lawas irâṅhinĕp i huwus irâpraŋ iŋ hĕnū,prāptêŋ ŧāni ḍusun kaḍatwan iŋ usāna parawaśa rinampak iŋ musuḥ,piṅgiṙ niŋ talagâwukiṙ wukiṙ anak patani nika manumpak aṅlĕnaŋ,ṅkāna śrī naranāŧaputra maṅĕnaḥ kakawin uliḥ irâṅdadak dadak*154:7:1012*

^dinĕlö ku jinarumanan iṅgut iŋ halis i kāla nika wahu mijil,Awuyuŋ miṅay anirirakĕn susup susup ikâsana nĕhĕṙ ahidu,Irikâkw-amĕgati turidaṅku tan wani mulat muwaḥ i muꝁa nikā,sahajâṅhuripakĕn atukup tukup ri pawahinku kadi kaluputan*155:1:1013*

^tĕwĕknya n inalap ni rena nika tan tahu katĕmu gĕnĕp tigaŋ tahun,lipuṙ turida ni ṅhulun mari rimaŋ sinapihan i lawasnya tan katon,kaŧañcana kapaṅgiḥ iŋ yaśa lawan panuluyan iriyâṅdadak lumuḥ,pĕpĕt pĕpĕt ikā ya ta n pinahaliṅsya nika ri paṅawenya ri ṅhulun*156:1:1014*

^nāhan wastu ni de nirâṅikĕt ikĕt winĕkasakĕn irêrikaŋ yaśa,prajñā śrîndumatī sirâmaca kapintiga tama tumurun sirâdulur,pawwat niŋ para pora tan papĕgatan tinĕmu nira sumaṅgrahêŋ hawan,secꞓecꞓā hanan aṅhinĕp sira hanan lumaku ri wijil iŋ niśākara*157:1:1015*

sāmpun rakwa gĕnĕp salek lawas irêŋ hawan asuꝁa suꝁan dudū gawe,lok niŋ māṙgga pasiṙ wukiṙ tinutakĕn lamakan ira macaṅkramâṅlĕṅĕŋ,ry-âyođyānagarī katon hada hadā ni dilaḥ i gupuranya mās maṇik,saŋ hyaŋ sūṙyya niśākarêŋ udayapaṙwwata paḍa nira kewalâhalĕp*157:2:1016*

wrĕtta śrī naranāŧaputra katĕkê nrĕpati raǥu lawan nareśwarī,An sāmpun sira labđakāṙyya ri widaṙbƀapura mamĕnaŋ iŋ swayambara,mwaŋ ry-âlaḥ para nāŧa riŋ praŋ aharĕp rumĕbuta naranāŧaputrikā,haṙṣa śrī parameśwarī makamuꝁa nrĕpati tĕhĕṙ akon anuṅsuṅa*157:3:1017*

wwaŋ ri jro paḍa muṅgaḥ iŋ paṅuṅaṅan rumĕṅĕ rĕṅĕ hanan siliḥ pĕḍĕk,Agyā gyān hana tan tulus sipat ikânahĕlay apan alaḥ girahyasĕn,len taŋ strī malajĕŋ wagĕd wagĕd anaṅga susu nika sinaṇḍuŋ iŋ saꝁī,Akweḥ mādĕg adan tapiḥ miriṙ iniṙ nika nĕhĕṙ akaluŋ kaluŋ sabuk*157:4:1018*

strī ry-âyođyapurī parĕŋ mijil anuṅsuŋ ahayu kadi paṅjraḥ iŋ sĕkar,ndan budđinya kaḍaṅhanan raras i denya mulat inuparĕṅgan iŋ guyu,rūm niŋ strī ri widaṙbƀarājya kadi pālĕman i hayu ni rūpa niŋ rakĕt,Aśrī denya mawâmbĕk abwat atĕrĕḥ tumiru tiru manaḥ suputrikā*157:5:1019*

Akweḥ rājasutā ry-ayođyanagarī mada makapaṅayāya rūm nikā,maṅgĕḥ rūpa nira n panampikakĕnê nrĕpawaraduhitā n pinaṅkwakĕn,maṅke n wruḥ ri halĕp narendratanayā kawĕdi wĕdi ni rūpa niŋ ratiḥ,mrĕm tan löŋ kadi wintaŋ iŋ wĕṅi katon akucĕm i kĕñaṙ iŋ niśākara*157:6:1020*

miṅgut piṇḍa nikaŋ kaḍatwan i sĕḍĕŋ saŋ aja tĕka lawan suputrikā,Āpan kādƀuta siŋ sapolaḥ ira kāƀinawa ri haliwat nirêŋ lĕbuḥ,sakweḥ kweḥ para taṇḍa söḥ parĕŋ anuṅsuŋ i sira paḍa haṙṣa gaṙjjita,Abyūṅan kumisik garantuŋ ira rāmya kadi papagut iŋ ṙyyak iŋ pasir*157:7:1021*

ṅhiŋ dewînalĕm iŋ mulat syapa ta taṇḍiṅa nira liŋ ikânulus dahat,yadyan sewu purī pametana mamaṙppatana hajĕŋ ira ndatan hana,strī sāmantasutā paḍâhyaŋ araras ndan arada kapalaŋ tiniṅhalan,byakta śrîndumatī pakapraƀu nirêŋ śayana pisaniṅū katampika*157:8:1022*

nā liŋnya n paṅalĕm katuhwan apa tan hana kadi sira ratnakanyakā,Āpan saṙwwa sĕkaṙ suganđa makanāyaka pĕnĕd i raras ni rūm nira,lāwan mađya nira pramāṇa ri kĕlab ni lĕmĕs ikaŋ aśokapādapa,śrī śrī niŋ muꝁa śudđa pūṙṇna gumawaŋ tuhu tuhu ratu niŋ niśākara*157:9:1023*

sāmpun śrī naranāŧaputra kalawan nrĕpawaraduhitā marê dalĕm,ƀakty-ânĕmbaḥ i jöŋ narendra raǥu karwa nrĕpatimahiṣī sirâpupul,budđi śrī parameśwarī makamuꝁa nrĕpati suꝁa tumon anak nira,prajñā śāstrawit iṅgitajña wani śakti lituhayu dumeḥ sirâsiha*157:10:1024*

śrī dewîndumatī kinon marĕka de nrĕpati raǥu kagöṅan iŋ suꝁa,lāwan śrī parameśwarī sira makon marĕka nĕhĕṙ aṅol sirâsĕgĕḥ,pāman penan awās marâṅgĕḥ ira de saŋ ahayu paḍa sūṙyyawaṅśaja,wet niŋ haṙṣa lumuḥ sira n marahakĕn pakadaṅan ira riŋ nrĕpātmajā*157:11:1025*

sĕmbaḥ śrī naranāŧa ƀoja ri narendra raǥu winaca maṙmma riŋ rasa,An dewîndumatī kaśudđyana pakānak anaka nira nitya kāsy-asiḥ,rājaswâdƀuta rājayogya maṇirāja pahula nira muṅgu riŋ raŧa,kesî sĕmbaḥ ira pramāṇa gumĕlaṙ hinaturakĕn irê nareśwara*157:12:1026*

budđi śrī parameśwarī suꝁa lawan nrĕpati raǥu tumon anak nira,An poliḥ maṇik iŋ kaḍatwan i widaṙbƀa saꝑala sira rājakanyakā,tĕkwan kapwanakan paḍâparĕk ikaŋ pakadaṅan awilĕt karaṅkĕpan,boṅgan rūpa nirâhañaṙ hañaṙ amantu saparan ira tan kasaḥ tumūt*157:13:1027*

budđi śrîndumatī rĕsĕp makabapebw-i sira puji puji n kināsihan,byātītan salawas nira n tĕka paḍâsuꝁa suꝁan aduluṙ macaṅkrama,mary-onĕŋ ri widaṙbƀarājya tuwi rāka nira sira marĕk manuṅgayap,ry-âyođyānagarī jugâṅinaki de ni siḥ ira ri nareśwarātmaja*157:14:1028*

sakweḥ niŋ makapuṇya rāga nira riŋ nrĕpatisuta paḍâṅhiḍĕp smara,sāmpun rakwa sinūkṣma riŋ pahula mās maṇi rajata suwastra kasturi,Aṅkĕn māsa silib silib wwaŋ irikaŋ wĕṅi pinaran irêŋ paḍaŋ wulan,wāwaŋ mātra karĕṅwan iŋ taṅis arūm winisikan ira māsku cĕp tuhan*157:15:1029*

māliḥ tan tĕka saprahāra ri huwus niŋ ulaḥ aṅaliḥ asriŋ iŋ tilam,maṙmmâṅdūmi karāsikan wruḥ i harĕp harĕpan iŋ aharĕp halĕmbaṅĕn,rakryan saŋ pinakādipūṙwwa niŋ amūṙwwa kataruṇan irêŋ pasaṅgaman,kañcit moǥa kapaṅgiḥ aṅliga ligā kinisapu nira sāhasâwuyuŋ*157:16:1030*

^kakâja winaliṅku tan wruha kitâṅlwaṅa turida ni rāga ni ṅhulun,hanânak anakanku ketaka miṅiŋ sahaja tan inakunta rakwa ya,putiḥ siki kaduṙyyaśaśruti wawaŋ katalu sagalakanta tak wĕdi,manaḥku wani tan surud pwa ya tat antu kita ya karaṇaṅku tan rara*158:1:1031*

Ahum yayi saliŋta māsku n awuyuŋ sapaṅucapan i māsku lampunĕn,ṅhulun yayi turuŋ wĕnaŋ maṅawayuḥ rumatakĕna wilāpa ni ṅhulun,ya hetu ni kakanta tan wĕnaŋ asiḥ lĕwu marika siḥ i ṅhulun yayi,hĕlĕm ṅhulun atĕmwa māsku kalawan kita ratakĕna haywa saṅśaya*158:2:1032*

paran tiki dumeḥ kitâṅucapa maṅkana dali dalihanta keraṅan,katon aṅawatāra denta tan asiḥ pati pati parihāra tan padon,tahâkw-alara denta yan kadi kadaŋ haji para kulaputra kāsy-asiḥ,kita pwa ta bakal ratu syapa ta tan kapanasana hatinya kinwakĕn*158:3:1033*

waliṅkw-asisinahwa tan wĕnaṅa miŧya kita ri rasa ni pralāpita,Apan kita sinamƀawâṅadĕga ratw-aṅalilirana kapraƀun haji,Ujaṙtta kita tan paṅakwa lĕpihanta nĕhĕṙ aśapaŧâṅdilat laṭi,Adalka kita tan panampa ri laraṅkw-apuji puji kita n tuhan tuhan*158:4:1034*

tuhanku yayi ni ṅhulun wruḥ aku yan kita mujarakĕna ŋ salaḥ kĕna,tuhun palaku ni ṅhulun siha ni māsku tumutakĕna budđi ni ṅhulun,rahasyan ibu polaḥ i ṅwaŋ apa tan wuruṅa kahaturê nareśwara,huwus kaka huwus nahan wuwus ira n winuwusan akĕcap miṅĕl miṅĕl*158:5:1035*

taṅeḥ yan ucapĕn paganti saŋ amālihi prĕman i narendraputrikā,paḍĕm pamanas iŋ smarānala ri budđi nira siniram iŋ karāsikan,nrĕpātmaja sirâmriḥ aṅliḥ amĕkul mĕkul amĕkasi turwan iŋ tilam,muliḥ sira bisâpi sāđu kanin iŋ jaja kakuku kinampu kampuhan*158:6:1036*

^jāti nikaŋ caritêṅgal aṅucap adawā n hiḍĕpĕn ri hati,śrī raǥu wrĕdđa sirâṅlwasi suꝁa ni pamukti nirêŋ nagara,Indriya tan wĕnaŋ iŋ wiṣaya ri sira niṙ pakĕnanya kabeḥ,kady-asalin rasa tan parasa wirasa salwiṙ ikaŋ wiṣaya*159:1:1037*

hetu nirâsraḥ i kapraƀun ira ri narāṙyyasutêŋ pasaƀān,kādƀuta de niŋ aṅastwakĕn i sira samâhalĕpêŋ nagara,saŋ ratu nora parāṅmuꝁa sahana nirâwĕdi sāmpun anūt,śrī raǥu paṇḍita walkalađara magawe patapan riŋ alas*159:2:1038*

yāwat alas ƀaya duṙggama paṅulilan iŋ mrĕga siṅha baroŋ,yan sinusuk patapan tĕkap ira paramaṙṣi saƀā wĕkasan,tonĕn ikaŋ wana śūnya tinaruka saŋ uttama niŋ karatun,lwiṙ suraloka tĕkânurun iŋ acala rāmya katon ahalĕp*159:3:1039*

saŋ hulu kĕmbaŋ anak wĕsi haji sira milw-anadin wiṣaya,tan tuna riŋ pariƀāṣa sira dahat alĕp nira yan paṅucap,Āpan inuttama tuwy-apatiḥ atiśayâdƀuta wīṙyya nira,tan hana śeṣa niŋ ambĕk aruhuṙ i huwus niŋ aḍampa wuluŋ*159:4:1040*

kweḥ nira saŋ ƀawika prakaśita milu wikw-anusup riŋ alas,ƀakti tuwin katĕkan tuha masa niŋ awalkala nora hiner,gīta lawan kakawin binisa pinakacaṇḍi nirêŋ nagara,māywan akīṙtti palambaŋ amanis alaṅö hibĕk iŋ patani*159:5:1041*

wuṅkuk aṅambĕkakĕn kawi milu kawilaŋ kawi wikw-alawas,saƀya jitākṣara hāsyakaraṇa pinakādi ni kawruḥ ikā,lumbu waluḥ hajujöŋ rasa ni manis i lambaŋ ikā rinasan,ṅhiŋ rwa tiwas dumadak lagi winaca wacâṅrahatîŋ amaca*159:6:1042*

^wikw-âpa ta ṅaran ira saŋ tamuy pili piliḥ wiku nagara sira,Akweḥ marĕk i sira maliŋ maliŋ rusi rusit kinahatakĕn ira,dondonan inucap ira rāmya rāmya niŋ aṅĕṇḍĕki turuŋ inucap,yapwan binuru sinulagaḥ luput liŋ ira soṙ saꝑala niŋ alayar*160:1:1043*

^yeki palambaŋ ira mpu tapa tucapa rāmya nikaŋ patapan,wāṇḍira sāmpun agöŋ pinakasaƀa saƀā para śiṣya lanā,campaka tañjuŋ aśoka pinatiga tinumpyatak iŋ harĕpan,bwat halu piṅgiṙ ikaŋ talaga ri harĕp iŋ gupurâṅharĕpi*161:1:1045*

sāmpun awās paripūṙṇna sahana hana niŋ waṅunan hinĕduk,bapra lumaṅkuŋ ikaŋ patani jamuṙ alaṅw-aṅuṅaŋ pasisi,tal tirisan pinakādi ni tuwu tuwuhanya huwus pinahat,saŋ para śiṣya paḍâṅigĕl aṅiduŋ i kāla nikaŋ tutuban*161:2:1046*

wet ni lawas naranāŧa lumaku wiku muṅgw-irikaŋ patapan,māṙ kumĕtĕṙ sahana ny-awayawa ni śarīra nirâṅlĕwasi,rūkṣa samāpta ni tĕṅran ira paṅanumānan ira n pĕjaha,kewalatattwa ginĕgwan ira pamariśudđa nira n lĕpasa*161:3:1047*

^sāmpun swaṙggasŧa rājaṙṣi saŋ aja winaraḥ māṙ gupe twas nirâṅrĕs,dadyâṅganyâhaṅan tan sapira lara nira n kantuna śrī sudewī,byakta pwâkālihan maṇḍyuṣa sira sahawan mantuk iŋ swaṙggaloka,tan pātma śrī narāṙyyâja winiđi pinĕgat siḥ nirârāma rena*162:1:1048*

Eṅgal mary-âlarâpan wihikan i puriḥ iŋ janma riŋ maṙttyaloka,An tan sŧitya ŋ śarīrânut i hala hayu niŋ kaṙmma tan sāḥ aṅinte,śꜽwaṙṣy-akweḥ ḍatĕŋ maṅgĕsĕṅi śawa mahaṙṣînutus śrī narendra,byātītan ƀasmi rājaṙṣi Inañut i tĕṅaḥ niŋ tasik śūnya rāmya*162:2:1049*

sāmpun līlā manaḥ saŋ praƀu mari siwuhĕn kewalâṅgöŋ kapūjān,mānak tuṅgal prasidđa hyaŋ atanu maśarīrâtĕmaḥ rājaputra,Anwam prajñā sirâpañji daśaraŧa huwus kaprakāśêŋ triloka,wahw-âṅajy-âhiḍĕp wruḥ ri samaya ni rusit niŋ đanurwedaśāstra*162:3:1050*

^saŋ mambaŋ kawidoṣa karwa jayawaspa suꝁa manĕmu wīṙyya de haji,sedĕmpaty-aduluṙ marĕk siliḥ asiḥ tumĕmu ꝑala nikâmalaṙ malar,sojaṙ saŋ praƀu kewalôjaṙ ika siŋ sawacana nika śabda saŋ praƀu,wet niŋ sāmpun anĕmwakĕn kahulunan satirun iŋ amalaṙ tuhan tuhan*163:1:1051*

Ekacꞓattra narendra saŋ para ratu praṇata paḍa wineḥ anugraha,Icꞓā nora kasaṅśaya prakaśitêŋ triƀuwana sira digwidikjaya,đaṙmma kṣatriyađaṙmma pinriḥ iniwö nira pamahayu đaṙmma saŋ wiku,mwaŋ taṙ kewĕhan iŋ giṇâmayuṅi rāt sakala tuhu tuhu prajāpati*163:2:1052*

śrī dewîndumatī lawan saŋ aja tan bĕsuṙ aṭika ṭikan sirâlawas,śrĕṅgārātmaka rāsikâṅdadi manuṣya sira pinakamaṅgalê dalĕm,hyaŋ niŋ saṅgama pāwak iŋ paṅĕsaḥ iŋ śayana sakala janma niŋ rĕṅiḥ,siḥ siḥ jaṅga wĕlas harĕp saḥ ira saŋsaya lumuŋ awilĕt paḍâlaṅö*163:3:1053*

^gĕrĕḥ wruḥ i masanya rāmya sinuluḥ duluṙ i raras i ganđa niŋ sĕkar,ya hetu nira lālanâmĕŋ amĕŋ iŋ taman aṅĕnĕs akālihan kĕmul,Adoḥ kahiḍĕpanya de ni pĕluk iŋ hawan i siluk ikaŋ latāgrĕha,hanâmbĕk ira mampirâpan asĕnĕt wulat ira muliṅânahā nahā*164:1:1054*

smarāśrama tĕkânurun sawaŋ ikaŋ taman aparimitêŋ giṇâlaṅö,hĕbun hana ri campakanya tumitis kadi lĕṅa waṅi rūmnya kāṅinan,lĕbūnya saḍĕk iŋ puḍak kahudanan mrik awaṅi kumukus turuŋ paḍĕt,tinumpyatak arurwa rurwan iŋ aśoka sinalisiṙ i laywan iŋ wuṅū*164:2:1055*

Ikaŋ talaga mesi pahyas iŋ acaṅkrama mahas ahasâṅañut laṅö,susup susup aśoka kombak i tĕpinya kasarakat arok lawan wĕrĕḥ,sare ni kalakānya söḥ salaga niŋ mĕnuṙ anuru nurū sakêŋ gĕluŋ,kasaṅlad i pasiṙ pasiṙnya śawa niŋ puḍak anak anakan hibĕk parab*164:3:1056*

narendramahiṣī lawan saŋ aja madyus akaramas aśokapādapa,paḍêñjuḥ akase wĕrĕḥ harĕp iŋ endaḥ araras awĕḍak wĕḍak lumut,siliḥ susu susū tĕka ŋ ṙyyak aduluṙ maṅupuk upuk anawwa nawwani,hilaŋ halĕp ikaŋ saroja tĕkap iŋ muꝁa kadi śaśiwimba riŋ bañu*164:4:1057*

ri sāmpun ira mĕntas ahyas asalin jayaꝑala kadi raṇḍi kābunan,raḥ iŋ ripukulâlaḥ iŋ samara tattwa nika sinuji niŋ surāṅganā,paḍâyugala rūmnya jāti kadi kasturi waṅi nika tan gawe gawe,Amānuṣa halĕpnya mūlya sakaḍatwan uliḥ iŋ amarājayêŋ musuḥ*164:5:1058*

muwaḥ sira mahas marêŋ upawanānta ri paraṅan arĕs gunuŋ gunuŋ,mahantĕn aṅuṅaŋ kaḍatwan alaṅö dunuṅan ira sinuṅsuŋ iŋ gĕrĕḥ,sĕlā ni paŋ i cāmaranya hawan iŋ kukus asĕmu walantagâṅadĕg,lĕṅĕŋ watu karaŋnya manda tan awās kadi gaṇapati kāmukan sĕkar*164:6:1059*

diṅaryan asalaḥ ri kāsiḥ ira tan paṅisapu pinarĕk pijĕṙ maṅö,palambaŋ inikĕt nirê hati rasanya pinakapamawan putĕk hati,linambaṅakĕn iŋ wilaḥ pupugan esi kakawin alawas huwus lĕbur,linolya rinasan manisnya winiweka winaca waca de nareśwarī*164:7:1060*

^rakryan riŋ lĕpihan taṅisku k aṅaraŋ waca lĕburĕn i luḥta yan tama,rĕsku n kawruhana n siliḥ kirim ujaṙ tinĕkakĕn i huwusta medĕman,maṅke n prāpta muwaḥ suwalta sipi wiṣṭi nika katĕṅĕrâmabak puḍak,yadyastun ṅwaŋ apaṅgihâwaka palambaŋ ibu kadi wuruŋ hana ŋ ƀaya*165:1:1061*

^nahan rasa nikaŋ palambaŋ alabuḥ saŋ ahayu sira moǥa kasrĕpan,prapañca hiḍĕpan sirê carita niŋ kakawin inayu rāgawādaka,sumaṅśaya ri budđi saŋ praƀu makolaḥ iŋ ulaḥ ika hetu niŋ wiwal,miṅe musapi luḥ nirâṅisĕk isĕk tinañan api kapĕñciṙ iŋ kuku*166:1:1063*

prahāsana narendra rakwa wihikan ri karaṇa ni wuyuŋ nareśwarī,sumatya ri laṅö nira n paṅikĕta ry-awak ira nĕhĕṙ aṅdilat pupur,Amaṅkwakĕn ameri luḥ tuhu tuhu n kawi siŋ ulaḥ ira n tĕkâmanis,raras raras i kapriyambadan irâṅhari hari saha luḥ mawoṙ taṅis*166:2:1064*

yayī mapa panĕmwanaṅkwa kadi māsku hayu saꝑala rājaputrikā,yadin susupanêŋ sahasranagara triƀuwana kapana n kapaṅgiha,hyaŋ iŋ kusuma sūkṣma tan wĕnaŋ aṅiṇḍarat awĕdi tumon kitêŋ taman,tulis kanaka tan kĕḍap kadi kapūhan aṅaraŋ alara n sinorakĕn*166:3:1065*

tĕwĕk niŋ akurĕn lawan kita kakanta karakĕtan amaṅkwakĕn laṅö,hirĕŋ siŋ ulaḥ iŋ karas kapana yan paṅalapana rarasta riŋ prĕman,lulutkw-i jarijinta riŋ kapana yan kawaśa taruhĕn iŋ tanaḥ garuŋ,sĕkaṙ pisaniṅūn panampikakĕna n hana kita ri kisapwan i ṅhulun*166:4:1066*

ṅhulun ratu niraṙŧa kady-usaŋ amak ri papaḍa nika sūṙyyawaṅśaja,siḥ iŋ hyaŋ aṅiriŋ ri siḥta riŋ anāśraya pinupu ri laywan iŋ puḍak,manaḥta kapalaŋ tuhun siha ni māsku pamuhun i kakanta tiṅhali,Unĕṅku ri raras rarasta yayi saṅwa niŋ ajaṙ ajarêŋ wanāśrama*166:5:1067*

Ujaṙ saŋ aja mātra maṙmma rinasan tuna tuna mamĕlas mĕlas harĕp,nimitta ni manaḥ narendramahiṣī wĕdi kaluputanê nareśwara,hilaŋ taṅis irâtĕmaḥ gĕrĕḥ arūm luḥ ira sumĕmu riŋ hudan muliḥ,Aminta sĕpaḥ esi de nira mulat kadi mawaraḥ i hĕnti niŋ lara*166:6:1068*

^lipuṙ suṅsut saŋ lwiṙ śaśađara lumiṅsiṙ karĕrĕban,parĕŋ mantuk hinrĕt ni pakusikan iŋ cāmara mure,I siṅgroŋ siṅgroŋ niŋ watu hawan irâlok trĕbis arĕs,siliḥ tuntun ṅkānêŋ juraŋ arupit awwat wwad alĕyö*167:1:1069*

guhā lambuŋ tistis kalĕṅĕṅan ikâwaṙṇna siluman,Asĕp ri jro lāwan sarasija pamūjā mrik awaṅi,kukus lagy-amrĕg tawwan aliwĕran iŋ ketaka mĕkar,bañunyânūt rĕṅkā ni muꝁa nika sumyuk manutupi*167:2:1070*

sudewī līlâpiṇḍa wayaŋ adĕgan muṅgu ri dalĕm,manaḥ saŋ swāmi prīti maṅudaŋ udaŋ santĕn arupit,Anāntwâṅlīlâñumbana kinĕliran wwe kadi jamaŋ,kiduŋ lālityârūm hawan ira muliḥ rāmya tumurun*167:3:1071*

^An kāmīrasa saṅgamênulahakĕn narapati kalawan nareśwarī,wwantĕn paṙwwata riŋ pasiṙ tĕpi kidul hinĕmukan i kukus niŋ ampuhan,riŋ gokaṙṇna ṅaranya rāmya kahujuŋ saray i suku nikâmĕgat harus,ṅkā n līlâmĕŋ amĕŋ ƀaṭāra mihat iŋ timi wijaḥ aṅalūŋ hanêŋ tasik*168:1:1073*

kāla dyaḥ hariṇī śināpa ri pamiǥna nika tapa madadya mānuṣa,mogâsiḥ wĕkasan dwijaṙṣi trĕṇawindu ri panaṅis ikâmaṅun wĕlas,ndan rakwânta ni śāpa saŋ rĕṣi sĕkaṙ sumanasa hawananya mantuka,ndaḥ yêkī ginawe ƀaṭāra paramāṙŧa karaṇa nika don ikêŋ jagat*168:2:1074*

saŋ saptaṙṣi sulakṣaṇâhalĕp asewa satata sira śuśruṣâguru,ndān aṅhiŋ rĕṣi nāradâṅgupit inuttama tuwi kawi gīta suswara,winwītan lalitâmanis tinĕṅahan raras inapi tinuṅtuṅan laṅö,kālap citta ƀaṭāra mūṙcꞓita saśoka hati nira kalĕswan aṅrĕṅö*168:3:1075*

lwiṙ strī stry-aṙjja kawîṅgitajña para gīta pawulatan i piṇḍa niŋ gupit,ṅkānê tuṅgul ikā sĕkaṙ sumanasênikĕt asĕmu sadak hanêŋ gĕluŋ,kady-ânumpiṅakĕn tanaḥ ri sĕḍĕŋ iŋ tabĕḥ inĕnaḥ i tambaŋ iŋ waluḥ,mwaŋ kady-âsidĕhâṅrĕṅiḥ rĕṅiḥ i pĕs ni lĕṅĕn ika lanā katiṇḍihan*168:4:1076*

srĕṣṭi hyaŋ madanâtikaŋ sumanasa mrik inalap iŋ aṅin huwus lĕwas,kāry-âśâlara piṇḍa niŋ gupit arūm sawaŋ anaṅis inambilan sĕkar,Akweḥ ṣaṭpada maṅrubuŋ milu katūt humuŋ aliwĕran iŋ naƀastala,saŋ hyaŋ lek alaṅö lumöŋ sĕmu nikaŋ sumanasa ḍumawuḥ sakêŋ tawaŋ*168:5:1077*

haṙṣa śrîndumatī mulat ri sĕkaṙ iŋ sumanasa kadi tan pamatyana, 
Āpan de ni laṅönya kāṅinan amet ri sira katĕmu riŋ pasaṅgaman,ndātan wruḥ sira yan sināđya ya ta hetu nira kahĕnĕṅan pijĕṙ maṅö,ndaḥ yêkī karaṇanya śīǥra tumibā ri jaja nira kasuṅsaŋ iŋ susu*168:6:1078*

ndātan wyaṙŧa ḍawuḥnya māti sira denya tuhu wĕkas i śāpa saŋ rĕṣi,mrĕm tan sāra tibê kisapwan i wulat saŋ aja milu tibā sirâpupul,kāliḥ māti sirêŋ tilam tuhun uđāni saŋ aja wĕkasan sirâṅlilir,Akrak taŋ sakaḍatwan aṅgyat adadak taṅis ika ri pĕjaḥ nareśwarī*168:7:1079*

göŋ niŋ duḥka kaƀukti de saŋ aja tan papaḍa wĕkas i tībra niŋ lara,kāla śrîndumatînalap ni sĕkaṙ iŋ sumanasa muliḥ iŋ surālaya,kāry-aṅhol śawa koŋ pinakpak inamĕṙ tinañan ira tĕhĕṙ pinaṅkwakĕn,rĕñcĕm twas nira hetu niŋ luḥ aṅasapta kalara lara de nirânaṅis*168:8:1080*

rakryan saŋ lumaḥ iŋ kisapwan ahurip karika kita mĕne n maliḥ yayi,haywântĕnkw-asuwe pĕjaḥ yayi tutuṙ tutuṙ ibu paṅucap kitê ṅhulun,heman māsku śawanta tiṅgalakĕnanta sĕḍĕŋ ahayu kāsiḥ i ṅhulun,maṅkin rūkṣa tuhanku tan patuluṅan dudut aku ta duluṙ duluṙ pĕjaḥ*168:9:1081*

prāṇaṅkw-indumatīṅku māsku pawuṅu ndak amalaku sĕrĕḥ lawan pucaŋ,Aṅgy-aṅgī saha pastikêbu palakuṅkwa muwaḥ i kita haywa tâsuwe,Agyâweha sĕpaḥ sakê waja kakanta yayi ri kita māsku paṅlilir,siḥ sihkw-î kita tan pahīṅan ibu sugyan asĕbĕla hatinta yan pĕjaḥ*168:10:1082*

maṅke n tan pakakāraṇa ŋ lara patinta pĕjaḥ i taṅan i ṅhulun kita,t asy-âsiḥ pawaraḥ ri doṣa ni kakanta karaṇa niŋ atiṅgal i ṅhulun,paṅheṙ māsku waluy muwaḥ ri śawa rakryan apa hamĕṅanaṅkw-inaryakĕn,suŋsuŋ wāhu ḍatĕŋ kisapwakĕn anakta si daśaraŧa māsku hĕmbanĕn*168:11:1083*

karwânakta karîŋ kaḍatwan aku denta yayi kadi linad twas i ṅhulun,sambatnya n patañê nimitta ni patinta kawĕlas arĕp aṅgamĕl taṅan,yâṅde syuḥ ni hatiṅku māṙ kapĕnĕtan humĕnĕŋ apĕga tan wĕnaŋ mulat,Aṅhiŋ luḥku lawan taṅisku sahuṙ i ṅhulun ibu ri kĕdö nikâtaña*168:12:1084*

yêkī sambat irânaṅis kasiḥ arĕp kaluputan i pĕjaḥ nareśwarī,maṅgā matya matêŋ aṅölakĕna duḥka pamĕkas ira saŋ huwus pĕjaḥ,maṅke n tiṅhal amaspadākĕn irikaŋ kusuma kasĕlaṅan taṅis nira,de niŋ krođa lawan putĕk hati mijil paṅuman uman irêrikaŋ sĕkar*168:13:1085*

Ꜽ koŋ kĕmbaŋ apaṅkwa ko kuṭila kewala ḍumawuḥ amatya matyani,denya n tan rujitĕṅkwa ko pĕjahi tâku saha bala sarājya hĕntyakĕn,maṅke ko tumibê jajaṅku ri hatiṅkw-apa karaṇamu tan pamatyani,sākṣāt ko wiṣapuṣpa dadyan i manaḥ niŋ aṅupĕt agawe prahelika*168:14:1086*

lāwan deṅkw-anahā nahā ri dadimu n kusuma tĕmahan iŋ warāpsarī,saṅkêŋ swaṙgga tĕkânurun harĕp aniwya ratu huwus akīṙtti riŋ jagat,ndātan haṙṣa n amaṙwwa hetumu n amatyani ri kasi kasiḥku putrikā,riŋ śūnya n waluyâpsarī marĕka tan saḥ anilihana saŋ huwus pĕjaḥ*168:15:1087*

nā de śrī naranāŧa mojaṙ irikaŋ sumanasa sĕkaṙ iŋ kadewatan,sakweḥ saŋ rĕṣi śꜽwa sogata kapaṙccaya haji marĕk aṅlawad lawad,mwaŋ ḍaŋ hyaŋ karuhun purohita nareśwara paḍa humatuṙ marê dalĕm,niṙwiǥna ŋ rumĕṅö pawitra ni taṅis taṅis ira paḍa wrĕdđapaṇḍita*168:16:1088*

<jagadnāŧa>:169 
⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^sĕḍĕŋ tinaṅisan narendramahiṣī lumay awĕnĕs apan huwus pĕjaḥ,taṅis nrĕpati rakwa mātra rinĕṅö nira tuna mamĕlas mĕlas harĕp,nimitta nira n aṅliliṙ tutuṙ irâmuhara wĕlas irê nareśwara,Aṅiṅkin atalaṅkup amwit i nareśwara pĕjaha nĕhĕṙ maṅañjali*169:1:1089*

praƀuṅku huniṅan taṅisku rasa mamwita pĕjaha ri jöŋ nareśwara,hilaŋ manĕ manĕḥta tan tĕmu kaƀaktin ika pahalawö kita praƀu,patikta kawĕlas harĕp syapa wiđin haji tumuta rumakṣa riŋ hĕnu,Ahā haji waliṅku rāmya parĕṅâku pĕjaha kalawan kita praƀu*169:2:1090*

narendra warahĕn ṅhulun ri paran iŋ mati tuduhakĕnanta riŋ hĕnū,ndya taŋ hiḍĕpĕn i ṅhulun karaṇa niŋ maluya siliḥ asiḥ lawan kita,Apan kasi kasiḥta ratnawanitā juga tĕmahana ni ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,sahasraśatajanma janma ni patikta huluna pakĕnaṅkwa de haji*169:3:1091*

<Aṙdđasamacatuṣpadī>
– – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 11
⏑ – ⏑ | – – ⏑ | ⏑ – ⏑ | – ⏓ = 11

^trĕṣṇāṅkw-i nāŧaṅku mapôlahaṅkwa,hilī ni luhtâkilayū hiḍĕpku,Aṅrĕs hatiṅku n rumĕṅö taṅista,Ay ay ṅhulun matya tuluŋ laraṅku*170:1:1092*

swāmiṅku nāŧaṅku wĕkasku maṅke,marĕk ri paṅkwanta cinumbananta,Amwīta mūrâku sakê jajanta,lalun patiṅku n lumaḥ iŋ kisapwan*170:2:1093*

yadyan kitâṅjanma muwaḥ dĕlāha,tĕṅaḥku tan sāha sakê lĕṅĕnta,haṙṣanta rokĕn kalawan lulutku,Iruŋta sotpattya lawan pipiṅku*170:3:1094*

nāhan taṅis śrī naranāŧapatnī,rasâmĕlas haṙṣa tĕkap nirâmwit,sāmpun sirâṅañjali satyaƀakti,pĕjaḥ sirâgĕgwan i jöŋ narendra*170:4:1095*

nitya prakampâmbĕt i mađya niŋ strī,praƀāwa saŋ satya matî kisapwan,truḥ truḥ luḥ iŋ śoka hañaṙ tinambaŋ,kĕtug kĕtīg iŋ wahu wahw-apaṅgiḥ*170:5:1096*

ƀakty-âtuhan dyaḥ jayaluḥ tumuṅkul,mulat kapūhan ri pĕjaḥ sudewī,tan samƀawā matya sirâpan anwam,hiḍĕpnya ri twasnya nĕhĕṙ masambat*170:6:1097*

Āḍā tuhankw-indumatīṅku māsku,ṅhulun tuhan pun jayaluḥ kasiḥta,yêki n humaṇḍĕm ri padadwayanta,Asiŋ sapatyanta tumūta bela*170:7:1098*

līlā tuhan pun kawidoṣa winwit,maweḥ tumūtêka pĕjaḥta māsku,Āpan katon milwa nipun dĕlāha,namaś śiwāya n pĕjaha praƀunta*170:8:1099*

patrĕm pabelan wulatîbu yêki,Umigrahâtmā ni manĕḥta maṅke,nāhan wuwusnya trus awaknya mūṙcꞓa,pĕjaḥ tumūt satya ri jöŋ sudewī*170:9:1100*

wahw-aṅliliṙ śrī naranāŧa meṅĕt,Apan katuhwan lara niŋ kapatyan,keṅĕṙ muꝁa śrîndumatī kalĕṅgak,huwus katon līna yayan tinaṅhi*170:10:1101*

Induŋ pawuṅw-îbu lihat kakanta,Ikaŋ turū haywa ginöŋta māsku,Āḍā pĕjaḥ kapwa tuhanku maṅke,dumeḥ si tan paṅliliṙ an tinaṅhi*170:11:1102*

Atyanta sihtêry-aku tan pahīṅan,Ujaṙtta matyê kapatiṅku liŋta,maṅke kitâniṅgalakĕn huripku,waliṅku tuhw-âsiha miŧya māsku*170:12:1103*

ṅhiŋ māsku māṙggaṅku suꝁêŋ kaḍatwan,huripku tuṅgal kalawan huripta,luṅhā pwa jīwanta sakê śawanta,hilaŋ pwa jīwaṅku sakê hatiṅku*170:13:1104*

nāhan śawa dyaḥ jayawaspa māsku,tumūt awās bela tĕlas mapatrĕm,swāminya lāwan tanayanya kāri,laranya tuṅgal kalawan laraṅku*170:14:1105*

nā de narendrâṅucap asrĕt ahrĕk,mawoṙ taṅis luḥ nira maṅkin adrĕs,ndan soca dewîndumatî tibānya,paḍânaṅis rūpa nira n paḍâṅluḥ*170:15:1106*

sāmpun śawa śrîndumatī pinuṇḍut,sakê kisapwan saŋ ajâlupâwak,mūṙcꞓā pĕjaḥ sakṣaṇa śīǥra meṅĕt,tuhun sira glāna masū masambat*170:16:1107*

Induṅku māskw-indumatīṅku paṅher,Aḥ aḥ yayi ndī parananta maṅko,Āḍâlalis tan panahā laraṅku,tuhanku toliḥ kawĕlas harĕpku*170:17:1108*

nāhan taṅis saŋ praƀu māṙ rasanya,tamuy nira prāpta mahāṙṣi wrĕdđa,ndan rakwa saṅkêŋ ƀagawān wasiṣṫa,narendra maswāgata sāṙjjawâtwaŋ*170:18:1109*

kṣāntabya rānak mapa don mahāṙṣi,ḍatĕŋ sĕḍĕŋ niŋ lara tan patambān,saŋ paṇḍitâtaḥ karaṇanya marya,prasidđa śudđāmrĕta saŋ munīndra*170:19:1110*

<bramitākṣara>:171 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 12

^kṣama yogya de saŋ ahulun mataña,ri ḍatĕŋ ƀujaṅga haji riŋ nagara,ƀagawān wasiṣṫa maṅutus marĕka,tumĕkākĕnôcapan irê nrĕpati*171:1:1111*

haji rakwa haywa kalaran dahatĕn,puriḥ iŋ dadi n dadi kalotakĕna,lara duḥka moǥa tumuwuḥ riŋ awak,ya tikā prihĕn saŋ ahulun paḍĕmĕn*171:2:1112*

suraputrikā kĕta saŋ indumatī,suƀagêŋ triloka maṅaran hariṇī,śuci rakwa janma nira śudđy-anulus,sira dewatī niŋ araras pinuji*171:3:1113*

ri sĕḍĕŋ dwijaṙṣi trĕṇawindw-atapa,hana saṅśayê hyaŋ amarendra mulat,I mahāpraƀāwa nira riŋ patapan,tinahā nirâṅadĕha kendran ira*171:4:1114*

Irikā ta rakwa sira saŋ hariṇī,katuduḥ mamiǥnana tapâṅĕnĕsa,I ḍataŋ nirêŋ patapan epw-aputĕk,ƀagawān sirâsĕgĕ sĕgĕḥ ya masiḥ*171:5:1115*

suraputrikâṅucapakĕn hyun ira,marĕk iŋ dwijaṙṣi sĕḍĕŋ iŋ majapa,Amahaywa kĕmbaŋ ira tan kasaha,Atĕhĕṙ manaṅhuluha riŋ śayana*171:6:1116*

<krĕti>:172 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 20

^mawuyuŋ dwijaṙṣi wĕkasan rumasa rasani de nirâṅucap,tumuluy śināpa nira tan waluya muwaḥ i jöŋ surāđipa,jĕnĕkêŋ manuṣyapada kewala matĕmaha janma mānuṣa,Ujaṙ iŋ wiśeṣapuruṣa pratiniyata tĕtĕpnya tan wuruŋ*172:1:1117*

I ḍawuḥ ni śāpa ƀagawān sira kapĕgan ikêpu keraṅan,Anaṅis nĕhĕṙ marĕk aminta tinurunan anugrahâṅĕdö,ƀagawān mulat ri kawĕlas harĕp ira wĕkasan sirâwĕlas,Ikaŋ antaśāpa sĕkaṙ iŋ sumanasa paṅanugrahêrika*172:2:1118*

<bramitākṣara>:173 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏓ = 12

^Irikā n pĕjaḥ ta sira riŋ patapan,tumuluy prakāśa dadi rājasutā,I widaṙbƀa maṙttyapada rājya nira,kraŧakeśikendra makawīja sira*173:1:1119*

pira taŋ tahun lawas irêŋ nagara,mĕtu dewatī nira n arūm rumara,sĕḍĕŋ iŋ swayĕmbara kināṙyya nira,naranāŧa kahyun ira nora muwaḥ*173:2:1120*

matutuṙ sirê sĕḍĕŋ ira n paniwi,I narendra riŋ surapada n patĕmu,dumadak pwa saŋ praƀu hilaŋ rumuhun,dadi rājaputra sira rājasutā*173:3:1121*

Akurĕn muwaḥ suꝁa tĕkêŋ karatun,tĕka ŋ antaśāpa maṅutus muliha,maluyê swajāti nira dewasutā,tumibā ŋ sĕkaṙ sumanasâmĕjahi*173:4:1122*

kaliṅanya saŋ praƀu hade kalarā,kĕna saŋ pĕjaḥ muliḥ iŋ indrapada,Apa tan wuruŋ haji matĕmwa muwaḥ,kalawan sirêŋ amaraloka hĕlĕm*173:5:1123*

nya wuwus mahaṙṣy-apitutuṙ I haji,Ahĕbaŋ hĕbaŋ lara nirâtĕlasan,Umuliḥ mahāṙṣi tumuluy kalaran,pitutuṙ nirê saŋ aja rakwa tumūt*173:6:1124*

^sāmpun śawa śrîndumatī ƀinasmi,murub siluŋluŋ nira ratnacetya,maṅkin prapañca nrĕpati wyamoha,wwaluŋ tahun kāla nira n katiṅgal*174:1:1125*

^Irikā ta saŋ daśaraŧâṅadĕg anilihi kapraƀun haji,budđi saŋ aja suꝁa haṙṣa mulat,I kasiṅha siṅhan ira digjayêŋ jagat*175:1:1126*

tadanantarêrika ta budđi saŋ aja siwuhĕn sirâlara,monĕŋ i hayu saŋ aniṅgalakĕn,muliḥ iŋ surālaya maluy surāpsarī*175:2:1127*

<Atiśakwarī>:176 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑­⏓ = 15

^hana tīṙŧa niṙmmala wĕkas niŋ anindyaśuci,I patĕmwan iŋ suranadī kalawan sarayū,naranāŧa karwa kawidoṣa pĕjaḥ lumabuḥ,muliḥ iŋ surālayapadântya pinaṅgiḥ ira*176:1:1128*

jayaluḥ dadi hyaŋ aṅaraŋ rumuhun katĕmu,tumuluy kataṅgamaŋ anĕmbaḥ i jöŋ saŋ aja,Anaṅis nĕhĕṙ mulat i saŋ kawidoṣa marĕk,Umucap lawasnya mapasaḥ mataṅis taṅisan*176:2:1129*

parameśwarī haji sirâṅdadi dewasutā,surarājya nandanawanāꝁya katĕmwan ira,pinĕkul pinaṅkwakĕn aweḥ pipi wet niŋ unĕŋ,Asalin śarīra paḍa māṙddawa rūpa nira*176:3:1130*

saŋ apiṇḍa puṣpa tamuyan ƀramarâṅarĕki,kamatĕṅgĕṅĕn sira mulat ri papaṅgiḥ ira,kadi tan patĕmwa muwaḥ iŋ paḍa sūkṣma pĕjaḥ,maduluṙ taṅis wara waraḥ nira maṙmma dahat*176:4:1131*

<jagadđita>:177 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^saŋ sākṣāt hurip i ṅhulun kawĕkas iŋ nagara ri sĕḍĕŋ i ṅhulun pĕjaḥ,duḥkantê ruhun i ṅhulun muliḥ iŋ indrapada karaṇa niŋ lanânaṅis,maṅke n prāpta paran tĕmunta kaka de ni kawĕlas arĕp i ṅhulun maṅö,Aṅhiŋ luḥku panuṅsuṅaṅkwa tarimanta kaka wijil i rāga ni ṅhulun*177:1:1132*

Induŋ tan sipi kapwa göŋ i lara niŋ huwus atĕmu rinudđa niŋ wiđi,saŋsāraṅkw-aṅajap tawaŋ karaṇa niŋ ḍatĕŋ i kita katalyan iŋ hayu,ndan maṅke n tĕka śūnyahasta yayi kewala ḍatĕŋ aṅisapw-aṅolakĕn,Aṅhiŋ kūŋ uliḥ i ṅhulun saha taṅiskw-asĕkĕl i hati māsku sanmatan*177:2:1133*

tonton ku n rumuhun pĕjaḥ karika hetu niŋ anĕmu larônĕŋ antya ya,tontonĕn taṅan i ṅhulun ri kita yan panipati nĕhĕṙ aṅdĕlö mata,mwaŋ tan kram waja ni ṅhulun kadi humeṙ kita masuṅa sĕpaḥ sakê waja,milw-âkuŋ tĕṅaḥ i ṅhulun kaka paṅawruhana lagi kaluṅsuran tapiḥ*177:3:1134*

hāḥ swāmiṅkw-alawas dahat kita tan antuk iŋ amarapadâparan hiner,mūṙcꞓâpriḥ ṅwaŋ aṅantyakĕn ri ḍatĕṅanta tumutura ri līna ni ṅhulun,trĕṣṇantê suꝁa niŋ hanêŋ kabinihajyan amuhara lalista ri ṅhulun,deṅkw-ânaṙkka ri tan tĕkanta tumuluy piliḥ aharĕp i patya ni ṅhulun*177:4:1135*

Aṅkĕn rātri ri tambwaŋ iŋ wulan awā ṅhulun aṅaraŋ anaṅhulun puḍak,de ny-ûnĕṅkw-i kitâṅutus taḍahasiḥ tumĕkakĕna taṅisku riŋ kulĕm,kālaṅkyaŋ jarumankwa riŋ masa kapat ḍatĕṅa ri kita kāla niŋ rĕmĕŋ,heṙ herĕn ri tĕkanta kewala kitâtiśaya kadi hinundaŋ iŋ patĕr*177:5:1136*

lwaḥ luḥ wāđaka ni ṅhulun drĕs i hilī nika kadi minahâmĕgat hawan,wwat goṅgaŋnya gaḍuŋ mure sĕkaṙ ika mrik awaṅi sinaluṇḍiŋ iŋ puḍak,luṅgaḥ niŋ katiraḥ lumuŋ pinakagĕgwan i tĕka niŋ aṅin kadînayun,Aṅlaṅwākĕn ululnya puṣpa winaṅun hinĕduk i hĕlaṙ iŋ mađubrata*177:6:1137*

ṅkâku n ton kakawinta riŋ wĕla wĕlaḥ paḍa paḍa tinatā limaŋ wiji,wwantĕn ṣaṭpada kanyakânaṅis i saṇḍiŋ ika karaṇa ni ṅhulun mulat,haṙṣaṅkw-ânuculî talinya tumuluy kinisapu hiniḍĕp hiḍĕp kita,tan pātmâkw-amacânaṅis katitisan luḥ araras ikaŋ akṣarâmanis*177:7:1138*

<nawahaṙṣa>:178 
⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 19

^saŋ apiṇḍa mađubrata taruṇa manĕḥta sawaŋ salaga,winaraŋ waraŋ iŋ masa kapat alaṅö kararas rarasan,Irikā ta tuwuhkw-asana wawaŋ alum kita kāry-anaṅis,maluyā sahanêŋ katiga kaka maran ṅwaŋ atĕmwa muwaḥ*178:1:1139*

kaka yan kita lūha niŋ amaca wilāpa suwal piniṅit,tĕmahaṅkwa taṅisnya winuni sinamaṙ samaṙ iŋ kakawin,yan adadyana ketaka kita tĕmahaṅkwa tulisnya ṭikā,kaka de ni laraṅkwa pinasahakĕn iŋ wiđi niṣkaraṇa*178:2:1140*

<jagadđita>:179 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^wruḥ kw-î tan wĕnaṅanta đāraka kumölakĕna lulut unĕŋta ri ṅhulun,wwat niŋ lwaḥ luḥ ariṅguṅan hawana saŋ praƀu tumutuṙ i līna ni ṅhulun,tiṅhaltê lara ni ṅhulun winaṅun akṣara rasa kakawin pralāpita,byaktâdadyana luḥ tutuṙtta ri hatinta yak amaca ri lambaŋ i ṅhulun*179:1:1141*

saŋ kārî nagari ndi siḥta winaliṅku tumuta saparanku tan saha,ry-antuk ni ṅhulun iŋ surālaya tĕwĕk niŋ anaṅis apasaḥ lawan kita,kālanta n panulis karas mwaŋ aṅikiṙ tanaḥ i kuku ya konĕŋ i ṅhulun,kāpan swāmi muwaḥ ṅhulun warahananta kakawin anĕhĕṙ pinaṅkwakĕn*179:2:1142*

lāwan pājara ni ṅhulun hana gaḍuŋ lumuŋ awaraḥ i tiṅkaḥ iŋ hĕnū,makweḥ luŋnya hanan paṅulwan aṅaloṙ hana lumuŋ aṅidul ya tan tutĕn,wwantĕn luṅgaḥ ikâṅawetan amĕnĕṙ sĕkaṙ ika kadi kĕmbaŋ iŋ laṅit,Aṅhiŋ tūtakĕnanta riŋ gagana nandanawana tinujunya nora len*179:3:1143*

<girisa>:180 
⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – – – | – – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 16

^yayi rasa ni palambaṅtêkī māṙ ṅhulun amaca,muwaḥ inĕnahakĕnku ry-uṅgwanyâlawas alaṅö,lumaku laku tumoliḥ rākantêbu karakĕtan,pawaraḥ ika tinūtkw-induŋ maṅke n tĕka ri kita*180:1:1144*

tarima yayi paṅolkw-î rakryan kuṅkw-amarĕpĕhi,syapa parana ni rāgaṅku n haṙṣaṅku katulaka,hĕnĕṅakĕna taṅankw-âmet met moǥa kajĕnĕkan,sapamalaku niŋ onĕŋ rakryan haywa pinihĕran*180:2:1145*

<jagadđita>:181 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^rakryan haywa kitâṅhĕmū guyu nĕhĕṙ miṅay amiru mirū tapiḥ lukar,rĕñcĕm twasku mulat raras paran ikā ṅaran ika lĕṅĕŋ aṅligā tĕṅaḥ,ndan mogârĕṅu tan tulus waśa kita n paṅutu taṅan inambilan tapiḥ,māskw-akras karikā manis manis i denta lumiriŋ anamaṙ linurwakĕn*181:1:1146*

<kilayu anĕḍĕŋ>:182 
– – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏓ = 22

^nāhan paṅucap ucap irêŋ taman sinĕlaṅan prĕman uwat iŋ akuŋ,saswaṙgga paḍa suꝁa tumon i rāmya ni papaṅgiḥ ira siliḥ asiḥ,ṅūnî sĕḍĕŋ ira ratu cakrawaṙtti suꝁa niŋ ratu tinĕmu nira,maṅke n suꝁa riŋ amaraloka maṅdaśaguṇê suꝁa nira mawa rāt*182:1:1147*

riŋ nandanawana sira karwa raśmi niŋ asaṅgama hinarĕp ira,riŋ pūṙṇnama mijil amaḍaŋ wulan sira marêŋ taman aṭika ṭikan,riŋ swapna tuwi sira yayâmanĕḥ manĕhi rāga nira tan awanĕḥ,kiŋkiŋ ni hati nira miniśra kāraṇa ni tuṅgal i turida nira*182:2:1148*

riŋ nandanawana wĕkas iŋ kaŧā sumanasāntaka riŋ aji raǥu,pinrākrĕta rasa kakawin tinīṙŧakĕn i jöŋ nrĕpati rasa laṅö,siḥ kāraṇa nira n anumāna mājara rikaŋ paṅikĕt amanisa,śudđāmrĕta waraḥ ira hetu niŋ kadi gaḍuŋ lumuŋ anĕmu kapat*182:3:1149*

<jagadđita>:183 
– – – | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | ⏑ ⏑ ⏑ | – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓ = 23

^sāmpun kekĕtan iŋ kaŧā sumanasāntaka winaṅun ahĕmbanan laṅö,kāla śrîndumatī lawan saŋ aja mantuk iŋ amarapadâkurĕn muwaḥ,yêkī tambay ira mpu monaguṇa milw-aṅikĕt ikĕt amaṙṇnana ŋ kaŧā,ṅhiŋ śrī waṙṣajaya prasidđa guru niŋ guru laǥu sira hantusâmuruk*183:1:1150*

dīṙgǥāyuṣya janapriyā saŋ amacâmahiḍĕpakĕna saŋ harĕp wruha,niṙwiǥnâstu saŋ aṅrĕṅö sakaharĕp nira katĕkana moǥa sanmatan,salwiṙ saŋ makapustaka ŋ sumanasāntaka kasihana de nareśwara,sidđi mpuṅkw-i garuŋ tirun saŋ anulis katĕkana sasināđya saŋ wiku*183:2:1151*
